### [1] [Phonological distances for linguistic typology and the origin of Indo-European languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11565)
*Marius Mavridis,Juan De Gregorio,Raul Toral,David Sanchez*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过信息论框架分析音素序列的二阶马尔可夫链模型，发现短程音素依赖关系能够编码语言亲缘性的大规模模式，并基于此量化了67种现代语言的语音距离，成功重建了主要语系并揭示了接触引发的趋同现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索短程音素依赖关系（short-range phoneme dependencies）如何编码语言亲缘性的大规模模式，这对定量类型学（quantitative typology）和演化语言学（evolutionary linguistics）具有直接意义。

Method: 采用信息论框架（information-theoretic framework），将音素序列建模为二阶马尔可夫链（second-order Markov chains）来捕捉语音系统的统计相关性，并利用包含音素发音特征的距离度量（distance metric）从多语言平行语料库中量化67种现代语言的距离。

Result: 生成的语音距离矩阵（phonological distance matrix）成功重建了主要语系，揭示了接触引发的趋同（contact-induced convergence）特征，并显示出与地理距离的明显相关性，从而能够为印欧语系限定一个合理的起源区域，与草原假说（Steppe hypothesis）一致。

Conclusion: 短程音素依赖关系可作为语言亲缘性的有效指标，基于语音距离的分析方法能够重建语言演化关系并揭示地理接触效应，为印欧语系起源的草原假说提供了支持证据。

Abstract: We show that short-range phoneme dependencies encode large-scale patterns of linguistic relatedness, with direct implications for quantitative typology and evolutionary linguistics. Specifically, using an information-theoretic framework, we argue that phoneme sequences modeled as second-order Markov chains essentially capture the statistical correlations of a phonological system. This finding enables us to quantify distances among 67 modern languages from a multilingual parallel corpus employing a distance metric that incorporates articulatory features of phonemes. The resulting phonological distance matrix recovers major language families and reveals signatures of contact-induced convergence. Remarkably, we obtain a clear correlation with geographic distance, allowing us to constrain a plausible homeland region for the Indo-European family, consistent with the Steppe hypothesis.

</details>

# math.QA [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Bicovariant Codifferential Calculi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12493)
*Andrzej Borowiec,Patryk Mieszkalski*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一种研究一阶余微分计算（FOCCs）的技术，将分类问题简化为对通用双余模中子双余模的分类，特别关注双协变余微分计算在Hopf代数上的分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于Doi和Quillen在循环上同调背景下提出的一阶余微分计算（FOCCs）。论文旨在发展系统方法研究这类结构，特别关注双协变余微分计算在Hopf代数上的分类问题。

Method: 方法包括：将给定余代数上FOCCs的分类简化为通用双余模中子双余模的分类；利用一维生成空间（singletons）辅助分类；将双协变余微分计算的分类进一步简化为Yetter-Drinfeld（Y-D）子模的分类。

Result: 研究发现存在两种相互对偶的Y-D结构：一种用于Woronowicz构造双协变微分计算，另一种用于FOCCs且与量子切空间的Woronowicz构造相关。结果表明这类余微分计算更适合Drinfeld-Jimbo型量子包络代数，并与量子李代数和量子向量场建立联系。

Conclusion: 论文建立了FOCCs与Woronowicz构造之间的对偶关系，表明余微分计算更适合量子包络代数，而微分计算更适合矩阵量子群。通过多个示例展示了具体的分类结果。

Abstract: We develop a technique for studying first-order codifferential calculi (FOCCs) initiated by Doi and Quillen in the context of cyclic cohomology. Their classification, for a given coalgebra, reduces to the classification of subbicomodules in the universal bicomodule. For completing this task, the role of one-dimensional generating spaces (a.k.a. singletons) is found to be useful. We are particularly interested in classifying bicovariant codifferential calculi, which we define over Hopf algebras. This, in turn, can be reduced to classifying Yetter-Drinfeld (Y-D) submodules. In fact, there are two, mutually dual, Y-D structures on arbitrary Hopf algebra: one used by Woronowicz for constructing bicovariant differential calculi, and the another used here for FOCCs and shown to be related with Woronowicz construction of quantum tangent space. This argues that such codifferential calculi are better suited to Drinfeld-Jimbo type quantized enveloping algebras, as they are dual to Woronowicz' bicovariant calculi over matrix quantum groups. Relations with quantum Lie algebras and quantum vector fields are also shown. Some classification results are presented in numerous examples.

</details>

# hep-lat [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Scalable Generative Sampling and Multilevel Estimation for Lattice Field Theories Near Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10209)
*A. Singha,J. Kauffmann,E. Cellini,K. Jansen,S. Nakajima*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种受重整化群启发的多尺度生成采样器，用于解决临界点附近晶格场论的采样难题。该方法通过粗粒化到精细化的层次结构建模玻尔兹曼分布，显著降低了自相关时间，并支持无偏的多级蒙特卡洛方差缩减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临界点附近的晶格场论采样受到临界慢化（critical slowing down）的严重阻碍，导致标准马尔可夫链方法在大晶格体积下效率急剧下降。这促使研究者开发能够有效处理多尺度物理的采样方法。

Method: 方法引入了一个受重整化群（renormalization-group）启发的多尺度生成采样器，通过从粗粒化到精细化的层次结构建模玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）。每个层级使用条件高斯混合模型（conditional Gaussian mixture model）捕捉新引入变量对已采样粗场的局部依赖，同时使用掩蔽连续归一化流（masked continuous normalizing flow）精化剩余条件结构。

Result: 对于二维标量φ⁴理论（scalar φ⁴ theory）在临界点的情况，该方法在大量积下实现了比混合蒙特卡洛（Hybrid Monte Carlo, HMC）小数个数量级的积分自相关时间（integrated autocorrelation times）。相对于其他生成基线方法，保持了较高的重要性采样效率，并再现了与长时间HMC模拟在统计上一致的无偏物理可观测量。

Conclusion: 该多尺度生成采样器架构通过精确保留粗场在精化过程中的信息，无需额外计算成本即可提供精确限制映射，并直接支持无偏的多级蒙特卡洛（Multilevel Monte Carlo, MLMC）方差缩减。这为解决临界慢化问题提供了一种有效的生成式采样框架。

Abstract: Sampling lattice field theories near criticality is severely hindered by critical slowing down, which makes standard Markov chain methods increasingly inefficient at large lattice volumes. We introduce a multiscale generative sampler, inspired by renormalization-group ideas, that models the Boltzmann distribution through a coarse-to-fine hierarchy across length scales. At each level, a conditional Gaussian mixture model captures the main local dependence of newly introduced variables on the already-sampled coarse field, while a masked continuous normalizing flow refines the remaining conditional structure. Coarse levels encode the dominant long-wavelength modes, and finer levels progressively add short-distance fluctuations. In addition, because the architecture preserves coarse fields exactly during refinement, it provides exact restriction maps at no additional computational cost and directly enables unbiased Multilevel Monte Carlo (MLMC) variance reduction. For the two-dimensional scalar $φ^4$ theory at criticality, the method achieves integrated autocorrelation times orders of magnitude smaller than Hybrid Monte Carlo (HMC) on large volumes, maintains high importance-sampling efficiency relative to other generative baselines, and reproduces unbiased physical observables in statistical agreement with long HMC simulations.

</details>

### [4] [Explosive Synchronization and Magnetic Chimeras via the Simplicial Bridge in Helimagnetic Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10773)
*Alok Yadav*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 该研究将螺旋磁体连续模型扩展至包含多自旋双二次交换，通过"单纯形桥"映射揭示高阶三体相位耦合引发爆炸性一级同步相变，并在二维蜂窝晶格中观测到宏观磁嵌合态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁材料中拓扑缺陷的宏观动力学通常采用成对相互作用建模，普遍产生连续热力学相变。本研究旨在探索高阶相互作用对相变特性的影响。

Method: 扩展螺旋磁体（helimagnetic）连续模型以包含多自旋双二次交换（multi-spin biquadratic exchange），运用Karpman-Solov'ev绝热微扰理论将非线性Landau-Lifshitz偏微分方程映射到在单纯复形（simplicial complex）上运行的广义Kuramoto网络。

Result: 高阶三体相位耦合（triadic phase couplings）诱导爆炸性一级同步相变，伴随巨大的双稳态滞后回线（bistable hysteresis loop）。在二维蜂窝晶格（bipartite honeycomb lattices）的谱分析显示几何阻挫（geometric frustration）的规避以及宏观磁嵌合态（magnetic chimera states）的出现。

Conclusion: 这些状态在强关联范德瓦尔斯异质结（van der Waals heterostructures）中具有物理表现，并在可重构磁振子储备计算（reconfigurable magnonic reservoir computing）方面具有潜在应用前景。

Abstract: The macroscopic dynamics of topological defects in magnetic materials are traditionally modeled using pairwise interactions, universally yielding continuous thermodynamic phase transitions. In this work, we extend the helimagnetic continuum model to include multi-spin biquadratic exchange. Using the Karpman-Solov'ev adiabatic perturbation theory, we rigorously map the non-linear Landau-Lifshitz partial differential equations onto a generalized Kuramoto network operating on a simplicial complex. This "Simplicial Bridge" reveals that higher-order, triadic phase couplings induce explosive, first-order synchronization transitions characterized by a massive bistable hysteresis loop. Furthermore, spectral analysis of these networks on bipartite honeycomb lattices demonstrates the evasion of geometric frustration and the emergence of macroscopic magnetic chimera states-spontaneous spatial domains of coexisting frozen and fluctuating spin textures. We discuss the physical manifestation of these states in strongly correlated van der Waals heterostructures and their potential application in reconfigurable magnonic reservoir computing.

</details>


<div id='math.AG'></div>

# math.AG [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Geometry of the Donaldson--Friedman Pushout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11719)
*Amedeo Altavilla,Maurício Corrêa*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文研究Donaldson-Friedman构造中奇异中心纤维的代数几何结构，将其视为两个爆破twistor空间沿例外二次曲面的Ferrand推出（pushout），并建立了半稳定光滑化的分量专业化公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究连通和（connected sums）的twistor空间在Donaldson-Friedman构造中出现的奇异中心纤维（singular central fibre），理解其代数几何结构及其在半稳定光滑化（semistable smoothings）中的行为。

Method: 将奇异中心纤维视为两个爆破twistor空间沿例外二次曲面（exceptional quadric）的Ferrand推出，使用运算Chow环（operational Chow ring）的等化子（equalizer）描述其结构，并通过Kato-Nakayama空间解释局部半稳定方程。

Result: 明确描述了运算Chow环作为两个分支Chow环的等化子，推导了半稳定光滑化的分量专业化公式（componentwise specialization formula），获得了跨双重轨迹（double locus）的曲面刚性粘合约束，并将固定相位边界（fixed-phase boundary）识别为例外二次曲面上的自然圆丛。

Conclusion: 该代数几何形式体系应用于源自Ward和Hartshorne-Serre数据的丛（bundles），证明了第二陈类循环（second Chern cycle）和极化电荷（polarized charge）在推出上的可加性结果（additivity results）。

Abstract: We study the singular central fibre arising in the Donaldson--Friedman construction for twistor spaces of connected sums, viewing it as a Ferrand pushout of two blown-up twistor spaces along the exceptional quadric. We describe its operational Chow ring explicitly as an equalizer of the Chow rings of the two branches, derive a componentwise specialization formula for semistable smoothings, and obtain rigid gluing constraints for surfaces across the double locus. We then interpret the local semistable equation through the Kato--Nakayama space, identifying the fixed-phase boundary as a natural circle bundle over the exceptional quadric and relating it to the topology of the neck. Finally, we apply this algebro-geometric formalism to bundles arising from Ward and Hartshorne--Serre data, proving additivity results for the second Chern cycle and for the polarized charge across the pushout.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.supr-con'></div>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Decoding Superconductivity in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7-δ}$ Thin Films via Ozone-Driven Structure and Oxidation Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09807)
*Mathieu Flavenot,Hoshang Sahib,Jérôme Robert,Marc Lenertz,Gilles Versini,Laurent Schlur,Alexandre Gloter,Nathalie Viart,Daniele Preziosi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）和电子能量损失谱（EELS）对La₃Ni₂O₇₋δ薄膜进行结构表征，揭示了氧化学计量、外延应变和结构基元对稳定镍酸盐超导相的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ruddlesden-Popper La₃Ni₂O₇（LNO327）在高压下的超导发现挑战了镍酸盐超导限于3d⁹电子构型和平面配位的共识。然而，由于LNO327相具有亚稳态特性，稳定超导所需的结构和电子先决条件仍不清楚。

Method: 采用扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）结合电子能量损失谱（EELS）对脉冲激光沉积在SrLaAlO₄衬底上生长的La₃Ni₂O₇₋δ外延薄膜进行详细结构研究。通过不同后处理条件调控薄膜的超导性能。

Result: 研究发现薄膜的超导特性随不同后处理条件而变化。通过将丰富的堆垛多型体（stacking polymorphs）与输运行为相关联，建立了理解双层镍酸盐薄膜中亚稳超导相的理论框架。

Conclusion: 研究强调了氧化学计量（oxygen stoichiometry）均匀性、外延应变（epitaxial strain）和结构基元（structural motif）在稳定超导中的关键作用，为设计常压超导镍酸盐提供了明确路径。

Abstract: The discovery of superconductivity in bulk Ruddlesden-Popper La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$(LNO327) under high hydrostatic pressure has redefined the recent experimental consensus that nickelate superconductivity is restricted to systems with a $3d^9$ electronic configuration and square-planar coordination. However, the structural and electronic prerequisites for stabilizing superconductivity, whether under pressure or at ambient conditions in the case of thin films, remain poorly understood, largely due to the metastable nature of the LNO327 phase. Here, we present a detailed structural study of epitaxial La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7-δ}$ thin films by using scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) combined with electron energy loss spectroscopy (EELS). Grown via pulsed laser deposition onto SrLaAlO$_4$ substrates, those films exhibit distinct superconducting properties as a function of the different post-annealing conditions used. By correlating the rich landscape of stacking polymorphs with transport behavior, this work establishes a framework for understanding the metastable superconducting phase in bilayer nickelate thin films. Our findings underscore the critical role of homogeneity in oxygen stoichiometry, epitaxial strain and structural motif in stabilizing superconductivity, offering a clear pathway for designing ambient-pressure superconducting nickelates.

</details>


### [7] [Strong Electron-Phonon Coupling and Multiband Superconductivity in Hexagonal BP3 Monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10026)
*Jakkapat Seeyangnok,Udomsilp Pinsook*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算结合各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg理论，研究发现六方BP3单层具有稳定的结构、多带金属态和较强的电子-声子耦合，其超导转变温度Tc = 9.7 K，表现为无节点但各向异性的多带二维超导体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索六方BP3单层的结构、电子和超导特性，为理解低维系统中轨道杂化在电子-声子介导超导中的作用提供见解。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg理论，通过声子色散分析和从头算分子动力学模拟验证结构稳定性。

Result: BP3单层呈现稳定的轻微弯曲结构，具有多带金属态，电子-声子耦合常数λ = 1.59，超导转变温度Tc = 9.7 K，超导能隙呈现无节点但各向异性特征，具有约2.25和1.74 meV两个不同能隙值。

Conclusion: BP3单层被确认为强耦合多带二维超导体，研究结果为理解低维系统中轨道杂化在电子-声子介导超导中的作用提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate the structural, electronic, and superconducting properties of a hexagonal BP3 monolayer using first-principles calculations combined with anisotropic Migdal-Eliashberg theory. The optimized structure exhibits a stable, slightly buckled configuration, as confirmed by phonon dispersion analysis and ab initio molecular dynamics simulations. The phonon spectrum indicates high-frequency vibrational modes associated with B-P bonding. Electronic band structure calculations reveal a multiband metallic state, with states near the Fermi level predominantly derived from pz orbitals of both boron and phosphorus atoms, forming two distinct Fermi surface sheets. The electron-phonon coupling is relatively strong, with a total coupling constant of lambda = 1.59, dominated by low- and intermediate-frequency phonon modes. Solving the anisotropic Migdal-Eliashberg equations yields a superconducting transition temperature of Tc = 9.7 K. The superconducting state is characterized by a nodeless but anisotropic gap structure, exhibiting two distinct gap values of approximately 2.25 and 1.74 meV associated with different Fermi surface sheets. These results identify the BP3 monolayer as a strongly coupled, multiband two-dimensional superconductor and provide insight into the role of orbital hybridization in electron-phonon-mediated superconductivity in low-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [8] [Hidden Universal Metal in Cuprate Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10133)
*Abigail Lee,Juergen Haase*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究基于铜氧化物超导体中平面Cu和O核弛豫数据，发展了一个简单唯象模型，揭示了普遍金属态与奇异金属态之间的转变，以及掺杂依赖的各向异性与最大临界温度的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核弛豫是探测超导金属中温度依赖电子激发的有力工具，但铜氧化物超导体中弛豫行为仍未得到充分理解。研究旨在基于现有文献中的平面Cu和O弛豫数据，建立统一的唯象描述框架。

Method: 基于文献中已有的平面Cu和O核弛豫数据，发展了一个简单的唯象模型。该模型核心是定义了一个普遍金属态（universal metal），其特征由1/(^{63}T_{1⊥})T_c ≈ 25/Ks的关系描述。

Result: 在所有材料中都发现了普遍金属态，表明T_c与Cu核弛豫率直接相关。在T_c以上，普遍金属态随温度升高逐渐转变为弛豫滞后的奇异金属态（strange metal regime）。平面O弛豫表现出预期的固定各向异性，而Cu弛豫的各向异性则随掺杂变化，从低掺杂的约3.6到高掺杂的约1。

Conclusion: 与掺杂相关的各向异性决定了该材料家族的最大临界温度，并与普遍金属态相关联，这可能需要两个弛豫分量来解释。新的唯象模型为理解铜氧化物的相图提供了更好的基础。

Abstract: Nuclear relaxation is a powerful probe of temperature dependent electronic excitations in superconducting metals. Their emergence from a condensed state near the critical temperature, $T_\mathrm{c}$, is of particular interest. In cuprate superconductors, the behavior is still not understood. Here, based on planar Cu and O relaxation data available in the literature, a simple phenomenology is developed. At its core is a universal metal, characterized by $1/{^{63}T}_{1\perp} T_\mathrm{c} \approx 25$/Ks, found in all materials, i.e. $T_\mathrm{c}$ is directly related to the Cu nuclear relaxation rate. Above $T_\mathrm{c}$, as a function of temperature, this universal metal crosses over into a strange metal regime where relaxation increasingly lags behind that of the universal metal. The latter is also tied to the metallic planar O relaxation, which only deviates from it at lower energies in underdoped materials with a doping dependent, but temperature independent pseudogap described earlier. Planar O relaxation has the expected fixed anisotropy, but for Cu it is doping dependent and varies between about 3.6 for lower and 1 for high doping levels. It is this doping-related anisotropy that sets the maximum critical temperature of the family and in that sense is tied to the universal metal. This likely requires two components of relaxation. The new phenomenology will be discussed and should give a better foundation for the understanding of the phase diagram of the cuprates.

</details>


### [9] [Ultrafast decoupling of the pseudogap from superconductivity in a pressurized cuprate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10207)
*Yanghao Meng,Wenjin Mao,Liucheng Chen,Elbert E. M. Chia,Yifeng Yang,Jianlin Luo,Lin Zhao,Xingjiang Zhou,Xiaohui Yu,Xinbo Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究利用超快光学光谱技术构建了欠掺杂铜酸盐Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ在高达37 GPa静水压下的相图，揭示了赝能隙与超导性之间的解耦关系，并观察到压力驱动的维度交叉和绝缘态转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 赝能隙（pseudogap）与超导性之间的关系是铜酸盐物理中的核心难题。静水压（hydrostatic pressure）提供了一种无化学无序的清洁调控参数，但在压缩条件下探测这些相的微观能标一直存在实验挑战。

Method: 研究采用超快光学光谱（ultrafast optical spectroscopy）技术，构建了欠掺杂铜酸盐Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ在高达37 GPa压力下的高压相图。

Result: 结果揭示了赝能隙态中的显著二分性：起始温度T*随压力单调上升，而能隙ΔPG持续被抑制。相比之下，临界温度Tc和超导能隙ΔSC呈现相关的圆顶状轨迹，表明超导性与赝能隙独立演化。在约8 GPa附近，能隙比2ΔSC/kBTc的突然崩溃标志着压力驱动的维度交叉（dimensional crossover），抑制了二维相位涨落并稳定了全局三维相干性。

Conclusion: 通过解析扩展的相演化，该研究解耦了赝能隙与超导序，为高温超导的配对机制建立了严格的实验基础。在37 GPa时，超导凝聚体完全淬灭为类绝缘态。

Abstract: The relationship between the pseudogap and superconductivity remains a central puzzle in the physics of cuprates. Hydrostatic pressure provides a clean tuning parameter free from chemical disorder, yet probing the microscopic energy scales of these phases under compression has remained experimentally challenging. Here, we utilize ultrafast optical spectroscopy to construct the high-pressure phase diagram of the underdoped cuprate Bi$_2$Sr$_2$CaCu$_2$O$_{8+δ}$ up to 37 GPa. Our results reveal a striking dichotomy within the pseudogap state: while the onset temperature $T^*$ rises monotonically with pressure, the energy gap $Δ_{\mathrm{PG}}$ is continuously suppressed. In contrast, the critical temperature $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ and the superconducting gap $Δ_{\mathrm{SC}}$ trace a correlated dome-like trajectory, demonstrating that superconductivity evolves independently from the pseudogap. Furthermore, an abrupt collapse of the gap ratio $2Δ_{\mathrm{SC}}/k_{\mathrm{B}}T_{\mathrm{c}}$ near 8 GPa marks a pressure-driven dimensional crossover, quenching two-dimensional phase fluctuations to stabilize global three-dimensional coherence. Upon reaching 37 GPa, the superconducting condensate is completely quenched into an insulating-like state. By resolving the extended phase evolution, our findings disentangle the pseudogap and superconducting orders, establishing a rigorous experimental basis for the pairing mechanism of high-temperature superconductivity.

</details>

### [11] [Microscopic mechanism for resonant light-enhanced pair correlations in K$_3$C$_{60}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10987)
*Juan I. Aranzadi,Joseph Tindall,Paul Fadler,Michael A. Sentef*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了K₃C₆₀中光诱导超导响应的共振增强机制：当泵浦频率接近10 THz时，光诱导的超导配对关联响应被显著增强，效率比非共振激发高出约两个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验发现K₃C₆₀在10 THz附近泵浦频率下，光诱导的超导响应出现巨大增强。研究旨在理解这种共振增强的微观机制，并确定其是否源于超导配对关联而非金属性改善。

Method: 基于第一性原理参数构建了K₃C₆₀的驱动电子模型，采用精确对角化分析小团簇，识别出对称性约束的双光子路径。随后开发了DMRG+Krylov方法处理更大团簇，并建立简化的单轨道模型扩展到14位点的面心立方团簇。

Result: 研究发现共振增强源于对称性约束的双光子路径：第一个光子将系统从偶宇称基态驱动到中间奇宇称态，第二个光子驱动到具有增强配对关联的偶宇称激发态。共振能量随系统尺寸下移，在14位点团簇中降至约30 THz。

Conclusion: 研究确立了K₃C₆₀中光增强配对关联的纯电子机制，支持实验观测的10 THz共振确实源于超导配对形成而非金属性改善。该机制可能存在于其他中等耦合哈伯德材料中，其中在位排斥U与电子带宽W尺度相当。

Abstract: Recent experiments on K$_3$C$_{60}$ revealed a giant enhancement of the light-induced superconducting-like optical response for pump frequencies near 10 THz, with an efficiency roughly two orders of magnitude larger than for off-resonant excitation. Here we show that a resonant enhancement of pair correlations arises naturally in a driven electronic model of K$_3$C$_{60}$ derived from \emph{ab initio} parameters. Exact diagonalization on small clusters identifies a symmetry-constrained two-photon pathway: the first photon drives the system from the even-parity ground state to an intermediate odd-parity manifold, and the second photon drives it to an even-parity excited state with enhanced pair correlations. Guided by this structure, we develop a DMRG+Krylov approach for larger clusters and find that the resonance energy shifts downwards with system size due to the kinetic-energy gain of the delocalized doublon excitation. A simplified single-orbital model reproduces the same scaling trend and allows us to reach a 14-site fcc cluster, where the resonant peak is pushed to $\sim$ 30 THz. Our results establish a purely electronic mechanism for resonant light-enhanced pair correlations in K$_3$C$_{60}$ and independently support the view that the experimentally observed 10 THz resonance is indeed due to superconducting-like coherent pair formation rather than improved metallicity. More broadly, they suggest that related resonant pathways may arise in other intermediate-coupling Hubbard materials with on-site repulsion $U$ and electronic bandwidth $W$ on comparable scales.

</details>


### [12] [Type-II superconductivity in the Dirac semimetal PdTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11047)
*Ritu Gupta,Catherine Witteveen,Debarchan Das,Fabian O. von Rohr,Rustem Khasanov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明PdTe2狄拉克半金属（Dirac semimetal）的微观超导特性，特别关注其镶嵌晶体（mosaic crystals）的超导性质，以澄清先前研究中关于其超导类型的矛盾报道。

Method: 采用零场和横向场μ子自旋弛豫/旋转（μSR）、交流磁化率（ac-magnetic susceptibility）和电阻率测量相结合的方法，系统研究了PdTe2镶嵌晶体的超导特性。

Result: 磁化率测量显示两个超导转变温度（1.8K和1.6K），μSR实验观察到明显的抗磁位移（diamagnetic shift）和高斯展宽（Gaussian broadening），证实其为II型超导体；穿透深度分析表明其具有完全能隙的s波对称超导态。

Conclusion: PdTe2是研究范德华材料（van-der-Waals material）中非平凡拓扑、表面超导性和II型体超导性相互作用的理想模型系统；系统无序（disorder）可轻易将其超导性从I型转变为II型。

Abstract: We report on the microscopic superconducting properties of the Dirac semimetal PdTe2. In this study, we have focused on mosaic crystals of PdTe2, and used detailed zero field and transverse field muon spin relaxation/rotation ($μ$SR), ac-magnetic susceptibility, and resistivity measurements to investigate their superconducting properties. The magnetic susceptibility measurements reveal two superconducting transition temperatures at 1.8 and 1.6~K, respectively, in agreement with earlier reports. In contrary to these reports, we find that these mosaic PdTe2 crystals, are not type-I, but rather type-II superconductors. In fact, we observe the clear manifestation of a flux line lattice through a clear diamagnetic shift and Gaussian broadening of the Fourier spectra in the superconducting state. This behavior is likely caused by the disorder in the mosaic crystals of PdTe2 studied here. Our analysis of the superconducting order parameter by the means of temperature dependent magnetic penetration depth $λ(T)$ reveals a fully gapped superconducting state that can be well-fitted using an s-wave symmetric gap. We find that PdTe2 is a promising model system for the investigation and interplay of non-trivial topology, surface superconductivity, and type-II bulk superconductivity in a van-der-Waals material. Moreover, our results indicate that the superconductivity in this material can be easily modified from type-I to type-II by disorder in the system.

### [13] [Statistical Signatures of Majorana Zero Modes in Disordered Topological Superconductor Antidot Vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11692)
*Zhibo Ren,Jukka I. Väyrynen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个通用理论来分析无序对三维拓扑绝缘体-超导体平台中反点钉扎涡旋系统的影响，重点区分Majorana零模与CdGM态，发现MZM概率密度方差是CdGM态的两倍，这一差异可通过扫描隧道显微镜测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在三维拓扑绝缘体-超导体平台的反点钉扎涡旋中，Majorana零模与众多CdGM态共存，需要发展理论来研究无序对这些态的影响，并强调两者之间的差异。

Method: 采用解析的随机矩阵理论方法和数值模拟相结合，推导这些态的统计分布，通过对比分析MZM和CdGM态在无序条件下的行为差异。

Result: 研究结果表明，Majorana零模的概率密度方差是CdGM态的两倍，这一差异源于MZM具有实波函数而CdGM态具有复波函数，该特征可在无序反点涡旋中通过扫描隧道显微镜测量。

Conclusion: MZM与CdGM态在无序条件下的统计分布差异为超越零偏压电导峰的Majorana零模特征提供了新的识别方法，为实验验证拓扑超导中的Majorana态提供了理论依据。

Abstract: An antidot-pinned vortex in a three-dimensional topological insulator-superconductor platform hosts a Majorana zero mode (MZM). However, numerous Caroli-de Gennes-Matricon (CdGM) states coexist with it. We develop a general theory to study the effects of disorder on the system, emphasizing the difference between Majorana zero mode and CdGM states. Using both an analytical random matrix theory approach and numerical simulations, we derive the statistical distributions of these states. Our results demonstrate that the variance of the MZM probability density is twice that of the CdGM states, a difference due to the former having a real wave function as opposed to a complex one. This distinction can be measured by using scanning tunneling microscopy in a disordered antidot vortex, providing a signature of MZM beyond the zero-bias conductance peak.

### [14] [Reduced pair breaking from extended disorder in unconventional superconductors: implications to 4Hb-TaS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11738)
*Yuval Tsur,Mark H. Fischer,Jonathan Ruhman*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 研究发现扩展杂质势（extended impurity potential）能显著降低非常规超导体的配对破坏率（pair-breaking rate），使其比输运散射率（transport scattering rate）低约1/3，从而解释了高电阻率材料中非常规超导的持久性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非常规超导（unconventional superconductivity）通常被认为会被非磁性无序（nonmagnetic disorder）强烈抑制，但某些过渡金属二硫化物（transition metal dichalcogenides）在高电阻率下仍表现出非常规配对特征，这挑战了动量弛豫（momentum relaxation）与配对破坏（pair breaking）之间的传统关系。

Method: 采用包含自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的多带模型（multiband model），引入模拟常见晶格缺陷（如硫族空位或吸附原子）的扩展杂质势（extended impurity potential），并与常用的点缺陷势（point defect potential）进行比较，在同等基础上评估动量弛豫率和配对破坏率。

Result: 扩展杂质势导致配对破坏率相对于输运散射率（transport scattering rate）参数化降低，在广泛参数范围内Γτ_D ∼ 1/3，这种降低源于无序势的动量结构与超导能隙（superconducting gap）内部结构的匹配，抑制了配对破坏过程。

Conclusion: 非常规配对态比标准Abrikosov-Gor'kov理论预测的更为稳健，这为强无序系统中非常规超导的持久性提供了自然解释，并显著缓解了高电阻率与非常规配对之间的明显矛盾。

Abstract: Unconventional superconductivity is generally expected to be strongly suppressed by nonmagnetic disorder, as captured by Abrikosov--Gor'kov (AG) theory. However, several materials, including transition metal dichalcogenides, exhibit signatures of unconventional pairing despite relatively high resistivities, suggesting a breakdown of the conventional relation between momentum relaxation and pair breaking. Here, we study this problem in H-phase transition metal dichalcogenides by computing the disorder-dressed pairing susceptibility. We employ a multiband model with spin-orbit coupling and include an impurity potential that mimics a common lattice defect, namely a chalcogen vacancy or site ad-atom. This yields to an extended impurity potential, which we compare with the commonly considered on-site (point defect) potential. We evaluate the momentum-relaxation rate and the pair-breaking rate on equal footing. We find that extended impurity potentials lead to a parametrically reduced pair-breaking rate compared to the transport scattering rate, with $Γτ_D \sim 1/3$ over a wide parameter range. This reduction originates from the momentum structure of the disorder potential, which partially matches the internal structure of the superconducting gap and suppresses pair-breaking processes. As a result, unconventional pairing states are significantly more robust than predicted by standard AG theory. Our results provide a natural explanation for the persistence of unconventional superconductivity in systems with strong disorder and substantially alleviate the apparent conflict between high resistivity and unconventional pairing in materials such as 4Hb-TaS$_2$.

</details>

The model response appears plausible in various deformation states.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三维Klein-Gordon-Schrödinger系统的全局适定性和散射性问题，特别是在小径向数据条件下的最佳全局适定性范围。

Method: 采用全局时间迭代方案，结合适应函数空间$U^2_Φ$、径向Strichartz估计以及双线性限制估计等方法。

Result: 证明了对于任意$ε>0$，在数据空间$(u_0, n_0, n_1)\in L^2\times H^{ -\frac{1}{2} + ε} \times H^{-\frac{3}{2} +ε}$中的小径向数据，系统具有全局适定性和散射性。

Abstract: We prove global well-posedness and scattering for the 3D Klein-Gordon-Schrödinger system for small radial data in the best known global well-posedness range $(u_0, n_0, n_1)\in L^2\times H^{ -\frac{1}{2} + ε} \times H^{-\frac{3}{2} +ε}$ for any $ ε> 0 $. The proof uses a global-in-time iteration scheme in the adapted function spaces $U^2_Φ$, radial Strichartz estimates, and bilinear restriction estimates.

### [17] [Differentiable free energy surface: a variational approach to directly observing rare events using generative deep-learning models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09769)
*Shuo-Hui Li,Chen Chen,Yao-Wen Zhang,Ding Pan*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出变分自由能面（VaFES）框架，无需数据集即可直接建模自由能面，通过生成模型一次性采样识别稀有事件构型，为复杂统计系统研究提供可扩展的系统性方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有事件（rare events）是复杂多体系统演化的核心，表现为自由能面（free energy surface, FES）上的关键过渡构型。传统方法需要充分采样稀有事件跃迁来获取FES，计算成本极高。

Method: 提出变分自由能面（variational free energy surface, VaFES）框架，使用易处理密度生成模型直接建模FES。通过将粗粒化集体变量（coarse-grained collective variable, CV）扩展为其可逆等价形式，VaFES构建了中间表示的潜空间，其中CV明确占据部分维度。

Result: 该方法能够复现双稳态二聚体势的精确解析解，并识别出与实验NMR结构高度一致的chignolin天然折叠态。单次优化即可获得连续、可微的FES，同时通过生成模型一次性采样生成稀有事件构型。

Conclusion: VaFES建立了可扩展、系统性的框架，通过保留CV的物理可解释性和透明可控性，同时适应任意CV公式，推动了复杂统计系统研究的进展。

Abstract: Rare events are central to the evolution of complex many-body systems, characterized as key transitional configurations on the free energy surface (FES). Conventional methods require adequate sampling of rare event transitions to obtain the FES, which is computationally very demanding. Here we introduce the variational free energy surface (VaFES), a dataset-free framework that directly models FESs using tractable-density generative models. Rare events can then be immediately identified from the FES with their configurations generated directly via one-shot sampling of generative models. By extending a coarse-grained collective variable (CV) into its reversible equivalent, VaFES constructs a latent space of intermediate representation in which the CVs explicitly occupy a subset of dimensions. This latent-space construction preserves the physical interpretability and transparent controllability of the CVs by design, while accommodating arbitrary CV formulations. The reversibility makes the system energy exactly accessible, enabling variational optimization of the FES without pre-generated simulation data. A single optimization yields a continuous, differentiable FES together with one-shot generation of rare-event configurations. Our method can reproduce the exact analytical solution for the bistable dimer potential and identify a chignolin native folded state in close alignment with the experimental NMR structure. Our approach thus establishes a scalable, systematic framework for advancing the study of complex statistical systems.

</details>


### [18] [A unified sharp-diffusive phase-field model for bulk and interfacial cohesive fracture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10623)
*Ye-Hang Qin,Ye Feng*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种尖锐-扩散相场模型，通过引入解析的强局域化界面源项，实现了界面韧性的独立精确控制，避免了传统方法中复杂的修正和精细网格需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多相材料相场建模面临的关键挑战在于断裂能正则化的非局域性，其中界面韧性（interfacial toughness）与周围体相性质固有耦合。实现与预设材料性质的一致性通常需要复杂的修正和界面附近异常精细的局部网格细化。

Method: 利用最近提出的Ω²-模型展现狄拉克型损伤集中和涌现位移不连续性的能力，同时在相场公式中引入解析的强局域化界面源项q_φ。该模型的"尖锐"特性表现为连续介质框架内自然涌现的强不连续性，从根本上区别于内聚单元法等固有离散方法。

Result: 理论分析表明，该框架能够使用统一的内聚律参数方程描述体相和界面区域的内聚失效，模型参数直接由局部材料性质确定而无需额外修正。数值验证证实该模型不仅能准确复现多样化的界面内聚律，还能捕捉界面脱粘与基体开裂之间的复杂竞争。

Conclusion: 这种尖锐-扩散相场模型（sharp-diffusive phase-field model）为预测复杂工程材料中的断裂轨迹提供了一个鲁棒且计算高效的工具，实现了界面韧性的独立精确控制。

Abstract: In traditional phase-field modeling of multiphase materials, a significant challenge arises from the non-local nature of fracture energy regularization, where interfacial toughness is inherently coupled with the properties of the surrounding bulk phases. Achieving consistency with prescribed material properties typically necessitates complex corrections and exceptionally fine local mesh refinement near the interfaces. To address this fundamental issue, we leverage the capacity of the recently proposed $Ω^2$-model to manifest Dirac-like damage concentration and emergent displacement discontinuities, while introducing an analytical, strongly localized interfacial source term $q_φ$ into the phase-field formulation. It should be emphasized that the ``sharp" nature of the proposed model manifests as a naturally emergent strong discontinuity within a continuum framework, fundamentally distinguishing it from inherently discrete approaches such as cohesive element method. This allows for the independent and precise control of interface toughness in a straightforward manner. Theoretical analysis further reveals that the proposed framework can describe the cohesive failure of both bulk and interfacial regions using a unified set of parametric equations for the cohesive law, where the model parameters are directly determined by the local material properties without the need for additional corrections. The model's versatility is numerically validated through a series of benchmarks. The results confirm that the proposed model not only accurately reproduces diverse interfacial cohesive laws but also captures the intricate competition between interfacial debonding and matrix cracking. This sharp-diffusive phase-field model may provide a robust and computationally efficient tool for predicting complex fracture trajectories in sophisticated engineering materials.

</details>

### [19] [Quantum to classical relaxation dynamics of the dissipative Rydberg gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10538)
*Viktoria Noel,Igor Lesanovsky*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了里德伯气体在相干过程与耗散竞争区域中的弛豫动力学。研究发现，在弱耗散极限下，系统表现出显著的弛豫减慢现象，并在一维和二维体系中识别出量子动力学约束的瞬态特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索里德伯气体中动力学约束在弱耗散极限下的演化。虽然强耗散极限下的动力学约束行为已被充分研究，但弱耗散极限下大尺寸系统（尤其二维以上）的动力学约束命运仍未被探索。

Method: 采用截断维格纳近似（truncated Wigner approximation）这一相空间方法，该方法能够捕捉超越经典速率方程的相关多体动力学。为研究相干与耗散过程相当时间尺度上的动力学约束涌现，分析了从两种初始态开始的弛豫动力学：完全极化态和属于量子疤痕（quantum scars）流形的奈尔态。

Result: 在两种初始条件下，均观察到磁化强度向稳态弛豫的显著减慢现象。研究在一维和二维体系中识别出量子动力学约束动力学的瞬态特征，表明即使在弱耗散极限下，动力学约束仍对弛豫过程产生重要影响。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在弱耗散极限下，里德伯气体仍表现出显著的弛豫减慢现象，并在一维和二维体系中存在量子动力学约束动力学的瞬态特征。这揭示了动力学约束在相干与耗散竞争区域中的持续影响，为理解量子多体系统的非平衡动力学提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the relaxation dynamics of a Rydberg gas in regimes where coherent processes and dissipation compete. In the strongly dissipative limit, the dynamics is known to be governed by an effective classical rate equation and to exhibit kinetically constrained, glassy relaxation towards a trivial stationary state. This behaviour originates from the Rydberg blockade, which prevents simultaneous excitations within a characteristic blockade radius. However, the fate of kinetic constraints in the weakly dissipative limit remains unexplored in large systems above one dimension. To access large system sizes and two-dimensional geometries, we employ the truncated Wigner approximation, a phase-space method that captures correlated many-body dynamics beyond classical rate equations. To probe the emergence of kinetic constraints on timescales where coherent and dissipative processes are comparable, we analyse the relaxation dynamics starting from two initial states: a fully polarised state and a Néel state, which belongs to a manifold of so-called quantum scars. In both cases, we observe a pronounced slowdown in the relaxation of the magnetisation towards the stationary state and identify transient signatures of quantum kinetically constrained dynamics in one and two dimensions.

</details>


### [20] [Tunable viscosity across the BCS-BEC crossover](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10759)
*Yunxiang Liao,Andrey Grankin,Archisman Panigrahi,Victor Galitski,Leonid Levitov*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究提出通过最小化超冷费米气体在Feshbach共振附近的剪切粘度来增强雷诺数，为量子流体湍流模拟提供新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷量子气体因其可调相互作用成为探索强关联区域流体动力学性质的独特平台。然而，实验系统中系统尺寸和流速受限，需要寻找增强雷诺数的新方法。

Method: 采用Keldysh表述的线性响应理论，研究在BCS-BEC交叉（crossover）附近剪切粘度的变化。分析包括Drude-like贡献和高阶顶点修正，特别是Maki-Thompson贡献。

Result: 理论证明剪切粘度在BCS-BEC交叉附近可变化数个数量级。在远离Feshbach失谐时Drude-like贡献占主导，而在近共振区域高阶顶点修正变得显著并抑制奇异行为。

Conclusion: 该研究为实现超冷量子流体中可调雷诺数提供了路线图，这些系统可作为桌面级湍流模拟器（table-top turbulence simulators）。

Abstract: Tunable interactions make ultracold quantum gases a unique platform for exploring hydrodynamic properties in the strongly correlated regime. Of particular interest are turbulent flows possible in the regime of high Reynolds numbers. Since the system size and flow velocity are limited in experimentally realistic systems, we propose an alternative approach to enhance the Reynolds numbers in an ultracold Fermi gas by minimizing the shear viscosity in the vicinity of the Feshbach resonance. By employing the Keldysh formulation of the linear response theory, we theoretically demonstrate that the shear viscosity can vary by several orders of magnitude in the vicinity of the BCS-BEC crossover. It is also shown that while Drude-like contributions generally dominate at large Feshbach detunings, higher-order vertex corrections, including the Maki-Thompson contribution, become significant and suppress singular behavior in the near-resonant regime. Our results provide a roadmap for achieving tunable Reynolds numbers in ultracold quantum fluids, which can serve as table-top turbulence simulators.

</details>


### [21] [Emergent Quantum Droplets in Logarithmic Klein-Gordon Models of Bose-Einstein Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10839)
*Kevin Hernández,Elías Castellanos*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析具有三次和对数相互作用的非线性克莱因-戈登方程，建立了自束缚玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的相对论性标量场模型。该模型捕捉了量子液滴的关键特征，并通过非相对论极限导出了具有对数修正的广义Gross-Pitaevskii方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在为自束缚玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BECs）建立一个相对论性标量场模型，以捕捉量子液滴（quantum droplets）的关键特征，如自束缚（self-trapping）和有限能量构型。该工作试图统一研究量子液滴中的相对论效应，并丰富具有非标准相互作用的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的理论框架。

Method: 通过分析具有三次和对数相互作用的非线性克莱因-戈登方程（nonlinear Klein-Gordon equation）来研究自束缚BECs。执行非相对论极限（non-relativistic limit）以导出具有对数修正的广义Gross-Pitaevskii方程。构建相应的拉格朗日密度（Lagrangian density），通过诺特定理（Noether's theorem）识别守恒量，并计算能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）。

Result: 数值解展示了BECs参数，为具有对数相互作用的相对论性凝聚体建立了场论描述基础。所得动力学表现出稳定的振荡状态，与自束缚凝聚体构型一致。该模型为研究量子液滴中的相对论效应提供了统一方法，并丰富了具有非标准相互作用的BECs理论体系。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了描述自束缚玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的相对论性标量场模型，该模型能够捕捉量子液滴的关键特征。通过非相对论极限导出的广义Gross-Pitaevskii方程与超越平均场理论（beyond mean-field theory）描述超冷原子气体的最新模型一致，为研究相对论性凝聚体提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study a relativistic scalar field model for self-bound Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs) by analyzing a nonlinear Klein-Gordon equation with cubic and logarithmic interactions. This framework captures essential features of quantum droplets, such as self-trapping and finite energy configurations, which emerge from the interplay between attractive and repulsive terms. By performing the non-relativistic limit, we derive a generalized Gross-Pitaevskii equation with a logarithmic correction, consistent with recent models used to describe ultra-cold atomic gasses beyond mean-field theory. We construct the corresponding Lagrangian density, identify conserved quantities via Noether's theorem, and compute the energy-momentum tensor. Numerical solutions of the BEC parameters are shown, establishing the foundations for a field theoretical description of relativistic condensates with a logarithmic interaction. This model provides a unified approach to investigate relativistic effects in quantum droplets and enriches the theoretical landscape of Bose-Einstein condensates with non-standard interactions. The resulting dynamics exhibit stable oscillatory regimes consistent with self-bound condensate configurations.

</details>


### [22] [Enhanced squeezing for quantum gravimetry in a Bose-Einstein condensate with focussing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10948)
*Lewis A. Williamson,Karandeep Gill,Andrew J. Groszek,Matthew J. Davis,Simon Haine*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种改进的自由落体原子干涉仪方案，通过在初始阶段施加突然的陷俘势（δ-kick）来聚焦玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体，增强单轴扭曲相互作用，从而产生更强的自旋压缩，使相位灵敏度相比标准量子极限提高约20倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自由落体原子干涉仪（free-fall atom interferometers）为精确的绝对重力传感提供了强大平台。先前Szigeti等人提出的量子增强方案使用自旋压缩（spin-squeezed）玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）作为输入态，但其自旋压缩受到凝聚体膨胀的限制。

Method: 改进方案在初始阶段施加突然的陷俘势——δ-kick（delta kick）来聚焦凝聚体。密度的增加增强了单轴扭曲相互作用（one-axis-twisting interactions），产生更强的自旋压缩。研究采用多模截断维格纳模拟（multimode truncated-Wigner simulations）量化干涉仪性能。

Result: 对于最优的kick强度，相位灵敏度（phase sensitivity）相比标准量子极限（standard quantum limit）提高了约20倍。这比原始无δ-kick方案提高了四倍，且结果与双模近似（two-mode approximation）吻合良好。

Conclusion: 通过δ-kick聚焦凝聚体显著增强了单轴扭曲相互作用，实现了更强的自旋压缩和更高的相位灵敏度，为量子增强原子干涉仪提供了改进方案。

Abstract: Free-fall atom interferometers offer a powerful platform for accurate, absolute gravitational sensing. Szigeti et al. [Phys. Rev. Lett. 125, 100402 (2020)] recently proposed a quantum-enhanced scheme that uses a spin-squeezed Bose-Einstein condensate as an input state to improve the phase sensitivity of the interferometer. The spin squeezing, generated via one-axis twisting interactions, was limited by condensate expansion. Here we present an improved state preparation in which a sudden trapping potential -- a delta kick -- is initially applied to focus the condensate. The resulting increase in density enhances the one-axis-twisting interactions and produces greater spin squeezing. Using multimode truncated-Wigner simulations, we quantify the performance of the interferometer and find that, for an optimal kick strength, the phase sensitivity surpasses the standard quantum limit by a factor of $\sim 20$. This represents a fourfold improvement over the original scheme without the delta kick and is well captured by a two-mode approximation.

</details>


### [23] [Emergence of the unexpected charge-density-wave phase driven by artificial gauge field in three-leg Bose-Hubbard ladder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11169)
*Takayuki Yokoyama,Yasuhiro Tada*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究在半填充的三腿梯子系统中引入均匀人工规范场，发现了一个包含多种超流和绝缘相的丰富量子相图，其中电荷密度波相在通量区域意外出现，并观察到CDW→涡旋超流→CDW的再入型量子相变序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索人工规范场下三腿梯子系统中硬核玻色子的量子相行为，特别关注通量增加时相图的演化规律，以理解涡旋态与密度波序之间的竞争关系。

Method: 通过分析电流模式和关联函数，系统研究了半填充条件下硬核玻色子在均匀人工规范场中的行为，重点关注通量变化对量子相的影响。

Result: 发现了包含多种超流和绝缘相的丰富量子相图，在预期出现涡旋态的通量区域意外观察到电荷密度波相，并识别出无法从强耦合极限理解的孤立CDW区域，以及CDW→涡旋超流→CDW的再入型相变序列。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了涡旋相与密度波序之间的强烈竞争，表明在玻色子梯子系统中，增加规范通量不仅会破坏迈斯纳相，还能在仅存在在位相互作用的情况下诱导出电荷密度波序。

Abstract: We investigate hard-core bosons at half filling on a three-leg ladder under the uniform artificial gauge field. By analyzing current patterns and correlation functions, we uncover a rich quantum phase diagram containing multiple superfluid and insulating phases. In bosonic ladder systems, increasing the gauge flux typically destabilizes the Meissner phase and leads to vortex phases characterized by circulating currents. In the present system, however, we find that charge-density-wave (CDW) phases emerge precisely in such a flux regime despite the presence of only an on-site interaction, where vortex states are naturally expected and are indeed realized in nearby parameter regions. While part of this behavior can be qualitatively understood from a strong-coupling perspective, we also identify an isolated CDW region that cannot be connected to such limits. Furthermore, upon increasing the artificial gauge flux, we observe a reentrant sequence of quantum phase transitions, CDW $\to$ vortex-superfluid $\to$ CDW, revealing a strong competition between the vortex phase and the density-wave order.

### [24] [Morphological false-vacuum decay in dipolar supersolids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11603)
*Wyatt Kirkby,Lauriane Chomaz,Thomas Gasenzer*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了偶极超固体（dipolar supersolid）中两种形态不同的相之间通过气泡成核（bubble nucleation）发生的假真空衰变（false-vacuum decay），发现气泡生长速度由超固体中最慢的声速决定，为研究假真空衰变提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究偶极超固体中假真空衰变的动机在于，该体系提供了丰富的亚稳态结构和集体激发，且气泡形成可直接在实空间密度中观测，与先前研究形成对比。

Method: 采用随机投影扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程（stochastic projected extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation）对亚稳态蜂窝状（honeycomb）超固体向条纹相（stripe phase）畴的形成进行数值模拟。

Result: 气泡生长速度由超固体中最慢的声速决定；数值提取了真空衰变率，并与连接两种超固体序的Coleman bounce解（Coleman bounce solution）的最小有效模型进行了比较。

Conclusion: 偶极超固体为研究假真空衰变提供了新颖且多功能的平台，其亚稳态结构和集体激发在衰变过程中发挥重要作用，且气泡形成可直接通过原位成像（in situ imaging）探测。

Abstract: False-vacuum decay between two morphologically distinct supersolid phases via bubble nucleation is studied in a uniform dipolar gas confined to the plane. Starting from a metastable honeycomb state, the formation of stripe phase domains is simulated numerically by means of a stochastic projected extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation. The speed of bubble growth is analyzed in relation to the multiple speeds of sound of the supersolid, and is found to be set by the slowest of these sounds. The vacuum decay rate is numerically extracted and compared against a minimal effective model for the Coleman bounce solution connecting the two supersolid orders. Our results establish dipolar supersolids as a novel and versatile platform for studying false-vacuum decay. This setting offers a rich structure of metastable states and collective excitations that come into play in the decay. Furthermore, here, in contrast to previous studies, bubble formation occurs directly in the real-space density and can be probed with \textit{in situ} imaging.

</details>

### [25] [ALD W-Doped SnO$_2$ TFTs for Indium-Free BEOL Electronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11333)
*Mansi Anil Patil,Devarshi Dhoble,Shivaram Kubakaddi,Mamta Raturi,Marco A Villena,Gaurav Thareja,Saurabh Lodha*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究报道了通过150°C原子层沉积（ALD）制备的亚10纳米钨掺杂氧化锡（TWO）通道薄膜晶体管（TFT），该器件与后端制程（BEOL）兼容。10%钨掺杂TFT表现出最佳性能，经300°C氧气退火后，器件特性显著改善，亚阈值摆幅降低近2倍，开关比从10⁷提升至10⁹，迟滞现象减少近3倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在开发与后端制程（back-end-of-line, BEOL）兼容的低温薄膜晶体管（thin-film transistors, TFTs），为单片三维集成（monolithic 3D integration）提供无铟（indium-free）平台。通过钨掺杂氧化锡（tungsten-doped tin oxide, TWO）通道材料，探索高性能BEOL兼容TFT的可行性。

Method: 采用150°C原子层沉积（atomic layer deposition, ALD）制备亚10纳米厚度的钨掺杂氧化锡（TWO）通道。研究了未掺杂SnOₓ、未掺杂WOₓ以及钨掺杂浓度分别为5%和10%的SnOₓ通道TFT。器件制备后进行了300°C、5分钟的氧气退火处理，并使用Ginestra™进行动力学蒙特卡洛模拟（kinetic Monte Carlo simulations）验证实验结果。

Result: 10%钨掺杂TFT表现出最佳的静电控制和整体器件性能。氧气退火后，亚阈值摆幅（subthreshold swing, SS）降低近2倍，开关比（Iₒₙ/Iₒff ratio）从10⁷提升至10⁹，迟滞现象（hysteresis）减少近3倍，正偏压应力诱导阈值漂移（positive bias stress-induced threshold shift）降低超过2倍至93 mV（4 MV/cm应力场下）。模拟结果支持实验观察，将偏压不稳定性归因于栅介质和界面处的电荷俘获。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了低温ALD生长的钨掺杂氧化锡TFT作为后端制程和单片三维集成的有前景的无铟平台。氧气退火显著改善了器件特性，为高性能BEOL兼容TFT的开发提供了有效途径。

Abstract: This work reports back-end-of-line (BEOL) compatible, thin-film transistors (TFTs) with sub-10 nm tungsten-doped tin oxide (TWO) channels deposited by atomic layer deposition (ALD) at 150 $^\circ$C. TFTs with undoped SnO$_{\mathrm{x}}$, undoped WO$_{\mathrm{x}}$, and W-doped SnO$_{\mathrm{x}}$ channels with W concentrations of 5% and 10% were investigated. TFT with 10% W doping exhibited the best electrostatic control and overall device performance. Post-fabrication O$_{\mathrm{2}}$ annealing at 300 $^\circ$C for 5 minutes significantly enhanced device characteristics, reducing the subthreshold swing (SS) by nearly 2$\times$, increasing the I$_{\mathrm{on}}$/I$_{\mathrm{off}}$ ratio from $10^7$ to $10^9$, decreasing hysteresis by nearly 3$\times$ and positive bias stress-induced threshold shift by over 2$\times$ to a low value of 93 mV at a stress field of 4 MV/cm. Kinetic Monte Carlo simulations using Ginestra$^{\mathrm{TM}}$ support the experimental observations and attribute the bias instability to charge trapping in the gate dielectric and at the interface. This work demonstrates low-temperature ALD-grown TWO TFTs as a promising indium-free platform for BEOL and monolithic 3D integration.

</details>

### [26] [Visible Neutrino Decay As An Open Quantum System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09776)
*Joachim Kopp,George A. Parker*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于开放量子系统理论的方法，用于全面描述任意复杂的振荡和衰变中微子系统，特别展示了如何使用Lindblad主方程、Liouvillian超算符和Kraus算符来实现此类系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超出标准模型（Standard Model）的物理场景中，如多于三种中微子味（neutrino flavours）或存在Majoron等新超轻粒子时，较重中微子质量本征态（neutrino mass eigenstates）向较轻态的衰变可能显著增强。然而，由于振荡与衰变之间的复杂相互作用、不同衰变通道间的干涉以及多步衰变级联（multi-step decay cascades）的可能性，完整的理论描述具有挑战性。

Method: 本文采用开放量子系统（open quantum systems）理论的方法，开发了一种完全通用的描述框架来处理任意复杂的振荡和衰变中微子系统。特别展示了如何使用Lindblad主方程（Lindblad master equation）、Liouvillian超算符（Liouvillian superoperator）以及Kraus算符（Kraus operators）来实现此类系统。

Result: 研究表明，Liouvillian超算符和Kraus算符这两种方法避免了求解微分方程的需求，从而显示出优越的数值性能。这为处理复杂的中微子振荡衰变系统提供了有效的计算框架。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个基于开放量子系统理论的通用框架，能够全面描述任意复杂的中微子振荡衰变系统，为研究超出标准模型的物理现象提供了有力的理论工具。

Abstract: Decays of heavier neutrino mass eigenstates into lighter ones, while very slow in the Standard Model, can be significantly enhanced in scenarios with more than three neutrino flavours, or in models with new ultra-light particles such as Majorons. A full theoretical description is challenging due to the intricate interplay between oscillations and decay, interference between different decay channels, and the possibility of multi-step decay cascades. In this paper, we develop a fully general description of arbitrarily complex systems of oscillating and decaying neutrinos using methods from the theory of open quantum systems. Notably, we demonstrate how such systems can be implemented using the Lindblad master equation, the Liouvillian superoperator, as well as Kraus operators. The last two methods eschew the need for solving a differential equation, thereby showing superior numerical performance.

</details>


### [27] [William A. Bardeen -- A Brief Biography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10204)
*Christopher T. Hill*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: William Allan Bardeen 是一位美国理论物理学家，以其在量子场论异常（anomalies）、量子色动力学（QCD）和电弱对称性破缺（electroweak symmetry breaking）方面的开创性工作而闻名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 摘要未明确陈述研究动机，但 Bardeen 的工作旨在解决量子场论中的基本问题，包括理解手征异常（chiral anomaly）、发展量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics）以及探索电弱对称性破缺机制。

Method: Bardeen 采用了理论物理方法，包括发展手征异常理论、非阿贝尔异常（non-Abelian anomaly）和引力异常（gravitational anomalies）的数学框架，以及通过顶夸克凝聚（top quark condensates）构建电弱对称性动力学破缺理论。

Result: 主要成果包括：建立了手征异常的 Adler-Bardeen 定理；发展了量子色动力学及其应用（如半轻子衰变和 Λ_MS-bar 方案）；提出了基于顶夸克凝聚的电弱对称性动力学破缺理论，构建了早期复合 Higgs 玻色子模型；正确预测了重-轻夸克束缚态手征对称性伙伴的长寿命共振态。

Conclusion: William Allan Bardeen 对理论物理学做出了基础性贡献，特别是在量子场论异常、量子色动力学和电弱对称性破缺机制方面，其工作对粒子物理学的发展产生了深远影响。

Abstract: William Allan Bardeen (September 15, 1941 $-$ November 18, 2025) was an American theoretical physicist who worked at the Fermi National Accelerator Laboratory. He is renowned for his foundational work on the chiral anomaly, the Adler-Bardeen theorem, the non-Abelian anomaly and gravitational anomalies. He was instrumental in the development of quantum chromodynamics and its applications, such as semileptonic decays and the $Λ_{\overline{MS}}$ scheme frequently used in perturbative analysis of high energy processes involving strong interactions. Bardeen also played a major role in developing a theory of dynamical breaking of electroweak symmetry via top quark condensates, leading to one of the first composite Brout-Englert-Higgs boson models. His work on the chiral symmetry dynamics of heavy-light quark bound states correctly predicted abnormally long-lived resonances which are chiral symmetry partners of the ground state.

</details>

*Xiang Chen,Zejia Lu,Liangwen Chen,Jun Gao,Shao-Feng Ge,Zhanxu Hao,Yang Hu,Bingzhi Li,Cen Mo,Zhiyu Sun,Huayang Wang,Chonghao Wu,Yu Xu,Xueheng Zhang,Yulei Zhang,Liang Li*

Method: DREAMuS采用固定靶实验设计，利用高强度重离子加速器设施（HIAF）产生μ子束流，通过μ子-核相互作用产生轻味破坏玻色子（矢量$Z'$或标量$φ$）。实验使用精密径迹测量和飞行时间测量技术来抑制标准模型背景。

Result: 研究发现DREAMuS能够在GeV能区的μ子亲和暗物质参数空间达到竞争性灵敏度，耦合常数灵敏度可达$10^{-4}$量级，特别是在几百MeV区域。补充的$μ^+$束流选项可将200 MeV以下暗物质的探测灵敏度提高一个数量级。

Conclusion: DREAMuS实验设计为探测轻味破坏玻色子介导的μ子亲和暗物质提供了有前景的方案，通过固定靶实验结合精密测量技术，能够在GeV能区参数空间达到高灵敏度，特别是结合$μ^+$束流选项可显著提升低质量暗物质的探测能力。

Abstract: We propose DREAMuS, a fixed-target experiment at the High Intensity Heavy-Ion Accelerator Facility (HIAF), to search for muon-philic dark matter mediated by light flavor-violating bosons. DREAMuS is designed to probe the parameter space of a muon-philic dark matter (DM) mediated by a light flavor-violating boson, specifically a vector $Z'$ (or a scalar $φ$) which is produced in muon-nucleus interactions and decays into dark matter particles with a distinctive detector signature. Precision tracking and time-of-flight measurements are used to suppress the Standard Model backgrounds. We find that DREAMuS can achieve competitive sensitivity in the GeV-scale muon-philic dark matter parameter space, reaching sensitivity to couplings at the $10^{-4}$, especially in the few-hundred-MeV region.In addition to a $μ^-$ run, we highlight the potential of a complementary $μ^+$ beam option, further improving sensitivity to dark matter below 200 $\mathrm{MeV}$ by an order of magnitude.

### [29] [Resonance $X(6600)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10626)
*S. S. Agaev,K. Azizi,H. Sundu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将X(6600)共振态解释为全粲四夸克结构，通过QCD求和规则计算其质量为(6609±50) MeV，宽度为(165±23) MeV，与实验数据相符，支持其作为张量双夸克-反双夸克态的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索X(6600)共振态作为全粲四夸克（all-charm tetraquark）结构的可能性，特别是其在双夸克-反双夸克（diquark-antidiquark）图像中的张量态性质。

Method: 采用QCD求和规则（QCD sum rule, SR）方法：使用两点求和规则（two-point SR）计算谱参数，三点求和规则（three-point SRs）计算不同衰变道的部分宽度。模型中将X态构建为由轴向矢量双夸克cCγ_μc和反双夸克\overline{c}γ_νC\overline{c}组成的张量态。

Result: 计算得到张量双夸克-反双夸克态的质量m=(6609±50) MeV，宽度Γ[X]=(165±23) MeV。研究了主要衰变道X→J/ψJ/ψ、X→η_cη_c和χ_{c1}(1P)η_c，以及次主导衰变道X→D_{(s)}^{(*)+}D_{(s)}^{(*)-}和D_{(s)}^{(*)0}\overline{D}_{(s)}^{(*)0}。

Conclusion: 计算结果与实验数据相符，支持将X(6600)解释为张量双夸克-反双夸克态的重要成分。研究还提供了X态第一径向激发（first radial excitation）的质量下限。

Abstract: The resonance $X(6600)$ is explored as the all-charm tetraquark structure with spin-parities $J^{\mathrm{PC}}=2^{++}$. It is considered in the diquark-antidiquark picture and modeled as a tensor state $X$ composed of the axial-vector diquark $cCγ_μc$ and antidiquark $\overline{c}% γ_νC\overline{c}$ with $C$ being the charge conjugation matrix. The mass and decay width of $X$ are evaluated in the framework of QCD sum rule (SR) methods. The two-point SR approach is applied to find its spectroscopic parameters, while three-point SRs used to calculate partial widths of different decay channels of $X$. We study its leading decays $X \to J/ψJ/ψ$, $X \to η_{c}η_{c}$ and $χ_{c1}(1P)η_{c}$ in which all four $c$-quarks constitute final-state mesons. We consider also the subleading channels $X\to D_{(s)}^{(\ast )+}D_{(s)}^{(\ast )-}$ and $% D_{(s)}^{(\ast )0}\overline{D}_{(s)}^{(\ast )0}$ generated by annihilation of $\overline{c}c$ quarks in the tetraquark. Comparison of the mass $m=(6609 \pm 50)~ \mathrm{MeV}$ and width $Γ[X]=(165 \pm 23)~ \mathrm{MeV}$ of the tensor diquark-antidiquark state $X$ with experimental data allows us to interpret it as an essential component of the resonance $X(6600)$. We also provide a lower limit for the mass of the first radial excitation of $X$.

### [30] [Novel analysis for the energy-energy correlation in electron-positron annihilation in the perturbative domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10723)
*Zhu-Yu Ren,Sheng-Quan Wang,Jian-Ming Shen,Xing-Gang Wu,Leonardo Di Giustino,Philip G. Ratcliffe,Stanley J. Brodsky*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用最大共形性原理（PMC）分析正负电子湮灭中的能量-能量关联（EEC），通过重整化群方程重求和β项消除重整化方案与能标不确定性，所得PMC能标随EEC角分布动态变化，理论预测与实验数据在微扰区域吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 能量-能量关联（EEC）在量子色动力学（QCD）精密测试和耦合常数测量中至关重要，但传统方法存在重整化方案与能标不确定性。本文旨在通过最大共形性原理（PMC）提供一种消除这些不确定性的新分析方法。

Method: 采用最大共形性原理（PMC）这一系统性方法，通过重整化群方程重求和支配QCD跑动耦合行为的非共形β项来确定PMC能标。该方法重新吸收了所有β项，包括与发散的重整化链项相关的n!β₀ⁿαₛⁿ项。

Result: 所得PMC能标随EEC角分布动态变化，反映了能标的物理行为。使用PMC得到的QCD微扰系数行为与传统系数完全不同，PMC预测的EEC分布在微扰区域与实验数据吻合良好。

Conclusion: PMC方法通过消除重整化方案与能标不确定性，为能量-能量关联提供了更可靠的理论分析框架，其动态变化的能标反映了QCD传播胶子的虚度，理论预测与实验数据的一致性验证了该方法的有效性。

Abstract: The energy-energy correlation (EEC) in electron-positron annihilation plays a crucial role in precision tests of quantum chromodynamics (QCD) and measurements of the QCD coupling constant. In this paper, we provide a novel analysis for the EEC by using the Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC), a systematic method for eliminating renormalization scheme-and-scale ambiguities. The PMC scales are determined by resumming the non-conformal $β$-terms that govern the behavior of the QCD running coupling via the renormalization group equation, and reflect the virtuality of the propagating gluons in QCD. It is noteworthy that the resulting PMC scale varies dynamically with the EEC's angular distribution, reflecting the expected scale's physical behavior. Moreover, due to the reabsorption of all $β$-terms, including also those related to the divergent renormalon terms such as $n!β^n_0α^n_s$, in the pQCD series, the behavior of the QCD perturbative coefficient using PMC, differs entirely from that of the conventional coefficient. Consequently, the PMC predicted EEC distribution agrees well with the experimental data in the perturbative domain.

### [31] [Study of doubly heavy baryon lifetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10939)
*Hai-Yang Cheng,Chia-Wei Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在重夸克展开（heavy quark expansion）框架下计算了双重味重子（doubly heavy baryons）的寿命和遍举半轻衰变宽度，揭示了双重粲重子和双重底重子的寿命层次模式，并强调了W交换过程在产生寿命分裂中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究双重味重子的寿命和衰变特性对于理解重子物理中的非微扰效应和衰变机制具有重要意义。这些计算有助于揭示重夸克展开框架下不同阶算符贡献的相对重要性。

Method: 采用重夸克展开（heavy quark expansion）框架，包含了次领头阶（next-to-leading-order）的维度-3、-5和-6算符修正以及领头阶维度-7贡献。非微扰矩阵元使用袋模型（bag model）计算，并采用了平移改进的重子波函数。

Result: 获得了双重粲重子寿命：$(τ_{Ξ_{cc}^{++}}, τ_{Ξ_{cc}^{+}}, τ_{Ω_{cc}^{+}}) = (2.67±0.94, 0.47±0.08, 1.79±0.62)×10^{-13}s$；双重底重子寿命：$(τ_{Ξ_{bb}^{0}}, τ_{Ξ_{bb}^{-}}, τ_{Ω_{bb}^{-}}) = (0.75±0.11, 0.92±0.15, 0.93±0.15)×10^{-12}s$。寿命层次模式为：$τ(Ξ_{cc}^{++})>τ(Ω_{cc}^+)>τ(Ξ_{cc}^+)$ 和 $τ(Ω_{bb}^{-})∼τ(Ξ_{bb}^-)>τ(Ξ_{bb}^0)$。

Conclusion: W交换过程（W-exchange contribution）在双重粲重子中产生显著的寿命分裂，在双重底重子中仍具有重要的唯象意义。研究还计算了非轻衰变和半轻衰变的单独贡献，以及遍举半轻衰变宽度和衰变宽度不对称性，为理解衰变机制提供了补充探针。

Abstract: We study the lifetimes and inclusive semileptonic decay widths of doubly heavy baryons within the framework of heavy quark expansion. Our analysis includes next-to-leading-order corrections to the dimension-3, -5, and -6 operators, together with the leading dimension-7 contributions, while the nonperturbative matrix elements are evaluated in a bag model with translationally improved baryon wave functions. We obtain $( τ_{Ξ_{cc}^{++}} , τ_{Ξ_{cc}^{+}} , τ_{Ω_{cc}^{+}} ) = ( 2.67 \pm 0.94,\, 0.47 \pm 0.08,\, 1.79 \pm 0.62 ) \times 10^{-13}\,{\rm s}$ and $( τ_{Ξ_{bb}^{0}} , τ_{Ξ_{bb}^{-}} , τ_{Ω_{bb}^{-}} ) = ( 0.75 \pm 0.11,\, 0.92 \pm 0.15,\, 0.93 \pm 0.15 ) \times 10^{-12}\,{\rm s}$, where the uncertainties here arise from the heavy quark pole masses and the hadronic scale adopted in the quark model. Hence, the lifetime hierarchy patterns are $τ(Ξ_{cc}^{++})>τ(Ω_{cc}^+)>τ(Ξ_{cc}^+)$ and $τ(Ω_{bb}^{-})\simτ(Ξ_{bb}^-)>τ(Ξ_{bb}^0)$ for doubly charmed and bottom baryons, respectively. The $W$-exchange contribution plays a crucial role in generating the large lifetime splitting in the doubly charmed sector and remains phenomenologically important for doubly bottom baryons. In addition to the total lifetimes, we calculate the separate nonleptonic and semileptonic contributions, which allow us to trace the pattern of spectator effects in each baryon channel. We also evaluate the inclusive semileptonic decay widths and the decay width asymmetries, which provide complementary probes of the underlying decay mechanisms.

### [32] [Study of $χ_{cJ}\to ηηη^\prime$ via intermediate charmed meson loop mechanisms and its implications for non-observation of $η_1(1855)$ in $χ_{cJ}$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10944)
*Xin-Ru Wang,Shu-Qi Wang,Shi-Dong Liu,Qi Wu,Gang Li,Ju-Jun Xie*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过有效拉格朗日量方法，利用含粲介子和标量介子f₀(1500)的盒图和三角图圈图机制，成功解释了χ_{cJ}→ηηη'衰变的实验分支比，并预测了相关不变质量谱，为理解χ_{cJ}衰变机制和η₁(1855)信号缺失提供了理论解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BESIII合作组首次观测到χ_{cJ}→ηηη'衰变以寻找1⁻⁺奇特态η₁(1855)，但ηη'不变质量谱的部分波分析未发现显著的η₁(1855)信号。本研究旨在通过理论模型解释这些实验现象。

Method: 采用有效拉格朗日量方法（effective Lagrangian approach），通过包含粲介子和标量介子f₀(1500)的盒图（box loops）和三角图（triangle loops）圈图机制，计算χ_{cJ}→ηηη'衰变过程。

Result: 理论计算很好地重现了χ_{cJ}→ηηη'衰变的实验分支比，并对χ_{c1}衰变中产生的ηη'和ηη不变质量谱（invariant mass spectra）给出了预测，这些预测总体上与BESIII测量结果一致。

Conclusion: 在现有模型中，χ_{c1}→ηηη'衰变主要由三角图和盒图圈图贡献主导。理论结果与BESIII测量的一致性揭示了χ_{cJ}衰变为轻介子的潜在机制，有助于理解η₁(1855)信号在χ_{cJ}→ηηη'衰变道中的缺失。

Abstract: Recently, the BESIII Collaboration reported the first observation of the decays $χ_{cJ} \to ηηη^\prime$ in order to search for the $1^{-+}$ exotic state $η_1(1855)$. A partial wave analysis of the $ηη^\prime$ invariant mass spectrum shows no significant signal for the $η_1(1855)$. In this work, we, using an effective Lagrangian approach, investigate the processes $χ_{cJ} \to ηηη^\prime$ via the box and triangle loops involving charmed mesons and the scalar meson $f_0(1500)$. Our calculations reproduce well the experimental branching fractions of $χ_{cJ} \to ηηη^\prime$. Furthermore, we present the predictions of the relevant invariant mass spectra of $ηη^\prime$ and $ηη$ produced in the $χ_{c1}$ decay, which seem overall consistent with the BESIII measurements. In the present model, the decay $χ_{c1} \to ηηη^\prime$ is dominated by the triangle and box loop contributions. The consistency between our theoretical results and the BESIII measurements sheds light on the underlying decay mechanism of the $χ_{cJ}$ decaying into light mesons and might be helpful to understand the absence of the $η_1(1855)$ signal in the decay channels $χ_{cJ} \to ηηη^\prime$.

### [33] [Searching for apparent baryon number violation in $Λ_c^+$ decays at the Super Tau-Charm Facility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11329)
*Zeren Simon Wang,Xin-Ru Tang,Yu Zhang,Yu Zhang,Xiaorong Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出在超τ-粲能区工厂（STCF）中通过Λc⁺→M⁺+丢失能量（M=π,K）衰变通道搜索表观重子数破坏（BNV），评估了信号效率并推导了模型无关的灵敏度，在两种理论框架下解释结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验室中观测到重子数破坏（baryon number violation, BNV）将是超出标准模型（Standard Model）物理的确凿证据。目前Λc⁺→M⁺+丢失能量衰变通道尚未被实验探索，而e⁺e⁻对撞机在Λc⁺Λc⁻阈值附近生产提供了相对清洁的环境。

Method: 采用最先进的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）评估超τ-粲能区工厂（Super Tau-Charm Facility, STCF）的信号效率，在假设背景可忽略的情况下推导模型无关的灵敏度。进一步在两种理论框架下解释结果：扩展无菌中微子的低能有效场论（νLEFT）和R宇称破坏（R-parity-violating, RPV）超对称模型。

Result: 在1 ab⁻¹积分亮度下，STCF能够在νLEFT描述中探测到几个TeV的新物理标度，并将RPV模型参数λ″₂₁₂/m²_q̃约束至约0.1 TeV⁻²。这些结果表明STCF在稀有粲重子衰变中探测BNV相互作用具有高度竞争力。

Conclusion: STCF为在稀有粲重子衰变中探测重子数破坏相互作用提供了极具竞争力的机会，能够探索新的物理标度并约束超对称模型参数，填补了实验上尚未探索的Λc⁺衰变通道的研究空白。

Abstract: Observation of baryon number violation (BNV) in laboratory experiments would constitute unambiguous evidence for physics beyond the Standard Model. We propose dedicated searches for \textit{apparent} BNV in charm-baryon decays, $Λ_c^+\to M^+ +$ missing energy ($M=π, K$) where the missing energy stems from a resonance. These channels have not been explored experimentally so far, despite the relatively clean environment potentially provided by near $Λ_c^+\overlineΛ_c^-$ threshold production at $e^+e^-$ colliders. Performing state-of-the-art Monte Carlo simulations for the proposed Super Tau-Charm Facility (STCF), we evaluate the signal efficiencies and derive projected model-independent sensitivities under the assumption of negligible background. We further interpret these sensitivities within two theoretical frameworks: a sterile-neutrino-extended low-energy effective field theory ($ν$LEFT) and R-parity-violating (RPV) supersymmetry. With an integrated luminosity of 1 ab$^{-1}$, STCF can probe new-physics scales of several TeV in the $ν$LEFT description and constrain the RPV model parameter $λ''_{212}/m^2_{\tilde{q}}$ down to about $0.1~\mathrm{TeV}^{-2}$. Our results demonstrate that STCF provides a highly competitive opportunity for probing BNV interactions in rare charm-baryon decays.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在扩展先前TQ4Q1.1框架，通过纳入非组分重夸克贡献并引入基于多尺度变化的不确定性量化策略，为全重奇特态四夸克提供完整的碎裂函数集。

Method: 采用非相对论QCD因子化方法，结合领头阶的胶子和重夸克引发碎裂道。初始尺度输入通过更新的势模型波函数建模，随后使用阈值感知的HF-NRevo方案进行DGLAP演化。

Result: 开发了TQ4Q2.0网格并以LHAPDF6格式公开发布，这是首个完整的全重奇特态现象学集，支持在全粲四夸克产生和喷注关联观测量方面的精确研究。

Abstract: We present the TQ4Q2.0 fragmentation functions for the production of all-heavy (fully heavy) $S$-wave tetraquarks ($T_{4Q}$) with scalar ($0^{++}$), axial-vector ($1^{+-}$), and tensor ($2^{++}$) quantum numbers in high-energy hadronic collisions. This work extends the previous TQ4Q1.1 framework by incorporating nonconstituent heavy-quark contributions and introducing a replica-based uncertainty-quantification strategy derived from multi-scale variations (MHOUs). The construction follows a nonrelativistic QCD factorization approach, combining gluon- and heavy-quark-initiated fragmentation channels at leading power. Initial-scale inputs are modeled through updated potential-inspired wave functions, while the subsequent DGLAP evolution is performed via the threshold-aware HF-NRevo scheme. A comprehensive systematic analysis of uncertainties is carried out, with contributions from color-composite long-distance matrix elements (LDMEs) and perturbative multiscale inputs. The resulting TQ4Q2.0 grids, publicly released in LHAPDF6 format, provide the first complete phenomenological set for all-heavy exotics, enabling precise studies of all-charm tetraquark production and jet-associated observables within the JETHAD environment. This article completes the high-energy resummation-driven generation of the TQ4Q program and establishes a definitive baseline for future collider-oriented analyses of all-heavy multiquark dynamics.

### [35] [Feynman integral reduction by covariant differentiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09810)
*Gero von Gersdorff,Vinicius Lessa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种高效约化费曼积分（Feynman integrals）到主积分（master integrals）的新方法，通过在对偶向量空间上进行协变微分（covariant differentiation），并开发了相应的Mathematica代码MERLIN实现该算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统费曼积分约化方法在处理不同内部传播子质量（internal propagator masses）配置时效率较低，需要针对每种质量配置重新计算连接（connections）。本研究旨在开发一种更高效的约化方法，能够一次性构建连接并适用于任意质量配置。

Method: 该方法基于在对偶向量空间（dual vector space）上进行协变微分，该空间与主积分张成的空间对偶。核心创新在于连接只需针对给定拓扑（topology）构建一次，即可应用于任意内部传播子质量配置。算法通过Mathematica代码MERLIN（Method for Reduction of Loop Integrals）实现。

Result: 研究成功开发了一种高效约化算法，能够处理一大类费曼积分。该方法显著提高了计算效率，因为连接构建只需进行一次，后续可重复用于不同质量配置的积分约化。MERLIN代码实现了该算法的具体计算。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于协变微分的高效费曼积分约化方法，通过一次性构建连接并适用于任意质量配置，显著提升了计算效率。MERLIN代码为该方法提供了实用的计算工具。

Abstract: We show how a large class of Feynman integrals can be efficiently reduced to master integrals by suitable covariant differentiation on the vector space dual to the one spanned by the master integrals. The connections needed in the covariant derivatives have to be built only once for a given topology and then apply to any configuration of internal propagator masses. We implement our algorithm in the Mathematica code Method for Reduction of Loop Integrals (MERLIN).

</details>

Method: 方法结合了截面水平的卷积形式（convolution-based formalism）与事件水平的实现，在NuWro核内级联（intranuclear cascade）中将相互作用分类为透明（transparent）或非透明（non-transparent），从而统一处理FSI效应。

Result: 通过与包容电子散射数据和排他MicroBooNE测量（CCQE-dominated observable）的比较，结果显示包含FSI显著改善了与实验数据的一致性，证明了该实现的有效性。

Conclusion: 该统一框架能够在包容可观测量和排他未态中实现FSI效应，为轻子-核散射模拟提供了改进的FSI处理方法，显著提升了理论预测与实验数据的一致性。

Abstract: In this proceeding, I present a modified treatment of final-state interactions (FSI) in quasielastic (QE) lepton-nucleus scattering within the spectra function (SF) framework of the NuWro Monte Carlo generator. Our approach establishes a consistent correspondence between inclusive cross-section calculations and exclusive descriptions of hadron-propagation by combining a convolution-based formalism at the cross-section level with an event-level implementation in which interactions are classified as transparent or non-transparent within the NuWro intranuclear cascade. This unified framework enables realization of FSI effects across inclusive observables and exclusive final states. We demonstrate the impact of this implementation by comparing predictions to both inclusive electron-scattering data and exclusive MicroBooNE measurements of CCQE-dominated observable, showing that the inclusion of FSI leads to a significant improvement in agreement with the data.

### [37] [Induced Multi-phase Inflation with Reheating: Leptogenesis and Dark Matter Production in Metric versus Palatini](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09843)
*Nilay Bostan,Rafid H. Dejrah,Anish Ghoshal,Zygmunt Lalak*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了度规（metric）和Palatini引力框架下非最小耦合标量诱导的多相暴胀模型，分析了暴胀观测参数、再加热过程、暗物质产生以及轻子生成机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索不同引力理论（度规与Palatini）框架下的暴胀模型，特别是非最小耦合标量场诱导的多相暴胀，并系统分析其对宇宙学观测参数的预测、再加热机制、暗物质产生以及轻子生成的影响。

Method: 研究方法基于度规和Palatini引力理论，考虑线性、Brans-Dicke-like和Higgs-like三种标量场耦合扇区，分析标量谱指数和张标比等暴胀观测参数。通过门户耦合（portal coupling）λ₁₂和Yukawa耦合yχ研究再加热过程，并在Type-I跷跷板框架下分析非热轻子生成。

Result: 标量谱指数n_s在0.93-0.98范围内，与Planck及Planck+ACT数据一致。度规模型中张标比r可达~0.03，而Palatini模型普遍预测r≲10⁻⁵。Palatini情形中场偏移保持亚普朗克尺度，微扰幺正性截断提高。再加热温度T_rh范围在4 MeV到10¹⁵ GeV之间，暗物质质量m_χ在keV到PeV范围内可行。

Conclusion: 研究表明Palatini引力框架下的暴胀模型能产生与观测一致的标量谱指数，同时预测极低的张标比。再加热过程通过暴胀子衰变实现，暗物质可通过非热机制产生。Palatini场景中更严格的稳定性约束和更低的最高温度进一步限制了轻子生成的参数空间。

Abstract: We study non-minimally coupled scalar-induced multi-phase inflation in metric and Palatini gravity, considering linear, Brans-Dicke-like, and Higgs-like sectors. The scalar spectral index lies in the range \( n_s \simeq 0.93 \ \text{--} \ 0.98 \), consistent with \textit{Planck} and combined \textit{Planck}+ACT data. The tensor-to-scalar ratio can reach \( r \sim 0.03 \) in metric, whereas Palatini models generically predict \( r \lesssim 10^{-5} \). In the Palatini case, field excursions remain sub-Planckian, and the perturbative unitarity cutoff is raised. Reheating proceeds via perturbative inflaton decays into Higgs bosons and fermionic dark matter (DM) through the portal coupling \( λ_{12} \) and Yukawa coupling \( y_χ\). Radiative stability of the inflationary plateau constrains the couplings to \( y_χ, λ_{12} \sim 10^{-7} \ \text{--} \ 10^{-3} \), implying \( 4\,\mathrm{MeV} \lesssim T_{\rm rh} \lesssim 10^{15}\,\mathrm{GeV} \). Palatini realizations require smaller couplings and thus a narrower reheating window. Non-thermal DM production $χ$ from inflaton decays is viable for DM mass \( m_χ\sim \mathrm{keV} \ \text{--} \ \mathrm{PeV} \) with \( y_χ\lesssim 10^{-6} \) over large parameter regions. We estimate the inflaton-right-handed neutrino (RHN) Yukawa coupling \( y_N \) required for successful baryogenesis via non-thermal leptogenesis within a Type-I seesaw framework, for the lightest RHN mass \( M_{N_1} \sim 10^{9} \ \text{--} \ 10^{14}\,\mathrm{GeV} \), provided \( M_{N_1} > T_{\rm max} \), where \( T_{\rm max} \) follows from radiatively consistent reheating. In Palatini scenarios, the lower maximal temperature and tighter stability bounds further restrict the leptogenesis parameter space.

### [38] [Dirac one-loop seesaw in a non-invertible fusion rule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11308)
*Hiroshi Okada,Labh Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过非可逆融合规则（non-invertible fusion rule）稳定的辐射狄拉克中微子质量模型，该模型同时解释了中微子振荡数据并提供了可行的暗物质候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在构建一个最小化的标准模型扩展框架，该框架能够同时解释中微子质量和混合现象，并提供暗物质候选者。研究动机在于探索非可逆融合规则作为构建统一辐射框架的组织原则的潜力。

Method: 通过引入$Z_3 \times Z_3'$规范对称性，该模型禁止了树级汤川耦合（tree-level Yukawa couplings），确保中微子质量仅通过奇异费米子（exotic fermions）和惰性标量（inert scalars）的单圈辐射修正生成。同时分析了轻子味破坏过程（lepton flavor violating processes）和轻子反常磁矩（lepton anomalous magnetic moments）。

Result: 模型成功容纳了与当前振荡数据一致的中微子质量和混合参数，所有轻子味破坏和反常磁矩贡献均远低于现有实验上限。在暗物质领域，玻色子单态（bosonic singlet）展现出与宇宙学观测相容的遗迹密度，而费米子选项则因湮灭截面（annihilation cross sections）被抑制而被强烈排除。

Conclusion: 研究表明，非可逆融合规则可以作为构建最小化且现象学一致的标准模型扩展的有力组织原则，在中微子物理和暗物质之间建立了统一的辐射框架联系。

Abstract: We propose a radiative Dirac neutrino mass model stabilized by a non-invertible fusion rule originating from a $Z_3 \times Z_3'$ gauging. The imposed symmetry forbids tree-level Yukawa couplings and ensures that neutrino masses are generated only at the one-loop level through the exchange of exotic fermions and inert scalars. This minimal framework simultaneously accommodates neutrino masses and mixings consistent with current oscillation data, while providing a viable dark matter candidate. We analyze lepton flavor violating processes and lepton anomalous magnetic moments, finding that all contributions remain well below present experimental bounds. In the dark matter sector, the bosonic singlet emerges as a promising candidate with relic density compatible with cosmological observations, whereas the fermionic option is strongly disfavored due to suppressed annihilation cross sections. Our study demonstrates that non-invertible fusion rules can serve as a powerful organizing principle for constructing minimal and phenomenologically consistent extensions of the Standard Model, linking neutrino physics and dark matter within a unified radiative framework.

### [39] [Emergence of Complex Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11481)
*Francisco-Shu Kitaura*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一框架，结合相空间动力学、输运几何、信息论和粗粒化有效模型，解释复杂结构从初始均匀状态中形成的表观熵增矛盾。该框架将密度放大与变形雅可比矩阵相联系，将各向异性塌缩与变形张量特征值关联，并通过位移场编码非局域性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决复杂结构从初始均匀或弱关联状态中形成时，表观的有序化与熵增长之间的张力。这一矛盾在宇宙结构形成等自组织过程中尤为突出，需要统一的理论框架来解释。

Method: 采用拉格朗日-欧拉输运映射（Lagrangian-Eulerian transport map），结合半微观相空间动力学、输运几何、信息论和粗粒化有效建模。通过变形雅可比矩阵描述密度放大，利用变形张量特征值分析各向异性塌缩，并将位移场作为非局域相互作用的编码机制。

Result: 框架表明密度放大由变形雅可比矩阵控制，各向异性塌缩源于变形张量特征值的层次结构。非局域相互作用通过位移场直接进入输运过程，非线性输运和非局域耦合产生尺度耦合、高阶关联和非高斯性。在宇宙学应用中，非局域潮汐水平在中等过密度时已变得相关。

Conclusion: 该框架为理解自组织系统提供了介观语言，其中输运、各向异性、非局域性和自组织是核心要素。虽然主要应用于宇宙结构形成，但框架具有更广泛的适用性，能够解释种子各向异性增长作为有效自由能较低分支的激活过程。

Abstract: Complex structures often emerge from initially homogeneous or weakly correlated states. We address the apparent tension between this ordering and entropy growth through a unified framework combining semi-microscopic phase-space dynamics, transport geometry, information theory, and coarse-grained effective modeling. The key point is that entropy depends on the level of description: a coarse-grained spatial field may become more ordered as structure forms, even while the full phase-space description becomes more complex through shell crossing, multistreaming, and the activation of velocity degrees of freedom. Using a Lagrangian--Eulerian transport map, we show how density amplification is governed by the Jacobian of the deformation and how anisotropic collapse arises from the eigenvalues of a hierarchy of deformation tensors. Long-range interaction or information flow is encoded in the displacement field, so that nonlocality enters directly through transport. We connect this geometric description to a maximum-entropy Gaussian baseline and show how nonlinear transport and nonlocal coupling generate scale coupling, higher-order correlations, and non-Gaussianity. We then formulate a Landau--Ginzburg description in which the growth of seed anisotropies is interpreted as the activation of lower effective free-energy branches, providing a coarse-grained realization of self-organization. Applied to generated cosmological fields, this framework indicates that the nonlocal tidal level becomes relevant already at moderate overdensity. Although cosmological structure formation is the main realization considered here, the framework is intended more broadly as a mesoscopic language for systems in which transport, anisotropy, nonlocality, and self-organization are central.

</details>


### [40] [Inflationary magnetogenesis from non-minimal coupling in large- and small-field potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10143)
*Orlando Luongo,Antonino Giacomo Marino,Tommaso Mengoni*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了暴胀磁生成（inflationary magnetogenesis）中，通过暴胀子与里奇标量的非最小耦合打破电磁学共形不变性的场景。研究发现非最小耦合作为时序参数调控电磁反作用和施温格效应，大幅增强大场暴胀模型中的磁场生成，而小场模型则产生可忽略的磁场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索通过暴胀子与里奇标量的非最小汤川型耦合打破电磁学共形不变性，从而在暴胀期间生成宇宙磁场的机制。该研究特别关注电磁反作用和施温格效应的影响，并分析不同暴胀模型下的磁生成效率。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）建立暴胀子与里奇标量的非最小汤川型耦合框架；2）考虑电磁反作用和施温格效应；3）分析标准单场暴胀和广义K-essence框架（称为准精质）；4）采用符合普朗克卫星约束的暴胀势能，包括大场的Starobinsky和α-attractor模型以及小场的hilltop情景；5）探索不同的电磁耦合函数形式，特别为小场模型引入新的ansatz。

Result: 研究结果显示：1）非最小耦合作为时序参数调控电磁反作用和施温格效应起始时间；2）大场暴胀模型中磁场振幅相比最小耦合情况增强数个数量级，现今值可达B₀∼10⁻¹³G；3）大场模型是唯一与观测约束兼容的情景；4）小场模型产生可忽略的磁场振幅，在非最小框架内缺乏预测性。

Conclusion: 结论表明非最小耦合在暴胀磁生成过程中起核心作用，通过调控电磁反作用和施温格效应起始时间，显著改变磁生成机制。大场暴胀模型（如Starobinsky和α-attractor模型）能够产生与观测兼容的显著磁场，而小场模型在该框架下效果有限。

Abstract: We investigate inflationary magnetogenesis in a scenario where conformal invariance of electromagnetism is broken through a \emph{non-minimal Yukawa-like coupling between the inflaton and the Ricci scalar}. We account for electromagnetic backreaction and the Schwinger effect, analyzing both standard single-field inflation and a generalized K-essence framework, \emph{dubbed quasi-quintessence}. We consider inflationary potentials compatible with Planck satellite constraints, including Starobinsky and $α$-attractor models for large fields, as well as hilltop scenarios for small fields. Moreover, we explore very different functional electromagnetic couplings, introducing a novel ansatz modeled for small-fields. We show that the non-minimal coupling plays a central role in controlling the dynamics, \emph{acting as a timing parameter that regulates the onset of electric backreaction and the Schwinger regime}. This leads to a deep modification of the magnetogenesis process. Indeed, the amplitude of the generated magnetic fields can be enhanced by several orders of magnitude with respect to the minimally coupled case, reaching present-day values up to $B_0 \sim 10^{-13}\,\mathrm{G}$ in large-field scenarios, \emph{which appear as the only ones compatible with observational bounds}. Conversely, small-field models yield negligible magnetic amplitudes and appear non-predictive within our non-minimal framework.
