Method: 首先通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）获得应变下的交换耦合项，并通过次近邻Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用引入拓扑性质。采用线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory）和Holstein-Primakoff变换计算磁振子哈密顿量，最后使用非平衡格林函数方法（non-equilibrium Green's function method）计算不同边缘应变下的自旋波产生电流。

Result: 计算显示，在略高于实验报道值的DMI参数和约3%的拉伸边缘应变下，能隙内会形成强局域化的边缘拓扑磁振子。与未应变样品相比，拉伸应变的CrI₃纳米带表现出更高的自旋电流和更长的特征衰减长度。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，应变工程为调控二维磁性材料中的拓扑磁振子提供了一条有效途径。应变可以显著增强拓扑磁振子的输运特性，为基于拓扑磁振子的自旋电子学器件设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: This work describes topological magnon transport in zigzag CrI$_3$ nanoribbons (ZNR) in presence of edge strain. Exchange coupling terms under strain are obtained from first-principles calculations, and the topological properties are introduced \emph{via} second-neighbor Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions. The magnon Hamiltonian is calculated using linear spin-wave theory and the Holstein-Primakoff transformation. Then, we use non-equilibrium Green's function method to calculate the spin-wave-generated currents in ribbons with different edge strain. Our calculations show the formation of strongly localized edge topological magnons within the gap for DMI values slightly higher than the ones reported experimentally and in the presence of a tensile edge strain of the order of 3\%. The magnon-mediated topological spin transport calculations shows an increase of the spin current and characteristic decay length in tensile-strained CrI$_3$ nanoribbons compared with unstrained ones. Our findings demonstrate that straintronics provides a powerful route to harness and control topological magnons in two-dimensional magnetic materials.

</details>


### [92] [Ultrafast ghost Hall states in a 2d altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11361)
*Ruikai Wu,Deepika Gill,Sangeeta Sharma,Sam Shallcross*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过Cr₂SO示例，揭示了二维交变磁体（2d altermagnets）中的能谷态可由飞秒激光控制，为超快自旋和电荷电流调控提供了新平台。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料中的自旋和能谷自由度为光与物质的超快相互作用提供了重要平台。研究旨在探索二维交变磁体（2d altermagnets）中飞秒激光对能谷态的控制能力。

Method: 以Cr₂SO为例，通过线性偏振飞秒激光脉冲激发两个不等效能谷中的电荷，能谷激发由偏振矢量方向决定。

Abstract: Two-dimensional materials that exhibit optically active spin and valley degrees of freedom represent one of the most fascinating -- and potentially most technologically useful -- platforms for the ultrafast interaction of light and matter. Here we show, via the example of Cr$_2$SO, that two dimensional altermagnets host valley states controllable by femtosecond laser light: linearly polarized light pulses excite charge at one of two inequivalent valleys, with which valley charge is excited at determined by the polarization vector direction. This underpins a rich spin and valley physics including: (i) valleytronics $-$ the generation of nearly 100$\%$ spin polarized valley currents, as well as (ii) a "ghost Hall" effect $-$ the ultrafast creation of states in which spin and charge currents are orthogonal without invoking Hall physics. Our findings establish 2d altermagents as a platform providing a new route for the control of spin- and charge currents at ultrafast times.

  <summary>Details</summary>

The electronic properties are modified when the amplitude of the curvature of the sheet increases, which induces Van Hove singularities of the electronic Density of States to approach the Fermi energy. The highly curved system exhibits coexisting flat and linear dispersions close to the Fermi level, which is a promising feature for thermoelectric applications. We also demonstrate, through the phonon dispersion curves, that respective systems are dynamically stable within the studied range of strains/curvatures. Method: 基于磁性外尔半金属（magnetic Weyl semimetal）Co3Sn2S2，研究采用多畴模型（multi-domain model）推导出霍尔磁阻的简洁公式，并通过实验验证该理论预测。

According to a multi-domain model, a concise formula of this Hall magnetoresistance was revealed and verified experimentally. Rather than the real change of longitudinal resistance, this Hall magnetoresistance originates from an additional electric field distribution induced by the transverse giant AHE through the domain wall, which can be directly correlated to the Berry phase of topological Weyl bands. In Co3Sn2S2 devices, the Hall magnetoresistance was an order of magnitude larger than that of conventional magnetic materials, indicating its potential for multi-resistance-state modulation via the Weyl-enhanced AHE.

Abstract: Low-energy electronic behavior in graphite crystals is highly dependent on the relative stacking arrangement of the constituent layers. Topologically non-trivial electronic states can arise due to interrupted rhombohedral (ABC) stacking, localized at the edges of the stacking region, but not in the case of Bernal (AB) stacking. Here, we study the electronic properties of junctions between half-crystals of graphite of either Bernal or rhombohedral stacking, using a charge self-consistent tight-binding method and embedding potentials to account for the influence of layers far from the junction. We find junction-localized electronic states to be a ubiquitous feature, and all systems but one involving a rhombohedral half-crystal support a flat-band expected to exhibit electronic instabilities and strongly-correlated states. Nascent flat-band states associated with finite rhombohedral stacking sequences extend the physics into pure Bernal systems.

### [96] [Semiclassical theory of frequency dependent linear magneto-optical transport in Weyl semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11527)
*Azaz Ahmad,Pankaj Bhalla,Snehasish Nandy,Tanay Nag*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究发展了一套用于外尔半金属（Weyl semimetals）频率依赖磁光输运的半经典玻尔兹曼理论，揭示了手性反常（chiral anomaly）在不同交流驱动机制下的抑制机制，以及外尔锥倾斜（Weyl cone tilt）对纵向磁光导率（LMOC）的显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解外尔半金属中频率依赖的磁光输运特性，特别关注手性反常、轨道磁矩（orbital magnetic moment）、外尔锥倾斜以及谷间散射（intervalley scattering）之间的相互作用，为兆赫-太赫兹磁光实验提供理论框架。

Method: 采用半经典玻尔兹曼理论（semiclassical Boltzmann theory）结合散射矩阵方法（scattering matrix approach）处理动量依赖的弛豫过程，在静态磁场存在下分析电磁驱动机制，获得完整的电导率张量。

Result: 在弱交流驱动下，强谷间散射导致纵向磁光导率符号反转，从而抑制手性反常；而在强交流驱动下，谷间散射无法在一个驱动周期内平衡手性不平衡。轨道磁矩产生线性磁场响应，而手性反常产生二次响应。横向倾斜导致对称非单调行为，平行倾斜导致不对称近单调响应，负纵向磁光导率在平行倾斜下本征出现，而在横向倾斜下需要轨道磁矩。

Conclusion: 频率依赖的电导率可作为兆赫-太赫兹磁光实验中手性弛豫的灵敏探针，研究结果揭示了外尔半金属中手性反常的抑制机制以及外尔锥倾斜对磁光响应的关键调控作用。

Abstract: We develop a semiclassical Boltzmann theory for frequency-dependent magneto-optical transport in Weyl semimetals (WSMs), incorporating momentum-dependent relaxation via a scattering matrix approach. The interplay of orbital magnetic moment, Weyl cone tilt, intervalley scattering, and electromagnetic driving is analyzed to obtain the full conductivity tensor in the presence of a static magnetic field. For untilted WSMs with orbital magnetic moment, strong intervalley scattering in the weak ac regime induces a sign reversal of the longitudinal magneto-optical conductivity (LMOC), thereby suppressing the chiral anomaly. In contrast, in the strong ac regime, intervalley scattering fails to neutralize the chiral imbalance within a driving cycle, and no sign reversal is observed. Orbital magnetic moment induces linear magnetic-field contributions, while chiral anomaly yields quadratic response accompanied by expected angular profiles. Tilt direction and orientation strongly affect LMOC such as, transverse tilt gives symmetric non-monotonic behavior, whereas parallel tilt leads to asymmetric, nearly monotonic response. Notably, negative LMOC arises intrinsically for parallel tilt, but requires orbital magnetic moment for transverse tilt. These results highlight frequency-dependent conductivity as a sensitive probe of chiral relaxation in MHz-THz magneto-optical experiments.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Bulk-boundary correspondence guarantees the presence of robust, anomalous states on the boundary of topological matter. In this work we show that step edges on the surface of three-dimensional topological metals have a robust conductance $K\, e^2/h$, where $K$ is also fixed by the bulk and assumes non-integer values. We explain this prediction on the basis of the topology of gapless systems, exemplify it on a lattice model, and connect to recent experimental observations of enhanced density of states at step-edges in topological metals.

### [99] [Geometry-controlled magnon-polariton excitations in a bilayer planar cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11690)
*S. Solihin,Ahmad R. T. Nugraha,Muhammad Aziz Majidi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了双层平面腔中两个磁性薄膜通过腔场和驻波图案相对位置相互作用的机制，揭示了通过几何、对称性和交换驱动模式层次控制集体磁子-极化子结构的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面腔磁子学（planar cavity magnonics）主要针对单个磁性薄膜发展，而多个磁性层在具有空间分辨率的腔散射框架中的作用尚未充分探索。本研究旨在填补这一空白，探索双层平面腔中磁性薄膜的相互作用机制。

Method: 首先在宏观自旋极限（macrospin limit）下推导了完整的双膜散射理论，并与已知的单膜平面结果进行基准测试。然后引入弱对称破缺（weak symmetry breaking）分析，并针对$J\neq 0$情况制定了简化的多模双层理论（reduced multimode bilayer theory）。

Result: 双层结构并非简单地通过增加磁性材料来增强磁子-光子相互作用（magnon-photon interaction），而是实现了对集体亮通道（collective bright channel）的位置依赖性控制。驻波波腹兼容位置增强有效耦合，而波节兼容位置抑制耦合。弱对称破缺将有限腔权重转移到对称极限下的暗模式，产生额外的光谱分支而不立即破坏主要的避免交叉（avoided crossing）。

Conclusion: 双层平面腔是通过几何、对称性和交换驱动模式层次（exchange-driven mode hierarchy）控制集体磁子-极化子（magnon-polariton）结构的最小但多功能平台，其中奇数驻自旋波族（odd standing-spin-wave families）重组为族分辨的亮和暗双层通道。

Abstract: Planar cavity magnonics has been developed predominantly for a single magnetic film, leaving the role of multiple magnetic layers in a cavity-scattering framework with spatial resolution largely unexplored. In this study, we introduce a bilayer planar cavity in which two magnetic films are embedded inside the same microwave cavity and interact through the cavity field and their relative placement within the standing-wave pattern. First, we derive a full two-film scattering theory in the macrospin limit and recover the exact zero-gap half-thickness limit to benchmark it against the known one-film planar result. This formulation reveals that the bilayer does not simply strengthen the magnon-photon interaction by adding magnetic material but instead enables position-dependent control of the collective bright channel. Antinode-compatible placements enhance effective coupling, whereas node-compatible placements suppress it. We then show that weak symmetry breaking between the two films transfers the finite cavity weight to a mode that is dark in the symmetric limit, producing an additional spectroscopic branch without immediately destroying the main avoided crossing. To extend the analysis beyond the macrospin regime, we formulate a reduced multimode bilayer theory for $J\neq 0$, where odd standing-spin-wave families reorganize into family-resolved bright and dark bilayer channels. Our results show that bilayer planar cavities are a minimal but versatile setting for controlling the collective magnon-polariton structure through geometry, symmetry, and exchange-driven mode hierarchy.

</details>

### [100] [Numerical Modeling of Solvent Diffusion through the Transition Metal Dichalcogenides based Nanomaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09751)
*Geetika Sahu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟分析了溶剂在过渡金属二硫化物基纳米材料中的扩散过程，揭示了溶剂热反应中溶剂扩散如何导致层剥离和纳米颗粒尺寸减小，并探讨了关键参数对颗粒尺寸均匀性的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解溶剂热反应（solvothermal reaction）过程中溶剂扩散对过渡金属二硫化物（transition metal dichalcogenide）基纳米材料结构演化的影响，特别是层剥离（layer exfoliation）和纳米颗粒尺寸减小的机制。

Method: 通过求解修正的菲克扩散定律（modified Ficks law of diffusion）并利用动态键渗流模型（dynamic bond percolation model），模拟纳米颗粒系统的演化过程；同时采用雪崩统计（avalanche statistics）和香农熵（Shannon entropy）分析平均纳米颗粒尺寸的波动。

Result: 模拟结果显示，扩散率变量（diffusivity variable）和迭代次数对纳米颗粒尺寸均匀性有显著影响；建立了最大熵对应的迭代次数与颗粒尺寸相对变化最小值之间的相关性，表明存在使系统达到纳米颗粒平均尺寸饱和状态的迭代点。

Conclusion: 数值模拟结果表明，实验参数如溶剂选择性（solvent selectivity）、扩散率（diffusivity）和反应时间（reaction time）对纳米颗粒尺寸和均匀性具有决定性作用，这些发现有助于优化材料性能并增强其潜在应用价值。

Abstract: This article presents a numerical simulation of solvent diffusion in transition metal dichalcogenide based nanomaterials during solvothermal reaction, leading to layer exfoliation and, consequently, a reduction in the average nanoparticle size. By solving modified Ficks law of diffusion and utilizing the dynamic bond percolation model, this study examines the evolution of a system of nanoparticles. During the simulation, the effects of key parameters, such as the diffusivity variable that determines the diffusion rate, and the number of iterations needed to achieve enhanced nanoparticle size uniformity, have been analyzed. To gain more insight into the size evolution of the nanoparticles, avalanche statistics, and fluctuations in the average nanoparticle size by Shannon entropy has been utilized. The size distribution observed for different diffusivity variables and iterations has also been studied, which predicts the probability of finding the nanoparticles of specific sizes within the system. A correlation between the iteration for maximum entropy and the minimum of relative change in particle size with iteration has been established, indicating that an iteration exists that takes the system towards saturation in terms of the average size of the nanoparticles. The numerical findings indicate that the experimental parameters, such as solvent selectivity and diffusivity, as well as reaction time, play significant roles in determining nanoparticle size and uniformity, thereby enhancing potential material applications.

</details>


### [101] [Heterogeneous Molecular Signatures of Human Odor Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09758)
*P. Zanineli,E. V. C. Lopes,G. R. Schleder,L. N. Lemos,F. Crasto de Lima,A. Fazzio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过可解释机器学习模型分析分子描述符对气味感知的贡献，发现不同气味类别具有特异性的物理化学特征重要性模式，而非单一描述符类别主导，表明嗅觉编码具有受体和气味依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解分子结构如何产生气味感知是一个长期挑战，存在关于嗅觉主要受分子形状、振动特性或它们在嗅觉受体层面相互作用的持续争论。本研究旨在探究不同气味是否依赖于共同的分子决定因素，还是源自不同的物理化学机制。

Method: 使用基于第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）推导的分子描述符训练可解释机器学习模型（interpretable machine-learning models），这些描述符涵盖电子、振动和结构特性。分析气味类别及其相关受体的特征贡献。

Result: 研究发现没有单一描述符类别普遍主导气味预测；相反，不同气味表现出强烈的气味特异性特征重要性模式，在物理化学领域存在显著变异性。这种异质性在不同模型间保持一致，表明通用编码方案无法捕捉气味感知。

Conclusion: 研究结果为竞争性嗅觉理论提供了统计约束，并为组织气味空间（odor space）提供了一个数据驱动的框架，表明气味感知反映了受体和气味依赖性的结构-气味关系（structure-odor relationships）。

Abstract: Understanding how molecular structure gives rise to odor perception remains a long-standing challenge, with ongoing debate over whether olfaction is primarily governed by molecular shape, vibrational properties, or their interplay at the level of olfactory receptors. Here, we ask whether different odors rely on common molecular determinants or instead emerge from distinct physicochemical regimes. Using interpretable machine-learning models trained on molecular descriptors derived from first-principles calculations that span electronic, vibrational, and structural properties, we analyze feature contributions for odor categories and their associated receptors. We find that no single descriptor class universally dominates odor prediction; instead, different odors exhibit strongly odor-specific patterns of feature importance, with substantial variability across physicochemical domains. This heterogeneity is consistent across different models, suggesting that a universal encoding scheme does not capture odor perception but reflects receptor- and odor-dependent structure-odor relationships. Our results provide statistical constraints on competing olfactory theories and offer a data-driven framework for organizing odor space.

</details>


### [102] [Ferromagnetic interlayer exchange coupling in a few layers of CrSBr on a gold thin film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09794)
*Rixt Bosma,Darius A. Pacurar,Daniel Sade,Jingbo Wang,Nicholas Dale,Cameron W. Johnson,Sergii Grytsiuk,Alexander Rudenko,Alexander Stibor,Malte Roesner,Marcos H. D. Guimaraes,Roberto Lo Conte*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过自旋极化低能电子显微镜直接观测了Au薄膜上CrSBr薄层的磁结构，发现厚度小于11 nm时呈现铁磁基态，而非传统的反铁磁态。这种磁性调控源于Au向CrSBr的电子转移，为二维磁体的基底工程调控提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维范德华（van der Waals）磁体因其可通过邻近效应和电刺激有效调控特性，在自旋电子学（spintronics）中具有应用前景。研究旨在探索通过基底工程调控二维磁体磁性的可能性。

Method: 采用自旋极化低能电子显微镜（spin-polarized low energy electron microscopy）直接成像Au薄膜上CrSBr薄层的磁结构。结合反射电子光谱（reflected-electron spectroscopy）分析未占据态密度差异，并通过第一性原理密度泛函理论（ab-initio density functional theory）计算验证电子转移机制。

Result: 发现厚度小于11 nm的CrSBr在Au基底上呈现铁磁（ferromagnetic）基态，而非传统反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）态。反射电子光谱显示薄层CrSBr与块体CrSBr的未占据态密度存在明显差异，表明电子能带结构发生了改变。

Conclusion: 铁磁有序的稳定源于Au薄膜向CrSBr薄片的电子转移，这一机制与第一性原理计算结果一致。该工作揭示了通过基底工程调控二维磁体磁性的可能性，为自旋电子学应用提供了新思路。

Abstract: The two-dimensional character of van der Waals magnets allows for efficient control of their properties via proximity effects and electrical stimuli, making them promising candidates for application in spin-electronics. We use spin-polarized low energy electron microscopy to directly image the magnetic texture of thin CrSBr on top of a Au film, uncovering a ferromagnetic ground state for CrSBr thicknesses smaller than 11 nm. We argue that the stabilization of the ferromagnetic ordering - as compared to the conventional antiferromagnetic one - is obtained via electron transfer from the Au film to the CrSBr flakes, in agreement with ab-initio density functional theory calculations. Reflected-electron spectroscopy shows clear differences in the unoccupied density of states between a few layers of CrSBr on Au and bulk CrSBr, pointing towards electronic band structure modification in thin CrSBr. This work sheds light on the possibility to tune magnetic properties of two-dimensional magnets via substrate engineering.

</details>


### [103] [Self-compensation by silicon $DX$ centers in ultrawide-bandgap nitrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09842)
*John L. Lyons,Darshana Wickramaratne*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了DX中心（DX centers）在超宽带隙氮化物（如AlN和c-BN）中对n型掺杂的限制机制，指出硅掺杂时DX中心会捕获两个电子形成负电荷态，导致自补偿效应，从而严重限制自由电子浓度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DX中心行为限制了超宽带隙氮化物（如氮化铝和立方氮化硼）中的n型载流子浓度。这些材料中，DX中心不是作为有效质量施主，而是捕获两个电子形成稳定的负电荷态，导致自补偿效应，这阻碍了实现高n型掺杂的目标。

Method: 通过结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算温度依赖的带隙和硅掺杂剂跃迁能级，分析了硅掺杂AlN中的补偿机制。该方法允许在没有其他缺陷的情况下评估DX中心对掺杂效率的影响。

Result: 研究发现硅掺杂AlN中存在显著补偿，即使没有其他缺陷。AlN中硅的DX能级位于导带最小值以下约270 meV，导致许多硅杂质带负电并补偿预期的n型掺杂。自由电子浓度变得与掺杂浓度无关，仅在轻掺杂情况下才有显著的施主激活。

Conclusion: DX中心引起的自补偿强烈限制了AlN中的自由电子浓度。在AlGaN合金或c-BN中，由于DX能级更接近导带最小值，可以获得更高的自由载流子浓度。这表明材料选择对克服DX中心限制至关重要。

Abstract: \textit{DX} behavior limits $n$-type carrier concentrations in ultrawide-bandgap nitrides such as aluminum nitride (AlN) and cubic boron nitride ($c$-BN). Instead of acting as effective-mass donors, \textit{DX} centers capture two electrons, stabilizing a negative charge state that leads to self compensation. Silicon is the most effective $n$-type dopant in this class of materials; in AlN, its \textit{DX} level [(i.e., the (+/$-$) transition level] is $\sim$270 meV from the conduction-band minimum. This implies that many silicon impurities incorporated into AlN will be negatively charged and compensate the intended $n$-type doping. By combining density functional theory calculations of temperature-dependent band gaps and Si dopant transition levels, we show here that significant compensation occurs in silicon-doped AlN, even in the absence of any other defects. This compensation strongly limits free electron concentrations which become independent of doping concentration, and donor activation is only significant for light doping scenarios. Higher free carrier concentrations can be achieved in AlGaN alloys or in $c$-BN, where the \textit{DX} level sits closer to the conduction-band minimum.

</details>


### [104] [Structural Motif Selection in Fluorinated Metal-Organic Chalcogenides Driven by Ligand Electrostatics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09864)
*Md. Saiful Islam,Tomoaki Sakurada,Yeongsu Cho*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论计算揭示了氟化苯配体在银硒基金属有机硫族化物（MOCs）中如何通过配体间静电相互作用主导结构基元选择，建立了基于配体堆积和静电控制的结构设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合有机-无机材料（hybrid organic-inorganic materials）通过有机配体的化学修饰可实现系统结构调控，但预测性控制需要理解配体化学与无机框架如何共同决定结构基元选择（structural motif selection）。金属有机硫族化物（metal-organic chalcogenides, MOCs）为此提供了理想平台。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）结合基于片段的能量分析（fragment-based energy analysis）识别结构基元选择的主要能量驱动因素。进一步使用对称性适配微扰理论（symmetry-adapted perturbation theory）分解配体间相互作用。

Result: 研究发现配体间相互作用（ligand-ligand interactions）是结构基元选择的主要能量驱动因素。静电相互作用（electrostatic interactions）通过选择性稳定特定堆积排列而决定优选基元。配体取向控制长程静电相互作用的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究建立了基于物理原理的设计原则，即通过靶向控制配体堆积（ligand packing）和静电特性来指导MOCs中的结构基元选择，为混合材料的预测性结构设计提供了机制性理解。

Abstract: Hybrid organic-inorganic materials enable systematic structural tuning through chemical modification of organic ligands. Predictive control, however, requires mechanistic understanding of how ligand chemistry and inorganic frameworks jointly determine structural motif selection. Metal-organic chalcogenides (MOCs), where metal-chalcogenide units are covalently bonded to organic ligands, offer an ideal platform in which ligand substitution directly alters crystal structure. Here, we investigate silver selenide-based MOCs with fluorinated phenyl ligands to elucidate governing interactions. Density functional theory with fragment-based energy analysis identifies ligand-ligand interactions as the primary energetic driver of motif selection. Symmetry-adapted perturbation theory further decomposes ligand-ligand interactions and shows that electrostatic interactions are decisive in selecting the preferred motif by selectively stabilizing specific packing arrangements. The results further show that ligand orientation controls the effectiveness of long-range electrostatic interactions, establishing a physically grounded design principle for directing structural motifs in MOCs through targeted control of ligand packing and electrostatics.

</details>


### [105] [Ultrasonic characterization of generally anisotropic elasticity implementing optimal zeroth-order elastic bounds and a wave-fitting approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09865)
*Diego Cowes,Juan I. Mieza,MArtín P. Gómez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种超声测角法，通过扫描球坐标测量波在样品中的传播，结合平面波模型和GPU加速，实现了对高度各向异性材料弹性特性的高效表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料的弹性行为对工业结构组件的设计、制造和测试至关重要。超声技术因能灵活改变波入射角度，特别适合表征各向异性（anisotropic）材料的方向依赖性特性。

Method: 开发了超声测角法（ultrasonic goniometry method），在样品传输波的同时扫描球坐标。建立了考虑流体-固体界面的平面波模型（plane-wave model），适用于多种样品厚度，并假设一般各向异性，可表征三斜晶系（triclinic）对称性材料。采用专门设计的换能器支持平面波近似，避免计算昂贵的有限束模型，并在GPU架构上实现前向模型以降低计算成本。

Result: 引入最优零阶边界（optimal zeroth-order bounds）紧密界定搜索空间，各向同性自洽解（isotropic self-consistent solution）提供了有效的初始猜测。板状样品的测量结果与文献和基于衍射的方法进行了比较。

Conclusion: 该方法无需精确样品对准，通过GPU加速显著降低了波形拟合反演（waveform fitting inversion）所需的多次评估计算成本，实现了对高度各向异性材料弹性特性的高效表征。

Abstract: The elastic behavior of materials is of critical importance for the design, fabrication, and testing of industrial and structural components. The ease with which the wave angle of incidence can be varied makes ultrasonic techniques well suited for the characterization of anisotropic materials, whose properties are direction-dependent. This work aims to develop an ultrasonic goniometry method in which a wave is transmitted through a sample while scanning over spherical coordinates. A plane-wave model is formulated that accounts for fluid-solid interfaces and is applicable to a wide range of sample thicknesses. The model assumes general anisotropy, enabling the characterization of materials with symmetries up to triclinic, and does not require precise sample alignment. Specially designed transducers support the plane-wave approximation, thereby avoiding the need for more computationally expensive finite-beam models. Furthermore, implementation of the forward model on GPU architectures significantly reduces the computational cost associated with the numerous evaluations required during the waveform fitting inversion. The introduction of optimal zeroth-order bounds is used to tightly delimit the search space, and an isotropic self-consistent solution is shown to provide an effective initial guess. Finally, measurements on plate-like samples are compared with the literature and diffraction-based methods.

</details>


### [106] [Closing the ultrahigh temperature metrology gap: non-contact thermal conductivity ($\mathrm{k}$) and spectral emittance ($\mathrm{\varepsilon_λ}$) of molybdenum up to 3200 K](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09873)
*Hunter B. Schonfeld,Elizabeth Golightly,Milena Milich,Scott Bender,Konstantinos Boboridis,Davide Robba,Luka Vlahovic,Rudy Konings,Ethan Scott,Patrick E. Hopkins*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种改进的超高温稳态温度差辐射测量法（SSTDR），用于在1500-3000K范围内测量高纯度钼的固态热导率，并同时获取固态和液态钼的光谱发射率数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代高超音速热结构、高热通量聚变或裂变组件以及激光增材制造的发展需要可靠的高温和超高温固态热导率数据。传统测量方法在这些条件下对接触电阻、不确定边界条件和非线性辐射损耗变得极为敏感。

Method: 该方法将锁相红外热成像与空间局域化、调制扰动激光相结合，形成传导主导的差分观测量，同时结合高光谱高温测量和经过验证的二维轴对称稳态传热模型。使用高纯度钼作为基准材料。

Result: 报告了1500-3000K范围内（至熔化起始点）固态热导率k(T)，通过全面的不确定度传播、敏感性分析和边界研究，不确定度为7.9-11%。同时提供了钼在固态和液态下500-1000nm范围内的法向光谱发射率。

Conclusion: 这些进展确立了SSTDR作为一种准确、非接触的方法，可用于填补高温k(T)数据空白，同时为熔体邻近和极端热通量应用提供急需的相依赖辐射特性数据。

Abstract: Advances in next-generation hypersonic hot structures, high heat-flux fusion or fission components, and laser based additive manufacturing depend on reliable solid state thermal conductivity data at high and ultrahigh temperatures, where conventional measurements become increasingly sensitive to contact resistances, uncertain boundary conditions, and nonlinear radiative losses. Building on our initial demonstration of ultrahigh temperature steady-state temperature differential radiometry (SSTDR), we present a substantially more robust platform aimed at making high temperature thermal and radiative property measurements more routine. The method integrates lock-in infrared thermography with a spatially localized, modulated perturbation laser to form a conduction dominant differential observable along with hyperspectral pyrometry and a validated 2D axisymmetric steady state heat transfer model. Using high purity molybdenum as a benchmark, we report solid state thermal conductivity k(T) from 1500 - 3000 K (to the onset of melting) with uncertainties of 7.9-11 % enabled by comprehensive uncertainty propagation, sensitivity analysis, and bounding studies. We additionally provide normal spectral emittance of molybdenum in both solid and liquid states over 500-1000 nm. These advances establish SSTDR as an accurate, non-contact route for closing the high temperature k(T) data gap while simultaneously producing much needed phase dependent radiative property data for melt adjacent and extreme heat-flux applications. Note: This is a shortened abstract; full version in manuscript.

</details>


### [107] [How Does Intercalation Reshape Layered Structures? A First-Principles Study of Sodium Insertion in Layered Potassium Birnessite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09891)
*Adriana Lee Punaro,Daniel Maldonado-Lopez,Jorge L. Cholula-Díaz,Marcelo Videa,Jose L. Mendoza-Cortes*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究采用第一性原理杂化密度泛函理论（hybrid-level density functional theory）分析了钠离子在层状钾锰矿（birnessite，δ-MnO₂）中的插层过程，系统研究了插层对结构稳定性、振动光谱、离子扩散、电子性质及磁性的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解δ-MnO₂的插层过程对于推进其创新应用至关重要。本研究旨在通过第一性原理计算全面分析钠离子插层对钾锰矿材料性质的影响，为其在能源、电子和自旋电子学领域的应用提供理论基础。

Method: 采用杂化密度泛函理论进行第一性原理计算，通过形成能（formation energy）分析结构稳定性，模拟拉曼光谱（Raman spectra）关联振动与结构性质，利用过渡态理论（transition state theory）研究Na⁺和K⁺离子扩散能垒，并通过模拟X射线衍射和几何分析表征系统对称性与平面密度。

Result: 研究发现Na⁺离子在接近饱和极限时与晶格结合更松散；插层显著改变电子性质，源于Mn氧化态变化、晶格畸变和对称性效应；部分插层结构表现为双极磁性半导体（bipolar magnetic semiconductors），具有自旋电子学应用潜力；体系的带隙和磁行为可通过插层调控。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了插层钾锰矿的全面分析，揭示了钠离子插层对材料结构、振动、扩散、电子和磁性质的影响，表明钾锰矿及其钠共插层体系可作为新一代能源、电子和自旋电子材料。

Abstract: This study presents a first-principles study at the level of hybrid-level density functional theory of the sodium intercalation process in a layered potassium birnessite (a layered manganese dioxide, δ-MnO2). Understanding the intercalation processes of δ-MnO2 is a vital step in advancing its potential innovative applications. Through a formation energy formalism, we analyze the stability of the structure as sodium ions (Na+) are intercalated between layers. Simulated Raman spectra allow us to find relationships between the vibrational and structural properties of the material, i.e. we identify the most important vibrational modes and related them to the structural/geometrical change. The diffusion of Na+ and K+ ions in birnessite is studied by transition state theory, determining the energy barriers to ion displacement in the interlayer. The symmetry and planar density of the system are characterized by simulated X-ray diffraction and geometrical analysis of the optimized structures. Through binding energy analysis, we also find that the Na+ ions are more loosely bound to the lattice as they reach the saturation limit. Finally, the electronic properties are studied via spin-polarized densities of states. As intercalants are added, the electronic properties are profoundly modified, resulting from modification of Mn oxidation states, lattice distortions, and symmetry effects. Moreover, some of the intercalated structures behave as bipolar magnetic semiconductors with potential applications in spintronics devices. In other words, the band gaps and magnetic behavior of the system can be controlled by intercalation. This work provides an overarching analysis of intercalated birnessite and describes the essential properties of potassium birnessite and co-intercalation with Sodium as a next-generation energy, electronic, and spintronic material.

</details>

### [109] [Exchange Frustration and Topological Magnetism in Electrostatically Doped SrRuO3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10019)
*Naafis Ahnaf Shahed,Himanshu Mavani,Zhonglin He,Kai Huang,Mohamed Elekhtiar,Evgeny Y. Tsymbal*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和原子蒙特卡洛模拟（atomistic Monte Carlo simulations），研究BaTiO₃/SrRuO₃界面处极化诱导的电荷调控。通过最小自旋模型（minimal spin model）识别交换挫败作为主要控制参数。

Abstract: Magnetism in transition-metal systems emerges from exchange interactions that depend sensitively on carrier density. Yet leveraging this sensitivity to deliberately engineer exchange frustration and associated topological spin textures remains largely unexplored. Here, combining first-principles calculations with atomistic Monte Carlo simulations, we demonstrate that ferroelectric polarization enables electrostatic control of exchange frustration in the itinerant ferromagnet SrRuO3. We show that electrostatic hole doping renormalizes competing exchange interactions, driving SrRuO3 away from its bulk ferromagnetic ground state toward frustrated regimes, whereas electron doping largely preserves ferromagnetism. At BaTiO3/SrRuO3 interfaces, polarization-induced charge depletion modulates layer dependent exchange couplings, enhancing competition among J1, J2 and J3. The resulting exchange frustration stabilizes a sequence of magnetic phases as a function of thickness and applied magnetic field, including stripe and spiral states, topological meron and bimeron textures, and diverse skyrmionic objects. A minimal spin model identifies exchange frustration as the primary control parameter governing these crossovers, with magnetic anisotropy, Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction, and external field selecting the emergent topology. Our results establish electrostatic doping as a route to engineer frustrated and topological magnetism in itinerant oxide metals.

### [113] [Continuous PT-Symmetry Breaking as a Design Variable for Giant Altermagnetic Spin Splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10173)
*Kichan Chun,Gunn Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种连续量化的对称性破缺指标MSBI，结合机器学习方法，实现了从二元对称性分类到连续定量优化的反铁磁体设计范式转变，发现了多个高性能候选材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出连续标量指标MSBI（Motif Symmetry-Breaking Index），直接从晶体坐标量化反平行磁矩之间的$\mathcal{PT}$对称性破缺。基于3,851个DFT标记的二元结构训练XGBoost代理模型，通过SHAP分析识别三个主导描述符：MSBI（对称性破缺轴）、MPF（超交换轴）和p/d电子比（共价性轴）。采用贝叶斯优化在三轴空间进行搜索，并通过独立DFT验证。

Result: 在相同P$6_3$/mmc宿主晶格内，VO-CrSb对比显示仅通过成分调控即可使SSE提升七倍。贝叶斯优化恢复了α-NiS（SSE = 0.823 eV），并识别出三个先前未认知的高SSE候选材料：平面四方FeS（1.297 eV）、八面体CoS（1.103 eV）和FeAs（1.089 eV），均达到或超过CrSb性能。提出平面四方Fe-S配位基元可作为实现巨大反铁磁自旋劈裂的可转移结构单元。

Conclusion: 该研究将反铁磁体设计从对称性分类推进到连续定量优化，通过建立MSBI指标与机器学习方法，实现了高性能反铁磁材料的理性设计与发现，为实验调控提供了明确的物理轴和可调参数。

Abstract: Magnetic point-group analysis classifies altermagnets but returns only a binary symmetry verdict, leaving spin-splitting energy (SSE) inaccessible without spin-polarized density functional theory (DFT). This binary ceiling is not fundamental. Sublattice symmetry breaking is promoted here to a continuous, DFT-free scalar -- the Motif Symmetry-Breaking Index (MSBI) -- that quantifies $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetry breaking between antiparallel magnetic motifs directly from crystal coordinates. SHAP analysis of an XGBoost surrogate trained on 3,851 DFT-labeled binary structures identifies three dominant descriptors: MSBI (symmetry-breaking axis), motif packing fraction MPF (superexchange axis), and the $p/d$ electron ratio (covalency axis), each mapping onto a directly tunable experimental handle. A controlled VO--CrSb comparison within the same P$6_3$/mmc host lattice demonstrates that composition alone boosts SSE sevenfold. Bayesian optimization over this three-axis space, followed by independent DFT validation, recovers $α$-NiS (SSE $= 0.823$\,eV) as cross-validation against an independent symmetry-based prediction and identifies three previously unrecognized high-SSE candidates -- square-planar FeS (1.297\,eV), octahedral CoS (1.103\,eV), and FeAs (1.089\,eV) -- all matching or exceeding CrSb. ### [114] [Brittle-to-ductile fracturing transition: A chemo-mechanical phase-field framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10184)
*Fanyu Wu,Chong Liu,Manolis Veveakis,Manman Hu*

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种完全耦合的化学-力学相场框架，用于捕捉矿物溶解与裂缝扩展之间的动态相互作用。该模型揭示了化学质量去除导致裂缝过程区扩大、裂纹尖端钝化以及材料失效模式从脆性向延性转变的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究提出了一个完全耦合的化学-力学相场框架（fully coupled chemo-mechanical phase-field framework）。该模型的关键特征是将局部质量去除与裂缝长度尺度动态耦合，同时纳入损伤加速的反应-扩散过程（damage-accelerated reaction-diffusion processes）。

Result: 研究结果捕捉到由化学质量去除驱动的扩大裂缝过程区（enlarged fracture process zone）的发展。这种化学诱导的加宽使尖锐裂纹尖端钝化，缓解了近尖端应力集中，导致材料在失效前出现显著的刚度退化。研究还揭示了明显的延性化效应，表现为损伤更渐进积累和宏观失效延迟发生。

Conclusion: 脆性与延性失效模式之间的转变由化学降解与力学变形竞争时间尺度决定。高酸性环境增强基质溶解并促进延性断裂，而快速力学加载限制化学相互作用并保持脆性失效模式。

Abstract: In chemically reactive environments, the mechanical integrity of geomaterials is fundamentally compromised by solid matrix dissolution. In this study, we propose a fully coupled chemo-mechanical phase-field framework to capture the dynamic interplay between mineral dissolution and fracture propagation. A key feature of the proposed model is the dynamic coupling of local mass removal to the fracture length scale, while also incorporating the damage-accelerated reaction-diffusion processes. Our results capture the development of an enlarged fracture process zone driven by chemical mass removal. This chemically induced widening blunts the sharp crack tip, alleviating the near-tip stress concentrations and causing a pronounced degradation in material stiffness before failure. Furthermore, we reveal a distinct ductilization effect, characterized by a more gradual accumulation of damage and a delayed onset of macroscopic failure. We show that the transition between brittle and ductile failure modes is dictated by the competing timescales of chemical degradation and mechanical deformation. Highly acidic environments enhance matrix dissolution and promote ductile fracture, whereas rapid mechanical loading limits chemical interaction and preserves brittle failure mode.

### [115] [Quantifying chirality of phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10231)
*Yu-Chi Huang,Gakuto Kusuno,Yusuke Hashimoto,Dominik Maximilian Juraschek,Hiroaki Kusunose,Takuya Satoh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了量化晶格振动手性（chirality）的理论框架，引入了动量分辨动态手性（momentum-resolved dynamical chirality）和体动态手性（bulk dynamical chirality）两种定量指标，并通过第一性原理计算验证其在手性和非手性材料中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管手性声子（chiral phonons）作为携带角动量并展现手性的晶格振动已引起广泛关注，但其作为动态性质的定量表征仍然缺乏。本研究旨在解决这一关键问题，为手性声子的定量分析提供理论框架。

Method: 研究提出了量化晶格振动动态手性的理论框架，引入两种定量指标：动量分辨动态手性提供模式（mode）和波矢（wave-vector）分辨的手性图像；体动态手性表征热占据手性声子的集体行为。通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）在手性和非手性材料中进行验证。

Result: 计算结果表明，这些定量指标能够有效捕捉声子模式的手性和占据不平衡性，并可作为区分手性晶体对映体（enantiomers）的手段。该框架为手性声子的动态特性提供了系统的定量描述。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了量化晶格振动动态手性的理论框架，提出的两种定量指标为手性声子的表征提供了新工具，有助于区分手性晶体的对映体，推动了手性声子研究从定性描述向定量分析的转变。

Abstract: Recent years have witnessed growing interest in chiral phonons, lattice vibrations carrying angular momentum and exhibiting handedness, as revealed by helicity-dependent optical phenomena. Despite this progress, a quantitative characterization of phonon chirality as a dynamical property has remained elusive. In this work, we propose a theoretical framework to quantify the dynamical chirality of lattice vibrations. We introduce two quantitative measures: momentum-resolved dynamical chirality, which provides a mode- and wave-vector-resolved picture of phonon chirality, and the bulk dynamical chirality, which characterizes the collective behavior of thermally populated chiral phonons. Using first-principles calculations for both chiral and achiral materials, we demonstrate how these quantities capture the handedness and population imbalance of phonon modes and serve as a means to distinguish the enantiomers of chiral crystals.

</details>


### [116] [Probing lattice fluctuations using solid-state high-harmonic spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10304)
*Lance Hatch,Navdeep Rana,Shoushou He,Jessica Yu,Boyang Zhao,Yu Zhang,Haidan Wen,Xavier Roy,Lun Yue,Mette Gaarde,Hanzhe Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和计算揭示了热晶格波动对固态高次谐波产生（HHG）的显著影响，发现低温下晶格振动被抑制时谐波产率急剧增加，并提出可用有效电子退相干时间解释这一现象。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过表征超原子半导体Re6Se8Cl2中高次谐波产生的温度依赖性来探究热晶格波动的影响。结合实验测量和理论计算，分析温度变化对谐波产率的影响机制。

Result: 当样品温度降低时，高次谐波产率呈现缓慢增加，在低于50K时出现急剧增加，这与晶格振动被强烈抑制的温度一致。计算表明热晶格波动既削弱单个扭曲构型的谐波响应，又引起整体相位弥散，从而显著抑制相干发射的谐波。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了高次谐波产生对热晶格波动的深刻敏感性，可用随温度变化的有效电子退相干时间（effective electronic dephasing time）解释。这一发现对包括光波电子学和Floquet工程在内的广泛强场现象中的退相干过程具有重要意义，超原子晶体的广泛可调性进一步实现了材料控制的强场物理。

Abstract: Solid-state high-harmonic spectroscopy allows the study of strongly driven ultrafast electron dynamics. Microscopically, high harmonics are generated by strong-laser-field acceleration of electron-hole pairs through the lattice. At finite temperatures, atomic-scale structural fluctuations are ubiquitous and are expected to influence the electron-hole trajectories. Yet, the effect of thermal lattice fluctuations on solid-state high-harmonic generation (HHG) has not been quantified. Here, we demonstrate a profound sensitivity of HHG to thermal lattice fluctuations, by characterizing the temperature dependence of HHG in Re6Se8Cl2, a superatomic semiconductor. As the sample temperature is decreased, the high-harmonic yield exhibits a slow increase, followed by an abrupt increase below 50 K, consistent with the temperature at which lattice vibrations are strongly suppressed. Our calculations show that thermal lattice fluctuations both weaken the harmonic response from individual distorted configurations and induce phase dispersion across the ensemble, leading to a pronounced suppression of the coherently emitted harmonics. We show that this effect can be interpreted in terms of an effective electronic dephasing time that varies with temperature. Our results are relevant to dephasing in broad strong-field phenomena, including lightwave electronics and Floquet engineering. The wide tunability of superatomic crystals further enables materials-controlled strong-field physics.

Abstract: Selenium, the world's oldest photovoltaic material, has experienced a renaissance in research over the past decade, with certified solar cell efficiencies climbing from the historical record of 5% to breaking the 10% barrier. Its wide bandgap makes it a particularly interesting candidate for tandem solar cells and indoor photovoltaic applications, yet despite steadily improving the carrier collection, devices consistently suffer from a substantial open-circuit voltage deficit. This review provides a critical analysis of the material properties and optoelectronic quality of state-of-the-art selenium thin films. Published results from independent groups are digitized and directly compared, collectively painting a comprehensive picture of the carrier dynamics, supported and contextualized by drift-diffusion simulations. Strategies for synthesizing and processing selenium thin films are also examined in detail, highlighting not only best practices but also the underlying crystal growth kinetics that ultimately govern material quality. ### [118] [The effect of grain boundaries on magnetic exchange interactions in iron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10489)

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论结合蒙特卡洛模拟，探究了晶界（grain boundaries）对bcc铁中磁性交换相互作用的影响，特别关注磷偏析（phosphorus segregation）的作用。研究发现晶界引起局部交换相互作用的显著变化，包括界面处的反铁磁耦合，但整体居里温度（Curie temperature）仅轻微下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在理解晶界如何改变bcc铁中的磁性交换相互作用，特别关注磷偏析对界面磁性的影响。动机源于需要建立原子尺度界面结构与化学性质与介观尺度磁行为之间的关联框架。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）结合Liechtenstein-Katsnelson-Antropov-Gubanov格林函数方法，计算了三种对称倾斜晶界的海森堡交换参数（Heisenberg exchange parameters）。这些参数随后用于蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）以评估有限温度磁行为。

Result: 所有清洁晶界均表现出与体材料交换相互作用的强烈局部偏差，包括界面平面的反铁磁耦合（antiferromagnetic coupling）。这些负交换相互作用不仅由原子间距决定，主要源于晶界处改变的局部配位和对称性破缺。磷偏析抑制了反铁磁耦合，并通过化学和电子效应显著重新分布局部交换景观。

Conclusion: 晶界强烈影响局部磁相互作用，但对全局磁有序影响有限。蒙特卡洛结果显示，尽管存在明显的局部扰动，实际晶界密度仅导致居里温度小幅下降，因为类体材料区域主导全局磁转变。只有在人为增加晶界体积分数时，居里温度才会显著降低。

Abstract: This work investigates how grain boundaries (GBs) modify magnetic exchange interactions in bcc iron, with particular focus on the effect of phosphorus segregation. Using density-functional theory combined with the Liechtenstein-Katsnelson-Antropov-Gubanov Green's-function approach, we calculate Heisenberg exchange parameters for three symmetric tilt GBs, $\Sigma5(310)$, $\Sigma13(510)$, and $\Sigma13(320)$, and use these parameters in Monte Carlo simulations to evaluate finite-temperature magnetic behavior. All clean GBs exhibit strong local deviations from bulk exchange interactions, including antiferromagnetic coupling across the boundary plane. These negative exchange interactions are not governed by interatomic distance alone, but arise primarily from the altered local coordination and symmetry breaking at the GB. Phosphorus segregation, modeled in both substitutional and interstitial configurations at the $\Sigma5(310)$ GB, suppresses the antiferromagnetic couplings and significantly redistributes the local exchange landscape through chemical and electronic effects. Monte Carlo results show that, despite pronounced local perturbations, realistic GB densities cause only a small reduction in the Curie temperature because bulk-like regions dominate the global magnetic transition. A substantial decrease in Curie temperature appears only when the GB volume fraction is artificially increased. The results demonstrate that GBs strongly influence local magnetic interactions while having a limited effect on global magnetic ordering, and they establish a general framework for linking atomistic interfacial structure and chemistry to mesoscale magnetic behavior in Fe-based materials.

### [119] [Holonomy-based Diagnostic of Strain Compatibility in Birefringence Imaging of Stress-induced Ferroelectric SrTiO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10521)

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于完整性的几何诊断方法，用于分析双折射导出的指向矢场，并将其应用于应力诱导的铁电SrTiO₃。该方法通过计算实空间闭合路径上累积的残余旋转来定义完整性角ω，揭示了局部梯度无法捕捉的全局旋转兼容性信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统局部梯度度量仅能量化局部取向变化，但无法探测闭合路径上的全局旋转兼容性。需要开发一种基于完整性（holonomy）的几何诊断工具，以分析双折射导出的指向矢场中的应变兼容性问题。

Method: 将指向矢（director）视为ℝP²中的线场，通过计算实空间闭合路径上累积的残余旋转来定义完整性角ω。将此方法与传统的局部梯度度量进行比较，并分析完整性旋转轴的排列方式。

Result: 完整性角ω的分布图无法通过局部梯度的简单粗粒化再现，表明该方法对回路级别的取向不兼容性具有敏感性。完整性旋转轴的分析揭示了冷却诱导的机电响应重组，与铁电转变温度以上应变或应力相关的不均匀性以及转变温度以下的额外有序化一致。

Conclusion: 完整性作为基于回路的几何诊断工具，能够有效分析双折射导出的取向场中的应变兼容性。该方法提供了超越局部梯度度量的全局几何信息，为研究应力诱导的铁电材料中的取向场特性提供了新视角。

Abstract: We introduce a holonomy-based geometric diagnostic for birefringence-derived director fields and apply it to stress-induced ferroelectric SrTiO$_3$. Treating the director as a line field in $\mathbb{R}P^2$, we define a holonomy angle $ω$ from residual rotations accumulated along closed loops in real space and compare it with a conventional local-gradient metric. Whereas the gradient quantifies local orientational variation, $ω$ probes the global compatibility of rotations along closed paths. The resulting $ω$ map cannot be reproduced by simple coarse-graining of local gradients, indicating sensitivity to loop-level orientational incompatibility. Analysis of alignment of holonomy rotation axes reveals a cooling-induced reorganization of the electromechanical response, consistent with strain- or stress-related inhomogeneity above the ferroelectric transition and additional ordering below it. These results demonstrate holonomy as a loop-based geometric diagnostic of strain compatibility in orientational fields derived from birefringence.

Tensile strain induces a pronounced band-gap reduction in the MoSSe/silk interface, exceeding that of the isolated constituents and indicating enhanced interlayer electronic coupling. The vdW heterostructure exhibits a significant work-function shift and a substantially larger dipole moment compared to MoSSe and silk alone, revealing strong interfacial charge redistribution driven by Fermi-level alignment and asymmetric polarization. This enhanced polarization directly amplifies the triboelectric surface charge density, producing values more than double those of pristine MoSSe and several orders of magnitude higher than silk. Consequently, the open-circuit voltage and overall triboelectric output are markedly improved across all strain levels. These results demonstrate that synergistic interfacial polarization and strain engineering can effectively elevate charge separation, storage, and transfer efficiencies, establishing the MoSSe/silk vdW heterostructure as a promising material for next-generation high-efficiency TENGs.

### [123] [On stress-assisted boundary migration during recrystallization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10653)
*Yubin Zhang,Qiwei Shi,Guilin Wu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高分辨率电子背散射衍射（high-resolution electron backscatter diffraction）与基于微观结构的数字图像相关应变分析（microstructure-based digital image correlation strain analysis）相结合的方法，对原位退火（in situ annealing）过程中的局部应变和应力张量进行表征。

Result: 结果显示再结晶晶粒内存在约10⁻³量级的局部残余应变，而相邻变形基体中的残余应变值高出数倍。再结晶晶粒中的残余应力是对周围变形晶粒中发展出的应力的被动响应，后者受位错边界（dislocation boundaries）的局部几何特征和特性以及相邻晶粒约束的强烈影响。尽管存在穿过晶界的剪切应力，但在再结晶晶界迁移过程中未观察到剪切耦合运动（shear-coupled motion）的证据。

Conclusion: 主应变分量的详细分析揭示了残余应变模式与晶界迁移方向之间的明确相关性。这些发现表明，再结晶晶界迁移受到局部内应力状态各向异性的调控。

Abstract: This study investigates the boundary migration mechanisms near the sample surface of recrystallizing grains in high-purity Al subjected to cryogenic rolling. Local strain and stress tensors were characterized during \textit{in situ} annealing by combining high-resolution electron backscatter diffraction with microstructure-based digital image correlation strain analysis. The results reveal local residual strains on the order of $10^{-3}$ within the recrystallizing grain, with values several times higher in the adjacent deformed matrix. The residual stresses in recrystallizing grains are a passive response to those developed within the surrounding deformed grains; the latter being strongly influenced by the local geometry and characteristics of dislocation boundaries, as well as by constraints imposed by neighboring grains. No evidence of shear-coupled motion was observed during the recrystallization boundary migration, despite the presence of shear stress across the boundary. In contrast, detailed analysis of the principal strain components reveals a clear correlation between residual strain patterns and boundary migration directions. These findings indicate that recrystallization boundary migration is modulated by the anisotropy of the local internal stress state.

</details>


### [124] [Surface ferrimagnetic order in RuO2 film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10659)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RuO2作为交变磁性（altermagnetism）的原型材料备受关注，但其磁性本质存在激烈争议。本研究旨在澄清RuO2的磁性来源，解决相互矛盾的研究报告。

Method: 采用自旋和角分辨光电子能谱（spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）直接探测表面态的自旋极化特征。结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析体相和表面的磁性状态。

Result: 实验检测到布里渊区中心（Brillouin-zone center）具有相同自旋极化的窄表面态，这与任何交变磁性序的自旋纹理不相容。计算证实体相为非磁性，而表面磁性源于完全氧终止表面，其中Ru向O的电荷转移触发了相邻Ru亚晶格间的铁磁排列，具有+0.48 μB和-0.04 μB的反平行磁矩。

Abstract: RuO2, widely proposed as a prototypical altermagnet, remains intensely debated with regard to its magnetic nature. Here, we demonstrate that RuO2 is non-magnetic in the bulk, but possesses a spontaneous surface ferrimagnetic order. Using spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, we directly detect a narrow surface state with identical spin polarizations at opposite momenta and at the Brillouin-zone center, incompatible with the spin texture of any altermagnetic order. First-principles calculations identify the non-magnetic bulk state and reveal that the detected magnetism is confined to the fully oxygen-terminated surface, where the charge transfer from Ru to O at surface triggers a ferrimagnetic alignment between adjacent Ru sublattices with antiparallel moments of +0.48 uB and -0.04 uB. Our findings provide a unified explanation reconciling debating reports on the magnetism of RuO2, establishing surface ferrimagnetism as the origin of the observed magnetic signals, and distinguishing it unambiguously from altermagnetism.

The model inherits the broad generalization capability of a large multi-task foundation model, SevenNet-Omni, trained on diverse materials datasets across chemical, configurational, and computational spaces. By learning chemical representations from high-quality inference data generated by the teacher model within a unified computational framework, SevenNet-Nano achieves high accuracy and strong transferability despite its compact architecture. The model also accurately captures a wide range of interatomic interactions, enabling reliable simulations under both equilibrium and extreme conditions, including plasma etching of SiO$_2$. Comprehensive benchmarks on static and dynamical properties--such as Li-ion diffusion and liquid densities--demonstrate its broad applicability with minimal fine-tuning. ### [126] [A first-principles study of bcc chromium beyond the generalized gradient approximation (GGA)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10956)
*Alma Partos,Igor Di Marco,Shivalika Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论（DFT）分析体心立方（bcc）铬的磁性，发现传统泛函无法预测其自旋密度波（SDW）基态，而元广义梯度近似（meta-GGA）泛函虽然能改善描述，但仍高估局域磁矩并增强磁阻挫，导致SDW状态失稳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 体心立方（bcc）铬因其自旋密度波（spin-density wave, SDW）基态而成为研究过渡金属磁性的典型案例，但传统密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）方法如广义梯度近似（generalized-gradient approximation, GGA）和局域密度近似（local-density approximation, LDA）无法预测这一实验观测到的非公度SDW基态，这构成了长期的理论挑战。

Method: 研究采用全面的DFT分析，对bcc铬同时应用GGA和多种元广义梯度近似（meta-GGA）泛函，评估了在广泛SDW波矢范围内的总能量、结构参数和磁性性质，系统比较了不同泛函的性能。

Result: 所有meta-GGA泛函都高估了局域磁矩并增强了节点磁阻挫（magnetic frustration），导致SDW状态相对于公度反铁磁（commensurate antiferromagnetic, AF）构型失稳；其中Tao-Perdew-Staroverov-Scuseria（TPSS）泛函的结果最接近GGA，在meta-GGA泛函中对bcc铬提供了最恰当的描述。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，需要进一步开发专门针对复杂磁性系统的非局域或杂化泛函（non-local or hybrid functionals），以更准确地描述如bcc铬这类具有SDW基态的材料。

Abstract: The study of magnetism in transition metals is a cornerstone in understanding complex electronic and magnetic interactions in condensed matter systems. Among transition metal elements, body-centered cubic (bcc) chromium stands out because of its spin-density wave (SDW) ground state, posing a long-standing challenge for density functional theory (DFT). Conventional functionals, such as the generalized-gradient approximation (GGA) and the local-density approximation (LDA), fail to predict this experimentally observed incommensurate SDW as the ground state. In this study, we present a comprehensive DFT analysis of bcc Cr employing GGA and a variety of meta-GGA functionals. We evaluated total energies, structural parameters, and magnetic properties across a wide range of SDW wave vectors. Our results show that all meta-GGA functionals overestimate the local magnetic moments and enhance the nodal magnetic frustration, destabilizing the SDW state relative to the commensurate antiferromagnetic (AF) configuration. Tao-Perdew-Staroverov-Scuseria (TPSS) yields results closest to those of the GGA, thus providing the most adequate description of bcc Cr among the meta-GGA functionals. These results emphasize the need for the further development of non-local or hybrid functionals tailored for complex magnetic systems.

### [127] [opt-DDAP: Optimisable density-derived atomic point charges via automatic differentiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10984)
*Mohith H.,Sudarshan Vijay*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出opt-DDAP方法，通过将密度衍生原子点电荷（DDAP）算法重构为可微分计算图，优化高斯基参数和倒空间截断，解决了传统DDAP方法依赖固定启发式参数和数值不稳定的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统密度衍生原子点电荷（DDAP）方法虽然能准确预测长程静电行为，但在实践中受到固定启发式参数和约束求解器的限制，对于复杂或共价体系会出现数值不稳定性，需要改进以增强其鲁棒性和适用性。

Method: 将DDAP算法重构为可微分计算图，利用自动微分（automatic differentiation）优化高斯基参数和倒空间截断；采用伪逆解（pseudo-inverse solution）和电荷重整化（charge renormalisation）替代传统的拉格朗日乘子法，确保数值稳定性。

Result: 在NaCl空位超晶胞和MoS₂体系上验证了该框架，证明其能够忠实地重建绝对电荷密度和差分电荷密度；优化后的电荷可作为机器学习势和包含长程相互作用的经验原子间势的有效静电模型输入。

Conclusion: opt-DDAP方法通过可微分重构和数值稳定化改进，解决了传统DDAP方法的局限性，为准确描述长程静电的原子间势提供了更可靠、更通用的原子中心电荷计算方法。

Abstract: Interatomic potentials which accurately describe long-range electrostatics require atom-centred charges. One such method to determine these atom-centred charges from density functional theory (DFT) calculations is the density-derived atomic point (DDAP) charge method. DDAP fits atom-centred Gaussians to the ground-state DFT charge density and preserves the multipole moments that govern long-range electrostatics. While these charges accurately predict long-range behaviour, in practice, they are limited by their reliance on fixed, heuristic parameters and a constrained solver that becomes numerically unstable for complex or covalent systems. In this work, we present opt-DDAP, which solves this limitation by reformulating the algorithm as a differentiable computational graph. This reformulation allows for the optimisation of Gaussian basis parameters and the reciprocal-space cutoff using automatic differentiation. To ensure numerical robustness through this automatic differentiation process, we replace the conventional Lagrange-multiplier approach with a pseudo-inverse solution followed by charge renormalisation, maintaining stability even in the presence of ill-conditioned matrices. We validate the framework on NaCl vacancy supercells and on MoS$_2$, demonstrating faithful reconstruction of both absolute and difference charge densities. The optimised charges are intended to serve as inputs to effective electrostatic models in machine-learning and empirical interatomic potentials that incorporate long-range interactions.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅酸盐框架在极端条件下的结构响应受水合作用显著影响，但水合驱动的拓扑修饰如何调控高压结构演化尚不清楚。本研究旨在通过对比无水和水合硅酸锆框架，揭示次级结构单元（secondary building units, SBUs）尺度上的水合效应。

Method: 采用高压同步辐射X射线衍射（high-pressure synchrotron X-ray diffraction）研究Na2ZrSi2O7及其水合物Na2ZrSi2O7·H2O在30 GPa压力范围内的结构变化，并结合电子结构计算（electronic structure calculations）分析能带特性。

Result: 无水相在约15 GPa发生相变，而水合相在整个压力范围内保持稳定。无水化合物具有更高的体模量（B0 = 77.1 GPa）和更低的各向异性压缩。压缩机制不同：无水框架通过[ZrO6]八面体畸变适应压力，而水合框架通过[Si2O7]基团倾斜压缩。电子结构显示两相带隙均随压力增大，但无水相发生直接-间接带隙转变（direct-to-indirect band gap transition），水合相保持直接带隙。

Conclusion: 水合驱动的次级结构单元（SBUs）尺度拓扑修饰决定了硅酸锆框架的压力诱导结构演化、相稳定性和电子性质。水合作用通过改变框架拓扑结构，显著影响高压下的相变行为、压缩机制和能带特性。

Abstract: Silicate frameworks exhibit diverse structural responses under extreme conditions, which are strongly influenced by hydration. Here, we present a comparative high-pressure synchrotron X-ray diffraction study of Na2ZrSi2O7 and its hydrated analogue Na2ZrSi2O7.H2O up to 30 GPa, combined with electronic structure calculations. At ambient conditions, both phases share the same primary building units (PBUs: [ZrO6] and [SiO4]) but differ in secondary building units (SBUs, M2T4 vs. M2T6). Under compression, Na2ZrSi2O7 undergoes a phase transition near 15 GPa, while the hydrated phase remains stable throughout the pressure range. The anhydrous compound exhibits a higher bulk modulus (B0 = 77.1 GPa) and less anisotropic compression compared with the hydrated phase (B0 = 66.3 GPa). Distinct deformation mechanisms are observed: the anhydrous framework accommodates pressure through [ZrO6] octahedral distortion, whereas the hydrated framework compresses via [Si2O7] group tilting. Electronic structure calculations indicate band gap widening with pressure in both phases; notably, Na2ZrSi2O7 shows a direct-to-indirect band gap transition, whereas the hydrated phase retains a direct gap. These results reveal how hydration-driven topological modifications at the secondary building unit scale dictate the pressure-induced structural evolution, phase stability, and electronic properties of zirconosilicate frameworks.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究镧系元素一氧化物（从La到Lu共15种）在静水压（hydrostatic pressure）作用下晶体结构的变化规律，探索压力诱导相变（pressure-induced phase transitions）的可能性。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）进行计算，环境压力下比较广义梯度近似（general gradient approximation, GGA）和局域密度近似（local density approximation, LDA）两种方法，高压研究仅使用与实验数据更吻合的GGA方法。分析B1（NaCl型）、B2（CsCl型）和B3（ZnS型）三种立方结构。

Result: GGA方法比LDA更符合现有实验数据；所有15种化合物在环境压力下B1结构具有最低焓值，是最稳定的热力学结构；高压下所有化合物均发生向B2结构的相变；建立了压力与晶胞体积的关系及等温状态方程（isothermal equation of state），确定了体弹性模量（bulk modulus）。

Abstract: Using density functional theory, we study the influence of hydrostatic pressure on the crystal structure of lanthanide monoxides, focusing on the monoxides formed by the fifteen elements of the lanthanide series, from La to Lu. Calculations are performed using two methods for the ambient pressure B1 (NaCl type) structure, the general gradient approximation (GGA) and the local density approximation (LDA). Through a systematic comparison with existent experimental data, we find that the first method agrees better with the experiments. In addition, considering other cubic structures previously reported for lanthanide monoxides, as B2 (CsCl type) and B3 (ZnS type), we explore the possibility of the occurrence of pressure-induced phase transitions. Based on the better accuracy of GGA to describe the B1 phase at ambient conditions, we exclusively use GGA for the high pressure study. We find, for the fifteen studied compounds, that, at ambient pressure, the B1 structure is the one with the lowest enthalpy, being therefore the most thermodynamically stable structure. We also determine that, at elevated pressures, all the studied compounds undergo a structural phase transition to the B2 phase. We finally establish the relationship between pressure and volume of the unit cell, along with the associated isothermal equation of state, determining the bulk modulus.

### [134] [Surface correlation functions of dead-leave models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11236)
*Cedric J. Gommes*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 孔-表面和表面-表面相关函数是理论材料科学和小角散射理论中的重要结构特征，但目前仅有极少数模型能提供这些函数的精确解析表达式。本文旨在为死叶模型这一通用类别推导此类表达式。

Method: 采用死叶模型方法，通过顺序随机填充空间来构建两相孔/固体结构，其中孔状或固体状颗粒以重叠方式覆盖任何预先存在的结构。推导过程适用于任意颗粒形状和任意维度。

Result: 获得了死叶模型中孔-表面和表面-表面相关函数的精确解析表达式。通过单分散球形颗粒和设计为具有指数型两点相关函数的Debye随机介质死叶实现进行了验证。与数值重建的Debye随机介质相比，死叶结构具有几乎相同的表面-表面相关函数，但孔-表面相关函数明显不同。

Conclusion: 成功推导了死叶模型中表面相关函数的通用解析表达式，填补了该领域的重要空白。作为分析的副产品，还提出了布尔模型（Boolean model）中孔-表面和表面-表面相关函数的通用表达式。

Abstract: The pore-surface and surface-surface correlation functions are structural characteristics that play an important role in theoretical materials science and in small-angle scattering theory. Exact analytical expressions for the surface correlation functions are available only for very few models, and we here derive such expressions for the general class of dead-leave models. Within these models, a two-phase pore/solid structure is created by sequentially and randomly filling space with pore-like or solid-like grains that overlap any preexisting structure, in the same way as dead leaves fall on the ground. The obtained mathematical expressions are valid for any grain shape, in arbitrary dimension. The results are illustrated with monodispersed spherical grains, as well as with a dead-leave realization of a Debye random medium. In the latter case, the size distribution of the grains is designed to produce a structure having exponential two-point correlation function. Compared to Debye random media obtained by numerical reconstruction, the dead-leave structure has almost identical surface-surface correlation function, but distinctly different pore-surface correlation function. As a byproduct of our analysis, we also submit a general expression for the pore-surface and surface-surface correlation functions of the Boolean model, valid for arbitrary grains.

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种基于原子力显微镜（AFM）的高通量机械清洁方法，通过改进的AFM悬臂梁实现对二维材料及其异质结构的高效清洁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料表面性质对其性能至关重要，但传统机械清洁方法存在通量低、优化过程复杂等问题，限制了其广泛应用。需要开发高效且易于实施的清洁技术。

Method: 通过聚焦离子束在AFM悬臂梁上沉积Pt楔形结构，改进机械清洁能力。该方法简化了清洁流程，实现了对二维材料及其异质结构的高通量清洁。

Result: 改进后的悬臂梁清洁速率达到3 μ²/s，相比传统尖头探针的0.01 μ²/s有显著提升。清洁后的单层WS2在h-BN上展现出更锐利的光致发光发射，且与清洁金电极的接触质量更高。

Conclusion: 该方法为基于AFM的二维材料集成清洁提供了可行且简便的路径，有望推动其大规模应用，特别是在异质结构清洁方面表现出高效性。

Abstract: The surface of ultra-thin materials plays a crucial role in determining the properties. This is particularly important in two-dimensional (2D) materials where the surface-bulk distinction is no longer present. While mechanical cleaning of two-dimensional materials to remove interfacial and surface contaminants is used to achieve better sample quality, low throughput and the challenging optimization of cleaning procedures hinder their widespread adoption. Here, we report on atomic force microscope (AFM)-based mechanical cleaning with modified AFM cantilevers for high-throughput and easy-to-implement cleaning of 2D materials and their heterostructures. A Pt-wedge is deposited via focused ion beam on the cantilever to improve the mechanical cleaning of samples and streamline the cleaning procedures. We demonstrate that a cleaning rate of 3 μ^2/s can be achieved with our modified cantilevers, compared to the 0.01 μ^2/s effective cleaning rate in pointy-tip cleaning. As showcases, we demonstrate that monolayer WS2 on h-BN exhibits much sharper photoluminescence (PL) emission at room temperature after AFM cleaning, and WS2 monolayers exhibit a higher quality contacts to cleaned Au electrodes as compared to uncleaned electrodes. We also showed that h-BN encapsulated heterostructures can be cleaned rapidly using the improved method. Overall, our results exhibit a feasible and facile path for the large-scale application of AFM-based cleaning of integrated 2D materials.

</details>


### [142] [A unified descriptor framework for hydrogen storage capacity and equilibrium pressure in interstitial hydrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11660)
*Seong-Hoon Jang,Di Zhang,Xue Jia,Hung Ba Tran,Linda Zhang,Ryuhei Sato,Yusuke Hashimoto,Yusuke Ohashi,Toyoto Sato,Kiyoe Konno,Shin-ichi Orimo,Hao Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究建立了一个物理可解释的数据驱动框架，用于揭示间隙氢化物中描述符与性能的关系，发现了储氢容量（w）和室温平衡压力（P_eq,RT）分别由不同机制控制，并提出了基于描述符趋势的组分优化路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢作为一种有前景的能源载体，其实际应用受到缺乏同时具备高储氢容量（w）和实用室温平衡压力（P_eq,RT）的存储材料的限制。间隙金属氢化物具有快速动力学和有利的热力学特性（高P_eq,RT），但存在固有的低储氢容量问题。

Method: 研究建立了一个物理可解释的数据驱动框架，利用精心策划的压力-组成-温度测量数据库（Digital Hydrogen Platform, DigHyd）和白盒符号回归（white-box symbolic regression）来揭示间隙氢化物中的描述符-性能关系。

Result: 分析揭示了控制机制的明显分离：储氢容量（w）由几何和晶格条件控制，通过平均原子半径（⟨r_M⟩）和平均热导率（⟨κ⟩）捕获，最佳区间为r_M ∼ 1.47 Å和相对较低的⟨κ⟩；而室温平衡压力（P_eq,RT）由弹性性质控制，通过平均剪切模量（⟨G⟩）和平均泊松比（⟨ν⟩）捕获，反映了晶格刚度和机械柔顺性的作用。

Conclusion: 这些关系被转化为遵循上述描述符趋势的组分优化路径，使得能够在实用平衡条件（P_eq,RT ∼ 0.1 MPa）下设计具有增强储氢容量的候选材料。这项工作为能源材料系统的物理信息设计建立了一个通用且可解释的策略。

Abstract: Hydrogen is a promising energy carrier, yet its practical deployment is limited by the lack of storage materials that simultaneously achieve high storage capacity ($w$) and practical equilibrium pressure at room temperature ($P_{\rm eq,RT}$). Interstitial metal hydrides offer fast kinetics and favorable thermodynamics (high $P_{\rm eq,RT}$) but suffer from intrinsically low w. Here, we establish a physically interpretable, data-driven framework to uncover descriptor-property relationships in interstitial hydrides using a curated database of pressure-composition-temperature measurements (Digital Hydrogen Platform, DigHyd) and white-box symbolic regression. Strikingly, the analysis reveals a clear separation of governing mechanisms, in which $w$ is governed by geometric and lattice conditions, captured by the average atomic radius ($\left\langle r_M \right\rangle$) and average thermal conductivity ($\left\langleκ\right\rangle$), with an optimal regime of $r_M \sim 1.47 Å$ and relatively low $\left\langleκ\right\rangle$. In contrast, $P_{\rm eq,RT}$ is governed by elastic properties, captured by the average shear modulus ($\left\langle G \right\rangle$) and average Poisson's ratio ($\left\langle ν\right\rangle$), reflecting the role of lattice rigidity and mechanical compliance. These relationships are translated into compositional optimization pathways that follow the descriptor trends above, enabling the design of candidate materials with enhanced w under practical equilibrium conditions ($P_{\rm eq,RT} \sim 0.1$ MPa). This work establishes a general, interpretable strategy for physics-informed design of energy materials systems.

</details>

Conclusion: 本研究通过第一性原理计算，系统分析了硅中多种铜相关缺陷的性质，并提出了新的缺陷模型来解释理论与实验的不一致性。这些计算可能为理解硅中电活性缺陷和铜沉淀的早期状态提供重要见解。

Abstract: Copper is a detrimental impurity in silicon with high diffusivity and a high tendency to precipitate. Interaction between Cu and other defects is essential for understanding the nature of Cu precipitation in silicon. Despite extensive experimental investigations of Cu-related defects in silicon, a comprehensive understanding remains elusive due to limitations of techniques in resolving defect configurations, as well as inconsistencies between theoretical and experimental results regarding transition levels. Moreover, the underlying formation mechanism of the well-known $\mathrm{Cu_{PL}}$ line is still unclear. In this work, configurations, formation energies, and transition levels of Cu-related defects in silicon are calculated using the HSE06 functional and finite-size correction. Defects involved in this study include $\mathrm{Cu_i}$, $\mathrm{Cu_{Si}}$, Cu-B, Cu-P, and Cu-H. A $\mathrm{Cu_{i4}V}$ model is proposed to explain the discrepancies between theory and experiment about $\mathrm{Cu_{PL}}$ defect. ### [144] [Multiple spiking functionalities in annealing-optimized Ag/Hf$_{0.5}$Zr$_{0.5}$O$_2$-based memristive neurons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11780)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究为基于脉冲神经网络（spiking neural networks）原理的下一代节能神经形态硬件的创建铺平了道路，展示了多功能人工神经元的可行性和应用潜力。

In this paper, we demonstrate an artificial neuron with multiple functionalities based on filamentary switching Ag/Hf$_{0.5}$Zr$_{0.5}$O$_2$ (HZO) memristors. To improve the parameters of memristors, we propose a two-step annealing method, which allows for better control of the crystallization of the functional dielectric layer (HZO) as well as of the diffusion of active electrode (Ag) atoms. Moreover, the neuron operation does not require the additional electronic overhead and is supported solely by a Ag/HZO memristor with a current limiting resistor connected in series. ### [145] [Investigating the onset of deconfinement with NA61/SHINE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09880)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的主要动机是探索解禁闭相变（onset of deconfinement）的起始点以及强相互作用物质的性质。NA61/SHINE作为多用途固定靶实验，旨在通过系统性的扫描来理解这些基础物理现象。

Method: 采用独特的二维扫描方法：在碰撞能量（$\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}} = 5.12 - 16.8/17.3$ GeV）和系统尺寸（从p+p到Pb+Pb）两个维度上进行系统研究。分析了核-核碰撞中产生的强子谱，包括中心Xe+La碰撞中的带电强子和中心Ar+Sc碰撞中的重子。

Abstract: NA61/SHINE is a multipurpose fixed-target experiment located at the CERN SPS. One of its main goals is to study the onset of deconfinement and the properties of strongly interacting matter. For this purpose, a unique two-dimensional scan in collision energy ($\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}} = 5.12 - 16.8/17.3$~GeV) and system size (from $p$+$p$ to Pb+Pb) was performed. Results on hadron spectra produced in nucleus-nucleus collisions, including the recent data on charged hadrons produced in central Xe+La collisions and baryons in central Ar+Sc collisions, are presented. The kinematic distributions and the measured multiplicities of identified hadrons are compared with NA49 Pb+Pb results and with available world data. The obtained results, particularly the $K^+/π^+$ ratio, are crucial for understanding the phenomena of the onset of deconfinement, which is one of the main aims of the strong interaction program of the NA61/SHINE Collaboration. Additionally, a comparison of proton rapidity spectra in nucleus-nucleus collisions from NA61/SHINE and NA49 is presented, providing a complete picture of the energy and system-size dependence of the mechanism of transport of baryon number at SPS energies.

*Charbel Abi Younes,Thomas Trogdon*

Result: 主要结果为建立了有限厄米特带状矩阵逆谱问题的完整理论框架，包括重构算法和谱测度表征条件，并揭示了谱分析与块三对角化算法及Toda格演化在带状矩阵上的深层联系。

Conclusion: 结论表明矩阵正交多项式理论为带状矩阵谱分析提供了有力工具，所建立的逆问题解决方案和谱测度表征条件完善了该类矩阵的谱理论，相关联系为数值算法和动力系统研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the direct and inverse spectral theory for a class of finite Hermitian banded matrices. Using the theory of matrix orthogonal polynomials, we provide an explicit procedure for reconstructing a banded matrix from a matrix-valued measure that encodes its spectral data. We establish necessary and sufficient conditions for a measure to be the spectral measure of a matrix in the examined class. We further analyze the connections between this spectral analysis, block tridiagonalization algorithms, and the Toda lattice evolution on banded matrices.

### [147] [Optimizing Riesz means of Robin Laplace operators on cuboids in a semiclassical limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11076)
*Matthias Baur,Simon Larson*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究固定测度立方体中Robin拉普拉斯算子特征值Riesz平均的渐近形状优化问题，发现在特定参数比例下，最大化序列会从收敛于单位立方体转变为完全无收敛子序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Robin拉普拉斯算子特征值Riesz平均在固定测度立方体中的渐近形状优化问题，特别关注当Robin参数与定义Riesz平均的谱参数平方根成比例时的行为。

Method: 采用两项谱渐近分析（two-term spectral asymptotics）和Riesz平均的一致不等式作为主要工具，分析参数比例对优化器行为的影响。

Result: 发现基于两个参数精确比例会出现转变：随着谱参数趋于无穷大，最大化序列从收敛于单位立方体转变为完全缺乏收敛子序列。控制优化器行为的转变点可能与第二渐近项改变符号的点不同。

Conclusion: 仅基于固定域渐近分析的启发式方法无法准确预测最大化器的渐近行为，这揭示了形状优化问题中渐近分析与优化器行为之间的复杂关系。

Abstract: We study asymptotic shape optimization for Riesz means of Robin Laplacian eigenvalues among cuboids of fixed measure. Our focus is the regime where the Robin parameter is proportional to the square root of the spectral parameter defining the Riesz means. Here, a transition emerges based on the precise ratio between the two parameters: as the spectral parameter tends to infinity, sequences of maximizers shift from converging to the unit cube to lacking convergent subsequences entirely. Key tools include two-term spectral asymptotics and uniform inequalities for the Riesz means. Notably, the transition point governing the behavior of optimizers may differ from the point at which the second asymptotic term changes sign. This shows that heuristics based solely on asymptotics for a fixed domain fail to accurately predict the asymptotic behavior of maximizers.

### [148] [Strictly correlated electrons in a quantum ring: from Kohn-Sham to Kantorovich potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09908)

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究对称多边际最优输运（symmetric multimarginal optimal transport）问题中Seidl猜想成立的相互作用类型，并将结果应用于量子环（quantum ring）中的电子系统。同时，严格推导强相互作用系统中绝热连接势（adiabatic connection potential）的渐近行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用最优输运理论（optimal transport theory）框架，研究对称多边际最优输运问题的结构。通过分析Seidl猜想成立的相互作用类型，并将结果应用于量子环电子系统。同时，在强相互作用极限下分析Lieb密度泛函（Lieb density functional）的收敛行为。

Conclusion: 本文成功扩展了对称多边际最优输运问题中Seidl猜想的适用范围，特别是涵盖了量子环中电子的物理相关相互作用。同时，严格建立了强相互作用极限下Lieb密度泛函与最优输运泛函的收敛关系，为相关物理系统的理论研究提供了数学基础。

Abstract: Our goal in this paper is twofold. First, we characterize the class of pairwise interactions for which the Seidl conjecture on the structure of optimal plans for the symmetric multimarginal optimal transport problem with one-dimensional marginal holds. This extends previous results by Colombo, De Pascale, and Di Marino [Can. Jou. Math., 67 (2015), https://doi.org/10.4153/CJM-2014-011-x], which treated the case of translation-invariant, convex and decreasing interactions. In particular, our results apply to physically relevant interactions for electrons living on a quantum ring. The second main goal of the paper is to rigorously derive the leading order asymptotics of the adiabatic connection potential for strongly interacting systems. More precisely, we show that for electrons in a quantum ring (or one-dimensional interval), not only the Lieb density functional converges to the optimal transport (or strictly correlated) functional in the semiclassical limit, but also the representing potential converges to a regular Kantorovich potential. As an intermediate step, we also extend previous results on the strongly interacting limit of the Lieb functional to periodic systems in arbitrary dimensions.

### [149] [Dual contractions and algebraic families](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10162)
*Eyal Subag*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文引入了一种针对Inönü-Wigner收缩的对偶性，该收缩与实对称李代数相关。主要结果表明原始收缩与其对偶作为单个复李代数代数族的实纤维出现，从而将两者置于统一的几何框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为与实对称李代数相关的Inönü-Wigner收缩建立对偶性理论。动机源于将两个看似不同的收缩置于统一的几何框架中，并连接最近关于收缩、实形式和隐藏对称性研究中发展的代数族方法。

Method: 方法从对称对$(\mathfrak{g},θ)$出发，在$\mathfrak{g}$的复化中定义对偶实形式$\mathfrak{g}^{*}$，并考虑关于公共不动点子代数$\mathfrak{g}^θ$的相应收缩。核心是证明原始收缩与其对偶作为配备反全纯对合的单个复李代数代数族的实纤维出现。

Result: 主要结果表明，原始Inönü-Wigner收缩与其对偶收缩出现在同一代数族中，作为该族的实纤维。这为两个收缩提供了统一的几何框架，并将它们与收缩、实形式和隐藏对称性研究中的代数族方法相连接。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了Inönü-Wigner收缩的对偶性理论，将原始收缩与其对偶置于统一的几何框架中。这一框架通过代数族方法连接了收缩、实形式和隐藏对称性的研究，为相关数学结构提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We introduce a duality for Inönü-Wigner contractions attached to real symmetric Lie algebras. Starting from a symmetric pair $(\mathfrak{g},θ)$, we define a dual real form $\mathfrak{g}^{*}$ inside the complexification of $\mathfrak{g}$ and consider the corresponding contraction with respect to the common fixed-point subalgebra $\mathfrak{g}^θ$. The main result shows that the original contraction and its dual appear as real fibers of a single algebraic family of complex Lie algebras equipped with an anti-holomorphic involution. This places the two contractions in one geometric framework and connects them with the algebraic-family methods developed in recent work on contractions, real forms, and hidden symmetries.

</details>

Abstract: We consider a two-dimensional Bose gas in the dilute regime where $ρa^2$ is small. ### [151] [Higher (gauged) Wess--Zumino--Witten terms based on Lie crossed modules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10416)
*Danhua Song*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文从严格高阶陈-西蒙斯（higher Chern-Simons）规范理论出发，推导了高阶Wess-Zumino-Witten（WZW）项和高阶规范WZW（gauged WZW）项。基于Cartan同伦公式，获得了严格李2群的高阶CS形式和超渡形式，并证明了相关规范不变性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 结论表明，从严格高阶CS理论可以系统推导出高阶WZW和规范WZW项，并建立了相关规范不变性性质。这为高阶规范理论在物理中的应用提供了坚实的数学基础，特别是在处理边界效应和规范依赖性方面。

Abstract: We derive higher Wess--Zumino--Witten (WZW) and gauged WZW (gWZW) terms within strict higher Chern--Simons (CS) gauge theory. Starting from the Cartan homotopy formula, we obtain the $(2n+2)$-dimensional higher CS forms and transgression forms for strict Lie 2-groups presented by Lie crossed modules. Given two 2-connections related by a higher gauge transformation, higher transgression forms yield canonical higher WZW and gWZW terms. We prove that, for the symmetric invariant polynomial associated with differential crossed modules, the pure-gauge higher WZW term vanishes identically, whereas the higher gWZW term is exact. Consequently, the higher CS action is higher-gauge invariant on closed manifolds, and on manifolds with boundary all gauge dependence is encoded in boundary terms.

### [153] [No-Go Theorem for Quasiparticle BEC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10838)
*Yoshitsugu Sekine*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文从算子代数角度证明了准粒子（声子）玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（BEC）的不可能性定理，通过van Hove模型展示了两种证明路径：时间簇性质排除BEC，以及非线性色散下红外发散处理自动约化可观测量代数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在从算子代数视角探讨准粒子（声子）玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation, BEC）的不可能性定理。虽然van Hove模型的β-KMS态满足arXiv:1207.4621中的自洽条件，但该条件仅涉及场定义约束，不足以建立BEC的不可能性定理。

Method: 采用van Hove模型，通过两条路径证明BEC的不可能性定理：首先，在β-KMS态上施加时间簇性质（time cluster properties）来排除BEC；其次，在s>2的非线性色散（nonlinear dispersion）条件下，红外发散（infrared divergences）的处理自动约化物理可观测量代数，在约化代数上数学排除BEC。

Result: 证明了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚的不可能性定理：时间簇性质直接排除了BEC的存在；在非线性色散条件下，红外发散处理导致可观测量代数自动约化，从而在数学上排除了BEC。后一性质可通过解析代数（resolvent algebra）的理想理论进行解释。

Conclusion: 从算子代数视角，准粒子（声子）的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚在van Hove模型中存在严格的不可能性定理，这通过时间簇性质和红外发散导致的代数约化两种机制得以证明，为BEC的理论研究提供了严格的数学基础。

Abstract: We discuss a no-go theorem for Bose-Einstein condensation (BEC) of quasiparticles (phonons) from the viewpoint of operator algebras, using the van Hove model. The $β$-KMS states of the van Hove model satisfy the self-consistency condition of arXiv:1207.4621. However, the self-consistency condition is a constraint concerning the definition of the field, and is insufficient to establish the no-go theorem for BEC. In this paper, we prove the no-go theorem for BEC via two routes. First, imposing time cluster properties on the $β$-KMS states precludes BEC. Second, under nonlinear dispersion with $s > 2$, the treatment of infrared divergences automatically reduces the algebra of physical observables, and BEC is mathematically excluded on the reduced algebra. In particular, the latter property admits an interpretation in terms of the ideal theory of the resolvent algebra.
