### [154] [Finite-difference zeta function regularisation and spectral weighting in effective actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11460)
*Keisuke Okamura*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于有限差分构造的尺度相关谱聚合方法，替代了传统的zeta函数正则化，在有限系统中产生Tsallis型量，在无限维中实现尺度依赖的谱加权。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的zeta函数正则化（zeta function regularisation）采用尺度无关的谱聚合方案，固定了谱贡献的相对权重。本文旨在放松这一约束，引入尺度依赖的谱加权机制。

Method: 通过用基于ζ_A(0)和ζ_A(q-1)的有限差分构造（finite-difference construction）替代s=0处的导数，建立了一个q控制的谱聚合框架。该方法在有限系统和无限维系统中分别产生不同的数学结构。

Result: 在有限系统中，宏观极限下产生Tsallis型量（Tsallis-type quantities）和q控制的信息几何结构（information-geometric structure）。在无限维中，得到变分δΓ_q=Tr(A^{-q}δA)的有效作用量（effective action），实现尺度依赖的谱加权。

Conclusion: 在该框架下，zeta函数正则化、有效作用量、非广延标度（nonextensive scaling）和信息几何都作为有限差分谱聚合（finite-difference spectral aggregation）共同原理的表现形式而统一出现。

Abstract: Standard zeta function regularisation enforces a scale-independent prescription for spectral aggregation, effectively fixing the relative weight of spectral contributions. We relax this constraint by replacing the derivative at $s=0$ with a finite-difference construction based on $ζ_{A}(0)$ and $ζ_{A}(q-1)$. In finite systems, it gives rise in the macroscopic limit to Tsallis-type quantities and a $q$-controlled information-geometric structure. In infinite dimensions, it yields an effective action whose variation $δΓ_{q}=\mathrm{Tr}(A^{-q}δA)$ realises scale-dependent spectral weighting. Within this framework, zeta function regularisation, effective action, nonextensive scaling, and information geometry emerge as manifestations of a common principle of finite-difference spectral aggregation.

### [155] [Passive two-plateau relaxation from Tricomi confluent hypergeometric kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11464)
*Marc Tudela-Pi,Ivano Colombaro*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Tricomi合流超几何函数（Tricomi confluent hypergeometric function）的非分数阶被动框架，用于建模具有记忆谱的异常弛豫现象。该框架包含Debye和Cole-Cole响应作为特例，并扩展为具有独立可调低频和高频指数的非对称双平台色散律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异常弛豫（anomalous relaxation）与记忆谱（memory spectra）广泛存在于无序固体、软物质、生物组织和电化学界面中。分数阶模型虽能有效捕捉宽幂律行为，但可能掩盖谱结构，且不便于被动实现或有限维模拟。

Method: 引入基于Tricomi合流超几何函数的非分数阶被动框架，结合有界莫比乌斯归一化（bounded Moebius normalisation）强制规定低频和高频平台，同时保持宽色散过渡。对于允许参数范围，证明有界块具有非负谱密度的Stieltjes表示（Stieltjes representation）。

Result: 该框架包含Debye和Cole-Cole响应作为精确子情况，扩展为具有独立可调低频和高频指数的非对称双平台色散律。推导出被动高斯-斯蒂尔吉斯离散化（passive Gauss-Stieltjes discretisation），得到Foster型有理逼近（Foster-type rational approximations）和具有正极点和留数的一阶状态空间实现。

Conclusion: 数值实验显示有限维逼近在中等记忆和长尾机制中收敛，实现了宽记忆响应的被动降阶表示。在宽带介电数据和电池电化学阻抗谱上验证了框架有效性，多块Tricomi混合在生物组织中相比经典Cole-Cole基线提高了复域拟合精度，同时保持了可解释的模态结构。

Abstract: Anomalous relaxation with memory spectra arises in disordered solids, soft matter, biological tissues and electrochemical interfaces. Fractional-order models capture broad power-law behaviour efficiently, but they can obscure spectral structure and are not always convenient for passive realisation or finite-dimensional simulation. We introduce a non-fractional passive framework based on the Tricomi confluent hypergeometric function, combined with a bounded Moebius normalisation that enforces prescribed low-frequency and high-frequency plateaux while preserving a broad dispersive transition. The resulting family contains the Debye and Cole-Cole responses as exact subcases, while extending them to asymmetric two-plateau dispersive laws with independently tunable low- and high-frequency exponents. For an admissible parameter range, we prove that the bounded block admits a Stieltjes representation with nonnegative spectral density, implying complete monotonicity, passivity, causality and compatibility with standard circuit and state-space descriptions. Building on this structure, we derive a passive Gauss-Stieltjes discretisation leading to Foster-type rational approximations and first-order state-space realisations with positive poles and residues. Numerical experiments show convergence of these finite-dimensional approximations across moderate-memory and long-tail regimes, enabling passive reduced-order representations of broad-memory responses. The framework is then validated on broadband dielectric data and battery electrochemical impedance spectra. In tissues, multi-block Tricomi mixtures improve complex-domain fitting accuracy relative to classical Cole-Cole baselines while preserving interpretable modal structure.

Method: 方法分为两部分：首先考虑广义波算符（generalized wave operators）和散射算符（scattering operators），推导当偏差因子（deviation factors）表现为渐近形式exp{itC±}时，散射算符与未微扰算符（unperturbed operators）对易关系（commutation relations）的修正。然后针对QED中的线性发散（linear divergence）情形，构造了次级广义散射算符（secondary generalized scattering operators）。

Result: 主要结果包括：推导了偏差因子具有特定渐近行为时散射算符对易关系的修正公式，并成功构造了适用于QED线性发散情形的次级广义散射算符。这些结果为奥本海默问题在特定情况下提供了肯定答案。

Conclusion: 结论表明，通过构造次级广义散射算符，可以在量子电动力学（QED）的线性发散情形下，摆脱ε展开的限制，对散射算符进行严格处理，从而为奥本海默的著名问题提供了特定情况下的解决方案。

Abstract: First, we consider generalized wave and scattering operators and derive modifications of commutation relations (between scattering operators and unperturbed operators) when the corresponding deviation factors behave as $\exp\{i t {\mathcal C}_{\pm}\}$ for $t\to \pm \infty$. Then, we construct so called secondary generalized scattering operators for the related case of linear divergence in QED, which gives a positive answer (in that case) to the well-known problem of J. R. Oppenheimer regarding scattering operators in QED: "Can the procedure be freed of the expansion in $\varepsilon$ and carried out rigorously?"

Abstract: In this paper, we study a system of bosons trapped in a confining potential, interacting with a quantized field of coherent photons in the mean field description of non-relativistic Quantum Electrodynamics (QED) obtained by [N. Leopold and P. Pickl , 2017]. We derive the effective nonlinear cascade equations governing the emission and absorption of coherent photons by the boson subsystem in a combined weak-coupling and kinetic-scaling limit. We demonstrate that solutions to this nonlinear cascade describe a monotone decreasing energy flow in the boson subsystem. Thereby, we prove that a Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC) forms dynamically, under conservation of the total boson $L^2$ mass. ### [158] [Effective Stability of Near-Rectilinear Halo Orbits in the Earth-Moon System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02466)
*Joan Gimeno,Luke T. Peterson*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对地月系统L2点附近的近直线晕轨道（NRHOs），建立了一个量化有限时间有效稳定性的严格框架。通过离散庞加莱映射和高阶泰勒展开，构建多项式正规形式，并推导离散型Nekhoroshev估计，确定了椭圆NRHOs在CR3BP中的非线性约束几何边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地月系统L2点附近的近直线晕轨道（NRHOs）在圆形限制性三体问题（CR3BP）中展现出复杂的动力学特性，包含嵌入强不稳定区域的正则椭圆轨道带。这种稳定与不稳定动力学的共存，加上近月飞越的数值敏感性，使得NRHOs附近的长期轨迹行为成为一个精细且本质非线性的问题。理解这些椭圆轨道的有效稳定性因此成为关键挑战，位于局部正规形式理论与全局不稳定机制的交叉点。

Method: 为量化有限时间约束，作者使用离散庞加莱映射（discrete Poincaré maps）构建了有效稳定性的严格框架。通过采用喷流传输（jet transport）计算高阶泰勒展开，构建了显式多项式正规形式（polynomial normal forms）。通过识别平衡映射解析域渐近收敛与低阶小除数累积惩罚的归一化阶数，推导了离散型Nekhoroshev估计（discrete Nekhoroshev-type estimates）。

Result: 将该框架应用于地月系统，将得到的几何限制直接映射到物理空间坐标。关键发现是，对于实际任务寿命（如10-50年），所需稳定性远短于特征Nekhoroshev累积时间。因此，有效稳定区域不受时间相关指数漂移的约束，而是完全由优化正规形式的最大解析域决定。这些推导的空间包络为椭圆NRHOs的固有局部稳定性建立了明确的几何边界。

Conclusion: 研究为圆形限制性三体问题（CR3BP）中近直线晕轨道（NRHOs）的非线性约束提供了严格的数学表征。推导的空间包络建立了椭圆NRHOs固有局部稳定性的显式几何边界，为实际任务设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Near-rectilinear halo orbits (NRHOs) around Earth-Moon L2 in the Circular Restricted 3-Body Problem (CR3BP) exhibit a complex dynamical landscape, featuring a band of normally elliptic orbits embedded within regions of strong instability. This coexistence of stable and unstable dynamics, amplified by the numerical sensitivity associated with close lunar passages, makes the long-term behavior of trajectories near NRHOs a delicate and intrinsically nonlinear problem. Understanding the effective stability of these elliptic orbits is therefore a critical challenge, lying at the intersection of local normal form theory and global instability mechanisms.
  To quantify finite-time confinement, we formulate a rigorous framework for effective stability using discrete Poincaré maps. By employing jet transport to compute high-order Taylor expansions, we construct explicit polynomial normal forms. We derive discrete Nekhoroshev-type estimates by identifying the normalization order, which balances the asymptotic convergence of the map's analyticity domain against the cumulative penalty of low-order small divisors.
  Applying this framework to the Earth-Moon system, we map the resulting geometric limits directly into physical spatial coordinates. Crucially, we demonstrate that for practical mission lifetimes (e.g., 10-50 years), the required stability is vastly shorter than the characteristic Nekhoroshev accumulation time. Consequently, the effective stability region is not constrained by the time-dependent exponential drift, but is instead governed entirely by the maximum analytical domain of the optimized normal form. These derived spatial envelopes establish explicit geometric boundaries for the intrinsic local stability of elliptic NRHOs, providing a rigorous mathematical characterization of their nonlinear confinement within the CR3BP.

</details>


### [159] [Which Phases Are Thermodynamically Realizable? A Local Entropy Criterion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10225)
*C. Evans Hedges*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 该论文证明了遍历测度（ergodic measure）成为某个连续势（continuous potential）的平衡态（equilibrium state）的充要条件是熵映射（entropy map）在该测度处上半连续（upper semicontinuous）。同时修正了Jenkinson（2006）关于平衡面（equilibrium face）实现的陈述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在统计力学（statistical mechanics）的变分方法中，平衡态是热力学相（thermodynamic phases）的严格类比。因此，研究哪些不变测度（invariant measures）可以作为平衡态出现，本质上是在探究哪些相是热力学可实现的（thermodynamically realizable）。

Method: 研究局部紧致可容群（locally compact amenable groups）在紧致可度量空间（compact metrizable spaces）上的连续作用，要求系统具有有限拓扑熵（finite topological entropy）。对于具有有界熵（bounded entropy）且能嵌入到紧致可度量系统作为不变子系统（invariant subsystem）的系统，采用相同的判据。

Result: 证明了一个遍历测度是某个连续势的平衡态，当且仅当熵映射在该测度处上半连续。不可实现的相恰好隐藏在自由能（free energy）的凸包络（convex envelope）之后。通过单点紧化（one-point compactification）得到了局部紧致σ-紧致系统的C₀-势实现定理，并应用于可数状态马尔可夫移位（countable-state Markov shifts）。

Conclusion: 修正了Jenkinson（2006）关于平衡面实现的陈述，指出其遗漏了必要的连续性假设。给出了精确的修正陈述：一个弱-*闭的遍历测度集确定一个平衡面，当且仅当熵映射在该集合上连续，且在集合的每个点处上半连续。

Abstract: In the variational approach to statistical mechanics, equilibrium states are the rigorous analogues of thermodynamic phases; the question of which invariant measures can arise as equilibrium states is therefore the question of which phases are thermodynamically realizable. We prove that for continuous actions of locally compact amenable groups on compact metrizable spaces with finite topological entropy, an ergodic measure $μ$ is an equilibrium state for some continuous potential if and only if the entropy map $h$ is upper semicontinuous at $μ$; equivalently, the unrealizable phases are exactly those hidden behind the convex envelope of the free energy.
  More generally, the same criterion applies whenever $(X, T)$ has bounded entropy and embeds as an invariant subsystem of a compact metrizable system. As a canonical case, one-point compactification yields a $C_0$-potential realization theorem for locally compact $σ$-compact systems, with applications to countable-state Markov shifts. We also show that the equilibrium-face realization stated by Jenkinson (2006) omits a necessary continuity hypothesis, exhibiting a counterexample on the full shift, and give the sharp corrected statement: a weak-$*$ closed set $\mathcal{E}$ of ergodic measures determines an equilibrium face if and only if $h|_{\mathcal{E}}$ is continuous and $h$ is upper semicontinuous at each point of $\mathcal{E}$.

</details>


### [160] [Reparametrizing the relativistic Kepler equation: a bridge to Levi-Civita-type models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11500)
*Alberto Boscaggin,Walter Dambrosio*

TL;DR: 该论文建立了不同相对论开普勒问题变体之间的联系，证明固定能量的狭义相对论模型解可重新参数化为具有额外$1/r^2$项引力势的广义开普勒方程解。

Method: 通过数学变换方法，将固定能量的狭义相对论模型解重新参数化（reparameterized），转化为具有额外$1/r^2$项引力势的广义开普勒方程（generalized Kepler equation）解。

Result: 研究结果表明，两种模型的动力学类型相同，仅系数存在差异，这种动力学类型与Levi-Civita修正（Levi-Civita correction）具有相似性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了不同相对论开普勒问题变体之间的数学联系，揭示了它们通过重新参数化可相互转化的本质关系。

Abstract: We establish a link between different relativistic variants of the Kepler problem. In particular, we show that solutions of the special relativistic model with fixed energy can be reparameterized as solutions of a generalized Kepler equation with an additional $1/r^2$ term in the gravitational potential. This yields a dynamics of the same type as the Levi-Civita correction, up to different coefficients.

### [161] [Miscibility and Transport Properties in Hydrogen-Neon Mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10355)
*Armin Bergermann,Siegfried Glenzer,Arianna Glaeson,Ronald Redmer*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论结合分子动力学模拟，发现氢-氖混合物发生相分离所需的最低压力显著低于氢-氦混合物，且氖的存在能稳定氢分子并大幅降低电导率，使其成为研究富氢混合物相分离的优良实验替代体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢与较重元素的混合行为对木星和土星等巨行星内部建模至关重要。研究氢-氖混合物有助于理解富氢混合物在行星内部条件下的相分离机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）结合分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，研究氢-氖混合物在极端条件下的行为。

Result: 氢-氖混合物触发相分离所需的最低压力显著低于氢-氦混合物。氖的存在能在10000 K温度和10 Mbar压力下稳定氢分子，同时使电导率相比纯氢降低数个数量级。

Conclusion: 结合氖较大的X射线散射截面，氢-氖体系成为研究富氢混合物相分离的宝贵实验替代品，为理解行星内部条件下氢与较重元素混合物的物理机制提供了新见解。

Abstract: The mixing behavior of hydrogen with heavier elements plays a key role in modeling the interiors of giant planets such as Jupiter and Saturn. Using density functional theory combined with molecular dynamics, we investigate hydrogen-neon mixtures and find that the minimum pressure required to trigger phase separation is substantially lower than in hydrogen-helium mixtures. Our simulations further reveal that the presence of neon stabilizes hydrogen molecules even at temperatures of 10000 K and pressures of 10 Mbar, similar to trends observed in hydrogen-helium mixtures but significantly more pronounced. This stabilization is accompanied by a reduction of several orders of magnitude in the electrical conductivity compared to pure hydrogen. These results, together with the larger X-ray scattering cross section of neon, establish hydrogen-neon as a valuable experimental surrogate for probing phase separation in hydrogen-rich mixtures and provide new insight into the physical mechanisms in hydrogen and mixtures with heavier elements under planetary interior conditions

### [162] [Exact Gravastar Solution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09719)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将引力真空星划分为三个区域，每个区域由爱因斯坦场方程的精确解描述，分析所得构型的关键物理性质，并检验其理论一致性和天体物理可行性。

Result: 提出了引力真空星（gravastar）的精确解框架，该框架展示了引力坍缩的替代终态，形成了与经典黑洞不同的致密天体。

Conclusion: 本研究对引力真空星作为黑洞潜在替代方案进行了清晰系统的评估，为理解致密天体提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Astrophysical black holes arise as exact solutions of the Einstein field equations. Therefore, any alternative, such as a gravastar, must satisfy the same level of mathematical rigor and internal consistency. A physically viable gravastar model should not rely on approximations or ad hoc matching of regions, but instead provide a single, exact, and self-consistent solution of the Einstein field equations throughout the entire spacetime.
  In this work, we propose an exact solution to the Einstein field equations in the context of gravitational vacuum stars (gravastars), originally introduced by Mazur and Mottola. This framework presents an alternative end state of gravitational collapse, leading to the formation of a compact object distinct from a classical black hole.
  Our model is constructed by dividing the gravastar into three regions, each described by exact solutions of the Einstein field equations. We analyze the key physical properties of the resulting configuration and examine its theoretical consistency and astrophysical viability. This study provides a clear and systematic assessment of gravastars as potential alternatives to black holes.

### [163] [Extended Gravity Theories from a Thermodynamic Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09739)
*H. R. Fazlollahi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了Jacobson框架下的引力热力学推导，通过引入非平凡熵泛函（nontrivial entropy functional）推广Clausius关系，构建了一类修正引力理论。研究发现传统熵修正不足以解决时空奇点问题，因此提出了包含量子特性的新熵形式，该模型在早期宇宙预言了非奇性相（nonsingular phase）和类de Sitter暴胀，在晚期宇宙重现了圈量子宇宙学（loop quantum cosmology）的有效动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于扩展Jacobson框架下的引力热力学推导，通过推广Clausius关系来探索修正引力理论。特别关注如何通过熵修正（entropy deformations）来修改有效引力耦合，并解决传统熵修正无法处理时空奇点（spacetime singularities）的问题。

Method: 方法包括：1）通过非平凡熵泛函推广Clausius关系；2）将熵形变（entropy deformations）表现为有效引力耦合的修正；3）在视界自由度（horizon degrees of freedom）层面引入量子特性，提出新的熵形式；4）在修正引力框架中实现该熵形式，研究其宇宙学含义。

Result: 主要结果：1）熵形变定义了广泛的修正引力理论类别；2）传统熵修正无法解决时空奇点；3）新熵模型在早期宇宙预言了有限哈勃参数（finite Hubble parameter）的非奇性相，产生具有有限熵和温度的类de Sitter暴胀（de Sitter-like inflationary expansion）；4）在晚期宇宙，该理论在一阶近似下重现了圈量子宇宙学的有效动力学。

Conclusion: 结论表明，通过在视界自由度层面引入量子特性构建的新熵形式，能够统一描述早期宇宙的非奇性暴胀相和晚期宇宙的圈量子宇宙学动力学。该研究为从热力学角度理解量子引力效应提供了新框架。

Abstract: We extend the thermodynamic derivation of gravity in the Jacobson framework by generalizing the Clausius relation through a nontrivial entropy functional. We show that entropy deformations appear as modifications of the effective gravitational coupling, defining a broad class of modified gravity theories. However, conventional entropy corrections are insufficient to resolve spacetime singularities within this approach. We then propose a new entropy form by incorporating quantum properties at the level of horizon degrees of freedom. Implementing this entropy in the modified gravitational framework, we study its cosmological implications at both early and late times. In the early Universe, the model predicts a nonsingular phase with a finite Hubble parameter, leading to a de Sitter-like inflationary expansion with finite entropy and temperature. At late times, the theory reproduces, at leading order, the effective dynamics of loop quantum cosmology.

### [164] [Spin-($0$, $1$, $\frac{1}{2}$) Field Perturbations, Quasinormal Modes, Overtones, Greybody Factors and Strong Cosmic Censorship of Einstein-Skyrme Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09740)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对四维爱因斯坦-斯格明子（Einstein-Skyrme）反德西特（AdS）黑洞进行了多自旋微扰理论研究，计算了准正规模（QNMs）和灰体因子（greybody factors），并检验了柯西视界处的强宇宙监督假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析四维爱因斯坦-斯格明子反德西特黑洞的微扰特性，该黑洞的度规函数包含来自强子模型的两个耦合参数：π介子组合K和斯格明子耦合e。通过研究该背景下的准正规模、灰体因子以及柯西视界稳定性，可以深入理解这类黑洞的物理特性。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）推导该背景下的克莱因-戈登（Klein-Gordon）、麦克斯韦（Maxwell）和狄拉克（Dirac）有效势；2）使用六阶WKB公式计算准正规模，并与十三阶帕德改进展开（Padé-improved expansion）和不稳定光子球设定的几何光学极限（eikonal limit）进行交叉验证；3）使用时域普朗尼拟合（time-domain Prony fit）独立再现主导标量模式；4）计算三种自旋的灰体因子。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）标量和电磁通道的第一泛音（n=1）显示出温和的Konoplya-Zhidenko异常，比值|Im ω₁|/|Im ω₀|从2.42单调漂移至2.54，明显低于施瓦西黑洞的近似值3；2）主导标量模式通过普朗尼拟合独立再现，精度优于0.2%；3）三种自旋的灰体因子遵循T_EM < T_scalar < T_Dirac的排序；4）在柯西视界测试强宇宙监督时，发现克里斯托多洛参数β ≲ 4×10⁻³，比阈值1/2低两个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，爱因斯坦-斯格明子反德西特黑洞在柯西视界处强宇宙监督假设得到满足，且理论本身保护了安全裕度。准正规模分析揭示了与施瓦西黑洞不同的微扰特性，灰体因子排序反映了不同自旋场与黑洞相互作用的差异。

Abstract: We carry out a multi-spin perturbation-theory study of the four-dimensional Einstein-Skyrme (ES) anti-de Sitter (AdS) black hole (BH), whose lapse $f(r)=1-8πK-2M/r+4πKλ/r^{2}$ inherits two couplings from the hadronic model -- the pion combination $K=F_π^{2}/4$ and the Skyrme coupling $e$ -- with $Kλ=1/e^{2}$ pinned by the theory rather than being a free integration constant. After deriving the Klein-Gordon, Maxwell and Dirac effective potentials on this background, we compute the quasinormal modes (QNMs) with the sixth-order WKB formula and cross-check them against the thirteenth-order Padé-improved expansion and the eikonal limit set by the unstable photon sphere. The first overtone $(n=1)$ of the scalar and electromagnetic channels reveals a mild Konoplya-Zhidenko anomaly: the ratio $|\mathrm{Im}\,ω_{1}|/|\mathrm{Im}\,ω_{0}|$ drifts monotonically from $2.42$ to $2.54$, sitting noticeably below the Schwarzschild value near $3$. The dominant scalar mode is independently reproduced to better than $0.2\%$ by a time-domain Prony fit. Greybody factors for all three spins follow the ordering $T_{\rm EM}<T_{\rm scalar}<T_{\rm Dirac}$. Testing strong cosmic censorship at the Cauchy horizon, we find the Christodoulou parameter $β\lesssim 4\times 10^{-3}$ across the admissible $(K,e)$ window -- more than two orders of magnitude below the threshold $1/2$ -- with the margin protected by the theory itself.

### [165] [Homothetic Killing horizons in generic Vaidya spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09760)
*Ritwika Ghoshal,Nilay Kundu,Srijit Bhattacharjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了包含旋转的Vaidya类时空的共形Killing方程，发现这类时空存在唯一的共形Killing矢量类，当质量、电荷或旋转参数是超前零时的线性函数时，这些矢量是相似Killing矢量。对于Kerr-Vaidya度规，共形Killing方程解的存在要求质量和旋转参数都变为动态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一般Vaidya类时空（包括旋转时空）的共形Killing方程，旨在理解这类动态时空的对称性结构及其物理意义。通过分析共形Killing矢量的存在条件，为研究动态黑洞的几何和热力学性质提供数学基础。

Method: 采用共形Killing方程（conformal Killing equation）分析方法，研究包含旋转的Vaidya类时空。特别关注Kerr-Vaidya度规，分析其共形Killing方程解的存在条件。通过相似Killing矢量（homothetic Killing vector, HKV）将动态时空共形映射到稳态时空。

Result: 发现Vaidya类时空存在唯一的共形Killing矢量类，当质量、电荷或旋转参数是超前零时（advanced null-time）的线性函数时，这些矢量成为相似Killing矢量。对于Kerr-Vaidya度规，共形Killing方程解的存在要求质量和旋转参数都变为动态。定义了相似Killing视界（homothetic Killing horizon）的概念，并研究了其热力学性质。

Conclusion: 相似Killing矢量的存在使得动态时空能够共形映射到稳态时空，从而可以利用与Killing视界相关的标准方法。建立了球对称Vaidya时空的第一定律（或通量平衡定律）版本，并研究了带电Vaidya度规的最大解析延拓及其在粒子产生研究中的意义。

Abstract: We study the conformal Killing equation for generic Vaidya-like spacetimes, including those with rotation. We show that these spacetimes admit a unique class of conformal Killing vectors that are homothetic for mass, charge, or rotation parameters being linear functions of the advanced null-time. For the Kerr-Vaidya metric, the solution to the conformal Killing equation exists iff both mass and rotation parameters become dynamic. The presence of a homothetic Killing vector (HKV) for such a spacetime enables one to conformally map the original dynamical spacetime to a stationary spacetime, enabling access to the standard methods pertaining to a Killing horizon. The surface where an HKV becomes null is termed the homothetic Killing horizon. We discuss the thermodynamic properties of such homothetic Killing horizons and formulate a version of the first law (or flux balance law) for spherically symmetric Vaidya spacetimes. We further study the maximal analytic extension of a charged Vaidya metric and indicate its implications for studying particle creation in such backgrounds.

### [166] [Testing the Kerr hypothesis beyond the quadrupole with GW241011](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09828)
*Rimo Das,N. V. Krishnendu,M. Saleem,Chandra Kant Mishra,K. G. Arun*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究利用引力波观测数据GW241011，首次对致密双星系统中自旋诱导的四极矩和八极矩偏离克尔黑洞预测值进行了同时检验，未发现偏离证据，并首次约束了致密双星的自旋诱导八极矩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克尔黑洞的所有多极矩（multipole moments）仅由其质量和自旋唯一确定。引力波观测可以通过测量致密双星并合（compact binary coalescence）旋进阶段（inspiral phase）的自旋诱导多极矩来检验这一预测。

Method: 利用最近报告的致密双星并合事件GW241011的引力波观测数据，同时检验双星组分的自旋诱导四极矩（spin-induced quadrupole）和八极矩（octupole moments）相对于其黑洞值的偏离。

Result: 未发现偏离克尔黑洞预测的证据，并首次对致密双星的自旋诱导八极矩施加了约束。该方法与基于铃荡阶段（ringdown phase）准正规模（quasinormal mode）测量的致密双星并合遗迹克尔性质检验形成互补。

Conclusion: 引力波观测GW241011为同时检验自旋诱导四极矩和八极矩的克尔黑洞预测提供了首个约束，未发现偏离证据，拓展了通过引力波测试黑洞基本性质的方法。

Abstract: All multipole moments of a Kerr black hole are uniquely determined by its mass and spin. Gravitational wave observations can test this prediction by measuring spin-induced multipole moments imprinted on the inspiral phase of compact binary mergers. In this Letter, we show that the recently reported compact binary coalescence GW241011 enables a simultaneous test of deviations in the spin-induced quadrupole and octupole moments of the binary components from their black hole values. We find no evidence for deviations from the Kerr prediction and place the first constraints on spin-induced octupole moments of the compact binary. This approach complements tests of the Kerr nature of compact binary merger remnants based on quasinormal mode measurements in the ringdown phase.

</details>


### [167] [Birkhoff rigidity from a covariant optical seed](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09830)
*D. A. Easson*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从局部种子到Kerr-Schild度规的途径，用于证明四维球对称真空引力中的Birkhoff刚性定理。通过构造精确的零种子形式并建立局部Eddington-Finkelstein坐标，证明了球对称性强制光学种子具有特定形式，从而唯一重构出Schwarzschild度规族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为四维球对称真空引力中的Birkhoff刚性定理提供一种新的证明途径。传统证明通常依赖于全局坐标变换，而本文则探索基于局部种子构造和Kerr-Schild形式的替代方法，特别是在平稳光学框架下建立相应的唯一性陈述。

Method: 在二维轨道空间上，利用面半径（areal radius）r定义标量F:=-(∇r)²，通过约化真空方程得到F(r)=1-2M/r。证明归一化一形式dr/F和(*dr)/F是闭形式，从而构造精确的零种子形式F⁻¹(dr±*dr)。通过积分这些形式获得局部Eddington-Finkelstein坐标，使度规在平坦背景上呈现Kerr-Schild形式。

Result: 证明了在平稳光学领域中相应的唯一性陈述：球对称性强制逆光学种子（inverse optical seed）ℛ等于±r，等价于光学种子ρ等于∓1/r。由此得到的种子数据唯一地重构出Schwarzschild度规族，从而建立了Birkhoff刚性定理与平稳光学框架中球对称逆定理的对应关系。

Conclusion: Schwarzschild度规是唯一由无处消失的光学种子（nowhere-vanishing optical seed）生成的球对称平稳真空Kerr-Schild几何。这一结果将Birkhoff刚性定理与平稳光学框架中的球对称逆定理配对，为理解球对称真空解的唯一性提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We present a local seed-to--Kerr--Schild route to Birkhoff rigidity in four-dimensional spherical vacuum gravity. On the two-dimensional orbit space, the areal radius \(r\) determines a scalar \(F:=-(\nabla r)^2\), and the reduced vacuum equations imply \(F(r)=1-2M/r\). We show that the normalized one-forms \(dr/F\) and \((*dr)/F\) are closed, so that the null combinations \(F^{-1}(dr\pm *dr)\) are exact null seed forms. Integrating these yields local Eddington--Finkelstein coordinates in which the metric takes Kerr--Schild form over a flat background. We then prove the corresponding uniqueness statement in the stationary optical sector: spherical symmetry forces the inverse optical seed \(\mathcal R\) to equal \(\pm r\), equivalently the optical seed \(ρ\) to equal \(\mp 1/r\), and the resulting seed data reconstruct the Schwarzschild family. Thus, Birkhoff rigidity is paired with a spherical converse theorem in the stationary optical framework: Schwarzschild is the unique spherically symmetric stationary vacuum Kerr--Schild geometry generated by a nowhere-vanishing optical seed.

Conclusion: 结论证明了在非真空时空中Wald解可与特定旋转带电流体相容，实现了相关守恒方程的解析积分，并通过数值方法验证了理论框架的有效性。

Abstract: We consider a self-gravitating, rigidly rotating charged perfect fluid immersed in the Wald magnetosphere, constructed out of two linearly independent Killing vectors present in stationary and axially-symmetric spacetimes. We show that in non-vacuum spacetimes, Wald's solution can be compatible with the electric current associated with a rotating charged perfect fluid characterized by the vanishing electric conductivity. We prove that for rigidly rotating fluids with a constant energy density or described by the polytropic equation of state, the resulting equations expressing the conservation of the energy-momentum tensor can be integrated. Consequently, the system can be described by nearly standard Einstein-Euler equations known from the theory of general-relativistic rotating fluids, with modifications introduced in the Euler-Bernoulli equation. Numerical solutions of the Einstein-Euler equations are provided for these two cases by introducing suitable modifications in the pseudospectral code by Ansorg, Kleinwächter, and Meinel.

### [169] [Constraining geometrically perturbed strange stars with minimal decoupling from heavy millisecond pulsar observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09976)
*K. N. Singh,S. K. Maurya,A. Errehymy,A. Altaibayeva,J. Rayimbaev,J. Kurbanov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了爱因斯坦场方程的一个精确解析解，用于描述广义相对论中奇异星（strange stars）的内部结构。通过引入正弦微扰 $g(r)=\sin(Ψr^2)$ 实现平滑时空变形，该变形自然产生各向异性 $Δ=P_t-P_r>0$，为抵抗引力坍缩提供额外支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超致密脉冲星（ultra-compact pulsars）因其强引力和稳定辐射，成为测试此类模型的理想实验室。研究旨在探索微小时空变形如何影响恒星平衡状态，为奇异星结构提供更精确的理论描述。

Method: 引入正弦微扰 $g(r)=\sin(Ψr^2)$ 实现平滑时空变形，自然生成各向异性 $Δ=P_t-P_r>0$。应用以色列-达穆瓦匹配条件（Israel-Darmois matching conditions）将内部解平滑连接到史瓦西外部（Schwarzschild exterior），常数用几何参数 $β$ 和 $Ψ$ 表示。

Result: 增加 $β$ 从 0 到 0.003（固定 $Ψ$）使最大质量升至 $2.28^{+0.10}_{-0.09}~M_\odot$，半径增至 $11.57^{+0.87}_{-0.10}$ km。类似趋势出现在 $Ψ$ 增至 $\sim 0.03$ 时。所得质量-半径关系与观测到的大质量脉冲星一致，密度和压力保持正定且规则，因果性（causality）满足声速亚光速条件，稳定性由绝热指数（adiabatic index）$Γ>4/3$ 确保。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了现实的质量-半径预测，并建立了研究奇异星对微小几何微扰响应的稳健框架。即使弱几何变形也能影响恒星结构，表现为质量和半径的轻微振荡变化。

Abstract: We present an exact analytical solution to the Einstein field equations describing the internal structure of strange stars in general relativity. A smooth spacetime deformation is introduced via the sinusoidal perturbation $ g(r)=\sin(Ψr^2) $, which naturally generates anisotropy $Δ=P_t-P_r>0$. This anisotropy provides additional support against gravitational collapse. Ultra-compact pulsars, due to their strong gravity and stable emission, serve as ideal laboratories for testing such models. Applying the Israel-Darmois matching conditions, the interior solution is smoothly connected to the Schwarzschild exterior, with constants expressed in terms of the geometric parameters $β$ and $Ψ$. Varying these parameters allows a controlled study of how small spacetime distortions affect stellar equilibrium. For example, increasing $β$ from 0 to 0.003 (with fixed $Ψ$) raises the maximum mass to $2.28^{+0.10}_{-0.09}~M_\odot$ and the radius to $11.57^{+0.87}_{-0.10}$ km before instability sets in. A similar trend appears when $Ψ$ increases to $\sim 0.03$ at fixed $β$. The resulting mass-radius relations agree with observations of massive pulsars. Density and pressures remain positive and regular throughout the star. Causality is satisfied as sound speeds stay subluminal, and stability is ensured by an adiabatic index $Γ>4/3$. Small increases in $β$ and $Ψ$ produce mild oscillatory variations in mass and radius, showing that even weak geometric deformations can influence stellar structure. Overall, the model provides realistic mass--radius predictions and a robust framework to study the response of strange stars to small geometric perturbations.

### [170] [Cosmological Parameters in $f(T)$ Gravity: Theoretical and Observational Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10061)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用函数形式f(T) = αT - βu^{-n} + γu^m（其中u = (-T/6)），通过相空间分析将宇宙学方程转化为自治系统，识别临界点并检验稳定性条件。同时使用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）统计技术，结合DESI DR2 BAO、哈勃（Hubble）和Pantheon+SH0ES等观测数据集对模型参数进行约束。

Abstract: The $f(T)$ gravity is one of the extensions of teleparallel equivalent of general relativity, in which more general functions of the torsion scalar $T$ can be described. With the proposed functional form of $f(T) = αT - βu^{-n} + γu^m$, where $u = (-T/6)$, we have analyzed the cosmological parameters using dynamical system analysis and cosmological datasets. The dynamical behavior of this model is analyzed with phase-space analysis by transforming the cosmological equations into an autonomous system. Critical points are identified, and their stability conditions examined, enabling the classifications of the early and late-time evolutionary phases of the Universe. The stability conditions are further demonstrated by phase-portrait diagrams that highlight transitions between radiation, matter, and dark-energy-dominated epochs. Then we used the Markov Chain Monte Carlo statistical technique to constrain the model parameters with the recent observational dataset, such as DESI DR2 BAO, and its combination with the Hubble and Pantheon+SH0ES data. The best-fit values for the model parameters were obtained by data analysis, $m \equiv 0.91^{+0.07}_{-0.09}$ and $n \equiv 0.69^{+0.09}_{-0.08}$, and are well within the stability range obtained ($m<1\land n>-1$) through dynamical system analysis. The combined theoretical and observational analysis shows that the proposed $f(T)$ gravity model successfully reproduces the observed cosmic expansion history of the Universe.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过解析延拓膜范式（membrane-paradigm）压力到整个时空，获得一个标量函数。该函数的零点、极点、高阶发散和渐近行为分别对应不同的几何特征。

Result: 该标量函数的零点定位内外视界，极点定位内外静止极限面，高阶发散识别环奇点（ring singularity），大r衰减捕获渐近区域。该函数可作为Kerr-Newman几何中临界面的统一全局探测器。

Abstract: Black hole spacetimes contain several geometrically distinguished hypersurfaces, including event and Cauchy horizons, stationary-limit surfaces, curvature singularities, and asymptotic infinity. These structures are usually identified by different geometric or causal criteria. Here, we show that for the Kerr-Newman black hole, a single scalar function encodes all of them at once. The function arises by analytically continuing the membrane-paradigm pressure of the stretched horizon into the full spacetime. In fully factorized form, its zeros locate the outer and inner horizons, its poles locate the outer and inner stationary-limit surfaces, its higher-order divergence identifies the ring singularity, and its decay at large $r$ captures the asymptotic region. Thus, the analytically continued membrane pressure serves as a unified global detector of the critical surfaces in the Kerr-Newman geometry. We further note that the same analytic structure admits a secondary interpretation as an effective generalized multi-component van der Waals-type equation of state, whose intrinsic scales are fixed by the distinguished radii of the spacetime itself.

Abstract: We study the effective dynamics of the Schwarzschild black hole interior by introducing entropic deformations derived from generalized superstatistical entropies $S_{+}$ and $S_{-}$. The resulting modified Hamiltonians $\bar{H}_{\pm}$, formulated in Ashtekar--Barbero variables, encode quantum gravity-inspired corrections that become significant near the Planck scale. Analytical solutions show that these corrections regularize the classical singularity, replacing it with a finite anisotropic core characterized by bounded canonical variables and a minimal internal area. For $S_{-}$ ($α_{-} > 0$), curvature invariants remain finite, yielding a completely regular interior, whereas $S_{+}$ ($α_{+} < 0$) leads to a localized region of high curvature associated with a cigar-like throat. The interior and exterior geometries are thus connected through this high-curvature region, indicating that the classical singularity is replaced by an entropic transition layer. These features reproduce loop quantum gravity phenomenology without invoking polymer discretization.

Conclusion: 半经典效应主要重整化而非改变霍金辐射的几何起源，近视界几何保持其普遍的Rindler²×S²结构，微扰展开由M_P²/M²量级的参数控制，确保了对宏观黑洞的有效性。

Abstract: We construct an analytic model of static semiclassical backreaction for a Schwarzschild black hole in the Hartle--Hawking state enclosed within a finite spherical cavity. Using a minimal renormalized stress--energy tensor consistent with conservation, thermal asymptotics, and horizon regularity, we integrate the reduced semiclassical Einstein equations under Dirichlet boundary conditions at the cavity wall. This yields explicit expressions for the corrections to the mass function, redshift factor, horizon location, and surface gravity. We obtain a closed-form first-order correction to the Hawking temperature in terms of a dimensionless backreaction parameter and the cavity radius. The temperature shift decomposes into redshift renormalization, geometric horizon displacement, and a local energy-density contribution at the horizon. The perturbative expansion is controlled by a parameter of order $M_P^2/M^2$, ensuring validity for macroscopic black holes. The near-horizon geometry retains its universal Rindler$^{2}\times S^{2}$ structure, indicating that semiclassical effects renormalize rather than modify the geometric origin of Hawking radiation.

</details>

Abstract: In this article, we derive the components of the entropy covector field for a relativistic kinetic gas composed of collisionless, spinless, massive, and uncharged particles following bound orbits in a curved spacetime background. We analyze the behavior of key macroscopic observables (including the anisotropy parameter and the kinetic temperature) which are constructed from the particle density, energy density, and principal pressures. We aim to characterize and compare the morphology of the resulting configurations, thereby extending and complementing a previous work. ### [176] [Quantum Entanglement of Circular Strings as a Probe for Topologically Charged Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10379)
*Ai-chen Li,Xin-Fei Li,Xuanting Ji*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法是将圆形弦（circular string）作为量子探针嵌入球对称弯曲时空，并使用压缩态形式（squeezed-state formalism）量化其二次涨落（quadratic fluctuations）。该构造自然产生双模量子态（two mode quantum states）和相关的冯·诺依曼熵（von Neumann entropy），作为粒子-反粒子纠缠的直接度量。

Result: 结果表明，探针弦产生的纠缠在具有拓扑电荷（topological charge）的背景（包括全局单极子（global monopole）和单极子虫洞（monopole wormhole）配置）之间表现出清晰的定性区别。纠缠对时空的全局结构高度敏感，特别是对亏角（deficit angle）。

Conclusion: 这些结果说明了量子关联（quantum correlations）作为诊断工具在探测经典范围之外的几何性质方面的效用，并为时空结构与量子纠缠之间的相互作用提供了补充视角。

Abstract: Motivated by the limited understanding of entanglement entropy in non-asymptotically AdS spacetimes, we develop a framework in which a circular string is embedded as a quantum probe in a spherically symmetric curved spacetime, and its quadratic fluctuations are quantized using the squeezed-state formalism. This construction naturally yields two mode quantum states and the associated von Neumann entropy, providing a direct measure of particle antiparticle entanglement. The resulting entanglement serves as an effective probe of the underlying geometry, granting access to intrinsic features that are not readily captured by classical observables such as geodesic motion. As a concrete application, and as representative toy models of spacetimes with topological defects, including wormhole geometries, we investigate backgrounds with topological charge, focusing on global monopole and monopole wormhole configurations. We show that the entanglement generated by the probe string exhibits a clear qualitative distinction between these backgrounds and is highly sensitive to the global structure of the spacetime, in particular to the deficit angle. These results illustrate the utility of quantum correlations as diagnostic tools for probing geometric properties beyond the classical regime and offer a complementary perspective on the interplay between spacetime structure and quantum entanglement.

*Houri Ziaeepour*

TL;DR: $SU(\infty)$-QGR是一种基于量子力学基本原理的引力与宇宙学模型，其中宇宙的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）表示$SU(\infty)$对称性，其碎片化产生近似孤立的子系统（粒子）。该模型在最低量子阶的有效作用量是4D参数空间$Ξ$上的杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory），但物理过程必须独立于$Ξ$的几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用$SU(\infty)$-QGR框架，证明参数空间$Ξ$的度规变化下的作用量不变性会导致类似爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equation）的约束条件。通过计算量子信息度量（quantum information measures）研究希尔伯特空间碎片化对经典时空演化和宇宙学现象的影响。

Result: 作用量在度规变化下的不变性导出了包含所有模型组分能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensors）的约束方程，包括自旋为1的引力子（gravitons）。量子信息分析表明，与宇宙膨胀（inflation）和晚期加速膨胀相关的场可能是集体呈现宇宙内容量子态演化的序参量（order parameters）。

Abstract: $SU(\infty)$-QGR is a recently proposed fundamentally quantum approach to gravity and cosmology. In this model the Hilbert space of the Universe represents $SU(\infty)$ symmetry. Its fragmentation generates approximately isolated subsystems (particles) representing, in addition to $SU(\infty)$, finite-rank local symmetries. The common $SU(\infty)$ is associated to quantum gravity, and at lowest quantum order the effective action for all symmetries is Yang-Mills on a 4D parameter space $Ξ$. Nonetheless, physical processes and measurables must be independent $Ξ$'s geometry. In previous works we demonstrated that diffeomorphism of $Ξ$ can be neutralized by $SU(\infty)$ gauge transformation. In this work we show that invariance of action under metric change leads to a constraint resembling Einstein equation. It consists of energy-momentum tensors for all components of the model, including the spin-1 gravitons. In addition, through calculation of quantum information measures we study the effect of Hilbert space fragmentation on the evolution of emergent classical spacetime and cosmological phenomena, namely inflation and late time accelerating expansion. The results show that fields associated to these processes may be order parameters collectively presenting the evolution of quantum states of the contents of the Universe.

### [181] [Discussion on the equivalence of two relativistic point-particle Lagrangians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10876)
*Liubin Wang,Xin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文严格证明了描述引力与物质场中粒子动力学的两个拉格朗日量 $\mathcal{L}_1$ 和 $\mathcal{L}_2$ 的等价性关键取决于外部势 $V$：当 $V$ 为零或对应电磁势时等价，但对一般外部势则不成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对 Lei 等人 (2021) 声称两个拉格朗日量 $\mathcal{L}_1$ 和 $\mathcal{L}_2$ 在描述引力与物质场中粒子动力学时完全等价的观点，本文旨在严格检验这一等价性声明，特别关注外部势 $V$ 对等价性的影响。

Method: 通过哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）形式化分析，严格推导两个拉格朗日量对应的哈密顿量及其质量壳约束（mass shell constraint）满足情况。采用施瓦西度规（Schwarzschild metric）加人工力学势作为玩具模型进行数值研究，对比分析两个拉格朗日量导出的动力学行为。

Result: 两个拉格朗日量仅在 $V$ 为零或对应电磁势时等价，此时哈密顿量严格满足质量壳约束。对于一般外部势，$\mathcal{L}_1$ 导出的哈密顿量固有地强制执行质量壳约束，而 $\mathcal{L}_2$ 则不然。数值研究表明，在施瓦西度规加人工势模型中，$\mathcal{L}_1$ 导致混沌行为（非可积动力学），而 $\mathcal{L}_2$ 可解析证明产生无混沌的可积动力学。

Conclusion: $\mathcal{L}_1$ 因其理论优越性和普适性被强烈推荐用于多数场景；$\mathcal{L}_2$ 适用于涉及低能量弱引力的经典近似问题，且在黑洞附近带电（或中性）粒子动力学等强场问题中因其数学简洁性和计算效率成为首选，但需对其哈密顿量施加额外约束以满足质量壳约束。

Abstract: In 2021, Lei et al. claimed the equivalence between the two Lagrangians $\mathcal{L}_1 =-mc\sqrt{-g_{μν}{\dot{x}}^μ{\dot{x}}^ν}-V$ and $\mathcal{L}_2 = \frac{1}{2}mg_{μν} {\dot{x}}^μ{\dot{x}}^ν-V$ for describing particle dynamics in combined gravitational and matter fields. In the present work, we rigorously demonstrate that their equivalence depends critically on the external potential V. Both Lagrangians yield identical Hamiltonians that strictly satisfy the mass shell constraint, and are therefore equivalent when V vanishes or corresponds to an electromagnetic potential. However, they are generally not equivalent for generic external potentials excluding the electromagnetic ones. This discrepancy arises because L1 and L2 correspond to different Hamiltonian formulations. The Hamiltonian derived from L1 inherently enforces the mass shell constraint, whereas the Hamiltonian from L2 does not. When the Schwarzschild metric supplemented with an artificial mechanical potential is taken as a toy model, numerical investigations reveal that L1 leads to chaotic behavior, which signifies non-integrable dynamics. By contrast, L2 can be shown analytically to produce integrable dynamics free of chaos. In many scenarios, L1 is strongly recommended due to its theoretical superiority and universality. L2 is generally suitable for classical approximate problems involving low energy and weak gravity. Nevertheless, it is the preferred choice for strong field problems concerning the dynamics of charged (or neutral) particles near black holes with (or without) external electromagnetic fields, owing to its mathematical simplicity and computational efficiency. Moreover, it can still satisfy the mass shell constraint when an additional constraint is imposed on its corresponding Hamiltonian.

Result: 获得了精粹（quintessence）、精粹-幽灵混合（quintom）和幽灵（phantom）等原初暴胀场景的精确解。研究发现，当前幂律标量势导出的宇宙体积函数与标准手征多场宇宙学（chiral multifield cosmology）中指数标量势的结果一致，而标量场在整个宇宙演化过程中保持动态存在。

Conclusion: 混合耦合项在负号情况下对参数施加了关键约束，为原初暴胀的不同场景提供了重要贡献。幂律势与指数势在体积函数上的等价性揭示了不同势函数形式在宇宙演化描述中的内在联系，同时标量场的持续动态存在强调了其在宇宙演化中的根本作用。

Abstract: An anisotropic Bianchi type I cosmological model with power-law scalar-field potentials of the form $V(ψ_1,ψ_2)=V_1ψ_1^{\pmλ_1}+V_2ψ_2^{\pmλ_2}$ is studied within a generalized Sáez--Ballester--K-essence-like theory involving standard kinetic terms and a mixed coupling contribution. In order to solve the corresponding field equations, for negative sign case, the mixed term introduces an essential constraint on the associated parameter, which yields relevant contributions to quintessence, quintom, and phantom scenarios in the context of primordial inflation. Exact solutions for these regimes are obtained through an appropriate change of variables. It is shown that the volume function of the universe derived from the present power-law scalar potential coincides with that obtained from exponential scalar potentials in standard chiral multifield cosmology, while the scalar fields remain dynamically present throughout the cosmic evolution.

### [184] [Probing Active Galactic Nuclei and Measuring the Hubble constant with Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10942)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于吸积盘环境对伴星轨道演化的修正，在贝叶斯框架（Bayesian framework）下分析多种参数配置的EMRI系统区分吸积盘环境效应的能力，并在α-盘模型（α-disk model）下进行验证。

Result: 在α-盘模型下，所有注入事件都能成功识别EMRIs所处的环境；正确识别吸积盘环境并约束相关盘参数后，使用暗警报方法（dark siren method）测量哈勃常数的精度可提高达20%。

Conclusion: 该工作强调了在未来EMRI数据分析中纳入环境效应的必要性，对这些效应的适当建模不仅有助于识别嵌入吸积盘环境的EMRI系统，还能进一步提高引力波宇宙学参数推断的精度。

Abstract: Extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) carry valuable information about their surrounding astrophysical environments. Over the course of their long-term evolution, interactions between the secondary object and the accretion disk can produce observable effects on both the orbital evolution and the emitted gravitational waveform. Based on the modifications to the companion's orbital evolution induced by the accretion disk environment, we investigate the feasibility of identifying the presence of accretion disk environmental effects in EMRI systems using gravitational wave signals. Within a Bayesian framework, we analyze the capability of EMRI systems with multiple parameter configurations to distinguish accretion disk environmental effects. Our results show that, under the $α$-disk model, all injected events can successfully identify the environment in which the EMRIs reside. Furthermore, we examined the improvement in the precision of Hubble constant measurements using the dark siren method after correctly identifying the accretion disk environment and constraining the relevant disk parameters. Constraining these environmental parameters may further deepen our understanding of the host environment, thereby enabling a more reliable inference of the physical properties of the accretion disk and its associated luminosity and ultimately improving the measurement of cosmological parameters. We find that the measurement precision for a single event can improve by as much as $20\%$. This work highlights the necessity of incorporating environmental effects into future EMRI data analysis. Proper modeling of such effects not only helps identify EMRI systems embedded in accretion disk environments but also further improves the precision of gravitational wave cosmological parameter inference.

### [185] [Open-Channel Operator Closure of the Finite-Cutoff JT Gravity Disk Amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10977)
*Ye Zhou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文为Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT)引力理论提供了有限截断（finite-cutoff）圆盘振幅的完整开通道（open-channel）算子表述，将几何数据与辅助问题结构相结合，并揭示了诱导的测地线扇区具有带限特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT)引力的有限截断圆盘振幅虽已通过闭通道谱方法和有限截断小号/帽（trumpet/cap）粘合技术获知，但其完整的开通道算子表述一直不完整。本文旨在提供该已知结果的算子层面的开通道闭合。

Method: 方法包括：分离从有限截断几何导入的数据（刚性长度-动量核、圆盘-小号粘合关系及目标帽重叠），与从偶宇称辅助问题导出的结构（诺依曼真空扇区、广义本征基及分支投影谱泛函）相结合。通过边界态矩阵元复现已知振幅。

Result: 成功复现了已知的有限截断圆盘振幅，并证明诱导的有限截断测地线扇区是带限的，因此允许相同物理扇区的采样和分支加倍离散表示，而非独立的微观晶格模型。此外，所得紧支撑分支差振幅并非任何单一有下界自伴β无关哈密顿量的普通热迹。

Conclusion: 该研究完成了JT引力有限截断圆盘振幅的开通道算子表述，揭示了其带限特性和非标准热迹性质，为理解该理论在有限截断下的微观结构提供了新的算子框架。

Abstract: The finite-cutoff disk amplitude of Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity is known from closed-channel spectral methods and finite-cutoff trumpet/cap gluing, while its complete open-channel operator formulation has remained incomplete. In this paper, we provide an operator-level open-channel closure of this known result. More precisely, we separate the data imported from finite-cutoff geometry -- the rigid length --momentum kernel, the disk-trumpet gluing relation, and hence the target cap overlap -- from the structures derived within the parity-even auxiliary problem, namely the Neumann vacuum sector, the generalized eigenbasis, and the branch-projecting spectral functional. When these ingredients are combined, the known finite-cutoff disk amplitude is reproduced as a boundary-state matrix element. We further show that the induced finite-cutoff geodesic sector is bandlimited and therefore admits sampled and branch-doubled discrete representations of the same physical sector, rather than an independent microscopic lattice model. Finally, we show that the resulting compact-support branch-difference amplitude is not the ordinary thermal trace of any single lower-bounded self-adjoint $β$-independent Hamiltonian.

### [186] [Probing Yukawa Gravity with Modulated Newtonian Cancellation in the CHRONOS Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11167)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在利用扭杆引力波探测器（torsion-bar gravitational-wave detector）探测牛顿引力之外的汤川型偏离（Yukawa-type deviations），特别是在亚赫兹频段（sub-Hz band）的探测能力评估。

Method: 采用差分引力校准器（differential gravitational calibrator, GCal），通过两个旋转质量系统抵消主导的牛顿力矩（Newtonian torque），推导残余力矩的精确表达式，并将汤川信号映射为应变等效响应。

Result: 在$(α_Y,λ)$参数空间中评估灵敏度，在尺度与实验几何尺寸相当（$λ= 8\mathrm{m}$）时达到最优性能$|α_Y| = 2.4\times10^{-5}$。灵敏度受限于不完全抵消产生的残余牛顿力矩而非统计噪声，系统误差平台在$T_{\rm eq} \simeq 9.25\times10^{4}\mathrm{s}$达到。

Conclusion: 差分构型即使在较大相互作用距离下仍保持灵敏度，能够在米尺度距离上施加约束。这些结果确立了扭杆探测器作为亚赫兹频段非牛顿引力的系统误差限制探测工具。

Abstract: We investigate the sensitivity of a torsion-bar gravitational-wave detector to Yukawa-type deviations from Newtonian gravity using a differential gravitational calibrator (GCal), where two rotating mass systems cancel the leading Newtonian torque. We derive an exact expression for the residual torque and map the Yukawa signal into a strain-equivalent response in the sub-Hz band. We evaluate the sensitivity in the $(α_Y,λ)$ parameter space, finding optimal performance at scales comparable to the experimental geometry, reaching $|α_Y| = 2.4\times10^{-5}$ at $λ= 8\mathrm{m}$. The sensitivity is limited by residual Newtonian torque from imperfect cancellation rather than statistical noise, with a systematic floor reached at $T_{\rm eq} \simeq 9.25\times10^{4}\mathrm{s}$ ($\sim 26$ hours). This limit is dominated by uncertainties in the source-mass geometry. The differential configuration retains sensitivity even at large interaction ranges, enabling constraints at meter-scale distances. These results establish torsion-bar detectors as a systematics-limited probe of non-Newtonian gravity in the sub-Hz band.

Abstract: We reveal that a fundamental minimal length naturally replaces the Schwarzschild singularity with future infinity, formalizing the ``asymptotic throat'' as a geometric inevitability. This scheme avoids the topology changes, multiple horizons, and universe towers characteristic of existing regular black hole models. ### [190] [Helicity-supported stationary spacetimes: A class of finite-energy, horizonless, axisymmetric solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11456)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造了一类稳态、轴对称、无视界的时空，其曲率完全由平滑局域微分旋转Ω(r)生成，而空间几何保持严格平坦。通过线性化爱因斯坦场方程，得到了Ω(r)轴对称扰动的波动方程。

Result: 这些构型尽管具有零ADM质量，但展现出非平凡曲率、有限潮汐力以及由旋转径向剪切产生的引力磁场。扭曲的稳态Killing共动产生全局参考系拖曳效应，包括引力萨尼亚克效应，有效势允许零质量和类时粒子的稳定圆轨道。

Abstract: We construct a class of stationary, axisymmetric, horizonless spacetimes whose curvature is generated entirely by smooth, localised differential rotation $Ω(r)$, while the spatial geometry remains exactly flat. Despite vanishing ADM mass, these helicity-supported configurations exhibit non-trivial curvature, finite tidal forces, and a gravitomagnetic field arising from the radial shear of the rotation. The twisted stationary Killing congruence produces global frame-dragging, including a gravitational Sagnac effect, and the effective potential admits stable circular orbits for null and timelike particles. The tidal tensor gives oscillatory restoring forces, ensuring stability against radial perturbations. Linearising the Einstein equations yields a wave equation for axisymmetric perturbations of $Ω(r)$; the effective potential is positive and localised, the operator is self-adjoint and positive definite, and the frequency spectrum is real, implying linear stability. Perturbations propagate as shear waves analogous to Alfvén waves. These results show that differential rotation alone can sustain a regular, asymptotically flat gravitational field with rich dynamics. This class of spacetimes provides a tractable platform for exploring gravitomagnetism, tidal and wave phenomena in smooth rotating backgrounds, with direct applications to rotating astrophysical structures.

### [191] [Optical Appearance of Scalarized Kerr-Newman Black Holes with Multiple Light Rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11652)
*Yiqian Chen,Li Li,Peng Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了指数耦合爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中旋转标量化Kerr-Newman黑洞的光学外观。通过研究赤道零测地线，这些黑洞根据其光环数量和性质被分为六类。数值光线追踪显示，标量化黑洞可产生额外的内光子壳层，导致内部临界曲线和新的高阶图像，这些特征可作为未来高分辨率观测的独特识别标志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索指数耦合爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量（Einstein-Maxwell-scalar）理论中旋转标量化Kerr-Newman黑洞的光学外观特征。与标准Kerr黑洞相比，标量化黑洞可能展现出不同的观测特征，这些特征可作为未来高分辨率天文观测的识别标志。

Method: 通过分析赤道零测地线（equatorial null geodesics），将黑洞根据光环（light rings）数量和性质分为六类。结合慢旋转分析（slow-rotation analysis）和完整数值光线追踪（full numerical ray tracing），研究由几何薄且光学薄的吸积盘（accretion disk）照亮的黑洞图像。

Result: 标量化Kerr-Newman黑洞可在事件视界外发展出额外的内光子壳层（inner photon shell），产生位于通常外临界曲线内部的内部临界曲线（inner critical curve）。该内部临界曲线可能缺失、部分存在或闭合，取决于黑洞参数和观测者倾角。此外，在两个临界曲线之间的区域产生新的高阶图像，其中一些呈现新月状形态（crescent-like morphologies），与Kerr黑洞的近似圆形高阶图像不同。

Conclusion: 标量化黑洞的光学外观比Kerr黑洞更为丰富，其独特特征（如额外的内光子壳层、内部临界曲线和新月状高阶图像）可作为未来高分辨率观测的独特观测特征（distinctive observational signatures），有助于区分标量化黑洞与标准黑洞模型。

Abstract: This study investigates the optical appearance of rotating scalarized Kerr-Newman black holes in the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory with exponential coupling. By analyzing equatorial null geodesics, these black holes are classified into six types according to the number and properties of their light rings. Combining slow-rotation analysis with full numerical ray tracing, we investigate images of black holes illuminated by a geometrically and optically thin accretion disk. Unlike the Kerr case, where the image is typically governed by a single outer photon shell and a single critical curve, scalarized Kerr-Newman black holes can develop an additional inner photon shell outside the event horizon. This extra shell gives rise to an inner critical curve inside the usual outer one, which may be absent, partial, or closed depending on the black hole parameters and the observer's inclination. Moreover, it generates new higher-order images in the region between the two critical curves, some of which exhibit crescent-like morphologies distinct from the nearly circular higher-order images familiar from Kerr black holes. These features enrich the optical appearance of scalarized black holes and could serve as distinctive observational signatures in future high-resolution observations.

</details>


### [192] [Ringing of rapidly rotating black holes in effective field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11755)
*Tom van der Steen,Simon Maenaut,Stef J. B. Husken,Pedro G. S. Fernandes,Maxim D. Jockwer,Vitor Cardoso,Thomas Hertog,Tjonnie G. F. Li*

TL;DR: 本文在有效场论框架下，利用数值旋转黑洞解计算了准正规模频率的立方曲率修正，解决了快速旋转区域中微扰展开失效的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有效场论（effective field theory）方法中，广义相对论的偏离可通过高阶曲率算符系统描述，但在快速旋转区域计算黑洞准正规模（quasinormal mode）谱的修正仍具挑战性，因为自旋的微扰展开会失效。

Method: 采用最近构建的数值旋转黑洞解，计算有效场论中领头阶的准正规模频率修正；聚焦于标量微扰，评估构成主要修正的立方曲率（cubic-curvature）项；使用伪谱配置法（pseudo-spectral collocation method）求解这些背景下的微扰方程。

Result: 获得了自旋高达a=0.99M时，所有m的l≤5基本模式以及所有m的2≤l≤5模式第一泛音的频率修正，相对误差低于10⁻⁴；观察到当自旋接近近极端区域时，某些模式的修正显著增大。

Conclusion: 研究成功计算了有效场论中立方曲率项对快速旋转黑洞准正规模的修正，揭示了在近极端自旋区域修正显著增强的现象，为检验引力理论提供了重要数值工具。

Abstract: Within the effective field theory approach to gravity, deviations from general relativity can be systematically described by higher-curvature operators. However, computing the resulting corrections to black hole quasinormal mode spectra remains challenging in the rapidly rotating regime, where perturbative expansions in the spin break down. We use recently constructed numerical rotating black hole solutions to compute quasinormal mode frequency corrections at leading order in the effective field theory. Focusing on scalar perturbations, we evaluate cubic-curvature corrections, which constitute the leading modifications. We employ a pseudo-spectral collocation method to solve the resulting perturbation equations on these backgrounds, enabling accurate computation across a broad parameter range. We obtain frequency corrections for fundamental modes with $l\le5$ for all $m$, and the first overtone of $2 \le l \le 5$ modes for all $m$ for spins up to $a=0.99M$, with relative errors below $10^{-4}$. We observe that corrections to certain modes grow significantly as the spin approaches the near-extremal regime.

### [193] [A Minimal Model of Representation Collapse: Frustration, Stop-Gradient, and Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09979)
*Louie Hong Yao,Yuhao Li,Shengchao Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过构建最小嵌入模型，分析了自监督学习中表征坍缩（representation collapse）的机制及其预防方法，揭示了分类困难样本如何引发坍缩，以及停止梯度（stop-gradient）等技术如何稳定表征结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自监督表征学习（self-supervised representation learning）是现代机器学习的核心，但常遭受表征坍缩（representation collapse）的困扰，即嵌入失去判别结构导致不同输入难以区分。本文旨在理解驱动坍缩的机制以及预防坍缩的关键要素。

Method: 引入一个最小嵌入模型（minimal embedding-only model），在分类-表征设置（classification-representation setting）中分析其梯度流动力学（gradient-flow dynamics）和固定点（fixed points）。通过标签-嵌入几何的收缩直接量化坍缩，并考察添加共享投影头（shared projection head）和应用停止梯度（stop-gradient）对训练动力学的影响。

Result: 当数据完全可分时模型不会坍缩，但少量无法一致分类的受挫样本（frustrated samples）会通过额外的慢时间尺度（slow time scale）引发坍缩。停止梯度能够实现非坍缩解，并在受挫条件下稳定有限的类别分离（finite class separation）。在线性师生模型（linear teacher-student model）中的实证验证表明该理论特征超越了纯嵌入设置。

Conclusion: 最小理论模型成功捕捉了自监督学习中表征坍缩的基本机制，揭示了分类困难样本的关键作用以及停止梯度等技术的预防效果，这些特征在更复杂的模型中依然存在。

Abstract: Self-supervised representation learning is central to modern machine learning because it extracts structured latent features from unlabeled data and enables robust transfer across tasks and domains. However, it can suffer from representation collapse, a widely observed failure mode in which embeddings lose discriminative structure and distinct inputs become indistinguishable. To understand the mechanisms that drive collapse and the ingredients that prevent it, we introduce a minimal embedding-only model whose gradient-flow dynamics and fixed points can be analyzed in closed form, using a classification-representation setting as a concrete playground where collapse is directly quantified through the contraction of label-embedding geometry. We illustrate that the model does not collapse when the data are perfectly classifiable, while a small fraction of frustrated samples that cannot be classified consistently induces collapse through an additional slow time scale that follows the early performance gain. Within the same framework, we examine collapse prevention by adding a shared projection head and applying stop-gradient at the level of the training dynamics. We analyze the resulting fixed points and develop a dynamical mean-field style self-consistency description, showing that stop-gradient enables non-collapsed solutions and stabilizes finite class separation under frustration. We further verify empirically that the same qualitative dynamics and collapse-prevention effects appear in a linear teacher-student model, indicating that the minimal theory captures features that persist beyond the pure embedding setting.

</details>


### [194] [Emergent Topological Universality and Marginal Replica Symmetry Breaking in Gauge-Correlated Spin Glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10309)
*Alok Yadav*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过张量网络采样发现二维修正西岛自旋玻璃存在有限温度临界相变，突破了传统Edwards-Anderson下临界维度的限制。理论框架证明离散Z₂规范约束改变了系统的普适类，导致动态上临界维度趋于零，产生无限阶BKT相变和1步复本对称破缺不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将算法无序分布映射到二维伊辛共形场论，证明涌现的空间方差产生分数动量算符，驱动动态上临界维度趋于零。采用谱角转移矩阵重整化群架构至宏观尺度（L=1024），定量验证拓扑标度论证。

Result: 理论框架表明离散Z₂规范约束从根本上改变了系统的普适类，导致动态上临界维度趋于零，产生无限阶Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless相变和非可积的replicon发散。通过隔离连续场论与微观晶格伪影，恢复了基本晶格度量L_0≈0.94。

Conclusion: 研究明确证实了存在一种独特的、拓扑驱动的自旋玻璃相，其拓扑标度论证G((T-T_c)ln(L/L_0))得到定量验证，为理解二维自旋玻璃的异常临界行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Recent tensor-network samplings of modified Nishimori spin glasses have revealed robust finite-temperature critical transitions in two dimensions, defying the standard Edwards-Anderson lower critical dimension boundary ($d_{l}\approx2.5$). We present a theoretical framework demonstrating that the discrete $Z_{2}$ gauge constraints utilized to bypass Monte Carlo kinetic traps fundamentally alter the system's universality class. By mapping the algorithmic disorder distribution to the 2D Ising Conformal Field Theory (CFT), we prove the emergent spatial variance generates a fractional momentum operator that drives the dynamic upper critical dimension to zero ($d_{u}\rightarrow0$). This marginal topology dynamically suppresses the replica-coupling vertices, yielding an infinite-order Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT) transition and a non-integrable replicon divergence that predicts a massive instability toward 1-step Replica Symmetry Breaking (1-RSB). Leveraging a spectral Corner Transfer Matrix Renormalization Group (CTMRG) architecture up to macroscopic scales ($L=1024$), we quantitatively validate the topological scaling argument $\mathcal{G}((T-T_{c})\ln(L/L_{0}))$. By isolating the continuum field theory from microscopic lattice artifacts, we recover the fundamental lattice metric $L_{0}\approx 0.94$, unequivocally confirming the existence of a distinct, topologically driven spin-glass phase.

</details>


### [195] [Anderson localization via Peierls phase modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10731)
*Arpita Goswami,Pallabi Chatterjee,Ranjan Modak,Shaon Sahoo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在磁场作用下的双腿梯子（two-leg ladder）系统中，通过调控Peierls相位（Peierls phase）来控制电子输运性质。研究发现均匀磁场下所有本征态保持离域（delocalized），随机磁场导致完全局域化（localized），而准周期（quasiperiodic）调制则能驱动从完全离域到完全局域的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索磁场对无杂质紧束缚模型（clean tight-binding model）中电子输运性质的影响，特别是通过Peierls相位工程（Peierls phase engineering）来控制局域化-离域化转变（localization-delocalization transition）。

Method: 研究方法包括：在Landau规范（Landau gauge）下为沿梯子腿（leg）的跳跃振幅引入Peierls相位；分析均匀Peierls相位、随机Peierls相位和准周期Peierls相位三种情况；构建类似广义Aubry-André型势（generalized Aubry-André type potential）的双参数准周期系统的相图；并进行半经典分析（semiclassical analysis）。

Result: 研究结果显示：均匀Peierls相位（对应均匀磁场）下所有本征态保持离域；随机Peierls相位（对应随机磁场）导致完全局域化；准周期Peierls相位调制能驱动从完全离域到完全局域的相变；相图（phase diagram）显示离域相、局域相以及中间混合相（mixed phase）区域；半经典分析定性地重现了类似的相图。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了通过Peierls相位工程控制输运性质的机制，为调控量子系统中的局域化转变提供了新途径，特别是在准周期调制下能够实现从完全离域到完全局域的可控相变。

Abstract: We investigate a two leg ladder system subjected to an external magnetic field. In the absence of a magnetic field, the system is described by a clean tight binding model, with no disorder in either the onsite potential or the hopping amplitudes. The effect of magnetic field in this system is studied by introducing the Peierls phases in the hopping amplitudes along a leg (appropriate when the Landau gauge is chosen). For a uniform magnetic field, characterized by a constant Peierls phase, we find that all eigenstates remain delocalized. In contrast, random Peierls phases, representing a random magnetic field, lead to complete localization of the eigenstates. We further show that a quasiperiodic modulation of the Peierls phase can drive a transition from a fully delocalized to a fully localized phase upon tuning the quasiperiodicity. For a two parameter quasiperiodic Peierls phase, varying analogously to a generalized Aubry Andre type potential, we construct the phase diagram of the system. The phase diagram exhibits regions of delocalized and localized phases, separated by intermediate regimes of mixed phase. We also perform a semiclassical analysis that qualitatively yields a similar phase diagram, capturing the localization transition. Our results demonstrate a mechanism for controlling transport properties via the Peierls phase engineering.

### [196] [Nexus-CAT: A Computational Framework to Define Long-Range Structural Descriptors in Glassy Materials from Percolation Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11476)
*Julien Perradin,Simona Ispas,Anwar Hasmy,Bernard Hehlen*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: Nexus-CAT是一个用于原子模拟轨迹中团簇检测和渗流分析的开源Python工具包，通过多种聚类策略分析非晶材料中的长程连通性变化，并应用于玻璃、冰和硅等材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统结构分析工具如对分布函数（pair distribution function）或结构因子（structure factor）无法捕捉玻璃态材料中非晶-非晶转变所涉及的长程连通性变化，因此需要开发专门工具来填补这一空白。

Method: 该工具包读取扩展XYZ轨迹文件，通过带路径压缩（path-compression）的并查集算法（Union-Find algorithm）识别团簇。采用策略工厂设计模式（Strategy Factory design pattern）实现了四种聚类策略：基于距离、基于键合、配位数过滤和共享邻居方法，以处理不同的网络拓扑结构。

Result: 程序基于严格的周期向量算法（period vector algorithm）计算关键渗流性质。验证了理论预测，并应用于不同键合环境的玻璃材料：二氧化硅玻璃、冰玻璃和非晶硅。一个重要发现是在非晶硅中观察到结晶前的渗流转变，表明压力诱导结晶最初由具有相似配位数的非晶转变驱动。

Conclusion: Nexus-CAT成功填补了非晶材料长程连通性分析的工具空白，其设计便于扩展到凝胶、水泥和其他无序材料。该工具包已在GitHub和PyPI上完全开源可用。

Abstract: Nexus-CAT (Cluster Analysis Toolkit) is an open-source Python package for cluster detection and percolation analysis of atomistic simulation trajectories. Standard structural tools, such as the pair distribution function or structure factor, fail to capture the long-range connectivity changes underlying amorphous-amorphous transitions in glassy materials. Nexus-CAT addresses this gap by reading extended XYZ trajectory files and identifying clusters via a Union-Find algorithm with path-compression. Four clustering strategies, i.e., distance-based, bonding, coordination-filtered, and shared-neighbor, are implemented through a Strategy Factory design pattern, enabling the treatment of diverse network topologies. The program computes key percolation properties with percolation detection based on a rigorous period vector algorithm. The package is validated against theoretical predictions and applied to glasses with different bonding environments, namely vitreous silica, vitreous ice, and amorphous silicon. One original result is the observation of a percolation transition prior to crystallization in the latter, indicating that pressure-induced crystallization is initially driven by an amorphous transformation with similar coordination number. The code is also designed to be readily extended to gels, cements, and other disordered materials. Nexus-CAT is fully available on GitHub and PyPI.

### [197] [Structure and rheology of multi-chain amphiphilic block copolymers under shear in dilute solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09684)

TL;DR: 本研究通过布朗动力学模拟，系统研究了多链两亲性嵌段共聚物在不同链长、结构、组成和剪切速率下的自组装与流变行为。研究发现三嵌段共聚物能形成更广泛的3D网络结构，具有更高的溶液粘度和更好的结构完整性，为聚合物基药物载体的理性设计提供了基础见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过计算模拟探究多链两亲性嵌段共聚物的自组装和流变行为，重点关注链长、结构、组成和剪切速率的影响。该研究为聚合物基药物载体的理性设计提供基础见解，通过结构选择和流动条件优化其性能。

Method: 采用布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics, BD）模拟方法，系统研究珠簧模型（bead-spring model）的多链二嵌段和三嵌段共聚物。模拟参数包括链长12-48个珠子、疏水分数（hydrophobic fraction, f）范围0-1.0、剪切速率范围0-0.1 1/ns。

Conclusion: 三嵌段共聚物体系表现出更优越的网络形成能力和流变特性，其终端弛豫时间随疏水分数增加而增加，而二嵌段保持稳定值。这些发现为通过结构选择和流动条件优化聚合物基药物载体设计提供了重要指导。

Abstract: This study presents a computational investigation of self-assembly and rheological behaviour of multichain amphiphilic block copolymers under varying chain length, architecture, composition, and shear rate. Using Brownian dynamics (BD) simulations, we systematically examined bead-spring model multi-chain diblock and triblock copolymers with chain lengths of 12-48 beads, hydrophobic fractions (f) ranging from 0 to 1.0, and shear rates spanning 0-0.1 1/ns. In the dilute regime, results demonstrate that triblock copolymers form extensive 3D networks with bridging architectures through hydrophobic end blocks, achieving solution viscosities up to half an order of magnitude higher than diblock systems, with superior structural integrity under weak shear. At shear rate=0.003-0.01 1/ns, both chain architectures show increased gyration radius of individual chains within each micelle and decreased cluster counts, indicating aggregation of clusters prior to breakdown at higher shear rates. Shape anisotropy analysis reveals that triblocks develop highly elongated prolate structures (L1/L3 = 11) at high shear rates, while diblocks form more discrete micellar assemblies (L1/L3 = 7.5). Chain length analysis shows systematic increases in radius of gyration, with triblocks exhibiting an increase in cluster count, indicative of network percolation. Rheologically, triblock systems maintain lower crossover frequencies with increasing hydrophobic fraction, reflecting slower network relaxation versus diblocks. The terminal relaxation time of triblock copolymer systems increases with hydrophobic fraction due to double-ended hydrophobic bridging, while diblocks maintain stable values. These findings provide fundamental insights for the rational design of polymer-based drug carriers through architectural selection and flow conditions.

### [198] [i-Rheo-Tempo: A Model-Free, Quadrature-Free Reconstruction of the Shear Relaxation Modulus from Complex Viscosity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09708)
*Jorge Ramírez,Manlio Tassieri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: i-Rheo-Tempo方法通过复粘度（complex viscosity）的二阶导数精确表示，实现了从动态测量数据直接重构剪切松弛模量（shear relaxation modulus），避免了数值积分、参数拟合和预定义松弛谱（relaxation spectra）的需要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在流变学（rheology）中，由于有限带宽、离散采样和实验噪声，频率域与时间域材料函数之间的可靠转换一直是线性粘弹性（linear viscoelasticity）的核心挑战。

Method: 该方法基于复粘度的精确二阶导数表示，当频谱近似为分段线性时，反演简化为仅基于局部频谱特性的紧凑区间-斜率公式，从而避免了数值积分、参数拟合和预定义松弛谱。

Result: 该方法在包括合成模型、聚合物熔体、工业弹性体、梳状聚合物和跨越近九个数量级频率的宽频微流变数据集在内的复杂流体上得到验证，重构的松弛模量与独立的时间域测量结果定量一致。

Conclusion: i-Rheo-Tempo为频率到时间的反问题提供了稳健、无模型的解决方案，并更广泛地建立了从实验测量的复频谱恢复时间域响应的框架。

Abstract: Reliable transformation between frequency- and time-domain material functions remains a central challenge in linear viscoelasticity due to finite bandwidth, discrete sampling, and experimental noise. We introduce \emph{i\text{-}Rheo-Tempo}, a quadrature-free method that reconstructs the shear relaxation modulus directly from dynamic measurements through an exact second-derivative representation of the complex viscosity. When the spectrum is approximated as piecewise linear, the inversion reduces to a compact interval-slope formulation based solely on local spectral properties, avoiding numerical quadrature, parametric fitting, and predefined relaxation spectra. The method is validated against a set of complex fluids including synthetic models, polymer melts, industrial elastomers, comb polymers, and broadband microrheology datasets spanning nearly nine decades in frequency. In all cases, the reconstructed relaxation modulus is in quantitative agreement with independent time-domain measurements. These results demonstrate that \emph{i\text{-}Rheo-Tempo} provides a robust, model-free solution to the frequency-to-time inverse problem and, more generally, establishes a framework for recovering time-domain responses from experimentally measured complex spectra.

</details>


### [199] [Turning Porous Functional Materials into Directional Transport Platforms with Unidirectional Surface Acoustic Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09755)
*Sujith Jayakumar,Jinan Parathi,Gideon Onuh,Feng Guo,Ofer Manor,James Friend*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: FEUDTs（浮动电极单向换能器）通过产生单向表面声波，将多孔材料转化为主动泵送平台，在亚瓦特输入功率下实现高达0.6 mm/s的定向流动，比单纯扩散快约600倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多孔介质在化学和诊断系统中支撑吸收、过滤、分离和高面积界面传输，但通过其的持续定向流动仍然困难，因为曲折的孔隙网络和强声学损失导致旁路、弱流和逆流。

Method: 使用浮动电极单向换能器（FEUDTs）产生主要单向的表面声波（SAWs），通过改变孔隙尺寸、渗透率、样品厚度和流体粘度，研究表面声波波长与特征孔隙尺寸可比时的传输增强效应。

Result: 当表面声波波长与特征孔隙尺寸相当时，传输显著增强；FEUDTs在亚瓦特输入功率下驱动高达0.6 mm/s的定向流速，比单纯扩散快约600倍；在预湿多孔介质中，泵送速度超过匹配条件下的毛细管驱动流动。

Conclusion: 简化的理论框架捕捉了主要实验趋势，并确定换能器架构、孔隙几何形状和驱动强度为控制多孔功能材料中长程可调传输的关键参数。

Abstract: Porous media underpin absorption, filtration, separation, and high-area interfacial transport in chemical and diagnostic systems, yet sustained directional flow through them remains difficult because tortuous pore networks and strong acoustic losses promote bypassing, weak flow, and counterflow. Here, we show that floating-electrode unidirectional transducers (FEUDTs) convert porous materials into actively pumped transport platforms by generating predominantly unidirectional surface acoustic waves (SAWs) that couple more effectively than conventional interdigital transducers across wet multilayer interfaces. By varying pore size, permeability, sample thickness, and fluid viscosity, we find that transport is strongly enhanced when the SAW wavelength is comparable to the characteristic pore dimension, providing a practical design rule for acoustically activated porous media. Under these conditions, FEUDTs drive directional flow velocities up to 0.6 mm s$^{-1}$ at sub-watt input power, about 600 times faster than diffusion alone. FEUDTs also sustain pumping in prewetted porous media, where capillary contributions are removed, yielding velocities that exceed capillary-driven flow under matched conditions while remaining far above thermally induced transport. A reduced theoretical framework captures the main experimental trends and identifies transducer architecture, pore geometry, and actuation strength as the key parameters governing long-range, tunable transport in porous functional materials.

### [200] [Spectral Signatures of Active Fluctuations in Semiflexible Polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10168)
*Love Grover,Anil Kumar Dasanna,Abhishek Chaudhuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了活性浴（active bath）如何影响半柔性聚合物（semiflexible polymer）的内部涨落谱。通过从显式活性布朗粒子浴的统计出发，推导出具有时间持续性和空间相关性的有效噪声描述，并发现活性主要通过重组聚合物涨落谱而非均匀增强的方式发挥作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解活性浴如何被转导（transduce）为半柔性聚合物的内部涨落谱，探索聚合物作为活性物质多尺度探针的能力，通过其模式谱解析非平衡驱动（nonequilibrium forcing）的时空结构。

Method: 从显式活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles）浴施加的活性力统计出发，推导出具有时间持续性和空间相关性的有效噪声描述。通过显式浴模型和隐式噪声（implicit-noise）模型的模拟进行验证，并与理论预测进行比较。

Result: 活性通过重组聚合物涨落谱而非均匀增强的方式发挥作用：增加活性力主要增强最低模式，而增加持续性（persistence）则将谱权重向更长波长转移。理论很好地捕捉了这种模式级重组，并在广泛参数范围内解释了显式和隐式活性浴之间的强定性对应关系。

Conclusion: 半柔性聚合物可作为活性物质的多尺度探针，通过其模式谱解析非平衡驱动的时空结构。然而，如回转半径（radius of gyration）等全局尺寸测量被系统性低估，这归因于活性诱导的键拉伸和轮廓长度重整化（contour-length renormalization），这些在当前固定轮廓理论中未予考虑。

Abstract: We study how an active bath is transduced into the internal fluctuation spectrum of a semiflexible polymer. Starting from the statistics of active forces exerted by an explicit bath of active Brownian particles, we derive an effective description in terms of temporally persistent and spatially correlated noise, and test it against simulations of both explicit-bath and implicit-noise models. We find that activity reorganizes polymer fluctuations spectrally rather than uniformly: increasing the active force predominantly enhances the lowest modes, while increasing persistence shifts the spectral weight toward progressively longer wavelengths. The theory captures this mode-level reorganization well and explains the strong qualitative correspondence between explicit and implicit active baths over a broad parameter range. In contrast, global size measures such as the radius of gyration are systematically underestimated, which we trace to activity-induced bond stretching and contour-length renormalization absent from the present fixed-contour theory. Our results show that a semiflexible polymer acts as a multiscale probe of active matter, resolving the temporal and spatial structure of nonequilibrium forcing through its mode spectrum.

### [201] [Concentration regimes in salt-free aqueous xanthan solutions under shear](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10211)
*Ammar El Menayyir,Markus Neuner,Polina Fuks,Vahid A. Z. Alashloo,Halim Altuntas,Zehau Luo,Melike Özgül,Claudia Seeberger,Sharadwata Pan,Andreas Wierschem*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析黄原胶（xanthan）溶液在不同剪切速率下的比粘度（specific viscosity）与浓度的标度关系（scaling laws），识别出六个不同的浓度区域（concentration regimes），并发现这些区域从零剪切粘度（zero-shear viscosity）平台平滑延伸到有限剪切速率区域。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过测量无盐黄原胶水溶液在整个剪切速率范围内的比粘度与浓度的关系，分析其幂律依赖（power-law dependencies），并基于标度定律（scaling laws）和当前对剪切速率依赖的相互作用机制的理解来解读数据。

Conclusion: 浓度区域从零剪切区域平滑延伸到有限剪切速率区域，表明临界浓度等指标在非热力学平衡条件下仍然有效。考虑剪切下的标度定律有助于识别剪切诱导解缠结（shear-induced disentanglement）或解聚（disaggregation）的阈值。

Abstract: Concentration regimes in polymer and polyelectrolyte solutions can be identified by scaling laws for the relation between specific zero-shear viscosity and concentration. Recently, we have shown that the same is true for the infinite-shear viscosity plateau. The shear-thinning range is usually accessed by focusing on the viscosity functions for the respective concentration regime. For salt-free aqueous xanthan solutions, we find power-law dependencies of the specific viscosity on concentration throughout the entire shear-rate range. We distinguish six different concentration regimes. Apart from those already known for the zero-shear viscosity of polyelectrolyte solutions, i.e. dilute, semidilute unentangled, semidilute entangled and neutral semidilute entangled, we identify a linear regime for low shear rates at high concentrations, where the solution gels and a regime at both, higher concentrations and higher shear rates. Within some regimes, the power-law exponents change smoothly with shear rate, particularly, when deviating from the zero-shear viscosity plateau before the power-law of the viscosity function. Some regimes merge as their power-law exponents approach each other. The fact that the regimes extend smoothly from the zero-shear regime into finite shear rates, i.e. away from thermodynamic equilibrium, shows that indicators such as critical concentrations remain valid at finite shear rates. This motivates us to interpret the data in the light of existing scaling laws and current knowledge about shear-rate dependent interaction mechanisms in polyelectrolyte solutions, particularly in xanthan solutions. It allows to follow the shift of relevant interaction mechanisms with shear rate. We think that the consideration of scaling laws under shear can be particularly helpful for identifying, for instance, thresholds for shear-induced disentanglement or disaggregation.

### [202] [On the selection of Saffman-Taylor fingers in a tapered Hele-Shaw cell](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10407)
*Dipa Ghosh,Satyajit Pramanik*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
