Method: 采用奇异摄动分析（singular perturbation analysis）和WKB近似方法，针对具有恒定深度梯度的直线几何结构，推导小深度梯度锥形Hele-Shaw槽的指选择机制表达式。

Result: 建立了无量纲指宽度Λ与修正毛细参数Cam之间的标度关系：Λ-1/2 ∼ f(α)Cam^{2/3}，其中f(α)是间隙梯度α的线性函数，当α=0时恢复平行Hele-Shaw槽结果。

Conclusion: Hele-Shaw槽间隙梯度在确定指宽度Λ中起关键作用，可通过梯度符号控制指状不稳定性，使单指稳态稳定或失稳，理论估计与实验数据和线性稳定性分析预测高度一致。

Abstract: We present an analytical study for predicting the finger width of the Saffman-Taylor finger in a tapered Hele-Shaw cell. We consider a rectilinear geometry with a constant depth gradient and apply analytical techniques of singular perturbation analysis and WKB approximation to derive an expression for the finger selection mechanism for such tapered Hele-Shaw cells with small depth gradients. We establish \[ Λ- \frac{1}{2} \sim f(α) Ca_m^{2/3} \quad \mbox{as} \quad Ca_m \rightarrow 0, \;\;\; \mbox{and} \;\;\; \lvert α\rvert \ll 1.\] Here, $Λ$ is the dimensionless finger width, $Ca_m$ denotes the modified Capillary parameter, and $f(α)$ is a linear function of the gap gradient $α$, such that $f(α= 0) = 1$ recovering the results of parallel Hele-Shaw cell (Hong and Langer \cite{hong1986analytic}, Combescot \emph{et al.} \cite{Combescot1986}, Shraiman \cite{shraiman1986velocity}). Our findings indicate that the Hele-Shaw cell gap gradient plays a crucial role in determining $Λ$, allowing for control over fingering instabilities such that the single-finger steady state can be stabilised or destabilised depending on the sign of the gradient, compared to the standard Hele-Shaw cell. The theoretical estimates reveal excellent agreement with experimental finger-width data and predictions from linear stability analyses.

### [203] [Dynamical Facilitation in Active Glass Formers: Role of Morphology and Persistence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10468)
*Dipanwita Ghoshal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过大规模模拟二维非热Ornstein-Uhlenbeck粒子模型，揭示了活性玻璃中动力学促进（dynamical facilitation）的机制。研究发现活性驱动会重塑协同重排区域（CRRs）的形态，但保持其大规模输运特性，支持了活性玻璃形成体系的广义促进框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非平衡玻璃形成系统中由活性力驱动的动力学促进（dynamical facilitation）机制仍是一个开放挑战。特别是在活性玻璃（active glasses）中，持续的自我推进打破了细致平衡并引入了方向记忆，促进机制是否仍然存在尚不清楚。

Method: 采用大规模模拟二维非热Ornstein-Uhlenbeck粒子模型，研究持续活性驱动如何改变协同弛豫。通过分析协同重排区域（cooperatively rearranging regions, CRRs）的形态和迁移率激发的空间输运，进行空间分辨的核-壳分解。

Result: 核-壳分解显示核与壳对活性有不同的响应：核经历全局形态变化但保持内部可塑性，而壳作为刚性支架主要支持轴向变形并促进输运。动力学可观测量（包括模态位移、壳占据概率和促进长度）对持续时间的依赖呈现显著的非单调性，反映了持续性与有效噪声之间的竞争。尽管形态发生显著变化，但促进长度在按持续长度$l_p=\sqrt{T_{\mathrm{eff}}τ_p}$重新标度后显示出近似标度坍塌，符合类扩散的时间-长度耦合关系$ξ_{\mathrm{fac}} \sim τ_α^{1/2}$。

Conclusion: 活性重塑了促进路径但不改变其大规模输运特性，研究结果支持了活性玻璃形成体系的广义促进框架（generalized facilitation framework）。

Abstract: Understanding dynamical facilitation in nonequilibrium glass-forming systems driven by active forces remains an open challenge. In particular, it is unclear whether facilitation survives in active glasses, where persistent self-propulsion breaks detailed balance and introduces directional memory. Here, we use large-scale simulations of a two-dimensional athermal Ornstein-Uhlenbeck particle model to investigate how persistent active forcing modifies cooperative relaxation. We analyze the morphology of cooperatively rearranging regions (CRRs) and the spatial transport of mobility excitations. A spatially resolved core-shell decomposition reveals distinct responses of the core and shell to activity: the core undergoes global morphological changes while retaining internal plasticity, whereas the shell acts as a rigid scaffold that supports primarily axial deformation and facilitates transport. Dynamical observables, including modal displacement, shell occupation probability, and facilitation length, exhibit a pronounced non-monotonic dependence on persistence time. This behavior reflects the competition between persistence and effective noise, leading to either coherent or trapping-dominated dynamics at large persistence, depending on temperature. Despite significant morphological changes, the facilitation length shows an approximate scaling collapse when rescaled by the persistence length, $l_p=\sqrt{T_{\mathrm{eff}}τ_p}$. This is consistent with a diffusive-like time-length coupling, $ξ_{\mathrm{fac}} \sim τ_α^{1/2}$, indicating that activity reshapes facilitation pathways without altering their large-scale transport character. Our results support a generalized facilitation framework for active glass formers.

Abstract: Colloid models have frequently been used to successfully describe the influence of protein-protein interactions on antibody solution properties, but they suffer from inherent problems due to the anisotropic shape of the particles. The net charge required to describe electrostatic interactions is an effective quantity that cannot directly be obtained from the known molecular structure of an antibody, and the solution structure caused by excluded volume interactions is strongly overestimated at high concentrations due to the assumption of hard sphere interactions. As a result, these models have descriptive rather than predictive power. Here we present an improved, soft penetrable sphere model based on analogies to soft colloids and star polyelectrolytes that take into account the Y-shaped antibody form and the corresponding charge and ion distribution. The model not only correctly describes the concentration and ionic strength dependence of thermodynamic and collective dynamics quantities such as the osmotic compressibility and the apparent hydrodynamic radius, but also reproduces the center-of-mass static structure factor obtained in computer simulations using a weakly coarse-grained model, in which the antibody is described at an amino acid level. These dynamic quantities followed a scaling relation with drop height, while the scaling coefficient decreased with the concave radius, indicating that the surface geometry directly governs the extent of energy dissipation. ### [206] [Regular and Anomalous Motion of Individual Magnetic Quincke Rollers Under Rotating Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11132)
*Zoran M. Cenev,Ville S. I. Havu,Jaakko V. I. Timonen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索由超顺磁性氧化铁纳米颗粒掺杂的二氧化硅颗粒组成的磁性Quincke滚子在旋转磁场中的运动行为，特别关注其轨迹模式的多样性和异常运动现象。

Method: 实验采用约11 mT的顺时针旋转磁场，频率范围0.2-2.75 Hz，观察单个颗粒的运动轨迹。理论模型结合了静电相互作用（electrostatic interactions）、远场流体动力学耦合（far-field hydrodynamic coupling）和磁偶极子近似（magnetic dipole approximation）。

Result: 低频时主要出现顺时针螺旋轨迹（CW helical trajectory），圆轨迹是其极限情况；高频时出现具有空间变化曲率的螺旋波状轨迹（helical wavy trajectories）。在特定条件下观察到异常的逆时针轨迹（anomalous CCW trajectories），颗粒滚动方向与外加磁场旋转方向相反。

Conclusion: 异常行为源于初始磁偶极矩（initial magnetic dipole moment）的大小和方向、旋转磁场频率以及初始平移速度（initial translational velocity）之间的相互作用，这些因素共同决定了颗粒呈现常规或异常旋转运动的可能性。

Abstract: We report the motion of individual magnetic Quincke rollers composed of silica particles doped with superparamagnetic iron oxide nanoparticles, whose activity arises from the coupling between Quincke rolling and an externally applied rotating magnetic field. We applied a clockwise (CW) rotating magnetic field of magnitude approximately 11 mT and rotational frequencies ranging from 0.2 to 2.75 Hz. At low frequencies, the dominant mode of motion is a CW helical trajectory. Circular trajectories emerge as a limiting case of this helical motion, in which lateral translation vanishes and the particle traces overlapping closed loops in the xy-plane. At higher frequencies, a second regular mode becomes prevalent, characterized by helical wavy trajectories in which the particle follows a CW helical path with a spatially varying curvature. Under specific conditions, however, we observe the unexpected emergence of anomalous counterclockwise (CCW) trajectories, in which individual particles roll in a direction opposite to that of the applied CW rotating magnetic field. A theoretical model incorporating electrostatic interactions, far-field hydrodynamic coupling, and a magnetic dipole approximation indicates that the anomalous behavior results from the interplay among the magnitude and orientation of the initial magnetic dipole moment, the frequency of the rotating magnetic field, and the magnitude of the initial translational velocity. Together, these factors determine the likelihood of a particle exhibiting regular or anomalous rotational motion.

### [207] [Pinch-off of non-Brownian rod suspensions: onset of heterogeneity and effective extensional viscosity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11219)
*Virgile Thiévenaz,Nathan Vani,Alban Sauret*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过液桥拉伸与断裂实验，探究了刚性尼龙纤维悬浮液从连续介质行为向离散行为转变的临界条件。研究发现断裂过程呈现三个连续区域，且纤维长度（而非直径）是控制异质变薄起始的关键离散尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液桥拉伸与断裂是探究颗粒悬浮液何时停止表现为连续介质的简单方法。本研究旨在理解各向异性悬浮液（特别是刚性纤维悬浮液）中连续介质行为失效的机制。

Method: 研究采用密度匹配的刚性尼龙纤维悬浮液，其长径比（aspect ratio）范围为2至84，体积分数φ覆盖从稀薄到浓密的区间。通过高速成像技术观察悬滴断裂过程，分析断裂动力学。

Result: 断裂过程呈现三个连续区域：早期等效流体区、对应纤维分离的位错区，以及颈部无纤维时的间隙液体控制区。区域间的阈值遵循先前提出的标度律，但以纤维长度而非直径作为相关离散尺度。等效流体区的有效拉伸粘度随体积分数和长径比增加而增大，但不等于平行板流变仪测得的剪切粘度。临界体积分数φ_c随长径比单调递减。

Conclusion: 断裂实验是探测各向异性悬浮液中连续介质失效的灵敏探针。对于刚性纤维，纤维长度控制着异质变薄的起始，而非纤维直径。Mills定律能很好地描述有效拉伸粘度和剪切粘度数据。

Abstract: The stretching and pinch-off of a liquid bridge is a simple way to probe when a suspension of particles stops behaving as a continuum. In this study, we consider density-matched suspensions of rigid nylon fibers with aspect ratios (length over diameter) ranging from 2 to 84, and volume fractions $φ$ spanning the dilute to dense regimes. High-speed imaging of pendant-drop breakup reveals three successive regimes, as previously observed for spherical particles: an equivalent-fluid regime at early times, a dislocation regime corresponding to the separation of the rods, and a final regime controlled by the interstitial liquid once the neck is devoid of rods. The thresholds between these regimes follow the previously proposed scaling for spherical particles, in which the rod length, rather than the rod diameter, is used as the relevant discrete scale. In the equivalent-fluid regime, pinch-off also leads to an effective extensional viscosity that increases with both volume fraction and aspect ratio. This viscosity is not equal to the shear viscosity measured in a parallel-plate rheometer, but both sets of data are well described by Mills' law using a critical volume fraction $φ_c$. Finally, the critical volume fraction $φ_c$ decreases monotonically with the aspect ratio and is well captured by an empirical law. These results show that pinch-off is a sensitive probe of continuum breakdown in anisotropic suspensions and that, for rigid rods, the rod length controls the onset of heterogeneous thinning.

</details>


### [208] [Machine Learning-Enabled Mechanical Analysis and Optimization of Bioinspired Functionally Graded Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11494)
*Zhangke Yang,Zhaoxu Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过构建肌腱-骨附着点（enthesis）的三维有限元模型，分析其分级结构和梯度矿化对力学性能的影响，并开发基于卷积神经网络的场预测器（CNNFP）优化生物启发功能梯度材料设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 肌腱-骨附着点（tendon-bone enthesis）能够连接力学性质差异显著的肌腱和骨组织，同时有效减少应力集中，这种能力在工程材料中罕见实现。其分级组织结构和梯度矿化变化被认为是实现优异性能的关键因素。

Method: 首先构建了界面纤维-骨附着点的三维有限元模型（3D FEM），其中局部材料特性取决于矿化水平、平均原纤维取向和角度分散度，基于多尺度连续介质理论。引入标量风险因子整合局部应力状态和原纤维组织结构来量化局部脆弱性。随后训练卷积神经网络场预测器（CNNFP）作为FEM的精确替代模型，并将其嵌入基于核的梯度优化框架中。

Result: 模拟结果表明，梯度和空间异质配置显著减少了应力集中，支持了现有的生物力学假设。优化设计通过FEM基准验证，建立了可推广的AI驱动优化路径用于生物启发功能梯度材料（bioinspired functionally graded materials）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将肌腱-骨附着点的力学洞察转化为生物启发工程材料设计，开发了基于CNNFP的优化框架，为功能梯度材料的智能化设计提供了通用方法。

Abstract: Tendon-bone enthesis connects tendon and bone, two mechanically dissimilar materials, while effectively minimizing stress concentrations, a capability rarely achieved in engineering materials. Its hierarchical organization and graded variations in composition or mineralization are widely recognized as key contributors to its exceptional performance. Here, we investigate the mechanics of enthesis, focusing on the insertion of interface collagen fibers into bone where hierarchical collagen fibril structures and graded mineralization are present, and translate these insights into bioinspired engineering material design using a convolutional neural network-based field predictor (CNNFP). We first construct a three-dimensional finite element model (FEM) of the interface fiber-bone enthesis, in which local material properties depend on mineralization level, mean fibril orientation, and angular dispersion, informed by a multiscale continuum theory. We introduce a scalar risk factor that integrates local stress states and constituent fibril organizations to quantify local vulnerability. Simulation results demonstrate that graded and spatially heterogeneous configurations markedly reduce stress concentrations, supporting prevailing biomechanical hypotheses. We then train the CNNFP as an accurate surrogate for FEM and embed it within a kernel-based gradient optimization framework to efficiently identify optimal field configurations. The optimized designs are validated against FEM ground truth, establishing a generalizable AI-enabled pathway for the optimization of bioinspired functionally graded materials.

</details>


### [209] [Kinematic and rheological equivalence of steady shearing and planar extensional flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11678)
*Nicholas King,Gareth H. McKinley*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了稳态剪切流与平面拉伸流之间的深层流变学等价性，通过消除剪切流的旋转分量，仅使用剪切流测量的材料函数即可重构未知流体的稳态平面拉伸粘度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稳态剪切（steady shearing）和平面拉伸（planar extension）通常被视为两种不同的流场类型，特别是在研究复杂流体流变学时。论文旨在探索这两种变形历史之间的深层流变学等价关系。

Method: 通过利用两种流动之间的运动学等价性，推导出材料元所经历的有效拉伸速率（effective extension rate），从而消除剪切流的旋转分量。该方法仅使用稳态剪切流中测量的材料函数来重构流体的稳态平面拉伸粘度（steady planar extensional viscosity）。

Result: 研究证明了剪切流与拉伸流之间的等价性，通过现象学模型和微观动机的框架不变本构模型（frame-invariant constitutive models）以及粘弹性聚合物溶液（viscoelastic polymer solution）的实验验证了这一等价关系。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了稳态剪切流与平面拉伸流之间的深层流变学等价性，为仅使用剪切流测量数据重构拉伸粘度提供了理论基础和实验验证。

Abstract: Steady shearing and planar extension are commonly viewed as two distinct types of flow field, especially in the context of probing the rheology of complex fluids. By leveraging the kinematic equivalence between the two flows, we derive an effective extension rate experienced by a material element which removes the rotational component of the shearing flow. This enables reconstruction of the steady planar extensional viscosity of an unknown fluid using only material functions measured in a steady shearing flow, revealing a deep rheological equivalence between the two deformation histories. We demonstrate this equivalency through phenomenological and microscopically motivated frame-invariant constitutive models as well as experiments with a viscoelastic polymer solution.

</details>


### [210] [Effect of Pre-Shear and Dispersity on Crystallization of a Model Polymer with Soft Pair Interactions using Molecular Dynamics Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11706)
*Tzortzis Koulaxizis,Antonia Statt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子动力学模拟探究预剪切（pre-shear）对聚合物结晶的影响，发现短链的加入能显著提高结晶度和初始生长速率，而预剪切仅在短链单分散熔体中效果明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物结晶在基础理论和工业应用中都具有重要意义，但加工处理对结晶初始阶段的影响尚未完全理解。本研究旨在探究预剪切对单分散熔体和双分散共混物结晶过程的影响。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）研究通用分段粗粒化聚合物模型（segmentally coarse-grained polymer model）。通过分析单分散熔体和双分散共混物在预剪切后的结晶行为，考察多分散性（polydispersity）对结晶的影响。

Result: 在长链熔体中加入短链使最终结晶度提高约10%，初始生长速率增加约两倍。预剪切仅在短链单分散熔体中显著提高生长速率和结晶度，并降低晶粒（crystal grains）的非球形度和扁长性。通过连接链（tie chain）和环链（loop chain）分析发现，仅单分散熔体的连接链分数随预剪切显著增加。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了预剪切条件下结晶度和晶簇形态的变化，为理解聚合物熔体在预剪切作用下的初始结晶过程提供了更深入的认识。多分散性对预剪切效果具有重要调节作用。

Abstract: Polymer crystallization is a process of great interest in both fundamental theory and industrial settings, particularly in polymer processing and applications involving semi-crystalline materials. The effect of processing on the initial stages of crystallization is not fully understood. Our study investigates the influence of pre-shear on monodisperse melts and bidisperse blends of a generic, segmentally coarse-grained polymer model. Through molecular dynamics simulations, we explore how polydispersity affects crystallization, where we found that the addition of short chains to a melt of longer chains increased the final crystallinity by about 10%, and increased the initial growth rate by roughly a factor of two. In contrast, however, pre-shearing the hot melt before quenching only showed a minor increase in both growth rates and final crystallinty, except in monodisperse melts of short chains. Crystal grain shapes were most influenced by pre-shearing monodisperse melts, where both asphericity and prolateness decreased. Additionally, we determined topological connectivity of crystal grains through tie- and loop-chain analysis. Again, only monodisperse melts showed a significant increase of tie chain fractions with pre-shear, while all other systems showed only modest increases. Our findings provide insight into the changes of crystallinity and cluster morphologies that emerge when pre-sheared, offering a deeper understanding of the initial crystallization processes in polymer melts when subjected to pre-shear.

</details>

Method: 文章避免使用数学方程和过度技术细节，通过日常例子培养物理直觉，重点阐述核心概念和论证精神，主要关注系统的动力学特性（dynamical aspects）。

Result: 文章介绍了软活性物质物理的基础知识、起源及其与传统平衡态凝聚态物理的区别，并以作者研究组发表的实验研究为例，简要讨论了归巢和迁徙生物轨迹的普适特征（universal features）。

Conclusion: 软活性物质物理作为一个新兴领域，在理解生物过程的物理机制方面展现出巨大潜力，本文通过通俗易懂的方式为该领域提供了入门指导，特别强调了动力学特性的重要性。

Abstract: This article aims to introduce the broad field of soft active matter physics and its relevance to the life sciences in simple, accessible language. Although this area of research is relatively new, it has already demonstrated significant potential in providing a physical understanding of many biological processes. While several review articles by leading researchers exist, they can be difficult to grasp for undergraduate students and even early-career researchers who wish to enter this field. In this article, I cover the basics, introduce the origins of soft active matter physics, and explain how it differs from traditional equilibrium condensed matter ideas at the fundamental level. For the most part, I will avoid mathematical equations and excessive technical precision in several statements. Instead, I will focus on communicating the core ideas and the overall spirit of the argument, using everyday examples to develop a physical intuition. The primary focus will be on the dynamical aspects of these systems. I will conclude by briefly discussing a published experimental study from our research group that examines universal features of the trajectories of homing and migrating organisms.

</details>

### [212] [Toward Neutrino and Dark Matter Detection with Ancient Minerals: TEM Study of Heavy-Ion Tracks in Olivine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09732)
*Andrew Calabrese-Day,Emilie LaVoie-Ingram,Kathryn Ream,Hannah Ross,Joshua Spitz,Patrick Stengel,Kai Sun,Alexander Takla*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该研究通过重离子辐照模拟天体粒子相互作用，利用STEM分析橄榄石中离子径迹宽度随深度的变化，验证了古探测器技术的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 太阳、超新星、大气中微子及WIMP暗物质粒子与地球相互作用数十亿年，古探测器技术旨在通过检测矿物中保存的晶体缺陷来探测这些事件。需要测试该技术可行性并研究橄榄石等候选矿物中径迹缺陷的形成与形态。

Method: 采用离子辐照技术人工植入径迹以模拟天体粒子相互作用。使用15 MeV Au⁺⁵辐照橄榄石晶体，通过聚焦离子束切片在不同深度进行测量，利用扫描透射电子显微镜分析重离子径迹宽度随深度的变化关系。

Result: 研究发现，在研究的能量范围（0.4-12.9 MeV）内，径迹连续性发生显著变化，表明电子阻止本领与核阻止本领主导地位的转变，这与SRIM软件模拟预测一致。橄榄石中产生的径迹表明该矿物是古探测的优良候选材料。

Conclusion: 橄榄石在MeV能量尺度下能够产生稳定的径迹，是古探测器技术的理想候选矿物。研究验证了通过离子辐照模拟天体粒子相互作用并分析径迹形态的方法可行性。

Abstract: Solar, supernova, and atmospheric neutrinos, and possibly weakly interacting massive particle (WIMP) dark matter, have been interacting in the Earth beneath our feet for billions of years. The ''paleo-detector'' technique seeks to detect and characterize the induced crystalline defects from these events, in particular from energetic nuclear recoils, which in some minerals can be preserved on these timescales. Such defects can manifest as nuclear recoil tracks, on the order of a few nanometers wide and extending up to hundreds of microns in length, which can be detected with nanoscale-resolution microscopy. In order to test the feasibility of the paleo-detector technique and to study the formation and morphology of track defects in promising mineral candidates like olivine, we use ion irradiation to artificially implant tracks to effectively mimic astrophysical particle interactions. We present a study of heavy-ion track width as a function of depth, which we relate to ion energy, in an olivine crystal irradiated with 15 MeV Au$^{+5}$ using scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM). Unlike previous studies, which measure tracks at the surface of the irradiated sample, we instead take measurements at various target depths via focused ion-beam sectioning of the irradiated sample. No etching techniques are used to enhance the tracks. In addition, we provide a comparison to predictions from simulations using SRIM software and previous results with a variety of ion species and energies. Notably, we find that a significant change in track continuity across the energy range studied (0.4-12.9 MeV) is indicative of the transition between electronic and nuclear stopping power dominance, consistent with the simulations' predictions. Overall, the tracks produced in olivine indicate that this mineral is an attractive candidate for paleo-detection, with robust track creation at the MeV scale.

</details>

*A. Tishelman-Charny,A. Buzzi,F. Capocasa,G. D'Amen,S. Diaw,D. Duan,M. H. Mohamed Farook,G. Giacomini,M. Kurth,D. Ponman,J. Roloff,E. Rossi,S. Stucci,A. Tricoli,H. Zhang*

Result: 实验观察到多种失效类别，每种对应不同的电气和机械损伤特征。这些结果深化了对硅器件永久辐射损伤的理解，特别是对单粒子烧毁（SEB）及其他损伤机制的认识，为未来探测器安全运行提供了关键信息。

Conclusion: 该研究通过系统实验进一步理解了硅器件在高辐射环境中的永久损伤机制，特别是单粒子烧毁（SEB）现象，为未来探测器在高辐射环境中的安全运行和损伤缓解策略提供了重要依据。

Abstract: Low Gain Avalanche Diodes are prime candidates for high-resolution timing applications in High Energy Physics, Nuclear science, and several other fields. Operating these devices in high-radiation environments presents various hazards, including the risk of their permanent degradation or destruction caused by effects such as Single Event Burnout. Studies using minimum ionizing particles found a greatly reduced Single Event Burnout risk by operating below a bias voltage corresponding to an average electric field of 12 V/$μ$m - however, as high energy particle colliders produce a wide energy spectrum of radiation, it is crucial to understand this phenomenon and other possible damage mechanisms at energy deposition levels greater than those of minimum ionizing particles. This was achieved by pre-irradiating LGADs and PiN diodes with active thicknesses of 20, 30, and 50 $μ$m up to 1.5 $\times$ 10$^{15}$ $\mathrm{n_{eq}/cm^2}$, and exposing them to beams of protons and heavy ions (C, O, Fe, Au) at the BNL Tandem van de Graaff accelerator. Several mortality categories were observed, defined by different electrical and mechanical damage signatures. This furthers our understanding of permanent radiation damage of silicon devices, crucial towards mitigating Single Event Burnout and other damage mechanisms to safely operate future detectors.

### [214] [Characterization of the 20-inch Photomultiplier Tubes for RENE Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11727)

Conclusion: 本研究结果将有助于解释RENE探测器信号，并为估计RENE数据潜在系统误差提供参考。同时，这些发现预计将为使用同类型光电倍增管的其他实验提供有价值的信息。

Abstract: To address the Reactor Antineutrino Anomaly (RAA) observed in neutrino experiments, the Reactor Experiment for Neutrino and Exotics (RENE) has been initiated using a liquid scintillation detector. In this study, we investigate the characteristics of two 20-inch Hamamatsu R12860 photomultiplier tubes (PMTs) intended for installation in the RENE detector. The charge and timing responses of the PMTs were evaluated at both the nominal and target gains expected during actual operation. In particular, gain non-uniformity arising from the large-diameter photocathode with a box-and-line type dynode structure was examined, and the maximum gain variation was measured. The occurrence rate, timing, and charge distributions of late pulses and afterpulses were also investigated to characterize the specific response features of the R12860 PMT. The results reported in this study will aid in the interpretation of signals from the RENE detector and serve as a reference for estimating potential systematic uncertainties in RENE data. Furthermore, these findings are expected to provide valuable information for other experiments employing the same type of PMTs.

### [215] [Generative Path-Finding Method for Wasserstein Gradient Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11519)
*Chengyu Liu,Xiang Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GenWGP提出了一种生成式路径寻找框架，用于计算Wasserstein梯度流（WGFs）的完整演化路径。该方法通过归一化流（normalizing flows）学习从初始分布到平衡分布的生成流，避免了传统方法的高维诅咒和时间步长约束，仅需少量离散点即可匹配高保真参考解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算Wasserstein梯度流从任意初始分布到平衡态的完整路径具有挑战性，特别是在高维情况下。欧拉方法（Eulerian methods）受维度诅咒影响，而现有的拉格朗日方法（Lagrangian approaches）基于粒子或生成映射，无法通过时间步长调优自然提升效率。

Method: GenWGP学习一个生成流，通过最小化路径损失将质量从初始密度传输到未知平衡分布。该损失源自几何作用泛函（geometric action functional），受Dawson Gartner大偏差理论（large deviation theory）启发。方法采用归一化流计算几何曲线，并在相邻网络层间强制近似恒定内禀速度，使离散化分布在Wasserstein度量下保持近似等距。

Result: 在Fokker Planck和聚集类型问题上的实验表明，GenWGP仅需约十几个离散点即可匹配或超越高保真参考解，同时捕捉复杂动力学。该方法避免了精细的时间步长约束，实现了基本独立于时间或几何离散化的稳定训练。

Conclusion: GenWGP框架为Wasserstein梯度路径提供了一种高效的生成式路径寻找方法，通过几何曲线计算和恒定内禀速度设计，克服了传统方法在高维情况下的计算挑战，实现了稳定且高效的梯度流路径计算。

Abstract: Wasserstein gradient flows (WGFs) describe the evolution of probability distributions in Wasserstein space as steepest descent dynamics for a free energy functional. Computing the full path from an arbitrary initial distribution to equilibrium is challenging, especially in high dimensions. Eulerian methods suffer from the curse of dimensionality, while existing Lagrangian approaches based on particles or generative maps do not naturally improve efficiency through time step tuning. We propose GenWGP, a generative path finding framework for Wasserstein gradient paths. GenWGP learns a generative flow that transports mass from an initial density to an unknown equilibrium distribution by minimizing a path loss that encodes the full trajectory and its terminal equilibrium condition. The loss is derived from a geometric action functional motivated by Dawson Gartner large deviation theory for empirical distributions of interacting diffusion systems. We formulate both a finite horizon action under physical time parametrization and a reparameterization invariant geometric action based on Wasserstein arclength. Using normalizing flows, GenWGP computes a geometric curve toward equilibrium while enforcing approximately constant intrinsic speed between adjacent network layers, so that discretized distributions remain nearly equidistant in the Wasserstein metric along the path. This avoids delicate time stepping constraints and enables stable training that is largely independent of temporal or geometric discretization. Experiments on Fokker Planck and aggregation type problems show that GenWGP matches or exceeds high fidelity reference solutions with only about a dozen discretization points while capturing complex dynamics.

</details>


### [216] [ReadMOF: Structure-Free Semantic Embeddings from Systematic MOF Nomenclature for Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10568)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 系统化学名称（如IUPAC风格的MOF命名法）包含丰富的结构和组成信息，但传统方法需要原子坐标或连接图。本研究旨在探索利用这些标准化文本格式的名称来建立结构-性质关系，提供一种几何独立的替代方案。

Method: ReadMOF采用预训练语言模型（pretrained language models），将剑桥结构数据库（CSD）中的系统MOF名称转换为向量嵌入（vector embeddings），这些嵌入能近似代表传统基于结构的描述符。结合大型语言模型（large language models），框架仅通过文本输入即可建立化学意义的推理能力。

Result: ReadMOF的向量嵌入支持材料信息学应用，包括性质预测、相似性检索和聚类，性能与几何依赖方法相当。仅使用文本输入即可建立化学意义的推理能力，表明结构化化学语言通过现代自然语言处理技术可提供可扩展、可解释的替代方案。

Conclusion: 结构化化学语言通过现代自然语言处理技术解释，可为传统分子表示提供可扩展、可解释且几何独立的替代方案。该方法为材料科学中的语言驱动发现开辟了新机遇。

Abstract: Systematic chemical names, such as IUPAC-style nomenclature for metal-organic frameworks (MOFs), contain rich structural and compositional information in a standardized textual format. Here we introduce ReadMOF, which is, to our knowledge, the first nomenclature-free machine learning framework that leverages these names to model structure-property relationships without requiring atomic coordinates or connectivity graphs. By employing pretrained language models, ReadMOF converts systematic MOF names from the Cambridge Structural Database (CSD) into vector embeddings that closely represent traditional structure-based descriptors. These embeddings enable applications in materials informatics, including property prediction, similarity retrieval, and clustering, with performance comparable to geometry-dependent methods. When combined with large language models, ReadMOF also establishes chemically meaningful reasoning ability with textual input only. Our results show that structured chemical language, interpreted through modern natural language processing techniques, can provide a scalable, interpretable, and geometry-independent alternative to conventional molecular representations. This approach opens new opportunities for language-driven discovery in materials science.

Method: 研究采用无模型强化学习框架（model-free reinforcement learning framework），训练一个智能体（agent）直接从劳厄衍射图案中学习识别和导航至高对称性取向（high-symmetry orientations），无需访问晶体学和衍射理论。

Here we introduce an autonomous system that aligns single crystals without access to crystallography and diffraction theory. Using a model-free reinforcement learning framework, an agent learns to identify and navigate towards high-symmetry orientations directly from Laue diffraction patterns. Despite the absence of human supervision, the agent develops human-like strategies to achieve time-efficient alignment across different crystal symmetry classes. With this, we provide a computational framework for intelligent diffractometers. As such, our approach advances the development of automated experimental workflows in materials science.

### [218] [Fundamental thermo-visco mechanical interactions governing the acoustic response of laser-excited nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10201)
*Stefano Giordano,Michele Diego,Francesco Banfi,Michele Brun*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了激光加热球形粒子在粘性流体中产生的热声球形波生成与传播机制，揭示了热声效应（thermophone）和机械声效应（mechanophone）在不同频率下的主导作用，并分析了流体粘度对声波衰减和穿透深度的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解激光加热球形粒子在粘性流体中产生热声波的物理机制，特别是热声效应和机械声效应的耦合作用，以及流体粘度对声波传播特性的影响，为生物医学诊疗应用提供理论基础。

Method: 基于两相质量、动量和能量守恒方程的耦合理论模型，明确考虑了热扩散和粘性损耗，完整描述了热场与声场的相互耦合关系。

Result: 热声效应在低频段占主导，而机械声效应在高频段更为显著，交叉频率由固-液界面热阻决定；流体粘度显著影响声波衰减和穿透深度，特别是在皮秒和亚皮秒激光脉冲激发下产生的超高频波中，粘性阻尼对机械声效应起关键作用。

Conclusion: 频率和流体粘度共同控制着实际介质中生成声波的穿透长度，这一发现对于优化嵌入生物组织中的激光激活粒子在诊疗（theranostics）应用中的性能具有重要意义。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the thermoacoustic generation and propagation of spherical waves in a viscous fluid induced by a laser-heated spherical particle. Periodic laser excitation gives rise to two coupled mechanisms of acoustic emission. Heat transfer from the particle to the surrounding fluid produces periodic compressions and rarefactions, giving rise to the thermophone effect, while periodic thermal expansion of the solid particle modulates its radius and launches acoustic waves through a piston-like action, known as the mechanophone effect. The thermophone contribution dominates at low frequencies, whereas the mechanophone mechanism becomes more relevant at higher frequencies, with the crossover governed by the interfacial thermal resistance at the solid-fluid boundary. We investigate the effect of nanoparticle embedding fluid viscosity on acoustic wave propagation. Viscous dissipation has a significant impact on attenuation and substantially alters the acoustic penetration depth, thereby affecting the effectiveness of the signal transmission. Viscous damping plays a key role in the mechanophone effect, where hypersonic frequency waves are generated, notably by photoacoustic excitation with picosecond and subpicosecond laser pulses. We develop a theoretical model based on the coupled conservation equations of mass, momentum, and energy in both phases, explicitly accounting for thermal diffusion and viscous losses. The reciprocal coupling between thermal and acoustic fields is fully described, allowing us to quantify how frequency and fluid viscosity jointly control the penetration length of the generated acoustic waves in realistic media. Finally, we discuss the implications for theranostics, highlighting how ensembles of laser-activated particles embedded in biological tissue may be optimized for diagnostic and therapeutic applications.

</details>


### [219] [Non-Monotonic Marangoni Suppression of Hydrodynamic Coarsening in Bicontinuous Liquid-Liquid Phase Separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10920)
*Tian Liu,Haohao Hao,Jiaxi Liu,Yongjie Zhou,Feiyu An,Huanshu Tan*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究通过相场模型和Navier-Stokes方程模拟，揭示了可溶性表面活性剂通过Marangoni应力（而非仅降低平均界面张力）非单调抑制双连续相流体动力学粗化的机制，最强抑制出现在中间Péclet数（Pe_ψ=10）时。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体动力学粗化（hydrodynamic coarsening）是液-液相分离的核心过程，但可溶性表面活性剂如何调控此过程仍不清楚。研究旨在阐明表面活性剂抑制双连续相（bicontinuous domains）粗化的具体机制。

Method: 采用经过验证的双序参量相场模型（two-order-parameter phase-field model），耦合不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程进行模拟分析。通过分析力演化、界面表面活性剂统计和分解的表面活性剂通量预算来探究机制。

Result: 研究发现流体动力学粗化主要被表面活性剂诱导的Marangoni应力抑制，而非仅通过降低平均界面张力。这种抑制对表面活性剂Péclet数（Pe_ψ）呈非单调依赖，最强抑制出现在中间值Pe_ψ=10。非单调性源于表面活性剂补充与梯度保留之间的竞争。

Conclusion: 研究确立了可溶性表面活性剂通过输运控制机制调控双连续相流体动力学粗化的原理：当足够的界面表面活性剂负载与持久的浓度梯度共存时，抑制效果最强。这为理解表面活性剂在相分离过程中的作用提供了新视角。

Abstract: Hydrodynamic coarsening of bicontinuous domains is a central process in liquid-liquid phase separation, yet how soluble surfactants regulate this process remains poorly understood. Using a validated two-order-parameter phase-field model coupled to the incompressible Navier-Stokes equations, we show that hydrodynamic coarsening is suppressed primarily by surfactant-induced Marangoni stresses rather than by the reduction of mean interfacial tension alone. These stresses hinder interfacial coalescence, reorganize the local vortical flow, and thereby redirect the morphological evolution of bicontinuous domains. A central result is that this suppression depends non-monotonically on the surfactant Péclet number, with the strongest inhibition occurring at an intermediate value, $Pe_ψ=10$, rather than at $Pe_ψ=1$ or 100. Analyses of force evolution, interfacial surfactant statistics, and decomposed surfactant flux budgets show that this non-monotonicity arises from a competition between surfactant replenishment and gradient retention. At low $Pe_ψ$, diffusion efficiently replenishes the interface but smooths interfacial concentration gradients; at high $Pe_ψ$, advection preserves interfacial heterogeneity but leaves the interface insufficiently supplied with surfactant. The strongest suppression therefore occurs when sufficient interfacial surfactant loading coexists with persistent concentration gradients. These results establish a transport-controlled mechanism by which soluble surfactants regulate bicontinuous hydrodynamic coarsening.

</details>


### [220] [From Sedimentation to Suspension: Critical Strain as a Predictor of Particle Resuspension Thresholds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11634)
*Mohammadreza Mahmoudian,Simon A. Rogers,Parisa Mirbod*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和建模揭示了粘性再悬浮（viscous resuspension）的应变控制机制，建立了预测稳态和振荡剪切流中悬浮行为的统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粘性再悬浮过程在环境污染物输运、河床侵蚀和生物地球化学循环等众多自然和工业系统中至关重要，但在振荡剪切条件下预测再悬浮的发生时机和机制仍具挑战性。

Method: 研究采用体流变测量（bulk rheometry）和原位流变显微镜技术（in situ rheo-microscopy），在宽范围颗粒体积分数（φ=0.30-0.55）下，对致密非布朗悬浮液（dense, non-Brownian suspensions）在稳态和振荡剪切条件下的再悬浮动力学进行了系统研究。

Result: 研究发现应变是控制从沉积床到完全悬浮状态转变的关键参数，这种应变驱动的起始由有效颗粒间碰撞（effective interparticle collisions）和集体颗粒运动（collective particle motion）介导。研究开发了能够捕捉观察到的应变阈值随体积分数变化的预测模型。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了稳健的应变控制再悬浮机制，建立了预测稳态和振荡流中悬浮行为的统一框架，为管理地球物理、生物和工业环境中的颗粒输运提供了新工具。构建了新的状态图（state diagram），界定了沉积、再悬浮和完全悬浮三种状态区域。

Abstract: Viscous resuspension, the process by which sedimented particles are re-entrained into a fluid under flow, is central to numerous natural and industrial systems, including environmental contaminant transport, riverbed erosion, and biogeochemical cycling. Despite its ubiquity and importance, predicting when and how resuspension occurs remains challenging, particularly under oscillatory shear, where particle interactions are nonlinear, collective, and time-dependent. Here, we examine the resuspension dynamics of dense, non-Brownian suspensions under both steady and oscillatory shear using bulk rheometry and in situ rheo-microscopy over a broad range of particle volume fractions (φ= 0.30 to 0.55). We demonstrate that strain is the key control parameter governing the transition from a sedimented bed to a fully suspended state. This strain-driven onset is mediated by effective interparticle collisions and collective particle motion. We develop a predictive model that captures the observed strain thresholds as a function of volume fraction, allowing for the construction of a new state diagram delineating sedimentation, resuspension, and full suspension regimes. These findings reveal a robust, strain-controlled resuspension mechanism and establish a unified framework for predicting suspension behavior across steady and oscillatory flows, offering new tools for managing particle-laden transport in geophysical, biological, and industrial environments.

### [221] [Schrödinger-Navier-Stokes equation for capillary fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11747)
*Luca Salasnich,Sauro Succi,Adriano Tiribocchi*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该论文分析了薛定谔-纳维-斯托克斯（Schrödinger-Navier-Stokes, SNS）方程在微流控和软物质物理中的性质，揭示了其与毛细流体Navier-Stokes-Korteweg方程的等价性，并推导了声模色散关系和受限流体的有效一维方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探讨薛定谔-纳维-斯托克斯（Schrödinger-Navier-Stokes, SNS）方程在微流控（microfluidics）和软物质（soft matter）物理中的相关性质，特别是该方程在描述复杂流动物质状态方面的潜在应用价值。

Method: 通过建立作用量泛函（action functional）的等价性，证明SNS方程与Navier-Stokes-Korteweg方程的正式等价性，其中作用量自然分解为Korteweg保守部分和Rayleigh耗散部分。同时推导了声模的色散关系（dispersion relation）以及受限毛细管中流体的有效一维SNS方程。

Result: 研究显示SNS方程在一般参数下与毛细流体的Navier-Stokes-Korteweg方程形式等价。色散关系分析表明，色散参数控制毛细刚度（capillary stiffness），耗散参数控制粘性阻尼（viscous damping），且在量子极限下可恢复Bogoliubov色散关系。此外，推导了窄毛细管中受限流体的有效一维SNS方程。

Conclusion: SNS方程可能为复杂流动物质状态的量子模拟（quantum simulation）提供便利，该方程在微流控和软物质物理中具有潜在的理论和应用价值。

Abstract: We highlight some properties of the Schrödinger-Navier-Stokes (SNS) equation [Salasnich, Succi, and Tiribocchi (2024)] of potential relevance for microfluidics and soft matter. Specifically, we show that the SNS equationwith generic parameters is formally equivalent to the Navier-Stokes-Korteweg equations for capillary fluids, with the equivalence established at the level of an action functional that decomposes naturally into a Korteweg conservative and a Rayleigh dissipative components, respectively. We derive the dispersion relation for sound modes, showing that the dispersive parameter controls capillary stiffness while the dissipative parameter controls viscous damping, and that the Bogoliubov dispersion relation is recovered in the quantum limit. We also derive an effective one-dimensional SNS equation for a fluid confined in a narrow capillary tube. Finally, it is argued that the SNS may facilitate the quantum simulation of complex states of flowing matter.

### [222] [Tiles from projections of the root and weight lattices of $A_n$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10574)
*Nazife Ozdes Koca,Mehmet Koca,Rehab Nasser Al Reasi*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种将权重格点（weight lattice）$A_n^\ast$的Voronoi镶嵌（Voronoi tessellation）进行投影的通用技术，并应用于$A_4^\ast$格点。该投影产生了与从$A_4$格点的Voronoi胞投影完全不同的铺砌方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文的主要目的是引入一种将权重格点$A_n^\ast$的Voronoi镶嵌进行投影的通用技术，并将其应用于$A_4^\ast$格点。该数学技术对于根格点（root lattice）$A_n$的投影同样有用。

Method: 引入了一组线性相关且非正交的$(n+1)$维向量$k_i$，将简单根（simple roots）和基本权重（fundamental weights）分别定义为$α_i=k_i-k_{i+1}$和$ω_i=k_1+k_2+\ldots+k_i$。当$k_i$向量在正交基中定义时，其前两个分量确定Coxeter平面（Coxeter plane）。

Result: $A_4^\ast$格点Voronoi胞的二维面在四维空间中包含正六边形和正方形，但投影后产生两种类型的六边形和两种类型的菱形，其边长比例符合黄金比例（golden ratio）。$A_n$和$A_n^\ast$的Delone胞在Coxeter平面上的投影显示相同类型的瓦片和铺砌，但Voronoi胞投影产生不同的瓦片和铺砌。

Conclusion: 权重格点$A_4^\ast$的Voronoi镶嵌投影产生与$A_4$格点Voronoi胞投影完全不同的铺砌方案。$A_n^\ast$的Voronoi胞$V(0)^\ast$是$(n+1)$阶置换多面体（permutohedron），其顶点为向量$k_i$的排列。

Abstract: Main purpose of this work is to introduce a general technique of projection of the Voronoi tessellation of the weight lattice $A_n^\ast$ and apply it for the lattice $A_4^\ast$. The projection of the Voronoi tessellation of the weight lattice $A_4^\ast$ produces a totally different tiling scheme than the tiling obtained from the Voronoi cell projection of the lattice $A_4$. The 2D faces of the Voronoi cell of the lattice $A_4^\ast$ are of two types: regular hexagons and squares in 4-dimensions but project into two types of hexagons and two types of rhombuses with edges of two lengths in proportion to golden ratio. The mathematical technique employed is also useful for the projections of the root lattice $A_n$. A convenient set of linearly dependent and non-orthogonal $\left(n+1\right)$ vectors $k_i$ is introduced. The simple roots and the fundamental weights are defined as $α_i=k_i-k_{i+1},\left(i=1,2,\ldots,n\right) ,ω_i=k_1+k_2+\ldots+k_i$, respectively. When the vectors $k_i$ are defined in an orthogonal basis, the first two components of $k_i$ determine the Coxeter plane. Projection of the Delone cells of $A_n$ and $A_n^\ast$ on the Coxeter plane displays the same type of tiles and tilings but the Voronoi cell projection of these lattices yields different tiles and tilings. Vertices of the Voronoi cell $V(0)$ of $A_n$ is the union of the orbits of the weight vectors $W(a_n){(ω}_1)\cup W\left(a_n\right)(ω_2)\cup\ldots\cup W\left(a_n\right)(ω_n)$ and the 2D faces are the rhombuses. The Voronoi cell ${V(0)}^\ast$ of $A_n^\ast$ is the permutohedron of order $(n+1)$ and its vertices are the permutations of the vectors ${k}_i$ of the vertex $\frac{1}{n+1}[\left(n+1\right)k_1+nk_2+\ldots+k_{n+1}]$. It has regular hexagons and squares as 2D faces in $n$-dimensions.

</details>

### [223] [Proof of entropic order in Generalized Ising Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09768)
*Enrico Andriolo,Mendel Nguyen,Emily Richards,Tin Sulejmanpasic*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文严格证明了广义伊辛模型（generalized Ising models）在参数p≥1时存在任意高温下的有序现象（entropic order），并揭示这些模型可解决图论中的最大独立集（Maximum Independent Set）优化问题，导致某些晶格系统出现玻璃相（glassy phases）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究认为，在广义伊辛模型中，当实相互作用参数p≥1时，系统可能在任意高温下出现有序现象（entropic order）。本文旨在严格证明这一猜想，并进一步探索这些模型在图论优化问题中的应用。

Method: 采用严格的数学证明方法，分析参数化广义伊辛模型（generalized Ising models parameterised by real interaction parameter p）在p≥1条件下的行为。研究这些模型在任意图（arbitrary graphs）上的性质，并将其与图论中的包装问题（graph packing problems）建立联系。

Result: 严格证明了entropic order猜想，即当p≥1时，广义伊辛模型确实存在任意高温下的有序现象。进一步发现这些模型能够解决最大独立集（Maximum Independent Set）优化问题，而该问题的NP-hard性质导致某些晶格系统出现玻璃相（glassy phases）。

Conclusion: 广义伊辛模型不仅严格证明了entropic order现象的存在，还揭示了其与图论优化问题的深刻联系。由于最大独立集问题的计算复杂性，该研究预测了entropic glass现象的出现，为理解复杂系统中的玻璃相提供了新视角。

Abstract: Ordering at arbitrarily high temperature - entropic order - has been argued to take place in a class of generalized Ising models parameterised by a real interaction parameter $p$ when $p\ge 1$. We give a rigorous proof of this conjecture. We further show that on arbitrary graphs, these models solve graph packing problems - crucially, the Maximum Independent Set optimisation problem. Due to the NP-hardness of this packing problem on generic graphs, some lattice systems will exhibit glassy phases. We call this phenomenon $entropic$ $glass$.

</details>


### [224] [Universality and ambiguity in extremes of anomalous diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10004)
*Sean D Lawley*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了多随机搜索者中最快者找到目标的极端首次通过时间（fFPT）特性，揭示了fFPT随搜索者数量对数衰减以及亚扩散搜索可能快于正常扩散的普遍性特征，同时指出这些特征对具体模型参数的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究指出，当搜索者速度无界时，最快首次通过时间（fFPT）会随搜索者数量对数衰减且亚扩散搜索可能更快，但这些结论对实际物理系统的适用性存疑。本研究旨在探讨速度有界或无界情况下，各类异常扩散和正常扩散模型中fFPT的普遍特性。

Method: 研究分析了包括尺度布朗运动（scaled Brownian motion）、黎曼-刘维尔分数布朗运动（Riemann-Liouville fractional Brownian motion）和分数布朗运动（fractional Brownian motion）在内的广泛扩散模型，涵盖速度有界和无界情况，系统考察了fFPT随搜索者数量变化的衰减规律。

Result: 研究发现，对于所有研究的扩散模型，fFPT随搜索者数量呈对数衰减（特征i），且亚扩散搜索可以快于正常扩散（特征ii），而超扩散搜索可能慢于正常扩散。这表明这些特征具有相当程度的普遍性。

Conclusion: 虽然fFPT的对数衰减特性和亚扩散优势具有普遍性，但这些特征的有效参数范围依赖于具体模型细节。因此，在将这些特征应用于特定物理系统时仍存在模糊性，需要根据具体模型参数进行判断。

Abstract: Many biophysical processes begin when the fastest searcher finds a target out of many random searchers, which is called an extreme or fastest first passage time (fFPT). In some models, (i) the fFPT vanishes logarithmically as the number of searchers grows, and (ii) the fFPT can be faster for subdiffusive search compared to normal diffusion. Though mathematically rigorous, the relevance of (i) and (ii) to actual physical systems is suspect since their derivations involve searchers which move with unbounded speed. Indeed, we previously proved that the fFPT for searchers with bounded speed converges exponentially to a strictly positive minimal search time as the number of searchers grows. In this paper, we study fFPTs for a broad class of anomalous and normal diffusion models with bounded or unbounded speed. These models include scaled Brownian motion, Riemann-Liouville fractional Brownian motion, and fractional Brownian motion. For all of these models, we show that the fFPT decays logarithmically in the number of searchers and that subdiffusion can be faster than normal diffusion (we further show that superdiffusion can be slower than normal diffusion). In this sense, features (i) and (ii) are rather universal. On the other hand, we show that the parameter regimes in which (i) and (ii) are valid depend on the particulars of the individual model, and thus ambiguities remain in the relevance of these features to specific physical systems.

</details>


### [225] [Confined kinetics and heterogeneous diffusion driven by fractional Gaussian noise: A path integral approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10663)
*David Santiago Quevedo,Felipe Segundo Abril-Bermúdez,Cristiane Morais Smith*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究从路径积分视角分析了由分数高斯噪声驱动的扩散过程，其中噪声具有长程相关性并以状态依赖的乘法方式耦合，推导了基于Lamperti变换的高斯传播子，并分析了乘法扩散与约束的相互作用效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多复杂系统由Langevin型方程描述，其中噪声呈现长程相关性并以状态依赖的乘法方式耦合到系统，导致异质非马尔可夫扩散。本研究旨在从路径积分视角探究这一扩散问题。

Method: 采用路径积分方法，使用平稳相位近似推导出基于过程Lamperti变换的高斯传播子。在Feynman-Kac框架下分析过程受制于湮灭率的情况，并开发了基于有效局域哈密顿量推导动力学方程的一般程序。

Result: 在加法极限下，结果恢复了基于Riemann-Liouville公式的分数布朗运动路径积分表示，并建立了其与Langevin构造的等价性。研究表明乘法扩散与约束的相互作用诱导出有效漂移项，导致概率在低噪声振幅区域累积。

Conclusion: 该研究为具有长程相关性和乘法噪声的复杂扩散系统提供了路径积分框架，揭示了乘法扩散与空间约束相互作用产生有效漂移的机制，为分析异质非马尔可夫扩散过程建立了理论基础。

Abstract: Many complex systems are described by Langevin-type equations in which the noise exhibits long-range correlations and couples to the system in a state-dependent, multiplicative manner, leading to heterogeneous non-Markovian diffusion. Here, we investigate the problem of diffusion driven by fractional Gaussian noise with a general multiplicative coefficient from a path-integral perspective. Using a stationary-phase approximation, we derive a Gaussian propagator expressed in terms of the Lamperti transform of the process. In the additive limit, our results recover the path-integral representation of fractional Brownian motion based on its Riemann-Liouville formulation and establish its equivalence with the Langevin construction. We further analyze the effect of subordinating the process to a killing rate within the Feynman-Kac framework, and develop a general procedure to derive kinetic equations in terms of effective local Hamiltonians. We show that the interplay between multiplicative diffusion and confinement induces an effective drift term, leading to probability accumulation in regions of low noise amplitude.

</details>


### [226] [Spectral Softening and the Structural Breakdown of Thermodynamic Equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10216)
*Ilki Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究表明，在驱动二次哈密顿系统（driven quadratic Hamiltonian systems）中，当软模频率（soft-mode frequency）崩溃时，即使驱动速度任意缓慢，热力学可逆性也会失效，因为平衡系综（equilibrium ensembles）变得无法定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热力学预测在足够缓慢的驱动下，系统会通过一系列平衡态（equilibrium states）实现可逆演化。本研究旨在探究这一预期在特定条件下是否成立，特别是在谱简并（spectral degeneracy）附近的二次哈密顿系统中。

Method: 通过分析驱动二次哈密顿系统，研究软模频率崩溃时的动力学行为。采用维格纳相空间表示（Wigner phase-space representation）及其经典对应进行分析，揭示哈密顿相空间几何（Hamiltonian phase-space geometry）的奇异结构。

Result: 当软模频率低于与驱动相关的有限阈值时，绝热跟随（adiabatic following）失效，导致时间尺度分离（timescale separation）崩溃。正则配分函数（canonical partition function）发散，使平衡系综无法定义，从而破坏准静态热力学过程的基础。

Conclusion: 热力学可逆性（thermodynamic reversibility）在谱软化（spectral softening）移除固有频率尺度时受到根本性约束，这种限制源于哈密顿相空间几何结构，而非量子效应特有。

Abstract: Under sufficiently slow driving, thermodynamics predicts reversible evolution through a sequence of equilibrium states. We show that this expectation fails near spectral degeneracy in driven quadratic Hamiltonian systems. As the soft-mode frequency collapses, the intrinsic dynamical timescale diverges and quadratic confinement is lost, leading to a breakdown of timescale separation and the failure of adiabatic following even under arbitrarily slow driving. More precisely, adiabaticity is lost once the soft-mode frequency falls below a finite, drive-dependent threshold, implying that the breakdown extends over a finite regime rather than being confined to a singular limit. Crucially, this dynamical instability is accompanied by a divergence of the canonical partition function, rendering equilibrium ensembles ill-defined and eliminating the foundation of quasistatic thermodynamic processes. This breakdown does not arise from unbounded Hamiltonians or critical slowing down, but emerges structurally from spectral softening within a bounded quadratic system. Analysis of the Wigner phase-space representation, together with its classical counterpart, reveals the same singular structure, demonstrating that this limitation is not uniquely quantum but originates from the underlying Hamiltonian phase-space geometry. These results show that thermodynamic reversibility is fundamentally constrained, as a direct consequence of the breakdown of equilibrium, whenever spectral softening removes an intrinsic frequency scale.

</details>


### [227] [Algorithmic overlaps as thermodynamic variables: from local to cluster Monte Carlo dynamics in critical phenomena](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10254)
*Ian Pilé,Youjin Deng,Lev Shchur*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov chain Monte Carlo）模拟中连续自旋构型的空间重叠，比较了局部Metropolis算法与Swendsen-Wang和Wolff团簇算法在不同普适性类模型中的动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究不同蒙特卡洛算法（局部Metropolis算法、Swendsen-Wang和Wolff团簇算法）在临界区域动力学行为的差异，特别关注连续构型空间重叠所反映的临界现象。

Method: 采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛模拟，比较三种算法：局部Metropolis算法、Swendsen-Wang团簇算法和Wolff团簇算法。研究对象包括两个不同普适性类模型：伊辛模型（Ising model）和三态波茨模型（Potts model with three components）。分析连续自旋构型的空间重叠作为算法动力学的探针。

Result: Wolff算法中连续团簇的重叠表现出临界行为，可作为算法动力学的序参量（order parameter）。Swendsen-Wang算法中连续晶格构型重叠的变化也呈现类似序参量行为。Metropolis算法未观察到类似现象，其临界区域动力学由自旋翻转频率（等价于接受率）决定。这些几何量（构型重叠或其变化）与Fortuin-Kastelein团簇的临界行为自然相关。

Conclusion: Wolff团簇重叠和Swendsen-Wang构型重叠变化均能反映相变的热力学性质，与几何对象Fortuin-Kastelein团簇的临界行为密切相关。而Metropolis算法的动力学则由自旋翻转频率主导，不表现出类似的几何序参量行为。

Abstract: We investigate the spatial overlap of successive spin configurations in Markov chain Monte Carlo simulations using the local Metropolis algorithm and the Swendsen-Wang and Wolff cluster algorithms. We examine the dynamics of these algorithms for two models in different universality classes: the Ising model and the Potts model with three components. The overlap of two successive Wolff clusters reflects critical behavior and can be used as an order parameter for the algorithm's dynamics. In the case of the Swendsen-Wang algorithm, similar behavior is demonstrated by the variation in the overlap of two consecutive lattice configurations, which behaves like order parameter. Nothing similar is observed for the Metropolis algorithm, and the dynamics in the critical region are determined by the spin flip frequency, which is equivalent to the acceptance rate. Thus, the critical behavior of Wolff cluster overlap and the variation of configuration overlap in the Swendsen-Wang algorithm are naturally related to the critical behavior of geometric objects - Fortuin-Kastelein clusters. Interestingly, in all cases, the geometric quantity - configuration overlap or its variation - reflects the thermodynamics of the phase transition.

</details>


### [228] [Beyond Whittle: exact finite-time multispectral statistics from a single Brownian trajectory in a harmonic trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10323)
*Isaac Pérez Castillo,François Leyvraz,Miguel Eduardo Gómez Quintanar,Andrés Álvarez Ballesteros*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对单条有限时长轨迹的谱分析问题，发展了精确的有限时间多谱理论，用于描述过阻尼布朗粒子在谐振势中的功率谱密度估计器联合分布，并构建了考虑频率间相关性的谱似然层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验研究中通常只能获得单条有限时长记录，导致谱估计器分布广泛且频率间独立性假设失效。现有方法主要依赖系综平均和长时间渐近分析，无法准确处理有限时间观测窗口引起的频率间相关性。

Method: 针对过阻尼布朗粒子在谐振势中的模型，推导了有限时间估计器集合$\{S(ω_i,T)\}$的精确联合分布律。建立了协方差显式的高斯表示来描述相关傅里叶投影，使观测窗口引起的频率间相关性变得显式。

Result: 理论揭示了频率间相关性随$T\to\infty$逐渐消失，恢复了渐近Whittle图像。基于此结构构建了从因子化Whittle近似到频率空间块状协方差感知近似的谱似然层次结构。蒙特卡洛模拟验证了有限时间理论并量化了忽略频率间相关性对陷阱参数估计的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究为超越渐近区域的谱推断提供了受控的有限时间基准，使单轨迹谱分析能够更准确地处理观测窗口引起的频率间相关性，为有限时间实验数据的谱分析提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Power spectral densities are often interpreted through ensemble averages and long-time asymptotics. In many experiments, however, only a single finite record is available, so spectral estimators remain broadly distributed and the usual independence assumptions across frequencies need not hold. Here we develop an exact finite-$T$ multispectral theory for an overdamped Brownian particle in a harmonic trap. For a collection of frequencies $\{ω_i\}$, we obtain an exact characterization of the joint law of the finite-time estimators $\{S(ω_i,T)\}$, together with a covariance-explicit Gaussian representation for the associated Fourier projections. This representation makes the observation-window-induced inter-frequency correlations explicit and shows how they vanish as $T\to\infty$, thereby recovering the asymptotic Whittle picture. We then use this structure to formulate a hierarchy of spectral likelihoods for inference from a single trajectory, ranging from the factorized Whittle approximation to blockwise covariance-aware approximations in frequency space. Monte Carlo simulations validate the finite-time theory and quantify the effect of neglected cross-frequency correlations on single-trajectory estimates of the trap parameters. Our results provide a controlled finite-time benchmark for spectral inference beyond the asymptotic regime.

</details>


### [229] [Heat Conduction in Momentum-Conserving Fluids: From quasi-2D to 3D systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10536)
*Rongxiang Luo,Jiaqi Wen,Juncheng Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过非平衡与平衡分子动力学模拟，研究多粒子碰撞动力学模型中的热传导，在准二维到三维系统中识别出三种输运机制：弹道、动力学和流体动力学机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究动量守恒介观流体中的热传导行为，特别关注从准二维（quasi-two-dimensional, q-2D）到三维（3D）系统的维度交叉效应，为理解微纳尺度热输运提供基础。

Method: 采用非平衡（nonequilibrium）与平衡（equilibrium）分子动力学模拟，基于多粒子碰撞动力学（multiparticle collision dynamics）模型研究介观流体系统。

Result: 识别出三种输运机制：弹道机制（ballistic regime）中热导率与系统尺寸线性相关；动力学机制（kinetic regime）显示尺寸无关的热导率；流体动力学机制（hydrodynamic regime）中q-2D系统呈现对数发散热导率，而3D系统为有限值。

Conclusion: 研究结果定量验证了热输运的标度预测，揭示了从二维类反常输运到三维傅里叶行为的维度交叉，为微纳尺度热器件设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Using nonequilibrium and equilibrium molecular dynamics simulations, we investigate heat conduction in a momentum-conserving mesoscopic fluid modeled by multiparticle collision dynamics. Across quasi-two-dimensional (q-2D) to three-dimensional (3D) systems, we identify three distinct transport regimes: (i) a \emph{ballistic regime}, where thermal conductivity scales linearly with system size ($κ\sim L$) and the total heat current autocorrelation function $C(t)$ remains constant; (ii)~a \emph{kinetic regime}, characterized by size-independent $κ$ and exponentially decaying $C(t)$, demonstrating that normal heat conduction dominated by kinetic effects is far more ubiquitous than previously observed in 1D systems; and (iii)~a \emph{hydrodynamic regime}, where the q-2D system exhibits logarithmically divergent conductivity ($ κ\sim \ln L $ ) with $ C(t) \sim t^{-1} $ , while the 3D system displays finite $ κ$ and $ C(t) \sim t^{-3/2} $. Our results, observed in the hydrodynamic regime, quantitatively validate the scaling predictions for heat transport and reveal a clear dimensional crossover -- from 2D-like anomalous transport to 3D Fourier behavior. These results lay a foundation for understanding thermal transport in q-2D to 3D systems and have practical implications for the design of micro- and nanoscale thermal devices.

</details>


### [230] [Location of the liquid-vapor critical point in aluminum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10561)
*Xuyang Long,Kai Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合深度势能分子动力学与基于高保真电子结构数据的大规模模拟，首次精确确定了铝的液-汽临界点参数，解决了数十年来临界温度估计值相差近4000K的不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铝的液-汽临界点（liquid-vapor critical point）位置数十年来一直难以确定，已报道的临界温度估计值相差近4000K。这种不确定性限制了在极端条件下（如激光烧蚀、冲击压缩和行星建模）对铝相行为的准确预测。

Method: 研究结合了深度势能分子动力学（deep potential molecular dynamics）与基于高保真电子结构数据的大规模模拟。通过将多种交换关联泛函（exchange-correlation functionals）与实验液体密度进行基准测试，确定PBEsol泛函提供最一致的描述。采用互补方法：状态方程（equation of state）的旋节线分析（spinodal analysis）和具有高斯混合相识别（Gaussian mixture phase identification）的直接共存模拟（direct coexistence simulations）。

Result: 研究收敛于临界温度6531-6576K、临界密度0.637 g/cm³和临界压力1.6 kbar，温度不确定度约50K。这些值的精度相比先前估计有显著提升，代表了数量级的改进。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了可迁移的策略来预测金属中的临界现象，对激光烧蚀（laser ablation）、冲击压缩（shock compression）和极端条件下的行星建模具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: The precise location of the liquid-vapor critical point (CP) in aluminum has remained elusive for decades, with reported critical temperatures spanning nearly 4000~K. Here we resolve this long-standing uncertainty by combining deep potential molecular dynamics with large-scale simulations trained on high-fidelity electronic-structure data. We benchmark multiple exchange-correlation functionals against experimental liquid densities and identify PBEsol as providing the most consistent description. Using complementary approaches -- spinodal analysis of the equation of state and direct coexistence simulations with Gaussian mixture phase identification -- we converge on a critical temperature of $6531$-$6576$~K, a critical density of $0.637$~g/cm$^{3}$, and a critical pressure of $1.6$~kbar. The precision of these values, with uncertainties of $\sim$50~K in temperature, represents a step change over previous estimates. Our framework establishes a transferable strategy for predicting critical phenomena in metals, with implications for laser ablation, shock compression, and planetary modeling under extreme conditions.

</details>

Result: 朗道分布在相同精度标准下，能匹配全球93%地点的极端降水，显著优于传统极值分布的76%匹配率。将历史回归时间映射到耦合模式比较计划第六阶段（CMIP6）的未来预测，发现不同排放情景下的回归时间曲线收敛到统一关系，揭示21世纪出生人群在大多数未来排放情景下面临的极端降水终身暴露风险急剧增加。

Conclusion: 朗道分布为极端降水统计提供了更准确的描述，基于此的大偏差框架能够预测超出历史观测强度的极端事件。研究揭示了不同排放情景下回归时间曲线的统一关系，表明21世纪出生人群将面临显著增加的极端降水风险，为气候风险评估提供了重要依据。

Abstract: Forecasting extreme precipitation is essential yet challenging due to its rarity and complexity. We develop a large deviation framework to estimate the return times of extreme precipitation events. We first find that the Landau distribution, originally introduced in plasma physics, accurately captures extreme precipitation at approximately 93% of global locations, outperforming conventional extreme value distributions with 76% matched locations under the same accuracy criterion. Enriching rare event samples by the fitted Landau distribution, we obtain more accurate estimates of large deviation rate functions and return times, enabling forecasts beyond historically observed precipitation intensities. Mapping historical return times to future projections from the Coupled Model Intercomparison Project Phase 6 (CMIP6), we show that return time curves under different emission scenarios collapse onto a unified relation, revealing a sharply increased lifetime exposure to extreme precipitation for 21st-century birth cohorts under most future emission scenarios.

### [232] [Dynamical Regimes of Discrete Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10961)
*Tomoei Takahashi,Takashi Takahashi,Yoshiyuki Kabashima*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管连续扩散模型的反向动力学（backward dynamics）已建立理论分析框架，但离散扩散模型（discrete diffusion models）尚未应用相同的理论标准。本研究旨在验证连续数据的理论框架是否适用于离散数据。

Method: 提出一个简单的有效模型（effective model）用于分析两类伊辛变量数据（two-class Ising variable data）的离散扩散模型，采用统计力学（statistical mechanics）方法分析其反向动力学，包括高温展开（high-temperature expansion）和随机能量模型（Random Energy Model）。

Result: 研究表明物种形成相变可通过二阶相变（second-order phase transition）分析确定，而塌缩相变对应随机能量模型描述的凝聚相变（condensation transition）。获得了物种形成时间的解析表达式，并证明其标度行为与实际扩散模型一致。

Conclusion: 连续数据的原始理论框架对离散数据仍然有效，这为在更现实场景下分析离散生成扩散的统计力学提供了有用的起点。

Abstract: Diffusion models generate high-dimensional data such as images by learning a process that gradually removes noise from corrupted data. Recent studies have shown that the backward dynamics of diffusion models exhibit two characteristic transitions: the speciation transition, at which generated samples begin to capture the global structure of the training data, and the collapse transition, at which the generation dynamics starts committing to individual training samples. While these transitions have been theoretically analyzed for continuous data, the same theoretical criteria have not been applied for discrete diffusion models, which are diffusion models for discrete data. In this work, we propose a simple effective model for discrete diffusion models trained on two-class Ising variable data with a general mixture ratio and analyze its backward dynamics using methods from statistical mechanics. We show that, as in the previous study on continuous data, the speciation transition can be determined through a second-order phase transition analysis using high-temperature expansion, while the collapse transition corresponds to a condensation transition described by the Random Energy Model. An analytical expression for the speciation time is obtained, and we show that its scaling becomes consistent with that of the continuous case when the noise increases with time as in practical diffusion models. These theoretical predictions are confirmed by numerical simulations and experiments with trained discrete diffusion models on real datasets. These results suggest that the original theoretical framework for continuous data remain valid for discrete data, and may provide a useful starting point for the statistical-mechanics analysis of discrete generative diffusion in more realistic settings.

Method: 通过局部约束（local constraints）实现疤痕子空间内的代数闭包（algebraic closure），构建$\mathfrak{su}(3)$不变疤痕子空间。该方法不依赖于单个本征态的精确可解性。

Result: 疤痕子空间的能谱不再等间距，而是形成由多个独立量子数参数化的多向晶格结构（multidirectional lattice structure）。动力学上表现出由不同能量尺度的整数线性组合控制的多频率振荡（multifrequency oscillations）。

Conclusion: 代数闭包是超越传统$\mathfrak{su}(2)$范式的疤痕子空间的统一机制，能够在不可解参考态上实现量子多体疤痕，为非可积量子系统中更丰富的非热动力学开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We construct a class of quantum many-body systems hosting an $\mathfrak{su}(3)$-invariant scar subspace, extending the conventional paradigm of quantum many-body scars beyond equally spaced spectra and single-directional tower structures. Our construction is based on local constraints that realize an algebraic closure within the scar subspace. As a result, the spectrum in the subspace is no longer equally spaced, but instead forms a multidirectional lattice structure parametrized by multiple independent quantum numbers. This leads to qualitatively new dynamical signatures: instead of single-frequency revivals, the system exhibits multifrequency oscillations governed by integer linear combinations of distinct energy scales. Importantly, the stability of the scar subspace does not rely on exact solvability of individual eigenstates. We show that algebraic closure preserves the invariant subspace even under perturbations that render the eigenstates analytically intractable, thereby realizing quantum many-body scars on an unsolvable reference state. Our results identify algebraic closure as a unifying mechanism underlying scar subspaces beyond the conventional $\mathfrak{su}(2)$ paradigm, and open a route toward richer nonthermal dynamics in nonintegrable quantum systems.

In TNPA, TN contractions are used only within a reliable temperature range to generate initial configurations that are close to the equilibrium distribution. The subsequent low-temperature equilibration is then carried out by PA. To stabilize the initialization process, we introduce a diagnostic based on the effective sample size that adaptively selects the initialization temperature. The proposed framework provides a practical and physically motivated route to low-temperature sampling by combining the complementary strengths of TN and PA.

### [235] [Sluggish quantum mechanics of noninteracting fermions with spatially varying effective mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11173)
*Giuseppe Del Vecchio Del Vecchio,Manas Kulkarni,Satya N. Majumdar,Sanjib Sabhapandit*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究一类具有位置依赖动能项的一维量子系统，称为"迟缓量子力学（sluggish quantum mechanics）"，其中有效质量随距离幂律增长，导致粒子运动在远离原点时被抑制。作者精确求解了无外势和谐势阱中的本征函数与量子传播子，并分析了N个无相互作用费米子的多体基态性质，发现原点附近的标度化核函数具有新的数学结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文动机源于研究具有空间变化跃迁幅度的非均匀紧束缚模型的连续极限，这类系统在位置依赖隧穿的光学晶格工程中具有潜在应用价值。作者旨在探索有效质量随距离幂律增长（$m_{eff}(x) = m_{eff}|x|^α$）的量子系统的精确可解性及其多体物理特性。

Method: 采用从非均匀紧束缚模型出发的连续极限方法，得到具有位置依赖动能项的薛定谔方程（BenDaniel-Duke形式）。通过精确求解无外势和谐势阱（$V_{ext}(x)=\frac{1}{2}m_{eff}ω^2 |x|^{α+2}$）情况下的本征函数和量子传播子，进而分析N个无相互作用自旋less费米子的多体基态波函数和位置联合概率密度函数。

Result: 研究发现多体基态量子概率密度形成行列式点过程（determinantal point process），其关联核函数可对任意N精确计算，从而获得平均密度和高阶关联函数。在大N极限下，关联核函数在体区、边缘区和原点附近呈现不同的标度形式，其中原点附近的标度化核函数既非标准的贝塞尔核（Bessel kernel）也非艾里核（Airy kernel），而是由两个不同指标的贝塞尔核之和构成的新核函数。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个适用于具有位置依赖隧穿的光学晶格工程的理论框架，揭示了迟缓量子力学系统中多体费米子统计的新奇标度行为。特别地，原点附近关联核函数的新数学结构为理解非均匀量子系统中的多体关联提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We analyze a class of one-dimensional quantum systems characterized by a position-dependent kinetic term arising as the continuum limit of an inhomogeneous tight-binding model with spatially varying hopping amplitudes. In this limit, the Schrodinger equation takes the so-called BenDaniel-Duke form with an effective mass, scaling as $m_{eff}(x) = m_{eff}|x|^α$ with $α> 0$, leading to a framework we term sluggish quantum mechanics, where particle motion is progressively suppressed at larger distances. Both without any external potential and with $V_{ext}(x)=\frac{1}{2}m_{eff}ω^2 |x|^{α+2}$, we obtain the eigenfunctions and the quantum propagators exactly. We then investigate the problem of $N$ noninteracting spinless fermions in the trap, determining the many-body ground-state wavefunction and the joint probability density function of the positions of the $N$ fermions. We show that the many-body quantum probability density in the ground state forms a determinantal point process whose correlation kernel can be computed for any $N$, giving access to the average density as well as higher order correlation functions for any finite $N$. Moreover, we analyze the scaling form of this kernel in the large $N$ limit in the bulk, near the edge, and close to the origin. Our results show that the scaled average density profile for large $N$ has a finite support symmetric with respect to the origin, but has a non-monotonic shape with a vanishing minimum at the origin for any $α>0$. One of the key findings of our work is that the scaled kernel near the origin $x=0$ for $α>0$ is neither the Bessel nor the Airy kernel (that are standard for trapped fermions), but is new, and is given by a sum of two Bessel kernels with different indices. Our results thus provide a framework relevant to engineered optical lattices with position-dependent tunneling.

### [236] [Absence of thermalization after a local quench and strong violation of the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11392)
*Peter Reimann,Christian Eidecker-Dunkel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究证明局域量子淬火（local quantum quench）可导致热化缺失，并伴随本征态热化假设（ETH）的强烈违反，即使在满足弱化版本ETH的系统中也是如此。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然可积多体系统中全局量子淬火（global quantum quench）后的热化缺失已被广泛观察，并与本征态热化假设（eigenstate thermalization hypothesis, ETH）违反相关，但许多此类系统仍满足弱化版本ETH。本研究旨在探究局域淬火是否也能导致热化缺失。

Method: 研究采用解析与数值相结合的方法：解析分析聚焦于开放边界条件下的XX自旋链模型（XX-spin-chain models），其中局域淬火通过系统从热平衡态开始，然后突然开启（或微调）链末端或中心处的单自旋杂质（single-spin impurity）实现。数值研究则扩展到更一般的XXZ模型（XXZ-models）。

Result: 解析与数值结果均表明，局域淬火可导致热化缺失，并伴随ETH的强烈违反——即使弱化版本ETH（wETH）也不再满足。对于末端杂质，在更一般的XXZ模型中观察到类似现象；但对于中心杂质，该现象仅出现在XX模型中。

Conclusion: 局域量子淬火足以导致热化缺失和ETH的强烈违反，这扩展了传统上仅与全局淬火相关的非热化行为理解，揭示了局域扰动在破坏热化机制中的关键作用。

Abstract: Absence of thermalization after a global quantum quench is a well-established numerical observation in integrable many-body systems, and can be empirically related to a violation of the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH) in such models. Still, in many of those examples a weaker version of the conventional ETH (wETH) has been numerically reported or even rigorously proven. In this paper we show analytically and illustrate numerically that the absence of thermalization is already possible after a local quench. A closely related finding is a strong violation of the ETH, meaning that not even the wETH is fulfilled anymore. In our analytical explorations we focus on XX-spin-chain models with open boundary conditions, where the local quench is generated by initiating the system in thermal equilibrium and then suddenly switching on (or slightly changing) a single-spin impurity either at the end or in the center of the chain. Numerically we observe qualitatively similar phenomena also for more general XXZ-models in the case of an end-impurity, but not in the case of a central impurity.

### [237] [Exact Criterion for Ground-State Overlap Dominance after Quantum Quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11420)
*Taisanul Haque*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究精确解决了平移不变自由费米子系统中的淬火问题，证明了在相同物理相区内淬火时，末态基态具有最大重叠的猜想对大多数系统成立，但在Kitaev链中存在反例，且该机制会导致不跨越相边界的动力学量子相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前在TIFM模型中提出并验证了一个猜想：在相同物理相区内进行突然淬火时，初态基态与末态本征态的重叠在末态基态处达到最大。本研究旨在精确解决这一普遍性问题。

Method: 研究精确求解了一大类平移不变自由费米子系统。对于可分解为独立2×2扇区的哈密顿量，建立了精确判据：当且仅当初态和末态扇区布洛赫矢量具有正点积时，末态基态才唯一具有最大重叠。

Result: 该精确判据证明了猜想对大多数系统成立，但也揭示了其普遍性不成立：在Kitaev链中，存在相同相区淬火时末态基态不是最大重叠态的情况。同一机制还导致了直接的动力学后果。

Conclusion: 相同相区淬火可以在不跨越物理相边界的情况下产生动力学量子相变（DQPTs），这挑战了关于淬火动力学与相边界关系的传统理解。

Abstract: Recently, conjectured and verified in TIFM model that for a sudden quench within the same physical phase region, the overlap of the initial ground state with the final eigenstates is maximal for the final ground state. We solve this problem exactly for a broad class of translationally invariant free-fermion systems. For Hamiltonians that factorize into independent $2\times2$ sectors, the final ground state is uniquely maximal if and only if the initial and final sector Bloch vectors have positive dot product. This exact criterion proves the conjecture for large classes, but also shows that it is false in general: in Kitaev chains there are same-phase quenches for which the final ground state is not the maximal-overlap state. The same mechanism has a direct dynamical consequence, implying that same-phase quenches can generate DQPTs without crossing an physical phase boundary.

### [238] [Optimization of cooling power of a thermoelectric refrigerator: A unified approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11441)

Motivation: 研究旨在统一热电器冷却功率优化的内可逆（endoreversible）和外可逆（exoreversible）近似框架，解决基于牛顿传热定律的内可逆模型中冷却功率不可优化的问题，为实际热电器性能提供更现实的估计。

Method: 采用稳态形式主义（steady-state formalism）分析热电器冷却功率优化，在近可逆区域（near-reversible regime）研究外部热导（external thermal conductances）大但有限的情况。将分析扩展到同时存在内部和外部不可逆性（internal and external irreversibilities）的情况。

Result: 推导出性能系数（coefficient of performance, COP）的闭式表达式，该表达式依赖于热电优值（thermoelectric figure of merit）和内部与外部热导之比。该模型将内可逆和外可逆极限作为特例重现。对于小温差情况，组合不可逆性将COP降低到1/2以下。

Conclusion: 该统一框架能够提供热电器性能系数的现实估计，其预测值与单级热电器（single-stage TER）的观测性能相符，特别是在小温差条件下，组合不可逆性导致COP降至1/2以下。

Abstract: We analyze the steady-state formalism for optimizing the cooling power of a thermoelectric refrigerator (TER), unifying the endoreversible and exoreversible approximations within one framework. Although the cooling power is non-optimizable within the endoreversible model based on Newtonian heat-transfer law, we show that the issue can be circumvented in the near-reversible regime where the external thermal conductances are large, but finite. We extend this analysis to optimize the cooling power in the presence of both internal and external irreversibilities and derive a closed-form expression for the coefficient of performance (COP) that depends on the thermoelectric figure of merit and the ratio of internal to external thermal conductances. The model reproduces the endoreversible and the exoreversible limits as special cases. We conclude that for small temperature differences, the combined irreversibilities reduce the COP to values below 1/2, which aligns with the observed performance of the single-stage TER, and can provide realistic estimates for the COP.

</details>


### [239] [Inverse engineering of cooling protocols: from normal behavior to Mpemba effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11486)
*Hartmut Löwen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了如何逆向设计外部温度协议$T_\text{ext}(t)$以实现预设的内部冷却曲线$T_\text{int}(t)$，而非传统的正向冷却分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究关注给定外部温度协议$T_\text{ext}(t)$对系统冷却行为$T_\text{int}(t)$的影响，本文考虑逆向问题：对于给定的系统冷却曲线$T_\text{int}(t)$，如何设计合适的外部温度协议$T_\text{ext}(t)$来实现预设的冷却行为。

Method: 使用现象学的牛顿冷却定律（Newtonian equation for cooling）和微观模型，包括离散两能级系统（discrete two-level system）和含时噪声的布朗谐振子（Brownian harmonic oscillator with time-dependent noise），解析计算实现预设$T_\text{int}(t)$所需的$T_\text{ext}(t)$协议。

Result: 研究表明逆向设计的协议并不总是存在，且可能具有非唯一性（non-unique）。研究还探讨了包含异常姆潘巴效应（anomalous Mpemba effects）、过冷（overcooling）、冷却与加热不对称性以及延迟现象的现象学推广牛顿定律。

Conclusion: 该研究结果为通过时变外部热源（time-varying external heat sources）系统性地调控冷却行为提供了重要理论基础，揭示了逆向冷却协议设计的基本限制和特性。

Abstract: When a cup of hot coffee is suddenly put into a cold environment, it cools down as a function of time $t$ until the internal temperature $T_\text{int}$ of the coffee equals the external ambient temperature $T_\text{ext}$. This instantaneous shock-freezing corresponds to an imposed cooling protocol of the external temperature $T_\text{ext}(t)$, ideally described as a step-function in time, causing the time-dependent change of the internal temperature $T_\text{int}(t)$. While the effect of different given protocols $T_\text{ext}(t)$ on the resulting system cooling behaviour, embodied in $T_\text{int}(t)$, has been studied extensively, we consider here the inverse question: for a given system cooling $T_\text{int}(t)$ how can an appropriate protocol $T_\text{ext}(t)$ be engineered to produce the desired prescribed $T_\text{int}(t)$. We use both the phenomenological Newtonian equation for cooling and microscopic models, such as a discrete two-level system and a Brownian harmonic oscillator with time-dependent noise, to compute analytically the protocol $T_\text{ext}(t)$ needed to achieve a prescribed $T_\text{int}(t)$. We then discuss the same question for phenomenological generalizations of the Newtonian law which include anomalous Mpemba effects, overcooling, asymmetries in cooling and heating as well as delay phenomena. It is shown that backward-engineered protocols do not always exist and can be non-unique. The results are important for steering the cooling behavior by time-varying external heat sources in a systematic way.

</details>


### [240] [The Widom line in the Ising model on a decorated bilayer lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11606)
*Joseph Chapman,Justas Gidziunas,Bruno Tomasello,Sam Carr*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期对一类展现尖锐热力学行为的一维受挫统计力学晶格模型产生了浓厚兴趣。本研究旨在将其中一种模型扩展到二维，探索其在装饰双层晶格上的行为。

Method: 研究采用二维装饰双层晶格上的伊辛模型（Ising model on a decorated bilayer lattice），作为先前研究的一维受挫统计力学模型的扩展。

Result: 研究发现一维模型的伪相变（pseudo-transitions）在二维类似物中转变为真实的一阶相变（first order phase transition）。此外，伪相变在双临界点（bi-critical point）以上仍然存在，可表征为Widom线。

Conclusion: 该研究通过二维扩展重新诠释了先前研究的一维模型的物理本质，揭示了伪相变与真实相变之间的深刻联系，为理解受挫系统的相变行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: There has been much recent interest devoted to a class of frustrated one-dimensional statistical mechanics lattice models which exhibit sharp thermodynamics. In this work, we study an extension of one of these models to two dimensions; the Ising model on a decorated bilayer lattice. We show that the pseudo-transitions of the one-dimensional models become a real first order phase transition in this two-dimensional analogue. Moreover, the pseudo-transition is found to still exist above a bi-critical point. This can be characterised as a Widom line, which allows a re-interpretation of the physics in the previously studied one-dimensional models.
