### [241] [Thermodynamic fluctuations in freely jointed chains under force](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11713)
*Michael R. Buche,Alvin Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了自由连接链（freely jointed chain）模型中的热力学涨落（thermodynamic fluctuations），量化了链延伸各分量的概率密度和标准差，揭示了在施加力较小时涨落显著，而增加链节数可降低除连接角外的所有量涨落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单链模型研究通常将统计力学关系视为确定性值而非具有内在不确定性的系综平均值（ensemble averages）。这种处理忽略了热力学涨落的重要性，需要对其进行理解和量化。

Method: 研究在自由连接链模型中考察热力学涨落，分析不同链节数和施加力下链延伸的纵向、横向、径向分量以及延伸角和连接角的概率密度与标准差。方法上尽可能采用解析求解，否则使用数值方法。

Result: 结果显示，在施加力较小时，所有量的涨落都相当显著。增加链节数逐渐降低除连接角外的所有量涨落，因为连接角在等张力系综（isotensional ensemble）中相互独立。当施加力变大时，涨落减小。

Conclusion: 这些结果为单聚合物链拉伸或整个聚合物网络变形建模提供了直观警示，强调需要考虑热力学涨落而非将系综平均值视为确定性值。

Abstract: It is common to study polymer physics through the use of idealized single-chain models, and the most popular of these is the freely jointed chain model. In certain thermodynamic ensembles, statistical mechanical treatment of this model is analytically tractable or sometimes exactly solvable. This enables useful relations to be ascertained, like the expected chain end-to-end length as a function of an applied force. However, most of these relations return ensemble averages, which are values with inherent uncertainty, as opposed to deterministic values with no variance. This is an important distinction to understand and quantify, because the majority of studies to date involving single-chain models effectively treat these values as deterministic rather than fluctuating. To address this issue, thermodynamic fluctuations are examined in the freely jointed chain model. Specifically, the probability densities and standard deviations of the longitudinal, lateral, transverse, and radial portions of the chain extension, as well as the extension and link angles, are examined for different numbers of links and applied forces. Fluctuations in these quantities are shown to be considerable until the applied force becomes large. Increasing the number of links in the chain gradually reduces fluctuations in all quantities except for the link angles, since they are independent for freely jointed chains in the isotensional ensemble. Quantities are obtained analytically whenever possible and numerically otherwise. Overall, these results provide intuitive admonitions to consider when modeling the stretching of single polymer chains or the deformation of entire polymer networks.

</details>


### [242] [Diffusing diffusivity model with dichotomous noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11800)
*Dongho Lee,Jae-Hyung Jeon,Pascal Viot,Gleb Oshanin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了由周围介质涨落引起的随机扩散率（stochastic diffusivity）的朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）。扩散率被建模为由对称二值噪声（symmetric dichotomous noise）驱动的奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克过程（Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process），将其限制在有限区间内。研究推导了粒子位移的短时概率密度函数（PDF）的解析表达式，并分析了其渐近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解在具有涨落介质的环境中随机输运（stochastic transport）的动力学行为。具体而言，关注由周围介质波动引起的随机扩散率如何影响粒子运动，这为分析有界或切换涨落（bounded or switching fluctuations）环境中的输运现象提供了一个最小化的分析框架。

Method: 研究方法采用朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）与随机扩散率相结合。扩散率被建模为由对称二值噪声（symmetric dichotomous noise）驱动的奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克过程（Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process），该过程将扩散率限制在有限区间内。通过推导粒子位移的短时概率密度函数（PDF）的解析表达式，并分析其渐近行为来研究系统特性。

Result: 研究结果显示，概率密度函数（PDF）在原点处保留了特征性的对数发散（logarithmic divergence）。然而，其尾部行为与高斯白噪声（Gaussian white-noise）情况不同：指数尾部被高斯尾部取代，并由具有切换率依赖指数（switching-rate-dependent exponent）的幂律调制。在长时间尺度上，动力学收敛于普通高斯扩散（ordinary Gaussian diffusion）。此外，确定了时间平均随机扩散率的方差和协方差，并证明其具有自平均性（self-averaging）。

Conclusion: 该模型为分析有界或切换涨落（bounded or switching fluctuations）环境中的随机输运（stochastic transport）提供了一个最小化且可解析处理（analytically tractable）的框架。研究揭示了随机扩散率如何改变粒子位移分布的特性，特别是在短时尺度上产生非高斯尾部行为，而在长时间尺度上恢复标准扩散行为。

Abstract: We study Langevin dynamics with stochastic diffusivity arising from fluctuations of the surrounding medium. The diffusivity is modeled as Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process driven by symmetric dichotomous noise, which confines it to a finite interval. We derive analytical expressions for the short-time probability density function (PDF) of the particle displacement and analyse its asymptotic behaviour. While the PDF retains the characteristic logarithmic divergence at the origin, its tails differ from the Gaussian white-noise case: exponential tails are replaced by Gaussian ones modulated by a power-law with a switching-rate-dependent exponent. At long times, the dynamics converges to ordinary Gaussian diffusion. We determine the variance and covariance of the time-averaged stochastic diffusivity and show that it is self-averaging. The model provides a minimal analytically tractable framework for stochastic transport in environments with bounded or switching fluctuations.

</details>

### [243] [Analysis of Log-Weighted Quadrature Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10394)
*Andrew Graven*

Main category: math.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究满足关于奇异权重ρ₀(w)=|w|⁻²的求积恒等式的平面区域，称为对数加权求积域（LQDs）。对数奇异性导致经典理论中不存在的现象，特别是当区域包含原点时，相关求积数据不再唯一。建立了LQDs的广义Schwarz函数表征，并在奇异背景下自然表述了逆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文动机在于研究具有对数奇异权重ρ₀(w)=|w|⁻²的求积域，这类奇异权重导致经典求积域理论中不存在的现象。特别关注当区域包含原点时，求积数据不再唯一而仅由原点处的点电荷确定的特殊情况。

Method: 方法包括建立对数加权求积域（LQDs）的广义Schwarz函数表征，并在奇异背景下自然表述逆问题。在单连通情况下，证明区域是LQD当且仅当其Riemann映射的外因子可延拓为有理函数的指数。该表征通过Faber变换给出了求积函数与Riemann映射之间的显式公式。

Result: 结果表明，对数奇异性导致经典理论中不存在的现象：当区域包含原点时，相关求积数据不再唯一，而是仅由原点处的点电荷确定。建立了LQDs的广义Schwarz函数表征，并给出了求积函数与Riemann映射之间通过Faber变换的显式公式，扩展了非奇异理论中的早期公式。

Conclusion: 本文建立了对数加权求积域（LQDs）的理论框架，涵盖奇异权重导致的独特现象。通过广义Schwarz函数表征和Riemann映射外因子的有理函数指数表示，提供了LQDs的完整描述。研究还覆盖了LQDs的几个基本类别，并计算了具体示例。

Abstract: This paper studies plane domains satisfying a quadrature identity with respect to the singular weight $ρ_0(w)=|w|^{-2}$. These are referred to as log-weighted quadrature domains (LQDs). The logarithmic singularity at $w=0$ leads to phenomena not present in the classical theory: in particular, when the domain contains the origin, the associated quadrature data are no longer unique, but are determined only up to a point charge at $0$. A generalized Schwarz function characterization of LQDs is established together with a natural formulation of the inverse problem in the singular setting. In the simply connected case, it is shown that a domain is an LQD if and only if the outer factor of its Riemann map extends to the exponential of a rational function. This characterization yields explicit formulae relating the quadrature function and the Riemann map via the Faber transform, thereby extending earlier formulae from the non-singular theory. Several basic classes of LQDs are also covered, and explicit examples are computed.

</details>

### [244] [Gas-rich ultra-diffuse galaxies: alleviating the MOND tension with HMG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09652)
*Robert Monjo*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究重新评估了六颗孤立富气超弥散星系（UDGs）在超锥修正引力（HMG）模型下的旋转速度，发现HMG虽能缓解MOND的困难，但仍无法完全解释观测数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 富气超弥散星系（gas-rich UDGs）为与重子Tully-Fisher关系相关的引力模型提供了独特测试，因为多个系统显示其旋转速度相对于重子质量过慢。本研究旨在检验超锥修正引力（hyperconical modified gravity, HMG）模型是否能解释这些异常观测。

Method: 采用Mancera Piña等人分析的六颗孤立富气UDGs数据，使用当前外半径处HMG模型，基于已发表的重子质量和外半径处的圆周速度进行扫描分析。通过邻域尺度参数扫描驱动模型趋向HMG的渐近分支。

Result: 在渐近分支极限下，HMG预测的速度仍系统性地高于六颗星系中的四颗观测值。固定渐近分支给出χ²≈18.1，牛顿重子模型为χ²≈9.7，而MOND插值表现最差（χ²≈615.7）。使用组合不确定性时，每颗星系的HMG张力范围为0.2σ至2.1σ，与牛顿模型的0.1σ至1.7σ相似，远小于MOND的3.7σ至5.9σ。

Conclusion: 当前外半径HMG实现虽能缓解MOND的困难，但仍不足以解释UDG样本的已发表中心值。富气超弥散星系因此为区分MOND和HMG提供了有效的判别依据。

Abstract: Gas-rich ultra-diffuse galaxies (UDGs) are an unusually sharp test for gravity models tied to the baryonic Tully--Fisher relation because several systems appear to rotate too slowly for their baryonic masses. This study revisits the six isolated gas-rich UDGs analysed by Mancera Piña et al. with the current outer-radius prescription of hyperconical modified gravity (HMG), using the published baryonic masses and circular velocities at the outer radii. The scan over the neighbourhood-scale parameter drives the model towards the asymptotic branch of HMG. For that limit, the HMG velocities are still systematically high for four of the six galaxies. Relative to the observed values, the fixed asymptotic branch gives $χ^2\simeq18.1$ for six objects, whereas Newtonian baryons alone give $χ^2\simeq9.7$, but MOND interpolation is much worse ($χ^2\simeq 615.7$). Using combined uncertainties, the per-galaxy HMG tension ranges from $0.2σ$ to $2.1σ$, very similar to the $0.1σ$ to $1.7σ$ found for Newtonian baryons, and much smaller than the $3.7σ$ to $5.9σ$ obtained for MOND. We conclude that the present outer-radius HMG implementation alleviates the difficulties of MOND, but is still not sufficient to account for the published central values of the UDG sample. Gas-rich UDGs therefore provide a useful discriminant between MOND and HMG.

Method: 从最小耦合哈密顿量出发，将吸收表达为电磁矢势与非局域电流响应的双线性泛函，将二色性信号识别为非局域响应核的螺旋度奇投影，并将响应分解为对称性、张量和模式空间三个部分。

Abstract: We develop a microscopic theory of optical absorption and structured-light dichroism in a nonlocal minimal-coupling framework. Starting from the minimal-coupling Hamiltonian, we express absorption as a bilinear functional of the electromagnetic vector potential and the nonlocal current response, providing a general description of light--matter coupling in optical vortex beams and other inhomogeneous fields. Dichroic signals are identified as helicity-odd projections of the nonlocal response kernel, and the response is resolved into symmetry, tensorial, and mode-space sectors. For single helical modes, the theory yields diagonal OAM-resolved contributions together with the corresponding selection rules and symmetry constraints. For mixed modes, interference between distinct OAM components provides access to off-diagonal coherence of the nonlocal kernel, with a tensor structure determined by the polarization composition of the field. The theory also clarifies how local structures associated with symmetric spatial dispersion, optical chirality, and tensorial anisotropy emerge as gradient-level manifestations of the underlying nonlocal response.

### [246] [Magnetic switching of self-hybridized exciton-polaritons in CrSBr photonic crystal slabs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11750)
*T. D. Gorelkina,I. E. Kalantaevskii,A. N. Abramov,K. A. Gasnikova,P. A. Alekseev,X. Zeng,D. Huang,T. Jiang,I. V. Iorsh,I. Y. Chestnov,V. Kravtsov*

TL;DR: 该研究展示了在CrSBr范德华反铁磁体中，通过中等面内磁场实现激子极化激元传播方向的磁控反转，为主动集成光子器件提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状范德华反铁磁体CrSBr支持强光-物质耦合和磁可调谐激子极化激元（exciton-polaritons）的形成，但对其传播方向的主动磁控制仍具挑战性。本研究旨在探索通过磁场调控极化激元传输的可能性。

Method: 研究采用从CrSBr薄片制备的光子晶体平板（photonic crystal slabs），利用角分辨反射和光致发光光谱（angle-resolved reflectance and photoluminescence spectroscopy）结合建模分析，考察了中等面内磁场诱导的反铁磁-铁磁自旋翻转转变（antiferromagnetic-to-ferromagnetic spin-flip transition）过程中自杂化激子极化激元的演化。

Result: 极化激元能量连续跟踪逐层磁化切换过程，揭示了临界场附近振荡器强度（oscillator strength）从反铁磁激子到铁磁激子的逐渐重新分布。最显著的是，仅需40 mT的外部磁场微小变化即可反转极化激元群速度（polariton group velocity）的符号，实现极化激元传播方向的完全切换。

Conclusion: CrSBr光子晶体平板可作为磁控极化激元传输的平台，为主动集成光子和极化激元器件（integrated photonic and polaritonic devices）开辟了新机遇。

Abstract: Layered van der Waals antiferromagnet CrSBr supports strong light--matter coupling and formation of magnetically tunable exciton-polaritons, yet active magnetic control over polariton propagation direction has remained elusive. Here, we investigate self-hybridized exciton-polaritons in photonic crystal slabs fabricated from CrSBr flakes and their evolution across the antiferromagnetic-to-ferromagnetic spin-flip transition induced by moderate in-plane magnetic fields. Using angle-resolved reflectance and photoluminescence spectroscopy supported by modeling, we show that the polariton energy continuously tracks the layer-by-layer magnetization switching, revealing a gradual redistribution of oscillator strength from antiferromagnetic to ferromagnetic excitons near the critical field. Most notably, we demonstrate that the sign of the polariton group velocity can be reversed by a small change in the external magnetic field of only 40 mT, resulting in complete switching of the polariton propagation direction. Our results establish CrSBr photonic crystal slabs as a platform for magnetically controlled polariton transport, opening opportunities for active integrated photonic and polaritonic devices.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构造方法使任意N个相互作用粒子的作用量在规范伽利略变换下保持协变（covariant），虽然所得拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）通常很复杂。

Result: 成功证明了任何相互作用粒子系统都可以实现规范伽利略不变性，得到的哈密顿量具有简单形式，包含作为相应规范变换生成元的一类约束。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了规范伽利略对称性在经典粒子系统中的普遍可实现性，为相关理论发展提供了数学基础。

Abstract: In this short note we show that any action for $N$ interacting particles can be made invariant under gauged Galilean transformations. While resulting Lagrangian is generally very complicated its Hamiltonian has simple form with first class constraints which are generators of corresponding gauge transformations included.

### [249] [Multi-soft theorems for cosmological correlators: Background wave method for scalars & gravitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09765)
*Farman Ullah*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文推导了宇宙学软定理（cosmological soft theorems），包括标量和张量关联函数（correlation functions）的树级多软定理（tree-level multi-soft theorems），并系统纳入了软交换贡献（soft-exchange contributions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学软定理（或一致性关系）为暴胀物理提供了有力探针，这些关系基于最小假设且普遍成立。违反这些关系将排除大量暴胀模型类别，例如违反标量软定理将排除所有吸引子单场暴胀模型（attractor single-field inflation models），指向多场动力学（multi-field dynamics）或非吸引子相（non-attractor phase）。

Method: 采用背景波方法（background-wave method），通过适当的空间坐标重标度（spatial coordinate rescaling）捕捉长波长模式效应。系统纳入了软交换贡献，包括标量关联函数中的张量交换（tensor exchanges）和张量关联函数中的标量交换（scalar exchanges）。

Result: 推导了标量和张量关联函数在软展开（soft expansion）主导阶的树级多软定理。分析表明这些关系在软展开的领头阶成立，为检验暴胀模型提供了理论框架。

Conclusion: 宇宙学软定理作为暴胀物理的普适探针，其违反将排除特定模型类别。本文推导的多软定理扩展了现有理论框架，为区分不同暴胀机制提供了更精细的检验工具。

Abstract: Cosmological soft theorems (or consistency relations) provide a powerful probe for the physics of inflation. These relations rely on minimal assumptions and hold very generally. Consequently, any violation of these relations would rule out a large class of inflationary models. For instance, a violation of the scalar soft theorem (or consistency relation) would rule out all attractor single-field inflation models and instead point toward either multi-field dynamics or a non-attractor phase. In this paper, we derive tree-level multi-soft theorems, at leading order in the soft expansion, for both scalar and tensor correlation functions. Our analysis employs the background-wave method, in which the effect of long-wavelength modes is captured by an appropriate spatial coordinate rescaling. In addition, we systematically incorporate soft-exchange contributions, including tensor exchanges in scalar correlators and scalar exchanges in tensor correlators.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该方法的核心是构建一个以体规范场（bulk gauge field）的特征数据为动力学场的理论模型。该模型结合了电分支卡罗尔动力学项（electric branch Carrollian kinetic term）和连接天球（celestial sphere）不同点的MHV型非局域相互作用。理论框架完全定义在零无限远上，不依赖于体空间的具体构造。

Result: 该理论明确恢复了杨-米尔斯理论中的所有MHV和NMHV树图振幅（tree amplitudes）。论文还概述了如何通过其费曼图展开（Feynman diagram expansion）获得任意树图振幅。特别值得注意的是，文中发现的NMHV振幅的详细表达式似乎是全新的结果。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个完全在零无限远（null infinity）上定义的理论，能够描述闵可夫斯基空间（Minkowski space）中的杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）。该理论不仅恢复了已知的MHV和NMHV树图振幅，还提供了获得任意树图振幅的框架，为从边界角度理解规范场理论开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We provide a theory defined purely on null infinity that describes Yang-Mills in the Minkowski space bulk. The dynamical field of our model is the characteristic data of the bulk gauge field, and the action combines an electric branch Carrollian kinetic term with non-local interactions of MHV type that link different points on the celestial sphere. We explicitly show how this theory recovers all MHV and NMHV tree amplitudes in Yang-Mills, and outline how arbitrary tree amplitudes may be obtained from its Feynman diagram expansion. The detailed expression we find for the NMHV amplitude appears to be new.

### [252] [Charges of supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09928)
*Remigiusz Durka,Jerzy Kowalski-Glikman,Rene Payne*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用协变相空间形式体系（covariant phase space formalism），推导了辛结构（symplectic structure）的体部和边界贡献，并构建了与洛伦兹变换（Lorentz transformations）、超对称性（supersymmetry）、平移（translations）和微分同胚（diffeomorphisms）相关的守恒荷。

Result: 边界荷的代数再现了预期的超代数（superalgebra），而平移荷由于超挠率约束（super-torsion constraint）在壳上消失，仅留下洛伦兹变换和超对称性作为非平凡生成元。

Conclusion: 在基于OSp(1|4)超代数的约束BF理论中，$\mathcal{N}=1$超引力的守恒荷结构表明，边界荷代数符合预期超代数，而平移荷在理论约束下消失，凸显了洛伦兹对称性和超对称性的基本作用。

Abstract: We study conserved charges of $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity formulated as a constrained BF theory based on the $\OSp(1|4)$ superalgebra. Using the covariant phase space formalism, we derive bulk and boundary contributions to the symplectic structure and construct charges associated with Lorentz transformations, supersymmetry, translations, and diffeomorphisms. We show that the algebra of boundary charges reproduces the expected superalgebra, while translational charges vanish on-shell due to the super-torsion constraint, leaving Lorentz and supersymmetry as the non-trivial generators.

### [253] [Quantum Energy Teleportation Across Lattice and Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09973)
*Kazuki Ikeda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子能量隐形传态（QET）在连续场论和晶格多体系统中的关系，通过大质量Thirring模型（等价于sine-Gordon理论）揭示了中性流（neutral current）与带电流（charged current）协议的区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子能量隐形传态（quantum energy teleportation, QET）在连续场论和晶格多体系统中已有研究，但两者在单一相互作用模型中的关系尚未明确。本文旨在通过大质量Thirring模型（massive Thirring model）——等价于sine-Gordon理论——来阐明这一关系。

Method: 在连续场论中，采用三角测量（trigonometric measurement）作为弱二元正算子值测度（Positive Operator-Valued Measure, POVM），其主导信号由玻色化理论（bosonized theory）中的守恒流关联函数（conserved-current correlator）决定。在晶格上，构建了中性流协议（neutral current protocol），其弱信号精确对应粗粒化流关联函数（coarse-grained current correlator）。

Result: 连续场论中，信号表现出无隙行为（gapless behavior）和有隙大距离渐近（gapped large-distance asymptotics）。晶格上，传统协议因U(1)选择定则（selection rule）无法访问中性流（neutral current）部分，信号位于带电扇区（charged sectors）。构建的中性流协议提取的能量与测量强度的平方成正比（scales quadratically with the measurement strength）。

Conclusion: 研究识别了晶格和连续描述共享的中性扇区（neutral sector），并将其与支配传统量子比特协议（conventional qubit protocol）的带电扇区（charged sector）区分开来，从而澄清了两种描述之间的关系。

Abstract: Quantum energy teleportation (QET) has been studied in continuum field theory and in lattice many-body systems, but the relation between the two within a single interacting model is still not well understood. To address this question, we consider the massive Thirring model, equivalently the sine--Gordon theory. In the continuum, the trigonometric measurement is a weak binary Positive Operator-Valued Measure (POVM), and its leading signal is set by a conserved-current correlator in the bosonized theory, with both gapless behavior and gapped large-distance asymptotics. On the lattice, the conventional protocol does not access this neutral current sector. For Alice's local measurement, a lattice $U(1)$ selection rule removes the neutral current contribution from Bob's subsystem, and the separated signal lies in charged sectors. On the same lattice Hamiltonian we construct a neutral current protocol whose weak signal is exactly a coarse-grained current correlator and whose extracted energy scales quadratically with the measurement strength. This identifies the neutral sector shared by the lattice and continuum descriptions, while separating it from the charged sector that governs the conventional qubit protocol.

</details>

Abstract: We report the experimental observation of holographically motivated quantum teleportation on a quantum processor, driven by the highly entangled, chaotic dynamics of a many-body system. This optimized approach dramatically reduces circuit depth for noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) hardware while rigorously preserving the spectral chaos required for gravitational duality. Diagnosing the teleportation signal via mutual information, we find that while inherent noise in NISQ hardware precludes perfect quantitative agreement with exact numerical simulations, our experimental results clearly demonstrate the essential qualitative signature: a sign-dependent asymmetry. This work establishes a practical, scalable framework for holographic quantum simulations, offering a novel empirical testbed for exploring holographic quantum gravity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用探针D膜方法（probe D-brane approach），将外电场视为恒定背景，同时将磁场（B）从小值变化到有限值，分析低温和高温区域中靠近和远离Misner弦位置的导电性。

Result: 计算表明，帧拖曳效应主要在较低温度、靠近Misner弦且磁场较小时显著；而在"有限"磁场下，即使温度较低，这些效应也变得可忽略。分析揭示了有限霍尔输运的存在，其根源在于新颖的帧拖曳效应。

Conclusion: 研究证实了Taub-NUT AdS黑洞中的帧拖曳效应对霍尔输运具有重要影响，特别是在特定参数区域（低温、小磁场、靠近Misner弦）下，这种效应主导了霍尔输运行为。

Abstract: We compute Hall transport coefficients associated with Taub-NUT AdS black holes in four space-time dimensions using the probe D-brane approach. In particular, we examine the effects due to the NUT parameter ($n$), or equivalently, the novel frame-dragging on the holographic charge transport properties. In our analysis, we treat the external electric field as a constant background, while varying the magnetic field ($B$) from small to finite. Within this framework, we analyze conductivities in both low and high temperature regions, focusing on locations that are both near and far from the Misner string. Our calculations show that frame-dragging effects are significant primarily at lower temperatures and near the Misner string, while a small magnetic field is maintained. However, these effects become negligibly small at a ``finite" magnetic field and even at lower temperatures. Our analysis reveals the existence of finite Hall transport, that has its origin in the novel frame-dragging.

*Batoul Banihashemi,Gauri Batra,Albert Y. T. Law,Eva Silverstein,Gonzalo Torroba*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于两个类时边界的微观全息对偶框架，用于描述包含未来楔形区的宇宙时空超越宇宙视界区域。通过两个拷贝的哈密顿量子理论构建，在谱的顶层获得扩展时空，并解决了纠缠熵计算中的鞍点极大化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一般时空拓扑包含类时边界（timelike boundaries），需要构建能够描述宇宙视界区域之外（包括未来楔形区）的微观全息对偶。这旨在解决正宇宙常数下量子重力理论的构建问题，特别是处理多个边界和因果楔形重叠区域的算子冗余性。

Method: 从两个拷贝的"dressed Hamiltonian quantum theories"出发，构建描述de Sitter时空的宇宙视界和极点区域。通过计算未重整化引力路径积分鞍点在纠缠熵计算中的极大性，在三维体空间中进行显式计算，并纳入UV敏感的量子超越广义相对论效应。

Result: 在谱的顶层，从近最大纠缠的（微）正则热场双重态获得扩展时空。较低能级产生高扩展时空，其中边界因果楔形重叠。正宇宙常数下，因果楔形重构比AdS/CFT设置更强大，且量子重力理论明确与多个态的存在一致。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了包含未来楔形区的宇宙时空微观全息描述，解决了正宇宙常数下量子重力理论中多个边界和因果楔形重叠的问题。与封闭宇宙的特殊情况不同，一般量子重力理论明确支持多个态的存在。

Abstract: A generic spacetime topology contains timelike boundaries. Making use of two such boundaries, we formulate a microscopic holographic dual that captures cosmological spacetime beyond the cosmic horizon patch, including the future wedge. We build this starting from two copies of the dressed Hamiltonian quantum theories which formulate the cosmic horizon and pole patches of de Sitter. At the top level of the spectrum we obtain the extended spacetime from a nearly maximally entangled (micro-)canonical thermofield double state. This requires addressing the maximality of the unrenormalized gravitational path integral saddle in the calculation of the entanglement entropy upon tracing out one sector. We resolve this in both ensembles via explicit computations in the constrained path integral for three bulk dimensions, incorporating UV-sensitive quantum beyond-GR effects when they contribute strongly. Lower energy levels in the spectrum generate tall extended spacetimes where the boundaries' causal wedges overlap. These arise in our theory via constraints on the doubled Hilbert space, which encode the operator redundancies arising from the reconstruction of bulk operators from either boundary within the region where their causal wedges overlap. With positive cosmological constant, the tallness implies that causal wedge reconstruction is more powerful than in the AdS/CFT setting. In contrast to the special case of a closed universe, generically quantum gravity with positive cosmological constant -- including the future wedge -- is manifestly consistent with the existence of multiple states.

</details>


### [257] [Some progress on the use of the variational method in quantum field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10284)
*Antoine Tilloy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该专著介绍了相对论连续矩阵乘积态（RCMPS）这一针对(1+1)维量子场论设计的变分拟设，并展示了其在多个模型中的非微扰应用，包括基态能量、局域可观测量计算，以及通过线性规划方法提取谱数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: (1+1)维强耦合量子场论的非微扰求解极为困难，而传统变分方法缺乏适应相对论性环境的自然拟设。因此需要开发专门针对相对论性量子场论的变分方法。

Method: 采用相对论连续矩阵乘积态（relativistic continuous matrix product states, RCMPS）作为变分拟设，并在RCMPS流形上进行黎曼优化（Riemannian optimization）。该方法还包含用于提取谱数据的原始线性规划方法（original linear programming approach）。

Result: 在φ⁴、Sine-Gordon和Sinh-Gordon模型中获得了具有竞争力的非微扰近似，包括强耦合区域（其中微扰理论失效）。该方法能够计算能量密度、局域可观测量、非局域可观测量（缺陷），并通过线性规划提取粒子质量等谱数据。

Conclusion: RCMPS框架为(1+1)维量子场论提供了有效的非微扰变分方法，在多个模型中表现出色。专著最后讨论了该方法的当前局限性和未来最有前景的研究方向。

Abstract: Strongly coupled quantum field theories in $(1+1)$ dimensions are notoriously hard to solve non-perturbatively. Variational methods, despite their success for quantum many-body physics on the lattice, have long lacked a natural ansatz adapted to the relativistic setting. This monograph explains the intuition behind relativistic continuous matrix product states (RCMPS), a variational ansatz tailored to $(1+1)$-dimensional QFT, and reports on several years of progress in developing and applying this approach. Using Riemannian optimization on the manifold of RCMPS, we obtain competitive non-perturbative approximations to ground state energies and local observables in the $φ^4$, Sine-Gordon, and Sinh-Gordon models, including in strongly coupled regimes where perturbation theory fails. We then describe extensions to models with several interacting fields. Beyond energy density and local observables, we show how the framework can be used to evaluate non-local observables (defects) and, through an original linear programming approach, to extract spectral data such as particle masses. We close by discussing the current limitations of the method and the most promising directions for future work.

</details>


### [258] [Connecting Supersymmetry to Non-Supersymmetric theories: the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa example](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10434)
*Mrigankamauli Chakraborty,Sven-Olaf Moch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 构建了一个统一Gross-Neveu-Yukawa、Nambu-Jona-Lasinio-Yukawa和Wess-Zumino模型的广义拉格朗日量（generalized Lagrangian），揭示了这些理论在临界点的结构联系和超对称（supersymmetry）涌现机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在阐明Gross-Neveu-Yukawa、Nambu-Jona-Lasinio-Yukawa和Wess-Zumino模型之间的结构联系，特别是临界点处涌现超对称（emergent supersymmetry）的机制。

Method: 在D维正规化（D-dimensional regularization）框架下，构建了允许任意标量和费米子味道（arbitrary scalar and fermion flavors）的广义拉格朗日量，统一了上述三种模型。

Result: 该统一框架揭示了理论间的结构联系，提供了额外的超对称Ward恒等式（supersymmetry Ward identities），简化了包括非超对称模型在内的圈图计算（loop calculations）。

Conclusion: 该技术能够降低计算twist-two算子反常维度（anomalous dimensions of twist-two operators）的计算成本，为相关研究提供了简化计算的统一框架。

Abstract: We construct a generalized Lagrangian that unifies the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa, Nambu-Jona-Lasinio-Yukawa, and Wess-Zumino models, allowing for arbitrary scalar and fermion flavors in $D$-dimensional regularization. This framework clarifies how emergent supersymmetry arises at critical points and reveals structural connections between these theories. The unified formulation provides additional supersymmetry Ward identities that simplify loop calculations, even for non-supersymmetric models. As an application, we show how this technique can reduce the computational cost of determining anomalous dimensions of twist-two operators.

### [259] [The Junction Law for Multipartite Entanglement in Confining Holographic Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10583)
*Norihiro Iizuka,Akihiro Miyata*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了禁闭全息背景中多部分纠缠的连接定律实现，使用真实多熵（genuine multi-entropy, GM）作为主要诊断工具。通过分析硬壁玩具模型和平滑禁闭几何，揭示了连接结构的鲁棒性特征以及相结构和短距离标度行为的背景依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究禁闭全息背景中多部分纠缠的连接定律如何实现，特别关注真实多熵（genuine multi-entropy, GM）作为诊断工具的有效性。通过比较不同几何背景下的行为，旨在区分连接图像中的鲁棒特征与背景依赖特征。

Method: 研究方法首先采用AdS₃硬壁玩具模型作为解析基准，分析多路切割和连接几何结构。随后扩展到平滑禁闭几何，包括D4-孤子（D4-soliton）、D3-孤子（D3-soliton）和Klebanov-Strassler背景，建立相应框架并比较相结构差异。

Result: 研究结果显示，在硬壁模型中真实多部分贡献由GM诊断并定域于连接点附近，相结构依赖于子系统尺寸、不对称性和禁闭尺度。在平滑几何中，连接图像持续存在但相结构不同：硬壁平台消失，GM单调递减并在有限临界尺度处消失。短距离行为具有背景依赖性，表现为不同的标度律。

Conclusion: 结论表明，连接定律图像在禁禁闭全息学中具有鲁棒性，但相结构和短距离标度行为具有背景依赖性。硬壁模型中的平台特征在平滑几何中不保留，而GM的单调递减和临界尺度消失行为成为普遍特征。

Abstract: We investigate how the junction law for multipartite entanglement is realized in confining holographic backgrounds, using genuine multi-entropy (GM) as our main diagnostic. We first study an AdS$_3$ hard-wall toy model as an analytic benchmark, where multi-way cuts and junction geometries can be analyzed explicitly. In this setup, we classify the relevant saddles, determine the dominant phases, and show that the genuinely multipartite contribution diagnosed by GM is localized near the junction. We also examine how this structure depends on subsystem sizes, asymmetry, and the confinement scale, including phase transitions between competing saddles. We then move beyond the hard-wall benchmark to smooth confining geometries, focusing on the D4-soliton and D3-soliton backgrounds and formulating the corresponding framework also for the Klebanov--Strassler background. In the smooth-cap examples, we find that the junction picture persists, while the detailed phase structure differs from the hard-wall case: in particular, the hard-wall plateau does not survive, and GM instead decreases monotonically and vanishes at a finite critical scale. We also find that the short-distance behavior is background-dependent, with $\mathrm{GM}^{(3)}\sim L^{-4}$ in the D4-soliton background, $\mathrm{GM}^{(3)}\sim L^{-2}$ in the D3-soliton background, and $\mathrm{GM}^{(3)}\sim L^{-2}\cdot (\log L)^{2}$ in the Klebanov--Strassler background. These results clarify which features of the junction-law picture are robust in confining holography and which features of the phase structure and short-distance scaling are background-dependent.

</details>


### [260] [Exact holographic thermal spectral functions: OPE, non-perturbative corrections, and black hole singularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10803)
*Hewei Frederic Jia,Mukund Rangamani*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究分析了全息共形场论（holographic CFTs）热谱函数的解析性质，证明了在偶数维闵可夫斯基时空下，整数维标量原初场的精确谱函数可分解为微扰/算子乘积展开（OPE）部分和非微扰部分，并建立了非微扰谱函数与黑洞奇点之间的明确联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究全息共形场论热谱函数的解析性质，特别是其在有限动量下的精确性质和大动量下的渐近行为。探索这些谱函数如何编码黑洞内部信息，包括视界和奇点。

Method: 采用全息对偶框架，研究偶数维闵可夫斯基时空上的全息CFT。对于整数维标量原初场，通过近边界分析确定微扰/OPE部分，并利用精确WKB技术计算体波方程的单值性（monodromy），从而获得非微扰部分在大类时动量下的完整跨级数展开（transseries expansion）。

Result: 证明了精确谱函数在有限动量下可分解为微扰/OPE部分和非微扰部分：前者由应力张量交换控制并由近边界分析确定；后者编码体内部信息，包括黑洞视界和奇点。获得了非微扰部分在大类时动量下的完整跨级数展开，并计算了复时间平面上空间平均热场双态关联子的奇异轨迹（singular loci）。

Conclusion: 研究建立了非微扰谱函数与黑洞奇点之间的明确联系，表明这些奇异轨迹在双CFT可观测量中提供了黑洞曲率奇点的印记。该结果在非零动量情况下也成立，进一步强化了全息对偶中非微扰效应与黑洞几何内在关联的理论框架。

Abstract: We study analytic properties of thermal spectral functions of holographic CFTs, examining both their (a) exact properties at finite momentum and (b) asymptotics at large momentum. For even-dimensional holographic CFTs on Minkowski spacetime and for scalar primaries with integer dimensions, we demonstrate that the exact spectral function at finite momentum factorizes into a perturbative/OPE piece and a non-perturbative piece. The former is controlled by stress tensor exchange and fixed by a near-boundary analysis. The latter encodes information about the bulk interior, including the black hole horizon and singularity. Utilizing the exact factorization, we obtain the full transseries expansion of the non-perturbative piece at large timelike momentum. This is achieved by employing exact WKB techniques to compute the monodromy of the bulk wave equation. Finally, we use these results to work out the singular loci of a spatially averaged thermofield double correlator in the complex time plane. These singular loci have been argued to provide imprints of the black hole curvature singularity in the dual CFT observables. Our result, which includes the case of non-vanishing momentum, gives a clear link between the non-perturbative spectral function and the black hole singularity.

*Wei Gu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高形式规范场框架，将真空结构编码在紧致三形式规范场中，其四形式通量标记拓扑扇区。在总电荷为N的带电物质存在下，这些扇区展现自然ℤ_N结构，分解为N个半经典贡献。这些贡献源于高形式扇区中的欧几里得点状构型，类似于分数瞬子（fractional instantons）。

Abstract: We present a semiclassical account of the Veneziano-Yankielowicz (VY) superpotential in four-dimensional $N=1$ super Yang-Mills theory. Motivated by two-dimensional gauged linear sigma models, where superpotentials arise from vortex dynamics, we reinterpret domain walls as fundamental objects associated with higher-form gauge fields. In this formulation, the vacuum structure is encoded in a compact three-form gauge field, whose four-form flux labels topological sectors. In the presence of charged matter with total charge $N$, these sectors exhibit a natural $\mathbb{Z}_N$ structure, leading to a decomposition into $N$ semiclassical contributions. These contributions arise from Euclidean point-like configurations in the higher-form sector, analogous to fractional instantons. We show that these configurations provide the relevant non-perturbative contributions to the effective superpotential. Integrating out the associated degrees of freedom reproduces the VY superpotential in the infrared. This gives a semiclassical origin of the VY superpotential in terms of higher-form gauge dynamics.

### [264] [Updating the holomorphic modular bootstrap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11277)
*Suresh Govindarajan,Akhila Sadanandan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文更新了全纯模自举方法，结合了在模线性微分方程框架内计算精确S矩阵的最新结果，系统分析了Wronskian指数小于6、有效中心荷不超过24的所有模线性微分方程的可容许解，并识别了具有良好融合规则的"可维持"解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于整合模线性微分方程框架内计算精确S矩阵的最新进展，系统探索具有特定参数限制的模线性微分方程的可容许解，并识别其中具有良好物理性质的解。

Method: 方法基于全纯模自举（holomorphic modular bootstrap）技术，结合模线性微分方程（MLDE）框架，利用允许指数模一的知识，分析Wronskian指数小于6、有效中心荷不超过24且含一个辅助参数的所有模线性微分方程。

Result: 获得了所有符合条件的模线性微分方程的可容许解（admissible solutions），并从中识别出具有良好融合规则的"可维持"解（tenable solutions），在可能情况下确定了对应的共形场论（CFT）及其在幺正情况下的模张量范畴（MTC）类别。

Conclusion: 研究成功更新了全纯模自举方法，系统分类了特定参数范围内的模线性微分方程解，为识别具有物理意义的共形场论候选提供了系统框架，并建立了可容许解与具体理论之间的对应关系。

Abstract: We update the holomorphic modular bootstrap incorporating a recent result that computes the exact S-matrix within the Modular Linear Differential Equation (MLDE) setting. Further, using knowledge of the allowed exponents modulo one, we obtain admissible solutions to all MLDE's with up to six characters and Wronskian index < 6 and one accessory parameter with c_eff <= 24. We then identify which of the admissible solutions have good fusion rules -- we call such solutions tenable. When possible, we identify the CFT and in the unitary cases the MTC class they belong to.

</details>


### [265] [GlobalCY I: A JAX Framework for Globally Defined and Symmetry-Aware Neural Kähler Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11404)
*Abdul Rahman*

Main category: hep-th

The gains are strongest at $λ=0.75$, while $λ=1.0$ remains more difficult. The current symmetry-aware model improves projective-invariance drift relative to the local baseline, but does not yet surpass the plain global invariant model. These results show that global invariant structure is a meaningful architectural constraint for learned Kähler-potential modeling in hard quartic Calabi--Yau settings.

Conclusion: 结论指出非对易时空为麦克斯韦-陈-西蒙斯理论提供了正则化框架，构建的精确解及其物理解释框架为理解非对易场论中的电荷和磁荷行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate Maxwell-Chern-Simons theory on a three-dimensional noncommutative spacetime endowed with a constant spacelike Poisson structure. By exploiting the residual rotational symmetry, we construct exact classical solutions corresponding to pointlike electric and magnetic charges. We demonstrate that noncommutativity acts as a natural regulator, ensuring a finite total electromagnetic energy and thereby resolving the classical self-energy divergence. Furthermore, some of these solutions exhibit a non-perturbative dependence on the noncommutativity parameter and allow for the generation of an arbitrary magnetic flux. We also present a noncommutative generalization of Gauss's law, providing a robust framework for the physical interpretation of these exact solutions.

### [269] [From Exact Space-Time Symmetry Conservation to Automatic Mesh Refinement in Discrete Initial Boundary Value Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11163)
*Alexander Rothkopf,W. A. Horowitz,Jan Nordström*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在作用量层面直接处理初边值问题的新方法，通过将坐标映射作为动力学自由度与传播场结合，实现了离散化后时空对称性的精确保持和基于诺特定律守恒的自适应网格细化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在发展初边值问题（Initial Boundary Value Problems, IBVPs）的现代变分作用量公式化方法，绕过传统的控制方程层面，直接在作用量层面处理这些问题。

Method: 基于经典动力学的现代变分作用量公式化，将坐标映射作为动力学自由度与传播场结合，使用SBP（Summation-By-Parts）算子进行离散化，并在1+1维标量波传播问题中进行了原理验证。

Result: 该方法实现了两个关键结果：离散化后时空对称性仍受保护，导致诺特荷（Noether charges）的精确守恒；坐标映射的动力学特性引导时空分辨率调整，实现了自动自适应网格细化（automatic adaptive mesh refinement）。

Conclusion: 只要使用SBP算子进行离散化，该方法的结果与在作用量层面还是控制方程层面求解动力学无关，特别是在高阶情况下也成立，为初边值问题提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: In this contribution we present recent developments in the formulation and solution of Initial Boundary Value Problems (IBVPs). Building upon a modern variational action formulation of classical dynamics, we treat Initial Boundary Value Problems directly on the action level, bypassing governing equations. We show that by including coordinate maps as dynamical degrees of freedom together with propagating fields two key results emerge. Space-time symmetries remain protected even after discretization, leading to an exact conservation of Noether charges even for discrete IBVPs. The dynamical nature of the coordinate maps leads to an adjustment of space-time resolution, guided by Noether charge conservation, realizing a form of automatic adaptive mesh refinement. We stress that as long as SBP operators are used for the discretization, our results are independent of whether the dynamics are solved on the action or governing equation level and hold in particular also at high order. As proof-of-principle for our approach we present its application to scalar wave-propagation in 1+1 dimensions.

Abstract: We prove that two half-space models in the KPZ universality class, exponential last-passage percolation and a family of Poisson-avoiding metrics generalizing colored TASEP, converge to a common scaling limit. This scaling limit is the directed landscape in half-space, a random directed metric in the half-plane indexed by a parameter which determines the strength of the boundary interaction.
  As part of our analysis, we characterize the half-space directed landscape in terms of the half-space KPZ fixed point, and prove convergence of geodesics. We also give an explicit construction of joint stationary measures (or horizons) in half-space for the log-gamma polymer, the KPZ equation, exponential and geometric last passage percolation, and the directed landscape itself.

### [271] [Semilocalization for inhomogeneous random graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11682)
*Thomas Buc-d'Alché,Antti Knowles*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文分析了从特定度序列构建的随机非均匀图（random inhomogeneous graph）邻接矩阵的特征向量。研究发现，在谱边缘附近，特征向量呈现半局域化（semilocalized）特性，其质量集中在少量共振顶点（resonant vertices）周围；对于极值特征值，则表现出围绕单个顶点的局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解具有有界均值和方差的经验度序列（empirical degree sequence）所构建的随机非均匀图中邻接矩阵特征向量的局域化行为。此类图的高度非均匀度分布对传统分析方法提出了挑战。

Method: 为应对高度非均匀度分布带来的分析困难，作者引入了一种新的经济剪枝程序（economical pruning procedure），从原图中精心提取出一个森林（forest）。通过构建适当的局部耦合（local coupling），将原图邻接矩阵与具有独立边的随机树（random trees with independent edges）的邻接矩阵进行比较。

Result: 研究结果表明，在谱边缘附近，特征向量呈现半局域化，其质量集中在少量共振顶点周围。对于极值特征值，特征向量表现出围绕单个顶点的局域化。这些结果在高度非均匀度分布条件下仍然有效。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了随机非均匀图中邻接矩阵特征向量在谱边缘附近的半局域化行为，并通过引入新的经济剪枝程序和局部耦合技术，为分析高度非均匀图提供了有效的估计方法。

Abstract: We analyse the eigenvectors of the adjacency matrix of a random inhomogeneous graph constructed from a specified degree sequence. We assume that the empirical degree sequence has bounded mean and variance. We show that near the edges of the spectrum, the eigenvectors are semilocalized in the sense that their mass concentrates around a small set of resonant vertices. For the extremal eigenvalues, we establish localization around a single vertex. In order to obtain effective estimates in the presence of highly inhomogeneous degrees, we introduce a new economical pruning procedure that carefully extracts a forest from the original graph, whose adjacency matrix is compared to that of the original graph using a suitably constructed local coupling to random trees with independent edges.

### [272] [Sensitivity of Neutron Star Observables to Transition Density in Hybrid Equation-of-State Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11046)
*N. K. Patra,Sk Md Adil Imam,Kai Zhou*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了中子星状态方程（EoS）混合构造中过渡密度ρ_tr的影响，发现即使在采用相同高密度参数化时，中子星半径和潮汐形变等性质仍显著依赖于低密度EoS的选择，特别是当ρ_tr≈2ρ_0时。降低过渡密度可减少模型间的差异，使预测更一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解过渡密度如何影响中子星状态方程的混合构造，其中低密度核子描述与基于声速参数化的模型无关高密度扩展相匹配。当前广泛采用的ρ_tr≈2ρ_0选择是否真能确保模型独立性尚不明确。

Method: 采用四种代表性核子模型——泰勒展开、n/3展开、Skyrme和相对论平均场模型，这些模型基于相同的核物质参数构建。通过平滑匹配方案，将低密度描述与两种不同的声速参数化高密度扩展连接，以隔离低密度EoS和过渡密度对中子星可观测量（如半径和潮汐形变）的影响。

Result: 研究发现，在ρ_tr≈2ρ_0时，1.4M_⊙中子星的半径和潮汐形变模型差异分别超过当前观测不确定性的~1.8倍和~1.4倍。当过渡密度降低至ρ_tr=ρ_0时，这些因子分别减少至~1.05和~0.4。不同低密度输入导致不同的有效高密度EoS，这种残余依赖性源于ρ_tr处匹配条件的差异。

Conclusion: 结论表明，广泛采用的ρ_tr≈2ρ_0选择并不能保证混合EoS构造的模型独立性，应被视为从中子星观测推断致密物质性质时的显式系统不确定性来源。降低过渡密度可系统性地减少模型间的差异，获得更一致的预测。

Abstract: We investigate how the transition density \(ρ_{tr}\) affects hybrid constructions of the neutron-star equation of state (EoS) in which a nucleonic description at low densities is matched to a model-agnostic high-density extension based on a speed-of-sound parametrization. Using four representative nucleonic models--Taylor expansion, \(\frac{n}{3}\) expansion, Skyrme, and relativistic mean-field--built from identical nuclear matter parameters, we isolate the impact of the low-density EoS and the transition density on neutron star observables. We find that, within the present smooth-matching prescription, neutron star properties such as radii and tidal deformabilities retain significant sensitivity to the choice of low-density EoS for commonly adopted transition densities around \(ρ_{tr} \approx 2ρ_0\), even when the same high-density parametrization is employed. This residual dependence arises from differences in the matching conditions at \(ρ_{tr}\), which propagate into the high-density extension, so different low-density inputs lead to different effective high-density EoSs. These findings are robust across two distinct speed-of-sound parametrizations. Quantitatively, the model spread in radius and tidal deformability at $1.4\,M_\odot$ exceeds the current observational uncertainty by factors of $\sim 1.8$ and $\sim 1.4$ at $ρ_{\mathrm{tr}} \approx 2ρ_0$, whereas these factors reduce to $\sim 1.05$ and $\sim 0.4$ at $ρ_{\mathrm{tr}} = ρ_0$. Lowering the transition density, therefore, systematically diminishes the spread among models and leads to more consistent predictions. Our results demonstrate that the widely used choice \(ρ_{tr} \approx 2ρ_0\) does not guarantee model independence in hybrid EoS constructions, and should be treated as an explicit source of systematic uncertainty when inferring dense matter properties from neutron star observations.

</details>

### [273] [Particle transformers for identifying Lorentz-boosted Higgs bosons decaying to a pair of W bosons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09809)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为"粒子变换器（Particle transformer, PaRT）"的新型深度神经网络分类器，用于识别在CMS实验中重建为单喷注的高度洛伦兹boost共振。该模型在多种拓扑结构上训练，首次在boosted希格斯玻色子衰变为W玻色子的喷注识别中表现出色，并在保持与喷注质量解相关的同时实现了超过50%的标记效率（背景效率1%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高能物理实验中，识别高度洛伦兹boost（Lorentz-boosted）的共振粒子（如希格斯玻色子）是一项挑战，因为它们衰变产物在探测器中被重建为单个多叉（multipronged）喷注。需要开发更有效的分类算法来提升标准模型测量和超出标准模型新物理寻找的灵敏度。

Method: 提出基于自注意力机制（self-attention mechanism）的粒子变换器（PaRT）深度神经网络分类器，该机制允许模型权衡不同粒子的重要性。模型在多种拓扑结构上训练，特别针对boosted希格斯玻色子衰变为W玻色子的喷注识别进行了优化。使用CMS在质心能量13 TeV下收集的质子-质子对撞数据进行校准，对应总亮度138 fb⁻¹。

Result: PaRT算法在boosted希格斯玻色子衰变为W玻色子的喷注识别中，在背景效率1%时达到超过50%的标记效率（tagging efficiency），同时保持与喷注质量（jet mass）的解相关（decorrelation）。数据到模拟选择效率比例因子（data-to-simulation selection efficiency scale factors）测量值在0.9-1.0范围内，相对不确定度在7-23%之间。

Conclusion: 粒子变换器（PaRT）算法显著提升了boosted希格斯玻色子衰变喷注的识别性能，其标记能力增强了标准模型测量和超出标准模型共振粒子衰变为强子双玻色子系统的寻找灵敏度。该模型首次在boosted希格斯玻色子衰变为W玻色子的喷注识别中表现出色，为高能物理数据分析提供了新的有效工具。

Abstract: A novel deep neural network classifier, a ``Particle transformer'' (PaRT), is introduced for the identification of highly Lorentz-boosted resonances reconstructed as single, multipronged jets in measurements and searches performed by the CMS Collaboration at the CERN LHC. Based on a self-attention mechanism that allows the model to weigh the importance of different particles, PaRT is trained on a wide variety of topologies, notably demonstrating strong performance for the first time on jets originating from boosted Higgs boson decays to W bosons. The PaRT algorithm achieves a tagging efficiency of more than 50\% for such jets at a background efficiency of 1%, while maintaining decorrelation from the jet mass. A calibration is performed in proton-proton collision data collected by CMS at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV, with a data set corresponding to a total luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Data-to-simulation selection efficiency scale factors are measured to be in the 0.9$-$1.0 range, with relative uncertainties between 7 and 23%. The tagging capability of PaRT enhances the sensitivity of standard model measurements and searches for beyond-the-standard-model resonances decaying to hadronic diboson systems.

</details>


### [274] [Semileptonic and Leptonic Decays at Belle II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09816)
*Raynette van Tonde*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该会议论文总结了Belle和Belle II探测器在Υ(4S)共振态收集的电子-正电子对撞数据中，关于半轻子和轻子B衰变的最新研究，这些研究为检验轻子味普适性（lepton flavour universality）和精确测定CKM矩阵元|V_ub|与|V_cb|提供了关键实验输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究半轻子和轻子B衰变的主要动机在于：这些过程能够对轻子味普适性（lepton flavour universality）进行严格检验，同时为最终提高包容性|V_ub|和|V_cb|矩阵元测定的精度提供关键的实验输入。

Method: 分析方法基于Belle和Belle II探测器在Υ(4S)共振态记录的电子-正电子对撞数据，包括Belle完整的711 fb⁻¹数据集以及Belle II在2019-2022年间收集的365 fb⁻¹数据样本。

Result: 论文总结了近期关于半轻子和轻子B衰变的研究进展，这些分析基于Belle和Belle II实验的大量数据样本，为检验标准模型的基本对称性和精确测定CKM矩阵元提供了重要结果。

Conclusion: 通过对Belle和Belle II实验数据的综合分析，半轻子和轻子B衰变研究为轻子味普适性检验和CKM矩阵元|V_ub|、|V_cb|的精确测定提供了重要进展，有助于深入理解标准模型的基本性质。

Abstract: This proceeding summarises recent studies on semileptonic and leptonic $B$ decays, which provide stringent tests of lepton flavour universality as well as key experimental inputs to ultimately increase the precision of inclusive $|V_{ub}|$ and $|V_{cb}|$ determinations. The presented analyses investigate electron-positron collision data recorded by the Belle and Belle II detectors at the $Υ(4S)$ resonance, comprising the complete Belle data set of 711 fb$^{-1}$ and 365 fb$^{-1}$ of Belle II data samples collected between 2019 - 2022.

### [275] [Search for dark sector and rare decays at BESIII](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10405)
*Zhi-Jun Li,Zheng-Yun You*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII实验利用粲偶素、粲介子、超子等大量数据样本，探索暗物质区（dark sector）和稀有衰变，包括亚GeV暗物质、暗重子粒子、轻矢量玻色子的寻找，以及重子数和轻子数破坏过程的研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BESIII实验收集了大量粲偶素（charmonium）、粲介子（charm mesons）、超子（hyperons）和轻介子（light mesons）数据样本，为探索暗物质区（dark sector）和稀有衰变提供了独特机会。

Method: 通过分析特定衰变道来搜索暗物质区信号：在$η\to π^0 + \text{invisible}$和$J/ψ\to φ+ \text{invisible}$中寻找亚GeV暗物质；在$Ξ^- \to π^- +\rm{invisible}$中寻找暗重子粒子；在$χ_{cJ} \to J/ψX$（$X \to e^+ e^-$）中寻找轻矢量玻色子。

Result: 论文展示了BESIII实验在暗物质区搜索的最新结果，包括亚GeV暗物质、暗重子粒子和轻矢量玻色子的寻找结果，以及稀有衰变搜索，如$ψ\to e μ$、重子数和轻子数破坏过程、多种粲偶素弱衰变的搜索。

Conclusion: BESIII实验利用其独特的数据样本，在暗物质区物理和稀有衰变研究方面取得了重要进展，为探索超出标准模型（beyond Standard Model）的新物理提供了关键约束。

Abstract: The BESIII experiment has collected a large data sample of charmonium, charm mesons, hyperons, and other light mesons. These data provide a unique opportunity to explore the dark sector and rare decays. We present recent dark sector results from the BESIII experiment, including searches for sub-GeV dark matter in $η\to π^0 + \text{invisible}$ and $J/ψ\to φ+ \text{invisible}$, searches for dark baryon particles in $Ξ^- \to π^- +\rm{invisible}$, and searches for light vector bosons in $χ_{cJ} \to J/ψX$, where $X \to e^+ e^-$. In addition, we also present the recent rare decay searches, including a search for $ψ\to e μ$, as well as searches for several baryon number and lepton number violation processes, and searches for various charmonium weak decays.

</details>

Zhao,J. Y. Zhao,J. Z. Zhao,L. Zhao,Lei Zhao,M. G. Zhao,R. P. Zhao,S. J. Zhao,Y. B. Zhao,Y. L. Zhao,Y. P. Zhao,Y. X. Zhao,Z. G. Zhao,A. Zhemchugov,B. Zheng,B. M. Zheng,J. P. Zheng,W. J. Zheng,W. Q. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究首次对单卡比玻压低的衰变过程 $D^+ \to π^+ π^{+(0)} π^{-(0)} η$ 进行了振幅分析，测量了绝对分支比，并首次观测到 $D^{+}\to a_0(980)^{+}f_0(500)$ 衰变过程，为理解 $a_0(980)$ 和 $f_0(500)$ 态的本质提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于对单卡比玻压低（singly Cabibbo-suppressed）的 $D^+$ 介子衰变过程进行首次振幅分析（amplitude analysis），以深入理解相关衰变机制，并为 $a_0(980)$ 和 $f_0(500)$ 共振态的本质提供新的实验证据。

Method: 采用 BESIII 探测器在质心能量 3.773 GeV 处收集的 $e^+e^-$ 对撞数据，对应积分亮度为 20.3 $\rm{fb}^{-1}$。对 $D^+ \to π^+ π^+ π^- η$ 和 $D^+ \to π^+ π^0 π^0 η$ 衰变过程进行振幅分析，测量绝对分支比（branching fractions）及相关衰变过程。

Result: 测得 $D^+ \to π^+ π^+ π^- η$ 的绝对分支比为 $(3.20\pm0.06_{\text{stat.}}\pm0.03_{\text{syst.}})\times 10^{-3}$，$D^+ \to π^+ π^0 π^0 η$ 为 $(2.43 \pm 0.11_{\text{stat.}} \pm 0.04_{\text{syst.}}) \times 10^{-3}$。首次观测到 $D^{+}\to a_0(980)^{+}f_0(500)$ 衰变，其分支比意外地大。同时首次观测到 $D^+ \to a_0(980)^{+(0)} ρ(770)^{0(+)}$ 衰变，并测得比值 $r_{+/0} = 0.55\pm0.08_{\text{stat.}}\pm0.05_{\text{syst.}}$。

Conclusion: 这些结果为理解 $a_0(980)$ 和 $f_0(500)$ 共振态的本质提供了新的实验视角，特别是首次观测到的 $D^{+}\to a_0(980)^{+}f_0(500)$ 衰变过程及其意外大的分支比，对相关理论模型提出了新的挑战。

Abstract: We perform the first amplitude analysis of the singly Cabibbo-suppressed decays $D^+ \to π^+ π^{+(0)} π^{-(0)} η$, using $e^+e^-$ collision data collected with the BESIII detector at the center-of-mass energy of 3.773\,GeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 20.3 $\rm{fb}^{-1}$. The absolute branching fractions of the $D^+ \to π^+ π^+ π^- η$ and $D^+ \to π^+ π^0 π^0 η$ decays are measured to be $(3.20\pm0.06_{\text{stat.}}\pm0.03_{\text{syst.}})\times 10^{-3}$ and $(2.43 \pm 0.11_{\text{stat.}} \pm 0.04_{\text{syst.}}) \times 10^{-3}$, respectively. % , both achieving three times better precision than the current PDG values. The decay process $D^{+}\to a_0(980)^{+}f_0(500)$ is observed for the first time with an unexpectedly large branching fraction. Moreover, we observe the decays $D^+ \to a_0(980)^{+(0)} ρ(770)^{0(+)}$ and measure the ratio $r_{+/0} \equiv \frac{\mathcal{B}(D^+ \to a_0(980)^+ ρ(770)^0)}{\mathcal{B}(D^+ \to a_0(980)^0 ρ(770)^+)}$ for the first time to be $0.55\pm0.08_{\text{stat.}}\pm0.05_{\text{syst.}}$. These results offer a novel insight into our comprehension of the nature of the $a_0(980)$ and $f_0(500)$ states.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文利用BESIII探测器收集的$(2712.4\pm14.3)\times 10^6$个$ψ(3686)$事例，通过辐射跃迁$ψ(3686)\toγχ_{cJ}$测量了$χ_{cJ}\toπ^+π^-π^0π^0$（$J=0,1,2$）的分支比，结果精度显著优于先前测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究粲偶素（charmonium）$χ_{cJ}$态衰变到四π末态的分支比，特别是通过辐射跃迁$ψ(3686)\toγχ_{cJ}$过程进行测量，以改进先前测量的精度。

Method: 使用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的$(2712.4\pm14.3)\times 10^6$个$ψ(3686)$事例，通过辐射跃迁$ψ(3686)\toγχ_{cJ}$过程测量$χ_{cJ}\toπ^+π^-π^0π^0$的分支比。

Result: 测得的分支比为：$\mathcal{B}(χ_{c0} \to π^{+}π^{-}π^{0}π^{0}) = (3.10 \pm 0.01 \pm 0.14) \times 10^{-2}$，$\mathcal{B}(χ_{c1} \to π^{+}π^{-}π^{0}π^{0}) = (1.16 \pm 0.01 \pm 0.05) \times 10^{-2}$，$\mathcal{B}(χ_{c2} \to π^{+}π^{-}π^{0}π^{0}) = (1.92 \pm 0.01 \pm 0.08) \times 10^{-2}$，其中第一项为统计误差，第二项为系统误差。主要中间态为$χ_{cJ}\toρ^+ρ^-$。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了$χ_{cJ}\toπ^+π^-π^0π^0$分支比的最精确测量结果，显著改进了先前测量的精度，并确认$ρ^+ρ^-$为主要中间态，这些结果取代了先前最精确的测量。

Abstract: Using $(2712.4\pm14.3)\times 10^6$ $ψ(3686)$ events collected with the BESIII detector operating at BEPCII, the branching fractions of $χ_{cJ}\toπ^+π^-π^0π^0$ ($J=0,~1,~2$) are measured via the radiative transition $ψ(3686)\toγχ_{cJ}$. The results are $\mathcal{B}(χ_{c0} \to π^{+}π^{-}π^{0}π^{0}) = (3.10 \pm 0.01 \pm 0.14) \times 10^{-2}$, $\mathcal{B}(χ_{c1} \to π^{+}π^{-}π^{0}π^{0}) = (1.16 \pm 0.01 \pm 0.05) \times 10^{-2}$, and $\mathcal{B}(χ_{c2} \to π^{+}π^{-}π^{0}π^{0}) = (1.92 \pm 0.01 \pm 0.08) \times 10^{-2}$, where the first uncertainties are statistical and the second systematic. The dominant intermediate states are found to be $χ_{cJ}\toρ^+ρ^-$. These results supersede the previous most precise measurements and provide significantly improved precision.

</details>


### [278] [Leptonic and semileptonic charm decays at BESIII](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10540)
*Chao Chen*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII合作组利用在质心能量3.773 GeV、4.128-4.226 GeV和4.237-4.669 GeV收集的数据样本，在粲纯轻子和半轻子衰变方面取得了重要测量结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过粲纯轻子和半轻子衰变（charmed purely leptonic and semileptonic decays）的精确测量，获取基本物理参数并检验标准模型理论。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在特定质心能量（center-of-mass energies）收集的数据样本，对粲纯轻子和半轻子衰变过程进行测量分析。

Result: 获得了包括分支比（branching fractions）、CKM矩阵元（Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa matrix elements）$|V_{cs}|$和$|V_{cd}|$、衰变常数（decay constants）和形状因子（form factors）在内的多项测量结果，并对轻子味普适性（Lepton flavor universality）进行了检验。

Conclusion: BESIII合作组在粲纯轻子和半轻子衰变研究方面取得了重要进展，为精确测定基本物理参数和检验标准模型提供了关键实验数据。

Abstract: The BESIII collaboration has achieved important measurements in charmed purely leptonic and semi-leptonic decays using data samples collected at center-of-mass energies of 3.773 GeV, 4.128-4.226 GeV, and 4.237-4.669 GeV. This proceeding presents recent BESIII results on charmed purely leptonic and semileptonic decays, including measurements of branching fractions, the Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa matrix elements $|V_{cs}|$ and $|V_{cd}|$, decay constants and form factors, as well as a test of the Lepton flavor universality.

</details>


### [279] [Search for a new heavy resonance decaying to a top quark and a neutral scalar boson in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10729)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次在LHC上搜索重共振态衰变为顶夸克和中性标量玻色子φ的全强子末态，其中φ玻色子通过其衰变为底夸克-反底夸克对来识别。分析使用CMS探测器在13 TeV质心能量下收集的138 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，未发现显著超出背景预期的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上搜索重共振态衰变为顶夸克和中性标量玻色子φ的全强子末态。该搜索关注矢量型顶夸克T'的单产生过程，作为信号过程的基准模型，以探索超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理现象。

Method: 分析采用全强子末态，其中高度洛伦兹（Lorentz）提升的顶夸克和φ玻色子的衰变产物各自被重建为具有明显子结构的大半径喷注。使用CMS探测器在2016-2018年期间记录的13 TeV质心能量下138 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，并将结果与先前使用顶夸克半轻子衰变的CMS搜索相结合。

Result: 未观察到数据相对于背景预测的显著超出。当中性标量玻色子为标准模型希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）且T'夸克宽度为其质量的5%时，在95%置信水平下排除了0.85-1.3 TeV质量范围的T'夸克，并为2 TeV以上质量设定了迄今最严格的限制。对于其他φ玻色子质量，T'夸克产生截面与其衰变为顶夸克和φ玻色子的分支比的乘积上限低至0.1 fb。

Conclusion: 该搜索首次在LHC上探索了重共振态衰变为顶夸克和中性标量玻色子的全强子通道，为矢量型顶夸克T'的存在设定了严格的排除限制。研究结果为超出标准模型的新物理探索提供了重要约束，特别是在高能标区域。

Abstract: A first search at the LHC for a new heavy resonance decaying to a top quark and a neutral scalar boson $φ$ in the fully hadronic final state is presented, where the $φ$ boson is identified by its decay into a bottom quark-antiquark pair. The search is focused on final states in which the decay products of the highly Lorentz boosted top quark and $φ$ boson are each reconstructed as a single, large-radius jet with distinct substructure. The analysis is performed using proton-proton collision data at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$, recorded with the CMS detector at the LHC in 2016$-$2018. The single production of a vector-like top quark, $\mathrm{T}'$, is used as a benchmark model for the signal process. The results of this search are combined with those of a previous CMS search in which semileptonic decays of the top quark were used. No significant excess of data is observed with respect to the background prediction. For the case where the neutral scalar is a standard model Higgs boson and the $\mathrm{T}'$ quark width is 5% of its mass, $\mathrm{T}'$ quark masses between 0.85 and 1.3 TeV are excluded at 95% confidence level and the most stringent limits to date are set for masses above 2 TeV. For other $φ$ boson masses, upper limits as low as 0.1 fb are set on the product of the $\mathrm{T}'$ quark production cross section and branching fraction for its decay to a top quark and a $φ$ boson.

</details>


### [280] [A search for microscopic black holes, string balls, and sphalerons in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10732)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于CMS探测器在LHC上收集的138 fb⁻¹ 13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，使用两种搜索策略对微观黑洞、弦球和电弱sphaleron进行搜索，并设置了模型无关和模型相关的产生截面限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过LHC的高能质子-质子对撞，探索超出标准模型（beyond Standard Model）的新物理现象，特别是微观黑洞（microscopic black holes）、弦球（string balls）和电弱sphaleron的产生，这些现象与额外维度（extra dimensions）和电弱相变（electroweak phase transition）等理论框架相关。

Method: 采用两种基于数据控制样本（control samples）的搜索策略：一是基于事件中所有对象横向动量标量和（scalar sum of transverse momenta）形状不变性的模型无关方法；二是新开发的基于相空间邻近性（phase space proximity）将事件分类的方法，用于识别具有特定运动学特征的对撞事件。

Result: 在大额外维度（large extra dimensions）模型背景下，以95%置信水平排除了质量分别低于8.4-11.4 TeV和9.0-10.7 TeV的半经典黑洞（semiclassical black holes）和弦球（string balls），显著超越了先前搜索的范围。对电弱sphaleron的专用搜索得出，在9 TeV的标称sphaleron跃迁能量阈值（sphaleron transition energy threshold）以上，夸克-夸克相互作用（quark-quark interactions）分数的95%置信水平上限为0.0034。

Conclusion: 研究通过创新的分析方法，在LHC的13 TeV对撞能量下，对微观黑洞、弦球和电弱sphaleron等新物理现象设置了严格的产生截面限制，为探索超出标准模型的物理提供了重要约束。

Abstract: A search for microscopic black holes, string balls, and electroweak sphalerons using proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV recorded with the CMS detector at the CERN LHC during the 2016$-$2018 data taking, and corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$, is presented. Two search strategies based on control samples in data are used. Model-independent limits on the cross section of physics phenomena with multiple energetic jets, leptons, and photons are set using a method that relies on the shape invariance of the scalar sum of the transverse momenta of all objects in the event. Model-dependent limits on black hole and sphaleron production are set using a newly introduced method that has been developed for the identification of collider events with distinct kinematic features by separating them into classes based on phase space proximity. In the context of models with large extra dimensions, semiclassical black holes and string balls with masses below 8.4$-$11.4 TeV and 9.0$-$10.7 TeV, respectively, are excluded at 95% confidence level, significantly extending the reach beyond previous searches. Results of a dedicated search for electroweak sphalerons are used to derive an upper limit of 0.0034 at 95% confidence level on the fraction of quark-quark interactions above the nominal sphaleron transition energy threshold of 9 TeV.

</details>


### [281] [Search for proton decay via $p \to e^{+}π^{0}π^{0}$ and $p \to μ^{+}π^{0}π^{0}$ in 0.401 megaton-years exposure of Super-Kamiokande I-V](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10975)

Sekiyama,T. Yamazumi,Y. Nakajima,S. Shima,N. Taniuchi,E. Watanabe,M. Yokoyama,P. de Perio,S. Fujita,C. Jesús-Valls,K. Martens,Ll. Marti,K. M. Tsui,M. R. Vagins,J. Xia,M. Kuze,S. Izumiyama,R. Matsumoto,K. Terada,R. Asaka,M. Ishitsuka,C. Ise,Y. Ommura,N. Shigeta,M. Shinoki,M. Sugo,M. Wako,K. Yamauchi,T. Yoshida,Y. Nakano,A. Yankelevich,F. Cormier,R. Gaur,V. Gousy-Leblanc,M. Hartz,A. Konaka,X. Li,B. R. Smithers,S. Chen,Y. Wu,B. D. Xu,A. Q. Zhang,B. Zhang,H. Adhikary,M. Girgus,P. Govindaraj,M. Posiadala-Zezula,Y. S. Prabhu,S. B. Boyd,R. Edwards,D. Hadley,M. Nicholson,M. O'Flaherty,B. Richards,A. Ali,B. Jamieson,S. Amanai,C. Bronner,D. Horiguchi,A. Minamino,Y. Sasaki,R. Shibayama,R. Shimamura,S. Suzuki*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: Super-Kamiokande实验首次搜索质子衰变为带电反轻子和两个中性π介子的过程，基于0.401兆吨-年的数据，为两个衰变模式设定了新的寿命下限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论研究表明，涉及两个π介子的三体质子衰变（proton decay）速率可能与$p \to e^{+}π^{0}$和$p \to μ^{+}π^{0}$相当，但此前Super-Kamiokande从未搜索过质子衰变为带电反轻子（charged anti-lepton）和两个中性π介子（neutral pions）的过程。

Method: 研究分析了Super-Kamiokande I-V期所有纯水探测器（pure water detector）阶段收集的0.401兆吨-年（megaton-years）数据，首次搜索了$p \to e^{+}π^{0}π^{0}$和$p \to μ^{+}π^{0}π^{0}$两种衰变模式。

Result: 每个衰变模式各发现一个候选事件，与预期的大气中微子背景（atmospheric neutrino background）一致；在90%置信水平下，设定了寿命下限$τ/B(p \to e^{+}π^{0}π^{0}) > 7.2 \times 10^{33}$年和$τ/B(p \to μ^{+}π^{0}π^{0}) > 4.5 \times 10^{33}$年。

Conclusion: 新设定的质子衰变寿命下限比先前实验提高了超过一个数量级，未观测到超出背景的显著信号，与理论预测的衰变速率相当性仍需进一步验证。

Abstract: We searched for proton decay via $p \to e^{+}π^{0}π^{0}$ and $p \to μ^{+}π^{0}π^{0}$ in 0.401 megaton-years of data collected in all pure water detector phases of Super-Kamiokande (SK) I-V. A theoretical study predicts proton decay rates without assuming a particular grand unified theory and suggests that three-body proton decays involving two pions can have decay rates comparable to those of $p \to e^{+}π^{0}$ and $p \to μ^{+}π^{0}$. This is the first search for proton decay into a charged anti-lepton and two neutral pions in SK. One data candidate event was found for each of the two decay modes, which is consistent with the expected atmospheric neutrino background. We set lower limits on the lifetime of $τ/B(p \to e^{+}π^{0}π^{0}) > 7.2 \times 10^{33}$ years and $τ/B(p \to μ^{+}π^{0}π^{0}) > 4.5 \times 10^{33}$ years at 90 $\%$ confidence level. These limits are more than one order of magnitude higher than those of the previous experiment.

</details>

Winn,W. Wislicki,M. Witek,L. Witola,T. Wolf,E. Wood,G. Wormser,S. A. Wotton,H. Wu,J. Wu,X. Wu,Y. Wu,Z. Wu,K. Wyllie,S. Xian,Z. Xiang,Y. Xie,T. X. Xing,A. Xu,L. Xu,M. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,S. Yadav,K. Yang,X. Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Y. Z. Zhang,Z. Zhang,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用LHCb Run 2数据，通过粲偶素衰变到φφ对，测量了b强子衰变中η_c(1S)、η_c(2S)和χ_c态的产生分支比，并以前所未有的精度测量了η_c(1S)的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究b强子衰变中粲偶素（charmonium）态η_c(1S)、η_c(2S)和χ_c的产生，旨在测量这些过程的产生分支比（production branching fractions），并提高对η_c(1S)质量测量的精度。

Method: 使用LHCb Run 2数据，对应积分亮度为5.9 fb⁻¹，通过粲偶素衰变到φφ对来研究。以b → η_c(1S) (→ φφ) X作为归一化道（normalisation channel），其中X表示任何额外粒子。

Result: 测量了χ_c(1P)态在b强子衰变中的产生分支比：B(b → χ_c0 X) = (1.34 ± 0.13 ± 0.06 ± 0.37) × 10⁻³，B(b → χ_c1 X) = (1.58 ± 0.12 ± 0.09 ± 0.44) × 10⁻³，B(b → χ_c2 X) = (0.55 ± 0.08 ± 0.05 ± 0.15) × 10⁻³。同时测量了η_c(2S)的产生分支比与其衰变到φφ的分支比的乘积为(4.0 ± 0.6 ± 0.6 ± 1.1) × 10⁻⁷。

Conclusion: 该研究以前所未有的精度测量了η_c(1S)的质量为M_{η_c(1S)} = 2984.1 ± 0.5 ± 0.5 MeV，并提供了b强子衰变中粲偶素态产生分支比的精确测量结果，其中不确定性包括统计、系统以及外部测量分支比知识有限带来的贡献。

Abstract: The inclusive production of the $η_c(1S)$, $η_c(2S)$ and $χ_{c}$ charmonium states in $b$-hadron decays is studied with LHCb Run~2 data, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $5.9~\text{fb}^{-1}$, using charmonia decays to $φφ$ pairs. The production branching fractions of the $χ_{c}(1P)$ states in $b$-hadron decays are measured, using $b \to η_c(1S) (\to φφ) X$ as a normalisation channel, with $X$ indicating any additional particles. The results are \begin{align*}
  &{\cal{B}} (b \to χ_{c0} X) = (1.34 \pm 0.13 \pm 0.06 \pm 0.37) \times 10^{-3},
  &{\cal{B}} (b \to χ_{c1} X) = (1.58 \pm 0.12 \pm 0.09 \pm 0.44) \times 10^{-3},
  &{\cal{B}} (b \to χ_{c2} X) = (0.55 \pm 0.08 \pm 0.05 \pm 0.15) \times 10^{-3}, \end{align*} where the first uncertainty is statistical, the second systematic and the last is due to the limited knowledge of externally measured branching fractions. The production branching fraction of $η_c(2S)$ times the branching fraction of its decay into $φφ$ is measured as ${\cal{B}} (b \to η_c(2S) X) \times {\cal{B}} (η_c(2S) \to φφ) = (4.0 \pm 0.6 \pm 0.6 \pm 1.1) \times 10^{-7}$. Furthermore, the mass of the $η_c(1S)$ state is measured to be $M_{η_c(1S)} = 2984.1 \pm 0.5 \pm 0.5$ MeV with the best precision to date.

</details>


### [283] [Observation of the charmless purely baryonic decay $Λ_b^{0} \to Λp \bar{p}$ at LHCb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11325)
*Alexande Brea Rodriguez*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 首次观测到无粲纯重子衰变 $Λ_b^{0} \to Λp \bar{p}$，使用完整的LHCb Run 2数据集，测量其相对于拓扑相似归一化模式 $Λ_b^{0} \to ΛK^+K^-$ 的分支比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在首次观测无粲纯重子衰变（charmless purely baryonic decay）$Λ_b^{0} \to Λp \bar{p}$，这类衰变过程在粒子物理中具有重要意义，有助于理解重子形成机制和强相互作用动力学。

Method: 使用完整的LHCb Run 2数据集，对应积分亮度为$6.0~fb^{-1}$。通过同时拟合长径迹（long-track）和下游径迹（downstream-track）类别，并采用拓扑相似的归一化模式$Λ_b^{0} \to ΛK^+K^-$进行相对测量。

Result: 信号显著性为$5.1σ$（包含系统不确定性），相对分支比测量值为$\left(5.13 \pm 1.28_{\rm stat} \pm 0.27_{\rm syst}\right)\times 10^{-2}$，测量区域为$m(h^+h^-)< 2.85$ GeV。

Conclusion: 首次成功观测到无粲纯重子衰变$Λ_b^{0} \to Λp \bar{p}$，为研究重子形成和强相互作用提供了重要实验数据，相对分支比的精确测量为理论模型验证奠定了基础。

Abstract: The first observation of a charmless purely baryonic decay, $Λ_b^{0} \to Λp \bar{p}$, is reported using the full Run 2 LHCb dataset, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $6.0~fb^{-1}$. The branching fraction is measured relative to that of the topologically similar normalisation mode $Λ_b^{0} \to ΛK^+K^-$. A simultaneous fit to the long- and downstream-track categories yields a signal significance of $5.1σ$ after including systematic uncertainties. The relative branching fraction is measured to be $\left(5.13 \pm 1.28_{\rm stat} \pm 0.27_{\rm syst}\right)\times 10^{-2}$ in the region $m(h^+h^-)< 2.85$ GeV.

</details>


### [284] [SemiCharmTag: a tool for Semileptonic Charm tagging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11574)
*Carolina Arata,Imanol Corredoira,Alisha Lightbody,Michael Winn*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于次级顶点强子径迹标记的方法，用于选择和/或拒绝来自粲夸克半轻衰变的轻子。该方法在LHCb的dimuon Drell-Yan测量中开发，通过背景抑制策略将信噪比提高约4倍，效率达81%，同时对Drell-Yan信号特性影响最小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在LHCb的dimuon Drell-Yan测量中，需要有效区分来自粲夸克半轻衰变（charm semileptonic decays）的背景轻子和Drell-Yan信号轻子。现有方法在背景抑制和信号保留之间存在平衡挑战，需要开发更精确的选择/拒绝策略。

Method: 提出基于次级顶点（secondary vertex）强子径迹标记的方法，利用质子-质子对撞的完整模拟在√s=13.6 TeV条件下开发。研究聚焦于不变质量范围2.9-5 GeV/c²且单μ子横向动量大于1 GeV/c的区域，详细阐述了两种策略：背景抑制策略和构建无偏背景纯样本的方法。

Result: 背景抑制策略在81%的效率下将信噪比（signal over background）提高约4倍，同时对Drell-Yan信号特性产生最小偏差。第二种方法构建了来自粲夸克衰变的单μ子无偏背景纯样本，在Drell-Yan效率为1.1%时实现了21.4%的粲夸克效率。

Conclusion: 该方法为LHCb实验中的dimuon Drell-Yan测量提供了有效的轻子选择/拒绝工具，显著改善了背景抑制能力，同时保持了信号完整性，并为粲夸克物理研究提供了高质量的背景样本。

Abstract: A method for selecting and/or rejecting leptons from charm semileptonic decays based on the tagging of the secondary vertex using a hadron track is introduced. The method is developed for dimuon Drell-Yan measurements in LHCb using full simulations in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV. We focus on the invariant mass range between 2.9 and 5 GeV/$c^2$ with single muon transverse momentum larger than 1 GeV/$c$. A novel strategy is detailed for background rejection, achieving an improvement of the signal over background of a factor $\sim 4$ at an efficiency of 81% with minimal bias on the Drell-Yan signal properties. Moreover, a second approach is presented for the construction of unbiased background-pure samples of single muons from charm decays, achieving a charm efficiency of 21.4% at a Drell-Yan efficiency of 1.1%.

</details>


### [285] [Rare top quark production and top quark properties in ATLAS and CMS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11586)
*Sergio Sánchez Cruz*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文回顾了ATLAS和CMS合作组对稀有顶夸克（top quark）产生过程的最新分析，这些过程包括多顶夸克产生以及与电弱规范玻色子（electroweak gauge bosons）的联合产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然稀有顶夸克产生过程的截面（cross section）远小于顶夸克对产生，但它们为顶夸克耦合（couplings）以及超出标准模型（beyond the standard model）的新物理效应提供了独特的探测灵敏度。

Method: 该论文采用综述方法，回顾了ATLAS和CMS合作组在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上进行的稀有顶夸克产生过程分析。

Result: 论文总结了多个稀有顶夸克产生过程的最新分析结果，包括多顶夸克产生和顶夸克与电弱规范玻色子的联合产生过程。

Conclusion: 稀有顶夸克产生过程虽然截面较小，但对于精确测量顶夸克性质和研究超出标准模型的新物理具有重要价值，ATLAS和CMS合作组的分析为此提供了重要数据。

Abstract: The production of top quark pairs is one of the most relevant production modes at the LHC, and allow for precise measurement of the properties of this particle. Top quarks are also produced through rarer mechanisms, including the production of multiple top quarks or the associated production of top quarks with electroweak gauge bosons. Although these processes have significantly smaller cross sections, they provide unique sensitivity to the couplings of the top quark and to possible effects of physics beyond the standard model (SM). This contribution reviews recent analyses of rare top quark production performed by the ATLAS and CMS Collaborations.

</details>


### [286] [Filtering hits for speeding up online track reconstruction at hadron colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11648)
*Andrea Coccaro,Carlo Schiavi,Alessandro Zaio*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于卷积神经网络（CNN）的新技术，用于在大型强子对撞机（LHC）实验中辅助径迹重建，通过过滤不必要的探测器信息来应对高亮度升级带来的计算挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型强子对撞机（LHC）实验面临高堆积顶点（pile-up vertices）导致的探测器层命中率极高的问题，使得径迹重建成为组合难题。未来高亮度大型强子对撞机（High-Luminosity LHC）升级将带来更高的探测器占用率，导致当前触发策略的计算成本显著增长。

Method: 提出了一种基于卷积神经网络（convolutional-neural-network, CNN）架构的新算法，该算法能够过滤掉不必要的探测器信息以辅助径迹重建。该架构设计便于在加速器卡上部署。

Result: 对该方法的性能影响进行了评估，并讨论了未来应用前景。该技术旨在解决高亮度升级带来的计算挑战，优化触发系统的径迹重建效率。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于卷积神经网络的过滤技术为应对未来高亮度大型强子对撞机升级带来的计算挑战提供了有前景的解决方案，能够有效辅助径迹重建并降低计算成本。

Abstract: Collider experiments are equipped with trigger systems that rapidly inspect the physics content emerging from collisions to decide whether the resulting products are worth saving for later analysis. One crucial aspect for analyzing the final states originating from the collisions is to process the information produced by charged particles in the innermost detectors to reconstruct the corresponding trajectories. This task is a challenge for the experiments running at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) at CERN because of the large number of secondary collisions per bunch crossing, the so-called pile-up vertices, giving rise to extremely high hit occupancies in the detector layers close to the beam line. Reconstructing tracks is a combinatorial problem and its processing time strongly depends on the average pile-up per event. The future accelerator-complex upgrade to the High-Luminosity LHC, implying even higher detector occupancies, will result in a considerable growth of the computational cost of the current trigger strategies. To face this issue, a new technique for assisting track reconstruction by filtering out unnecessary detector information is presented and characterized in this work. The algorithm is based on a convolutional-neural-network architecture which can be easily deployed on accelerator cards. The impact of this approach is assessed and future prospects are also discussed.

</details>


### [287] [Implementation and commissioning of an experimental system towards sub-eV axion-like particle searches with 0.1 PW laser at ELI-NP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11676)
*Yoshihide Nakamiya,Kensuke Homma,Madalin-Mihai Rosu,Liviu Neagu,Mihai Cuciuc,Vanessa Rozelle Maria Rodrigues,Stefan Ataman,Catalin Chiochiu,Georgiana Giubega,Kyle Juedes,Jonathan Tamlyn,Stefan Victor Tazlauanu,Yuri Kirita,Akihide Nobuhiro,Masaki Hashida,Shunsuke Inoue,Shuji Sakabe,Vicentiu Iancu,Dan-Gheorghita Matei,Mihai Risca,Anda-Maria Talposi,Ovidiu Tesileanu,Kazuo A. Tanaka,Calin Alexandru Ur*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究在ELI-NP激光设施中开发并调试了一个用于寻找类轴子粒子（ALPs）的实验系统，基于四波混频（FWM）原理，通过子系统集成实现了背景源识别，验证了系统性能并为激光能量逐步升级提供了平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是在全球10拍瓦级激光设施ELI-NP中开展类轴子粒子（axion-like particles, ALPs）的搜寻工作。需要开发专门的实验系统来探索这种可能的新物理现象。

Method: 方法基于四波混频（Four-Wave Mixing, FWM）过程，在共轴组合的两束激光的焦区进行。系统集成了控制真空压力、区域尺寸、时空重叠和触发事件模式的子系统，专门用于识别来自残余原子和光学元件的可能背景源。

Result: 通过评估激光特性、稳定性和FWM信号检测，验证了子系统的性能和功能。在真空压力为1.3×10⁻⁷ mbar条件下，使用20 mJ级激光脉冲展示了背景研究的调试结果。系统完全按设计功能运行。

Conclusion: 集成实验系统完全按设计功能运行，为ALP搜索的背景研究提供了合适平台。该系统支持激光脉冲能量从20 mJ逐步升级到0.1 PW实验区的最大能量2.5 J，为后续研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We have developed and commissioned an experimental system at ELI-NP towards searches for axion-like particles (ALPs) in the worldwide 10~PW-class laser facility. The search principle is based on the Four-Wave Mixing (FWM) process at a focal region of coaxially combined two laser beams. The subsystems to control vacuum pressure, area size, spatiotemporal overlap and trigger-event pattern, are integrated into the experimental area for 0.1 PW laser output at ELI-NP. The integrated system is dedicated to identifying the possible background sources originated from the residual atoms and the optical elements. The performance and functionality of the subsystems were validated through the evaluations of laser characteristics, their stability and the FWM signal detections. Furthermore commissioning results for the background studies were demonstrated with 20 mJ-level laser pulses at the vacuum pressure of $1.3 \times 10^{-7}$ mbar. In conclusion, the integrated experimental system is fully functional as designed and provides a suitable platform for the background studies towards the ALP searches, enabling a stepwise scale-up of the laser pulse energies from 20 mJ to the maximum energy of 2.5 J in the 0.1 PW experimental area.

</details>


### [288] [Neutron Reconstruction via Blips in Liquid Argon Time Projection Chambers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11774)
*Miguel Hernandez Morquecho,Bryce Littlejohn,Paola Sala,Linyan Wan*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在液态氩时间投影室（LArTPC）探测器中重建中子的模拟概念验证研究，利用中子非弹性散射产生的孤立MeV尺度能量沉积（blips）来识别中子并重建其方向和能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子是中微子相互作用中的重要未态粒子，但在当前大多数中微子LArTPC物理分析中未被考虑或重建。本研究旨在探索LArTPC探测器中子重建的可行性。

Method: 采用基于模拟的概念验证研究，利用中子非弹性散射产生的孤立MeV尺度能量沉积（blips），并基于已发表实验结果采用真实的blip响应模型。

Result: 研究证明了在亚GeV中微子相互作用中识别中子并重建未态中子系统的方向和能量的能力。探索了中子相关blip属性如何改进中微子相互作用物理研究。

Conclusion: 这项简单研究提供了LArTPC中子重建能力的初步量化评估，预计随着未来blip重建、识别、分类算法以及中子建模的进步，重建能力将得到提升。

Abstract: Neutrons are important final-state particles in neutrino interactions, yet they are not considered or reconstructed in most current neutrino LArTPC physics analyses. In this paper, we present a simulation-based proof-of-concept study of neutron reconstruction in a generic LArTPC detector. Leveraging isolated, MeV-scale energy deposits, or blips, from neutron inelastic scattering, and using realistic blip response from published experimental results, we demonstrate the capability to identify neutrons and to reconstruct the direction and energy of the final-state neutron system in sub-GeV neutrino interactions. We then explore how neutron-related blip attributes can be used to improve physics studies of neutrino interactions, such as enhancing neutrino-antineutrino separation in atmospheric neutrinos and reverse-horn-current beam neutrinos. This simple study provides an initial quantification of LArTPC neutron reconstruction capabilities, which we expect to improve with future advancements in blip reconstruction, identification, and classification algorithms, as well as the modeling of neutrons.

</details>
